 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet vyāsaṃ vasiṣṭhanaptāraṃ śakteḥ pautram akalmaṣam parāśarātmajaṃ vande śukatātaṃ taponidhim vyāsāya viṣṇurūpāya vyāsarūpāya viṣṇave namo vai brahmanidhaye vāsiṣṭhāya namo namaḥ janamejaya uvācaa kathaṃ yuyudhire vīrāḥ kurupāṇḍavasomakāḥc pārthivāś ca mahābhāgā nānādeśasamāgatāḥd pratyayudhyanta samare kārayām āsa vidhivat kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa śūnyeva pṛthivī sarvā bālavṛddhāvaśeṣitāc niraśvapuruṣā cāsīd rathakuñjaravarjitāa yāvat tapati sūryo hi jambūdvīpasya maṇḍalamc tāvad eva samāvṛttaṃ balaṃ pārthivasattamaa ekasthāḥ sarvavarṇās te maṇḍalaṃ bahuyojanamc paryākrāmanta deśāṃś ca nadīḥ śailān vanāni caa teṣāṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā sarveṣāṃ puruṣarṣabhac ādideśa savāhānāṃ bhakṣyabhojyam anuttamama saṃjñāś ca vividhās tās tās teṣāṃ cakre yudhiṣṭhiraḥc evaṃvādī veditavyaḥ pāṇḍaveyo yam ity utaa abhijñānāni sarveṣāṃ saṃjñāś cābharaṇāni cac yojayām āsa kauravyo yuddhakāla upasthitea dṛṣṭvā dhvajāgraṃ pārthānāṃ dhārtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥc saha sarvair mahīpālaiḥ pratyavyūhata pāṇḍavāna pāṇḍureṇātapatreṇa dhriyamāṇena mūrdhanic madhye nāgasahasrasya bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritama dṛṣṭvā sāgarayor ivaa śūnyāsīt pṛthivī sarvā bālavṛddhāvaśeṣitāc tena senāsamūhena samānītena kauravaiḥd tatas te samayaṃ yuddhe syāt prītiś ca parasparamd samantān nagakalpena garjamānena rvataḥa tatas te pravṛtte no vācaiva pratiyodhanamc niṣkrāntaḥ pṛtanāmadhyān na hantavyaḥ kathaṃ canaa rathī ca rathinā yodhyo gajena gajadhūrgataḥc aśvenāśvī padātiś ca padātenaiva bhārataa yathāyogaṃ yathāvīryaṃ smṛtiḥc kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca mānyaś cāsi pitāmahaḥd kuruṣva kāryaṃ yat satyaṃ tvatto mānyo na vidyate vyāsa uvācaa vaicitravīrya nṛpate yat te manasi vartatec abhidhatsva yathākāmaṃ chettāsmi tava saṃśayam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa yāni liṅgāni saṃgrāme bhavanti vijayiṣyatāmc tāni sarvāṇi bhagavañ śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ vyāsa uvācaa prasannabhāḥ pāvaka ūrdhvaraśmiḥpradakṣiṇāvartaśikho vidhūmaḥc puṇyā gandhāś cāhutīnāṃ pravāntijayasyaitad bhāvino rūpam āhuḥa gambhīraghoṣāś ca mahāsvanāś caśaṅkhā mṛdaṅgāś ca nadanti yatrac viśuddharaśmis tapanaḥ śaśī cajayasyaitad bhāvino rūpam āhuḥa iṣṭā vācaḥ pṛṣṭhato vāyasānāṃsaṃprasthitānāṃ ca gamiṣyatāṃ cac ye pṛṣṭhatas te tvarayanti rājanye tv agratas te pratiṣedhayantia kalyāṇavācaḥ śakunā rājahaṃsāḥśukāḥ krauñcāḥ śatapatrāś ca yatrac pradakṣiṇāś caiva bhavanti saṃkhyedhruvaṃ jayaṃ tatra vadanti viprāḥa alaṃkāraiḥ kavacaiḥ ketubhiś camukhaprasādair hemavarṇaiś ca nṝṇāmc bhrājiṣmatī duṣpratiprekṣaṇīyāyeṣāṃ camūs te vijayanti śatrūna hṛṣṭā vācas tathā sattvaṃ yodhānāṃ yatra bhāratac na mlāyante srajaś caiva te taranti raṇe ripūna iṣṭo vātaḥ praviṣṭasya dakṣiṇā pravivikṣataḥc paścāt saṃsādhayaty arthaṃ purastāt pratiṣedhatea śabdarūparasasparśagandhāś cāviṣkṛtāḥ śubhāḥc sadā yodhāś ca hṛṣṭāś ca yeṣāṃ teṣāṃ dhruvaṃ jayaḥa anv eva vāyavo vānti tathābhrāṇi vayāṃsi cac anuplavante meghāś ca tathaivendradhanūṃṣi caa etāni jayamānānāṃ lakṣaṇāni viśāṃ patec bhavanti viparītāni mumūrṣūṇāṃ janādhipaa alpāyāṃ vā mahatyāṃ vā senāyām iti niścitamc harṣo yodhagaṇasyaikaṃ jayalakṣaṇam ucyatea eko dīrṇo dārayati senāṃ sumahatīm apic taṃ dīrṇam anudīryante yodhāḥ śūratamā apia durnivāratamā caiva prabhagnā mahatī camūḥc apām iva mahāvegas trastā mṛgagaṇā ivaa naiva śakyā samādhātuṃ saṃnipāte mahācamūḥc dīrṇā ity eva dīryante yodhāḥ śūratamā apie bhītān bhagnāṃś ca saṃprekṣya bhayaṃ bhūyo vivardhatea prabhagnā sahasā rājan diśo vibhrāmitā paraiḥc naiva sthāpayituṃ śakyā śūrair api mahācamūḥa saṃbhṛtya mahatīṃ senāṃ caturaṅgāṃ mahīpatiḥb śaknoti na samādhātuṃ dīrṇām indrasamo yudhic upāyapūrvaṃ medhāvī yateta satatotthitaḥa upāyavijayaṃ śreṣṭham āhur bhedena madhyamamc jaghanya eṣa vijayo yo yuddhena viśāṃ patee mahādoṣaḥ saṃnipātas tato vyaṅgaḥ sa ucyatef paraspareṇa saṃdṛṣṭā surair api mahācamūḥf naiva sthāpayituṃ śakyā prabhagnā bhayavihvalāa parasparajñāḥ saṃhṛṣṭā vyavadhūtāḥ suniścitāḥc pañcāśad api ye śūrā mathnanti mahatīṃ camūme atha vā pañca ṣaṭ sapta vijayanty anivartinaḥa na vainateyo garuḍaḥ praśaṃsati mahājanamc dṛṣṭvā suparṇopacitiṃ mahatīm api bhārataa na bāhulyena senāyā jayo bhavati bhāratac adhruvo hi jayo nāma daivaṃ cātra parāyaṇame jayanto hy api saṃgrāme kṣayavanto bhavanty uta vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktvā yayau vyāso dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dhīmatec dhṛtarāṣṭro pi tac chrutvā dhyānam evānvapadyataa sa muhūrtam iva dhyātvā viniḥśvasya muhur muhuḥc saṃjayaṃ saṃśitātmānam apṛcchad bharatarṣabhaa saṃjayeme mahīpālāḥ śūrā yuddhābhinandinaḥc anyonyam abhinighnanti śastrair uccāvacair apia pārthivāḥ pṛthivīhetoḥ samabhityaktajīvitāḥc na ca śāmyanti nighnanto vardhayanto yamakṣayama bhaumam aiśvaryam icchanto na mṛṣyante parasparamc manye bahuguṇā bhūmis tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa bahūni ca sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni cac koṭyaś ca lokavīrāṇāṃ sametāḥ kurujāṅgalea deśānāṃ ca parīmāṇaṃ nagarāṇāṃ ca saṃjayac śrotum icchāmi tattvena yata ete samāgatāḥa divyabuddhipradīpena yuktas tvaṃ jñānacakṣuṣāc prasādāt tasya viprarṣer vyāsasyāmitatejasaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa yathāprajñaṃ mahāprājña bhaumān vakṣyāmi te guṇānc śāstracakṣur avekṣasva namas te bharatarṣabhaa dvividhānīha bhūtāni trasāni sthāvarāṇi cac trasānāṃ trividhā yonir aṇḍasvedajarāyujāḥa trasānāṃ khalu sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhā rājañ jarāyujāḥc jarāyujānāṃ pravarā mānavāḥ paśavaś ca yea nānārūpāṇi bibhrāṇās teṣāṃ bhedāś caturdaśac araṇyavāsinaḥ sapta saptaiṣāṃ grāmavāsinaḥa siṃhavyāghravarāhāś ca mahiṣā vāraṇās tathāc ṛkṣāś ca vānarāś caiva saptāraṇyāḥ smṛtā nṛpaa gaur ajo manujo meṣo vājyaśvataragardabhāḥc ete grāmyāḥ samākhyātāḥ paśavaḥ sapta sādhubhiḥa ete vai paśavo rājan grāmyāraṇyāś caturdaśac vedoktāḥ pṛthivīpāla yeṣu yajñāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥa grāmyāṇāṃ puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ siṃhaś cāraṇyavāsināmc sarveṣām eva bhūtānām anyonyenābhijīvanama udbhijjāḥ sthāvarāḥ proktās teṣāṃ pañcaiva jātayaḥc vṛkṣagulmalatāvallyas tvaksārās tṛṇajātayaḥa eṣāṃ viṃśatir ekonā mahābhūteṣu pañcasuc caturviṃśatir uddiṣṭā gāyatrī lokasaṃmatāa ya etāṃ veda gāyatrīṃ puṇyāṃ sarvaguṇānvitāmc tattvena bharataśreṣṭha sa lokān na praṇaśyatia bhūmau hi jāyate sarvaṃ bhūmau sarvaṃ praṇaśyatic bhūmiḥ pratiṣṭhā bhūtānāṃ bhūmir eva parāyaṇama yasya bhūmis tasya sarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamamc tatrābhigṛddhā rājāno vinighnantītaretaram dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa nadīnāṃ parvatānāṃ ca nāmadheyāni jagat sthitāni sarvāṇi samāny āhur manīṣiṇaḥa bhūmir āpas tathā vāyur agnir ākāśam eva cac guṇottarāṇi sarvāṇi teṣāṃ bhūmiḥ pradhānataḥa śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥc bhūmer ete guṇāḥ proktā ṛṣibhis tattvavedibhiḥd śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca rasaś cāpi prakīrtitāḥa catvāro psu guṇā rājan gandhas tatra na vidyatec śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca tejaso tha guṇās trayaḥe śabdaḥ sparśaś ca vāyos tu ākāśe śabda eva caa ete pañca guṇā rājan mahābhūteṣu pañcasuc vartante sarvalokeṣu yeṣu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥa anyonyaṃ nābhivartante sāmyaṃ bhavati vai yadāc yadā tu viṣamībhāvam aiśvarama tatra tatra hi dṛśyante dhātavaḥ pāñcabhautikāḥc teṣāṃ manuṣyās tarkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣatea acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvā na tāṃs tarkeṇa sādhayetc prakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yat tu tad acintyasya tato haimavataṃ paramb tataḥ kiṃpuruṣāvāsaṃ varṣaṃ himavataḥ paramc hemakūṭāt paraṃ caiva harivarṣaṃ pracakṣatea dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa cac prāgāyato mahārāja mālyavān nāma parvataḥa tataḥ paraṃ mālyavataḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥb tenaiva kramayogena parvato gandhamādanaḥc parimaṇḍalas tayor madhye meruḥ kanakaparvataḥa ādityataruṇābhāso vidhūma iva pāvakaḥc yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi prekṣya vāyasāna merur uttamamadhyānām adhamānāṃ ca pakṣiṇāmc aviśeṣakaro yasmāt tasmād enaṃ tyajāmy ahama tam ādityo nuparyeti satataṃ jyotiṣāṃ patiḥc candramāś ca sanakṣatro vāyuś caiva pradakṣiṇama rudraś ca śakraś cāpi sureśvaraḥc sametya vividhair yajñair yajante nekadakṣiṇaiḥa tumburur nāradaś caiva viśvāvasur hahā huhūḥc abhigamyāmaraśreṣṭhāḥ stavai stunvanti cābhibhoa saptarṣayo mahātmānaḥ kaśyapaś ca prajāpatiḥc tatra gacchanti bhadraṃ te sadā parvaṇi parvaṇia tasyaiva mūrdhany uśanāḥ kāvyo daityair mahīpatec tasya hīmāni ratnāni tasyeme ratnaparvatāḥa tasmāt kubero bhagavāṃś caturthaṃ bhāgam aśnutec tataḥ kalāṃśaṃ vittasya manuṣyebhyaḥ prayacchatia pārśve tasyottare divyaṃ sarvartukusumaṃ śivamc karṇikāravanaṃ ramyaṃ śilājālasamudgatama tatra sākṣāt paśupatir divyair bhūtaiḥ samāvṛtaḥc umāsahāyo bhagavān ramate bhūtabhāvanaḥa karṇikāramayīṃ mālāṃ bibhrat pādāvalambinīmc tribhir netraiḥ kṛtoddyotas tribhiḥ sūryair ivoditaiḥa tam ugratapasaḥ siddhāḥ suvratāḥ satyavādinaḥc paśyanti na hi durvṛttaiḥ śakyo draṣṭuṃ maheśvaraḥa tasya śailasya śikharāt kṣīradhārā nareśvarac triṃśad bāhuparigrāhyā bhīmanirghātanisvanāa puṇyā puṇyatamair juṣṭā gaṅgā bhāgīrathī śubhāc pataty ajasravegena hrade cāndramase śubhee tayā hy utpāditaḥ puṇyaḥ sa hradaḥ sāgaropamaḥa tāṃ dhārayām āsa purā durdharāṃ parvatair apic śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ śirasā vai maheśvaraḥa meros tu paścime pārśve ketumālo mahīpatec jambūṣaṇḍaś ca tatraiva sumahān nandanopamaḥa āyur daśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tatra bhāratac suvarṇavarṇāś ca narāḥ striyaś cāpsarasopamāḥa anāmayā vītaśokā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥc jāyante mānavās tatra niṣṭaptakanakaprabhāḥd pūrveṇa yasya vikhyātaḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥa gandhamādanaśṛṅgeṣu kuberaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥc saṃvṛto psarasāṃ saṃghair modate guhyakādhipaḥa gandhamādanapādeṣu pareṣv aparagaṇḍikāḥc ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ paramāyuṣaḥa tatra kṛṣṇā narā rājaṃs tejoyuktā mahābalāḥc striyaś cotpalapatrābhāḥ sarvāḥ supriyadarśanāḥa nīlāt parataraṃ śvetaṃ dakṣiṇottarec ilāvṛtaṃ madhyamaṃ tu pañca varṣāṇi caiva haa uttarottaram etebhyo varṣam udricyate guṇaiḥc āyuṣpramāṇam ārogyaṃ dharmataḥ kāmato rthataḥa samanvitāni bhūtāni teṣu varṣeṣu bhāratac evam devarṣigaṇapūjitaḥa asty uttareṇa kailāsaṃ mainākaṃ parvataṃ pratic hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ sumahān divyo maṇimayo giriḥa tasya pārśve mahad divyaṃ śubhaṃ kāñcanavālukamc ramyaṃ bindusaro nāma yatra rājā upāsyate tigmatejā vṛto bhūtaiḥ samāgataiḥe naranārāyaṇau brahmā manuḥ sthāṇuś ca pañcamaḥa tatra tripathagā devī prathamaṃ tu pratiṣṭhitāc brahmalokād apakrāntā saptadhā pratipadyatea vasvokasārā gandharvā niṣadhe śaile nīle brahmarṣayo nṛpae śṛṅgavāṃs tu mahārāja pitṝṇāṃ pratisaṃcaraḥa ity etāni mahārāja sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥc bhūtāny upaniviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi caa teṣām ṛddhir etad dvitīyaṃ dvīpasya dṛśyate śaśasaṃsthitam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa meror athottaraṃ pārśvaṃ pūrvaṃ cācakṣva saṃjayac nikhilena mahābuddhe mālyavantaṃ ca parvatam saṃjaya uvācaa dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya meroḥ pārśve tathottarec uttarāḥ kuravo rājan puṇyāḥ siddhaniṣevitāḥa tatra vṛkṣā madhuphalā nityapuṣpaphalopagāḥc puṣpāṇi ca sugandhīni rasavanti phalāni caa sarvakāmaphalās tatra ke cid vṛkṣā janādhipac apare kṣīriṇo nāma vṛkṣās tatra narādhipaa ye kṣaranti sadā kṣīraṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ hy amṛtopamamc vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣv ābharaṇāni caa sarvā maṇimayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣmakāñcanavālukāb maṇiratnanibhaṃ ramyaṃ vajravaiḍūryasaṃnibhamb bhūbhāgo dṛśyate tatra padmarāgasamaprabhamc sarvatra sukhasaṃsparśā niṣpaṅkā ca janādhipad puṣkariṇyaḥ śubhās tatra sukhasparśā manoharāḥa devalokacyutāḥ sarve jāyante tatra mānavāḥc tulyarūpaguṇopetāḥ sameṣu viṣameṣu caa mithunāni ca jāyante striyaś cāpsarasopamāḥc teṣāṃ te kṣīriṇāṃ kṣīraṃ pibanty amṛtasaṃnibhama mithunaṃ jāyamānaṃ vai samaṃ tac ca pravardhatec tulyarūpaguṇopetaṃ samaveṣaṃ tathaiva cae ekaikam anuraktaṃ ca cakravākasamaṃ vibhof mṛtyuś ca samakālaṃ ca tayor mithunayugmayoḥa nirāmayā vītaśokā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥc daśa varṣasahasrāṇi daśa varṣaśatāni cae jīvanti te mahārāja na cānyonyaṃ jahaty utaa bhāruṇḍā nāma śakunās tīkṣṇatuṇḍā mahābalāḥc te nirharanti hi mṛtān darīṣu prakṣipanti caa uttarāḥ kuravo rājan vyākhyātās te samāsataḥc meroḥ pārśvam ahaṃ pūrvaṃ vakṣyāmy atha yathātathamd bhadrāśvaṃ nāma varṣaṃ tu puro vai gandhamādanāta tasya pūrvābhiṣekas tu bhadrāśvasya viśāṃ patec bhadrasālavanaṃ yatra kālāmraś ca mahādrumaḥa kālāmraś ca mahārāja nityapuṣpaphalaḥ śubhaḥc dvīpaś ca yojanotsedhaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥa tatra te puruṣāḥ śvetās tejoyuktā mahābalāḥc striyaḥ kumudavarṇāś ca sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥa candraprabhāś candravarṇāḥ pūrṇacandranibhānanāḥc candraśītalagātryaś ca nṛttagītaviśāradāḥa daśa varṣasahasrāṇi tatrāyur bharatarṣabhac kālāmrarasapītās te nityaṃ saṃsthitayauvanāḥa dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tuc sudarśano nāma mahāñ jambūvṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥa sarvakāmaphalaḥ puṇyaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥc tasya nāmnā samākhyāto jambūdvīpaḥ sanātanaḥa yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ ca śataṃ ca bharatarṣabhac utsedho vṛkṣarājasya divaspṛṅ manujeśvaraa aratnīnāṃ sahasraṃ ca śatāni daśa pañca cac pariṇāhas tu vṛkṣasya phalānāṃ rasabhedināma patamānāni tāny urvyāṃ kurvanti vipulaṃ svanamc muñcanti ca rasaṃ rājaṃs tasmin rajatasaṃnibhama tasyā jambvāḥ phalaraso nadī bhūtvā janādhipac meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃprayāty uttarān kurūna pibanti tad rasaṃ hṛṣṭā janā nityaṃ janādhipac tasmin phalarase pīte na jarā bādhate ca tāna tatra jāmbūnadaṃ nāma kanakaṃ devabhūṣaṇamb indragopakasaṃkāśaṃ jāyate bhāsvaraṃ tu tatc taruṇādityavarṇāś ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥa tathā mālyavataḥ śṛṅge dīpyate tatra havyavāṭc nāmnā saṃvartako nāma kālāgnir bharatarṣabhaa tathā mālyavataḥ śṛṅge pūrve pūrvāntagaṇḍikāc yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi pañcāśan mālyavān sthitaḥa mahārajatasaṃkāśā jāyante tatra mānavāḥc brahmalokāc cyutāḥ sarve sarve ca brahmavādinaḥa tapas tu tapyamānās te bhavanti hy ūrdhvaretasaḥc rakṣaṇārthaṃ tu bhūtānāṃ praviśanti divākarama ṣaṣṭis tāni sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭir eva śatāni cac aruṇasyāgrato yānti parivārya divākarama ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭim eva śatāni cac ādityatāpataptās te viśanti śaśimaṇḍalam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa varṣāṇāṃ caiva nāmāni parvatānāṃ ca saṃjayac ācakṣva me yathātattvaṃ ye ca parvatavāsinaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa dakṣiṇena tu śvetasya nīlasyaivottareṇa tuc varṣaṃ ramaṇakaṃ nāma jāyante tatra mānavāḥa śuklābhijanasaṃpannāḥ sarve supriyadarśanāḥc ratipradhānāś ca tathā jāyante tatra mānavāḥa daśa varṣasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca cac jīvanti te mahārāja nityaṃ muditamānasāḥa dakṣiṇe śṛṅgiṇaś caiva śvetasyāthottareṇa cac varṣaṃ hairaṇvataṃ nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadīd yatra cāyaṃ mahārāja pakṣirāṭ patagottamaḥa yakṣānugā mahārāja dhaninaḥ priyadarśanāḥc mahābalās tatra sadā rājan muditamānasāḥd yakṣaḥ so pi mahārāja yakṣarājānugauta gottamaḥa ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te janādhipac āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca caa śṛṅgāṇi vai śṛṅgavatas trīṇy eva manujādhipac ekaṃ maṇimayaṃ tatra tathaikaṃ raukmam adbhutama sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ bhavanair upaśobhitamc tatra svayaṃprabhā devī nityaṃ vasati śāṇḍilīa uttareṇa tu śṛṅgasya samudrānte janādhipac varṣam airāvataṃ nāma tasmāc chṛṅgavataḥ parama na tatra sūryas tapati na te jīryanti mānavāḥc candramāś ca sanakṣatro jyotir bhūta ivāvṛtaḥa padmaprabhāḥ padmavarṇāḥ padmapatranibhekṣaṇāḥc padmapatrasugandhāś ca jāyante tatra mānavāḥa aniṣpandāḥ sugandhāś ca nirāhārā jitendriyāḥc devalokacyutāḥ sarve tathā virajaso nṛpaa trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te janādhipac āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti narā bharatasattamaa kṣīrodasya samudrasya tathaivottarataḥ prabhuḥc harir vasati vaikuṇṭhaḥ śakaṭe kanakātmakea aṣṭacakraṃ hi tad yānaṃ bhūtayuktaṃ manojavamc agnivarṇaṃ mahāvegaṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtama sa prabhuḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vibhuś ca bharatarṣabhac saṃkṣepo vistaraś caiva kartā kārayitā ca saḥa pṛthivy āpas tathākāśaṃ vāyus tejaś ca pārthivac sa yajñaḥ sarvabhūtānām āsyaṃ tasya hutāśanaḥd sthitaḥ sthānasahasreṣu vyāpya vai sa carācaram vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktaḥ saṃjayena dhṛtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥc dhyānam anvagamad rājā putrān prati janādhipaa sa vicintya mahārāja punar evābravīd vacaḥc asaṃśayaṃ sūtaputra kālaḥ saṃkṣipate jagate sṛjate ca punaḥ sarvaṃ neha vidyati jambūkhaṇḍas tvayā prokto yathāvad iha saṃjayac viṣkambham asya prabrūhi parimāṇaṃ ca tattvataḥa samudrasya pramāṇaṃ ca samyag acchidradarśanac śākadvīpaṃ ca me brūhi kuśadvīpaṃ ca saṃjayaa śālmalaṃ saṃjaya yat tvayāc prajāḥ kathaṃ sūtaputra saṃprāptāḥ śyāmatām iha saṃjaya uvācaa sarveṣv eva mahāprājña dvīpeṣu kurunandanac gauraḥ kṛṣṇaś ca varṇau dvau tayor varṇāntaraṃ nṛpaa śyāmo yasmāt pravṛtto pravibhāgaśaḥc varṣāṇi teṣu kauravya saṃproktāni manīṣibhiḥa mahāmerur mahākāśo jaladaḥ kumudottaraḥc jaladhārāt paro rājan sukumāra iti smṛtaḥa raivatasya tu kaumāraḥ śyāmasya tu maṇīcakaḥc mahāmṛdhec jigāyaikarathenaiva kāśipuryāṃ mahārathaḥa jāmadagnyaṃ raṇe rāmam āyodhya vasusaṃbhavaḥc na hato jāmadagnyena sa hato dya śikhaṇḍināa mahendrasadṛśaḥ śaurye sthairye ca himavān ivac samudra durutsahaḥa yaḥ spardhate raṇe nityaṃ jāmadagnyaṃ mahābalamc ajitaṃ jāmadagnyena śakratulyaparākramama taṃ hataṃ samare bhīṣmaṃ mahārathabalocitamc saṃjayācakṣva me vīraṃ yena śarma na vidmahea maurvīghoṣastanayitnuḥ pṛṣatkapṛṣato mahānc dhanurhvādamahāśabdo mahāmegha ivonnataḥa yad abhyavarṣat kaunteyān sapāñcālān sasṛñjayānc nighnan pararathān vīro dānavān iva vajrabhṛta iṣvastrasāgaraṃ ghoraṃ bāṇagrāhaṃ durāsadamc kārmukormiṇam akṣayyam advīpaṃ samare plavame gadāsimakarāvartaṃ hayagrāhaṃ gajākulamf padātimatsyakalilaṃ śaṅkhadundubhinisvanama hayān gajān padātāṃś ca rathāṃś ca tarasā bahūnc nimajjayantaṃ samare paravīrāpahāriṇama vidahyamānaṃ kopena tejasā ca paraṃtapamc veleva makarāvāsaṃ ke vīrāḥ paryavārayana bhīṣmo yad akarot karma samare saṃjayārihāc duryodhanahitārthāya ke tadāsya puro bhavana ke rakṣan dakṣiṇaṃ cakraṃ bhīṣmasyāmitatejasaḥc pṛṣṭhataḥ ke parān vīrā upāsedhan yatavratāḥa ke purastād avartanta rakṣanto bhīṣmam antikec ke rakṣann uttaraṃ cakraṃ vīrā vīrasya yudhyataḥa vāme cakre vartamānāḥ ke ghnan saṃjaya sṛñjayānc sametāgram anīkeṣu ke bhyarakṣan durāsadama pārśvataḥ ke bhyavartanta gacchanto durgamāṃ gatimc samūhe ke parān vīrān pratyayudhyanta saṃjayaa rakṣyamāṇaḥ kathaṃ vīrair gopyamānāś ca tena tec durjayānām anīkāni nājayaṃs tarasā yudhia sarvalokeśvarasyeva parameṣṭhiprajāpateḥc kathaṃ prahartum api te śekuḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavāḥa yasmin dvīpe samāśritya yudhyanti kuravaḥ paraiḥc taṃ nimagnaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmaṃ śaṃsasi saṃjayaa yasya vīrye samāśvasya mama putro bṛhadbalaḥc na pāṇḍavān agaṇayat kathaṃ sa nihataḥ paraiḥa yaḥ purā vibudhaiḥ sendraiḥ sāhāyye yuddhadurmadaḥc kāṅkṣito dānavān ghnadbhiḥ pitā mama mahāvrataḥa yasmiñ jāte mahāvīrye śaṃtanur lokaśaṃkarec śokaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca dainyaṃ ca prājahāt putralakṣmaṇia prajñā parāyaṇaṃ tajjñaṃ saddharmanirataṃ śucimc vedavedāṅgatattvajñaṃ kathaṃ śaṃsasi me hatama sarvāstravinayopetaṃ dāntaṃ śāntaṃ manasvinamc hataṃ śāṃtanavaṃ śrutvā manye śeṣaṃ balaṃ hatama dharmād adharmo balavān saṃprāpta iti me matiḥc yatra vṛddhaṃ guruṃ hatvā rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥa jāmadagnyaḥ purā rāmaḥ sarvāstravid anuttamaḥc ambārtham udyataḥ saṃkhye bhīṣmeṇa yudhi nirjitaḥa tam indrasamakarmāṇaṃ kakudaṃ sarvadhanvināmc hataṃ śaṃsasi bhīṣmaṃ me kiṃ nu duḥkham ataḥ parama asakṛt kṣatriyavrātāḥ saṃkhye yena vinirjitāḥc jāmadagnyas tathā rāmaḥ paravīranighātinād na hato yo mahābuddhiḥ sa hato dya śikhaṇḍināa tasmān nūnaṃ mahāvīryād bhārgavād yuddhadurmadātc tejovīryabalair bhūyāñ śikhaṇḍī drupadātmajaḥa yaḥ śūraṃ kṛtinaṃ yuddhe sarvaśāstraviśāradamc paramāstravidaṃ vīraṃ jaghāna bharatarṣabhama ke vīrās tam amitraghnam anvayuḥ śatrusaṃsadic śaṃsa me tad yathā vṛttaṃ yuddhaṃ bhīṣmasya pāṇḍavaiḥa yoṣeva hatavīrā me senā putrasya saṃjayac agopam iva codbhrāntaṃ gokulaṃ tad balaṃ mamaa pauruṣaṃ sarvalokasya paraṃ yasya mahāhavec parāsikte ca vas tasmin katham āsīn manas tadāa jīvite py adya sāmarthyaṃ kim ivāsmāsu saṃjayac ghātayitvā mahāvīryaṃ pitaraṃ lokadhārmikama agādhe salile magnāṃ nāvaṃ dṛṣṭveva pāragāḥc bhīṣme hate bhṛśaṃ duḥkhān manye śocanti putrakāḥa adrisāramayaṃ nūnaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ hṛdayaṃ mamac yac chrutvā puruṣavyāghraṃ hataṃ bhīṣmaṃ na dīryatea yasminn astraṃ ca medhā ca nītiś ca bharatarṣabhec aprameyāṇi durdharṣe kathaṃ sa nihato yudhia na cāstreṇa na śauryeṇa tapasā medhayā na cac na dhṛtyā na punas tyāgān mṛtyoḥ kaś cid vimucyatea kālo nūnaṃ mahāvīryaḥ sarvalokaduratyayaḥc yatra śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ hataṃ śaṃsasi saṃjayaa putraśokābhisaṃtapto mahad duḥkham acintayanc āśaṃse haṃ purā trāṇaṃ bhīṣmāc chaṃtanunandanāta yadādityam ivāpaśyat patitaṃ bhuvi saṃjayac duryodhanaḥ śāṃtanavaṃ kiṃ tadā pratyapadyataa nāhaṃ sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ vā buddhyā saṃjaya cintayanc śeṣaṃ kiṃ cit prapaśyāmi pratyanīke mahīkṣitāma dāruṇaḥ kṣatradharmo yam ṛṣibhiḥ saṃpradarśitaḥc yatra śāṃtanavaṃ hatvā rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥa vayaṃ vā rājyam icchāmo ghātayitvā pitāmahamc kṣatradharme sthitāḥ pārthā nāparādhyanti putrakāḥa etad āryeṇa kartavyaṃ kṛcchrāsv āpatsu saṃjayac parākramaḥ paraṃ śaktyā tac ca tasmin pratiṣṭhitama anīkāni vinighnantaṃ hrīmantam aparājitamc kathaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ tāta pāṇḍuputrā nyapātayana kathaṃ yuktāny anīkāni kathaṃ yuddhaṃ mahātmabhiḥc kathaṃ vā nihato bhīṣmaḥ pitā saṃjaya me paraiḥa duryodhanaś ca karṇaś ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥc duḥśāsanaś ca kitavo hate bhīṣme kim abruvana yac charīrair upastīrṇāṃ naravāraṇavājināmc śaraśaktigadākhaḍgatomarākṣāṃ bhayāvahāma prāviśan kitavā mandāḥ sabhāṃ yudhi durāsadāmc prāṇadyūte pratibhaye ke dīvyanta nararṣabhāḥa ke jayan ke jitās tatra hṛtalakṣā nipātitāḥc anye bhīṣmāc chāṃtanavāt tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa na hi me śāntir astīha yudhi devavrataṃ hatamc pitaraṃ bhīmakarmāṇaṃ śrutvā me duḥkham āviśata ārtiṃ me hṛdaye rūḍhāṃ mahatīṃ putrakāritāmc tvaṃ siñcan sarpiṣevāgnim uddīpayasi saṃjayaa mahāntaṃ bhāram udyamya viśrutaṃ sārvalaukikamb taṃ vimagnaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmaṃ śaṃsasi saṃjayac dṛṣṭvā vinihataṃ bhīṣmaṃ manye śocanti putrakāḥa śroṣyāmi tāni duḥkhāni duryodhanakṛtāny ahamc tasmān me sarvam ācakṣva yad vṛttaṃ tatra saṃjayaa saṃgrāme pṛthivīśānāṃ mandasyābuddhisaṃbhavamc apanītaṃ sunītaṃ vā tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa yat kṛtaṃ tatra bhīṣmeṇa saṃgrāme jayam icchatāc tejoyuktaṃ kṛtāstreṇa śaṃsa tac cāpy aśeṣataḥa yathā tad abhavad yuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥc krameṇa yena yasmiṃś ca kāle yac ca yathā ca tatd yac ca yasmiṃś ca kāle ca vṛttaṃ yac ca yathā ca tat saṃjaya uvācaa tvadyukto yam anupraśno mahārāja yathārhasic na tu duryodhane doṣam imam āsaktum arhasia ya ātmano duścaritād aśubhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥc enasā tena nānyaṃ sa vanea hayānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca śūrāṇāṃ cāmitaujasāmc pratyakṣaṃ yan mayā dṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yogabalena caa śṛṇu tat pṛthivīpāla mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥc diṣṭam etat purā nūnam evaṃbhāvi narādhipaa namaskṛtvā pitus te haṃ pārāśaryāya dhīmatec yasya prasādād divyaṃ me prāptaṃ jñānam anuttamama dṛṣṭiś cātīndriyā rājan dūrāc chravaṇam eva cac paracittasya vijñānam atītānāgatasya caa vyutthitotpattivijñānam ca sudakṣiṇaḥd bhagadatto mahāvīryaḥ kausalyaś ca bṛhadrathaḥa śrutāyudhaś ca kāliṅgo jayatsenaś ca pārthivaḥc bṛhadbalaś ca kauśalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥa daśaite puruṣavyāghrāḥ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥc akṣauhiṇīnāṃ patayo yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥa ete cānye ca bahavo duryodhanavaśānugāḥc rājāno rājaputrāś ca nītimanto mahābalāḥa saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta sveṣv anīkeṣv avasthitāḥc baddhakṛṣṇājināḥ sarve dhvajino muñjamālinaḥa sṛṣṭā duryodhanasyārthe brahmalokāya dīkṣitāḥc samṛddhā daśa vāhinyaḥ parigṛhya vyavasthitāḥa ekādaśī dhārtarāṣṭrī kauravāṇāṃ mahācamūḥc agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ yatra śāṃtanavo graṇīḥa śvetoṣṇīṣaṃ śvetahayaṃ śvetavarmāṇam acyutamc apaśyāma mahārāja bhīṣmaṃ candram ivoditama hematāladhvajaṃ bhīṣmaṃ rājate syandane sthitamc śvetābhra iva tīkṣṇāṃśuṃ dadṛśuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥa dṛṣṭvā camūmukhe bhīṣmaṃ samakampanta pāṇḍavāḥc sṛñjayāś ca maheṣvāsā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥa jṛmbhamāṇaṃ mahāsiṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣudramṛgā yathāc dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhāḥ sarve samudvivijire muhuḥa ekādaśaitāḥ śrījuṣṭā vāhinyas tava bhāratac pāṇḍavānāṃ tathā sapta mahāpuruṣapālitāḥa unmattamakarāvartau mahāgrāhasamākulauc yugānte samupetau dvau dṛśyete sāgarāv ivaa naiva nas tādṛśo rājan dṛṣṭapūrvo na ca śrutaḥc anīkānāṃ sametānāṃ samavāyas tathāvidhaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ubhayoḥ senayos tatra dṛṣṭvā ca kurupāṇḍavān animittāny atho brūhi kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa yathā sa bhagavān vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano bravītc tathaiva sahitāḥ sarve samājagmur mahīkṣitaḥa maghāviṣayagaḥ somas tad dinaṃ pratyapadyatac dīpyamānāś ca saṃpetur divi sapta mahāgrahāḥa dvidhābhūta ivāditya udaye pratyadṛśyatac jvalantyā śikhayā bhūyo bhānumān udito divia vavāśire ca dīptāyāṃ diśi gomāyuvāyasāḥc lipsamānāḥ śarīrāṇi māṃsaśoṇitabhojanāḥa ahany ahani pārthānāṃ vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥc bharadvājātmajaś caiva prātar utthāya saṃyataua jayo stu pāṇḍuputrāṇām ity ūcatur ariṃdamauc yuyudhāte tavārthāya yathā sa samayaḥ kṛtaḥa sarvadharmaviśeṣajñaḥ pitā devavratas tavac samānīya mahīpālān idaṃ vacanam abravīta idaṃ vaḥ kṣatriyā dvāraṃ svargāyāpāvṛtaṃ mahatc gacchadhvaṃ tena śakrasya brahmaṇaś ca salokatāma eṣa vaḥ śāśvataḥ panthāḥ pūrvaiḥ pūrvatarair gataḥc saṃbhāvayata cātmānam avyagramanaso yudhia nābhāgo hi yayātiś ca māndhātā nahuṣo nṛgaḥb arjunaḥ sagaro vainyo ye cānye kṣatriyottamāḥc saṃsiddhāḥ paramaṃ sthānaṃ gatāḥ karmabhir īdṛśaiḥa adharmaḥ kṣatriyasyaiṣa yad vyādhimaraṇaṃ gṛhec yad ājau nidhanaṃ yāti so sya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥa evam uktā mahīpālā bhīṣmeṇa bharatarṣabhac niryayuḥ svāny anīkāni śobhayanto rathottamaiḥa sa tu vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ sāmātyaḥ saha bandhubhiḥc nyāsitaḥ samare śastraṃ bhīṣmeṇa bharatarṣabhaa apetakarṇāḥ putrās te rājānaś caiva tāvakāḥc niryayuḥ siṃhanādena nādayanto diśo daśaa śvetaiś chatraiḥ patākābhir dhvajavāraṇavājibhiḥc tāny anīkāny aśobhanta rathair atha padātibhiḥa bherīpaṇavaśabdaiś ca paṭahānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥc rathanemininādaiś ca babhūvākulitā mahīa kāñcanāṅgadakeyūraiḥ kārmukaiś ca mahārathāḥc bhrājamānā vyadṛśyanta jaṅgamāḥ parvatā ivaa tālena mahatā bhīṣmaḥ pañcatāreṇa ketunāc vimalādityasaṃkāśas tasthau kurucamūpatiḥa ye tvadīyā maheṣvāsā rājāno bharatarṣabhab putrāś ca tava rājendra sārohā sarathā gajaiḥc avartanta yathādeśaṃ rājañ śāṃtanavasya tea sa tu govāsanaḥ śaibyaḥ sahitaḥ sarvarājabhiḥc yayau mātaṅgarājena rājārheṇa patākināe padmavarṇas tv anīkānāṃ sarveṣām agrataḥ sthitaḥa aśvatthāmā yayau yattaḥ siṃhalāṅgūlaketanaḥc śrutāyuś citrasenaś ca purumitro viviṃśatiḥa śalyo bhūriśravāś caiva vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥc ete sapta maheṣvāsā droṇaputrapurogamāḥe syandanair varavarṇābhair bhīṣmasyāsan puraḥsarāḥa teṣām api mahotsedhāḥ śobhayanto rathottamānc bhrājamānā vyadṛśyanta jāmbūnadamayā dhvajāḥa jāmbūnadamayī vediḥ kamaṇḍaluvibhūṣitāc ketur ācāryamukhyasya droṇasya dhanuṣā sahaa anekaśatasāhasram anīkam anukarṣataḥc mahān duryodhanasyāsīn nāgo maṇimayo dhvajaḥa tasya pauravakāliṅgau kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥc kṣemadhanvā sumitraś ca tasthuḥ pramukhato rathāḥa syandanena mahārheṇa ketunā vṛṣabheṇa cac prakarṣann iva senāgraṃ māgadhaś ca nṛpo yayaua tad aṅgapatinā guptaṃ kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanāc śāradābhracayaprakhyaṃ prācyānām abhavad balama anīkapramukhe tiṣṭhan varāheṇa mahāyaśāḥc śuśubhe ketumukhyena rājatena jayadrathaḥa śataṃ rathasahasrāṇāṃ tasyāsan vaśavartinaḥc aṣṭau nāgasahasrāṇi sādinām ayutāni ṣaṭa tat sindhupatinā rājan kekayās tathāc sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcyodīcyamālavāḥa dvādaśaite janapadāḥ sarve śūrās tanutyajaḥc mahatā rathavaṃśena te bhyarakṣan pitāmahama anīkaṃ daśasāhasraṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvināmc sukhinaḥ syāma mādhavaa yady apy ete na paśyanti lobhopahatacetasaḥc kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ mitradrohe ca pātakama kathaṃ na jñeyam asmābhiḥ pāpād asmān nivartitumc kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ prapaśyadbhir janārdanaa kulakṣaye praṇaśyanti kuladharmāḥ sanātanāḥc dharme naṣṭe kulaṃ kṛtsnam adharmo bhibhavaty utaa adharmābhibhavāt kṛṣṇa praduṣyanti kulastriyaḥc strīṣu duṣṭāsu vārṣṇeya jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥa saṃkaro narakāyaiva kulaghnānāṃ kulasya cac patanti pitaro hy eṣāṃ luptapiṇḍodakakriyāḥa doṣair etaiḥ kulaghnānāṃ varṇasaṃkarakārakaiḥc utsādyante jātidharmāḥ kuladharmāś ca śāśvatāḥa utsannakuladharmāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ janārdanac narake niyataṃ vāso bhavatīty anuśuśrumaa aho bata mahat pāpaṃ kartuṃ vyavasitā vayamc yad rājyasukhalobhena hantuṃ svajanam udyatāḥa yadi mām apratīkāram caiva na bhaviṣyāmaḥ sarve vayam ataḥ parama dehino smin yathā dehe kaumāraṃ yauvanaṃ jarāc tathā dehāntaraprāptir dhīras tatra na muhyatia mātrāsparśās tu kaunteya śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkhadāḥc āgamāpāyino nityās tāṃs titikṣasva bhārataa yaṃ hi na vyathayanty ete puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabhac samaduḥkhasukhaṃ dhīraṃ so mṛtatvāya kalpatea nāsato vidyate bhāvo nābhāvo vidyate sataḥc ubhayor api dṛṣṭo ntas tv anayos tattvadarśibhiḥa avināśi tu tad viddhi yena sarvam idaṃ tatamc vināśam avyayasyāsya na kaś cit kartum arhatia antavanta ime dehā nityasyoktāḥ śarīriṇaḥc anāśino prameyasya tasmād yudhyasva bhārataa ya enaṃ vetti hantāraṃ yaś cainaṃ manyate hatamc ubhau tau na vijānīto nāyaṃ hanti na hanyatea na jāyate mriyate vā kadā cinnāyaṃ bhūtvā bhavitā vā na bhūyaḥc ajo nityaḥ śāśvato yaṃ purāṇona hanyate hanyamāne śarīrea vedāvināśinaṃ nityaṃ ya enam ajam avyayamc kathaṃ sa puruṣaḥ pārtha kaṃ ghātayati hanti kama vāsāṃsi jīrṇāni yathā vihāyanavāni gṛhṇāti naro parāṇic tathā śarīrāṇi vihāya jīrṇānyanyāni saṃyāti navāni dehīa nainaṃ chindanti śastrāṇi nainaṃ dahati pāvakaḥc na cainaṃ kledayanty āpo na śoṣayati mārutaḥa acchedyo yam adāhyo yam akledyo śoṣya eva cac nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sthāṇur acalo yaṃ sanātanaḥa avyakto yam acintyo yam avikāryo yam ucyatec tasmād evaṃ viditvainaṃ nānuśocitum arhasia atha cainaṃ nityajātaṃ nityaṃ vā manyase mṛtamc tathāpi tvaṃ mahābāho nainaṃ śocitum arhasia jātasya hi dhruvo mṛtyur dhruvaṃ janma mṛtasya cac tasmād aparihārye rthe na tvaṃ śocitum arhasia avyaktādīni bhūtāni vyaktamadhyāni bhāratac avyaktanidhanāny eva tatra kā paridevanāa āścaryavat paśyati kaś cid enamāścaryavad vadati tathaiva cānyaḥc āścaryavac cainam anyaḥ śṛṇotiśrutvāpy enaṃ veda na caiva kaś cita dehī nityam avadhyo yaṃ dehe sarvasya bhāratac tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni na tvaṃ śocitum arhasia svadharmam api cāvekṣya na vikampitum arhasic dharmyād dhi yuddhāc chreyo nyat kṣatriyasya na vidyatea yadṛcchayā copapannaṃ svargadvāram apāvṛtamc sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pārtha labhante yuddham īdṛśama atha cet tvam imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ na kariṣyasic tataḥ svadharmaṃ kīrtiṃ ca hitvā pāpam avāpsyasia akīrtiṃ cāpi bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti te vyayāmc saṃbhāvitasya cākīrtir maraṇād atiricyatea bhayād raṇād uparataṃ maṃsyante tvāṃ mahārathāḥc yeṣāṃ ca tvaṃ bahumato bhūtvā yāsyasi lāghavama avācyavādāṃś ca bahūn vadiṣyanti tavāhitāḥc nindantas tava sāmarthyaṃ tato duḥkhataraṃ nu kima hato vā prāpsyasi svargaṃ jitvā vā bhokṣyase mahīmc tasmād uttiṣṭha kaunteya yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥa sukhaduḥkhe same kṛtvā lābhālābhau jayājayauc tato yuddhāya yujyasva naivaṃ pāpam avāpsyasia eṣā te bhihitā sāṃkhye buddhir yoge tv imāṃ śṛṇuc buddhyā yukto yayā pārtha karmabandhaṃ prahāsyasia nehābhikramanāśo sti pratyavāyo na vidyatec svalpam apy asya dharmasya trāyate mahato bhayāta vyavasāyātmikā buddhir ekeha kurunandanac bahuśākhā hy anantāś ca buddhayo vyavasāyināma yām imāṃ puṣpitāṃ vācaṃ pravadanty avipaścitaḥc vedavādaratāḥ pārtha nānyad astīti vādinaḥa kāmātmānaḥ svargaparā janmakarmaphalapradāmc kriyāviśeṣabahulāṃ bhogaiśvaryagatiṃ pratia bhogaiśvaryaprasaktānāṃ tayāpahṛtacetasāmc vyavasāyātmikā buddhiḥ samādhau na vidhīyatea traiguṇyaviṣayā vedā nistraiguṇyo bhavārjunac nirdvaṃdvo nityasattvastho niryogakṣema ātmavāna yāvān artha udapāne sarvataḥ saṃplutodakec tāvān sarveṣu vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥa karmaṇy evādhikāras te mā phaleṣu kadā canac mā karmaphalahetur bhūr mā te saṅgo stv akarmaṇia yogasthaḥ kuru karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā dhanaṃjayac siddhyasiddhyoḥ samo bhūtvā samatvaṃ yoga ucyated yasya sarve samārambhā nirāśīrbandhanās tv ihad tyāge yasya hutaṃ sarvaṃ sa tyāgī sa ca buddhimāna dūreṇa hy avaraṃ karma buddhiyogād dhanaṃjayac buddhau śaraṇam anviccha kṛpaṇāḥ phalahetavaḥa buddhiyukto jahātīha ubhe sukṛtaduṣkṛtec tasmād yogāya yujyasva yogaḥ karmasu kauśalama karmajaṃ buddhiyuktā hi phalaṃ tyaktvā manīṣiṇaḥc janmabandhavinirmuktāḥ padaṃ gacchanty anāmayama yadā te mohakalilaṃ buddhir vyatitariṣyatic tadā gantāsi nirvedaṃ śrotavyasya śrutasya caa śrutivipratipannā te yadā sthāsyati niścalāc samādhāv acalā buddhis tadā yogam avāpsyasi arjuna uvācaa sthitaprajñasya kā bhāṣā samādhisthasya keśavac sthitadhīḥ kiṃ prabhāṣeta kim āsīta vrajeta kim śrībhagavān uvācaa prajahāti yadā kāmān sarvān pārtha manogatānc ātmany evātmanā tuṣṭaḥ sthitaprajñas tadocyatea duḥkheṣv anudvignamanāḥ sukheṣu vigataspṛhaḥc vītarāgabhayakrodhaḥ sthitadhīr munir ucyatea yaḥ sarvatrānabhisnehas tat tat prāpya śubhāśubhamc nābhinandati na dveṣṭi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitāa yadā saṃharate cāyaṃ kūrmo ṅgānīva sarvaśaḥc indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyas tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitāa viṣayā vinivartante nirāhārasya dehinaḥc rasavarjaṃ raso py asya paraṃ dṛṣṭvā nivartatea yatato hy api kaunteya puruṣasya vipaścitaḥc indriyāṇi pramāthīni haranti prasabhaṃ manaḥa tāni sarvāṇi saṃyamya yukta āsīta matparaḥc vaśe hi yasyendriyāṇi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitāa dhyāyato viṣayān puṃsaḥ saṅgas teṣūpajāyatec saṅgāt saṃjāyate kāmaḥ kāmāt krodho bhijāyatea krodhād bhavati saṃmohaḥ saṃmohāt smṛtivibhramaḥc smṛtibhraṃśād buddhināśo buddhināśāt praṇaśyatia rāgadveṣaviyuktais tu viṣayān indriyaiś caranc ātmavaśyair vidheyātmā prasādam adhigacchatia prasāde sarvaduḥkhānāṃ hānir asyopajāyatec prasannacetaso hy āśu buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhatea nāsti buddhir ayuktasya na cāyuktasya bhāvanāc na cābhāvayataḥ śāntir aśāntasya kutaḥ sukhama indriyāṇāṃ hi caratāṃ yan mano nuvidhīyatec tad asya harati prajñāṃ vāyur nāvam ivāmbhasia tasmād yasya mahābāho nigṛhītāni sarvaśaḥc indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyas tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitāa yā niśā sarvabhūtānāṃ tasyāṃ jāgarti saṃyamīc yasyāṃ jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyato muneḥa āpūryamāṇam acalapratiṣṭhaṃsamudram āpaḥ praviśanti yadvatc tadvat kāmā yaṃ praviśanti sarvesa śāntim āpnoti na kāmakāmīa vihāya kāmān yaḥ sarvān pumāṃś carati niḥspṛhaḥc nirmamo nirahaṃkāraḥ sa śāntim adhigacchatia eṣā brāhmī sthitiḥ pārtha naināṃ prāpya vimuhyatic sthitvāsyām antakāle pi brahmanirvāṇam ṛcchati arjuna uvācaa jyāyasī cet karmaṇas te matā buddhir janārdanac tat kiṃ karmaṇi ghore māṃ niyojayasi keśavaa vyāmiśreṇaiva vākyena buddhiṃ mohayasīva mec tad ekaṃ vada niścitya yena śreyo ham āpnuyām śrībhagavān uvācaa loke smin dvividhā niṣṭhā purā proktā mayānaghac jñānayogena sāṃkhyānāṃ karmayogena yogināma na karmaṇām anārambhān naiṣkarmyaṃ puruṣo śnutec na ca saṃnyasanād eva siddhiṃ samadhigacchatia na hi kaś cit kṣaṇam api jātu tiṣṭhaty akarmakṛtc kāryate hy avaśaḥ karma sarvaḥ prakṛtijair guṇaiḥa karmendriyāṇi saṃyamya ya āste manasā smaranc indriyārthān vimūḍhātmā mithyācāraḥ sa ucyatea yas tv indriyāṇi manasā niyamyārabhate rjunac karmendriyaiḥ karmayogam asaktaḥ sa viśiṣyatea niyataṃ kuru karma tvaṃ karma jyāyo hy akarmaṇaḥc śarīrayātrāpi ca te na prasidhyed akarmaṇaḥa yajñārthāt karmaṇo nyatra loko yaṃ karmabandhanaḥc tadarthaṃ karma kaunteya muktasaṅgaḥ samācaraa sahayajñāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā purovāca prajāpatiḥc anena prasaviṣyadhvam eṣa vo stv iṣṭakāmadhuka devān bhāvayatānena te devā bhāvayantu vaḥc parasparaṃ bhāvayantaḥ śreyaḥ param avāpsyathaa iṣṭān bhogān hi vo devā dāsyante yajñabhāvitāḥc tair dattān apradāyaibhyo yo bhuṅkte stena eva saḥa yajñaśiṣṭāśinaḥ santo mucyante sarvakilbiṣaiḥc bhuñjate te tv aghaṃ pāpā ye pacanty ātmakāraṇāta annād bhavanti bhūtāni parjanyād annasaṃbhavaḥc yajñād bhavati parjanyo yajñaḥ karmasamudbhavaḥa karma brahmodbhavaṃ viddhi brahmākṣarasamudbhavamc tasmāt sarvagataṃ brahma nityaṃ yajñe pratiṣṭhitama evaṃ pravartitaṃ cakraṃ nānuvartayatīha yaḥc aghāyur indriyārāmo moghaṃ pārtha sa jīvatia yas tv ātmaratir eva syād ātmatṛptaś ca mānavaḥc ātmany eva ca saṃtuṣṭas tasya kāryaṃ na vidyatea naiva tasya kṛtenārtho nākṛteneha kaś canac na cāsya sarvabhūteṣu kaś cid arthavyapāśrayaḥa tasmād asaktaḥ satataṃ kāryaṃ karma samācarac asakto hy ācaran karma param āpnoti pūruṣaḥa karmaṇaiva hi saṃsiddhim āsthitā janakādayaḥc lokasaṃgraham evāpi saṃpaśyan kartum arhasia yad yad ācarati śreṣṭhas tat tad evetaro janaḥc sa yat pramāṇaṃ kurute lokas tad anuvartatea na me pārthāsti kartavyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kiṃ canac nānavāptam avāptavyaṃ varta eva ca karmaṇia yadi hy ahaṃ na varteyaṃ jātu karmaṇy atandritaḥc mama vartmānuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśaḥa utsīdeyur ime lokā na kuryāṃ karma ced ahamc saṃkarasya ca kartā syām upahanyām imāḥ prajāḥa saktāḥ karmaṇy avidvāṃso yathā kurvanti bhāratac kuryād vidvāṃs tathāsaktaś cikīrṣur lokasaṃgrahama na buddhibhedaṃ janayed ajñānāṃ karmasaṅgināmc joṣayet sarvakarmāṇi vidvān yuktaḥ samācarana prakṛteḥ kriyamāṇāni guṇaiḥ karmāṇi sarvaśaḥc ahaṃkāravimūḍhātmā kartāham iti manyatea tattvavit tu mahābāho guṇakarmavibhāgayoḥc guṇā guṇeṣu vartanta iti matvā na sajjatea prakṛter guṇasaṃmūḍhāḥ sajjante guṇakarmasuc tān akṛtsnavido mandān kṛtsnavin na vicālayeta mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi saṃnyasyādhyātmacetasāc nirāśīr nirmamo bhūtvā yudhyasva vigatajvaraḥa ye me matam idaṃ nityam anutiṣṭhanti mānavāḥc śraddhāvanto nasūyanto mucyante te pi karmabhiḥa ye tv etad abhyasūyanto nānutiṣṭhanti me matamc sarvajñānavimūḍhāṃs tān viddhi naṣṭān acetasaḥa sadṛśaṃ ceṣṭate svasyāḥ prakṛter jñānavān apic prakṛtiṃ yānti bhūtāni nigrahaḥ kiṃ kariṣyatia indriyasyendriyasyārthe rāgadveṣau vyavasthitauc tayor na vaśam āgacchet tau hy asya paripanthinaua śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitātc svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ arjuna uvācaa atha kena prayukto yaṃ pāpaṃ carati pūruṣaḥc anicchann api vārṣṇeya balād iva niyojitaḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa kāma eṣa krodha eṣa rajoguṇasamudbhavaḥc mahāśano mahāpāpmā viddhy enam iha vairiṇamd arjuna uvācad bhavaty eṣa kathaṃ kṛṣṇa kathaṃ caiva vivardhated śrībhagavān uvācad kim ātmakaḥ kim ācāras tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥd eṣa sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ śatrur dehinām indriyaiḥ sahad sukhatantra ivāsīno mohayan pārtha tiṣṭhatid kāmakrodhamayo ghoraḥ stambhaharṣasamudbhavaḥd ahaṃkāro bhimānātmā dustaraḥ pāpakarmabhiḥd harṣam asya nivartyaiṣa śokam asya dadāti cad bhayaṃ cāsya karoty eṣa mohayaṃs tu muhur muhuḥd sa eṣa kaluṣaḥ kṣudraś chidraprekṣī dhanaṃjayad rajaḥpravṛtto mohātmā manuṣyāṇām upadravaḥa dhūmenāvriyate vahnir yathādarśo malena cac yatholbenāvṛto garbhas tathā tenedam āvṛtama āvṛtaṃ jñānam etena jñānino nityavairiṇāc kāmarūpeṇa kaunteya duṣpūreṇānalena caa indriyāṇi mano buddhir asyādhiṣṭhānam ucyatec etair vimohayaty eṣa jñānam āvṛtya dehinama tasmāt tvam indriyāṇy ādau niyamya bharatarṣabhac pāpmānaṃ prajahihy enaṃ jñānavijñānanāśanama indriyāṇi parāṇy āhur indriyebhyaḥ paraṃ manaḥc manasas tu parā buddhir yo buddheḥ paratas tu saḥa evaṃ buddheḥ paraṃ buddhvā saṃstabhyātmānam ātmanāc jahi śatruṃ mahābāho kāmarūpaṃ durāsadam śrībhagavān uvācaa imaṃ vivasvate yogaṃ proktavān aham avyayamc vivasvān manave prāha manur ikṣvākave bravīta evaṃ paraṃparāprāptam imaṃ rājarṣayo viduḥc sa kāleneha mahatā yogo naṣṭaḥ paraṃtapaa sa evāyaṃ mayā te dya yogaḥ proktaḥ purātanaḥc bhakto si me sakhā ceti rahasyaṃ hy etad uttamam arjuna uvācaa aparaṃ bhavato janma paraṃ janma vivasvataḥc katham etad vijānīyāṃ tvam ādau proktavān iti śrībhagavān uvācaa bahūni me vyatītāni janmāni tava cārjunac tāny ahaṃ veda sarvāṇi na tvaṃ vettha paraṃtapaa ajo pi sann avyayātmā bhūtānām īśvaro pi sanc prakṛtiṃ svām adhiṣṭhāya saṃbhavāmy ātmamāyayāa yadā yadā hi dharmasya glānir bhavati bhāratac abhyutthānam adharmasya tadātmānaṃ sṛjāmy ahama paritrāṇāya sādhūnāṃ vināśāya ca duṣkṛtāmc dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya saṃbhavāmi yuge yugea janma karma ca me divyam evaṃ yo vetti tattvataḥc tyaktvā dehaṃ punarjanma naiti mām eti so rjunaa vītarāgabhayakrodhā manmayā mām upāśritāḥc bahavo jñānatapasā pūtā madbhāvam āgatāḥa ye yathā māṃ prapadyante tāṃs tathaiva bhajāmy ahamc mama vartmānuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśaḥa kāṅkṣantaḥ karmaṇāṃ siddhiṃ yajanta iha devatāḥc kṣipraṃ hi mānuṣe loke siddhir bhavati karmajāa cāturvarṇyaṃ mayā sṛṣṭaṃ guṇakarmavibhāgaśaḥc tasya kartāram api māṃ viddhy akartāram avyayama na māṃ karmāṇi limpanti na me karmaphale spṛhāc iti māṃ yo bhijānāti karmabhir na sa badhyatea evaṃ jñātvā kṛtaṃ karma pūrvair api mumukṣubhiḥc kuru karmaiva tasmāt tvaṃ pūrvaiḥ pūrvataraṃ kṛtama kiṃ karma kim akarmeti kavayo py atra mohitāḥc tat te karma pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā mokṣyase śubhāta karmaṇo hy api boddhavyaṃ boddhavyaṃ ca vikarmaṇaḥc akarmaṇaś ca boddhavyaṃ gahanā karmaṇo gatiḥa karmaṇy akarma yaḥ paśyed akarmaṇi ca karma yaḥc sa buddhimān manuṣyeṣu sa yuktaḥ kṛtsnakarmakṛta yasya sarve samārambhāḥ kāmasaṃkalpavarjitāḥc jñānāgnidagdhakarmāṇaṃ tam āhuḥ paṇḍitaṃ budhāḥa tyaktvā karmaphalāsaṅgaṃ nityatṛpto nirāśrayaḥc karmaṇy abhipravṛtto pi naiva kiṃ cit karoti saḥa nirāśīr yatacittātmā tyaktasarvaparigrahaḥc śārīraṃ kevalaṃ karma kurvan nāpnoti kilbiṣama yadṛcchālābhasaṃtuṣṭo dvaṃdvātīto vimatsaraḥc samaḥ siddhāv asiddhau ca kṛtvāpi na nibadhyatea gatasaṅgasya muktasya jñānāvasthitacetasaḥc yajñāyācarataḥ karma samagraṃ pravilīyatea brahmārpaṇaṃ brahmahavir brahmāgnau brahmaṇā hutamc brahmaiva tena gantavyaṃ brahmakarmasamādhināa daivam evāpare yajñaṃ yoginaḥ paryupāsatec brahmāgnāv apare yajñaṃ yajñenaivopajuhvatia śrotrādīnīndriyāṇy anye saṃyamāgniṣu juhvatic śabdādīn viṣayān anya indriyāgniṣu juhvatia sarvāṇīndriyakarmāṇi prāṇakarmāṇi cāparec ātmasaṃyamayogāgnau juhvati jñānadīpitea dravyayajñās tapoyajñā yogayajñās tathāparec svādhyāyajñānayajñāś ca yatayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥa apāne juhvati prāṇaṃ prāṇe pānaṃ tathāparec prāṇāpānagatī ruddhvā prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇāḥa apare niyatāhārāḥ prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvatic sarve py ete yajñavido yajñakṣapitakalmaṣāḥa yajñaśiṣṭāmṛtabhujo yānti brahma sanātanamc nāyaṃ loko sty ayajñasya kuto nyaḥ kurusattamaa evaṃ bahuvidhā yajñā vitatā brahmaṇo mukhec karmajān viddhi tān sarvān evaṃ jñātvā vimokṣyasea śreyān dravyamayād yajñāj jñānayajñaḥ paraṃtapac sarvaṃ karmākhilaṃ pārtha jñāne parisamāpyatea tad viddhi praṇipātena paripraśnena sevayāc upadekṣyanti te jñānaṃ jñāninas tattvadarśinaḥa yaj jñātvā na punar moham evaṃ yāsyasi pāṇḍavac yena bhūtāny aśeṣeṇa drakṣyasy ātmany atho mayia api ced asi pāpebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpakṛttamaḥc sarvaṃ jñānaplavenaiva vṛjinaṃ saṃtariṣyasia yathaidhāṃsi samiddho gnir bhasmasāt kurute rjunac jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathāa na hi jñānena sadṛśaṃ pavitram iha vidyatec tat svayaṃ yogasaṃsiddhaḥ kālenātmani vindatia śraddhāvāṃl labhate jñānaṃ tatparaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥc jñānaṃ labdhvā parāṃ śāntim acireṇādhigacchatia ajñaś cāśraddadhānaś ca saṃśayātmā vinaśyatic nāyaṃ loko sti na paro na sukhaṃ saṃśayātmanaḥa yogasaṃnyastakarmāṇaṃ jñānasaṃchinnasaṃśayamc ātmavantaṃ na karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanaṃjayaa tasmād ajñānasaṃbhūtaṃ hṛtsthaṃ jñānāsinātmanaḥc chittvainaṃ saṃśayaṃ yogam ātiṣṭhottiṣṭha bhārata arjuna uvācaa saṃnyāsaṃ karmaṇāṃ kṛṣṇa punar yogaṃ ca śaṃsasic yac chreya etayor ekaṃ tan me brūhi suniścitam śrībhagavān uvācaa saṃnyāsaḥ karmayogaś ca niḥśreyasakarāv ubhauc tayos tu karmasaṃnyāsāt karmayogo viśiṣyatea jñeyaḥ sa nityasaṃnyāsī yo na dveṣṭi na kāṅkṣatic nirdvaṃdvo hi mahābāho sukhaṃ bandhāt pramucyatea sāṃkhyayogau pṛthag bālāḥ pravadanti na paṇḍitāḥc ekam apy āsthitaḥ samyag ubhayor vindate phalama yat sāṃkhyaiḥ prāpyate sthānaṃ tad yogair api gamyatec ekaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyatia saṃnyāsas tu mahābāho duḥkham āptum ayogataḥc yogayukto munir brahma nacireṇādhigacchatia yogayukto viśuddhātmā vijitātmā jitendriyaḥc sarvabhūtātmabhūtātmā kurvann api na lipyatea naiva kiṃ cit karomīti yukto manyeta tattvavitc paśyañ śṛṇvan spṛśañ jighrann aśnan gacchan svapañ śvasana pralapan visṛjan gṛhṇann unmiṣan nimiṣann apic indriyāṇīndriyārtheṣu vartanta iti dhārayana brahmaṇy ādhāya karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā karoti yaḥc lipyate na sa pāpena padmapatram ivāmbhasāa kāyena manasā buddhyā kevalair indriyair apic yoginaḥ karma kurvanti saṅgaṃ tyaktvātmaśuddhayea yuktaḥ karmaphalaṃ tyaktvā śāntim āpnoti naiṣṭhikīmc ayuktaḥ kāmakāreṇa phale sakto nibadhyatea sarvakarmāṇi manasā saṃnyasyāste sukhaṃ vaśīc navadvāre pure dehī naiva kurvan na kārayana na kartṛtvaṃ na karmāṇi lokasya sṛjati prabhuḥc na karmaphalasaṃyogaṃ svabhāvas tu pravartatea nādatte kasya cit pāpaṃ na caiva sukṛtaṃ vibhuḥc ajñānenāvṛtaṃ jñānaṃ tena muhyanti jantavaḥa jñānena tu tad ajñānaṃ yeṣāṃ nāśitam ātmanaḥc teṣām ādityavaj jñānaṃ prakāśayati tatparama tadbuddhayas tadātmānas tanniṣṭhās tatparāyaṇāḥc gacchanty apunarāvṛttiṃ jñānanirdhūtakalmaṣāḥd smaranto pi muhus tv etat spṛśanto pi svakarmaṇid saktā api na sajjanti paṅke ravikarā ivaa vidyāvinayasaṃpanne brāhmaṇe gavi hastinic śuni caiva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinaḥa ihaiva tair jitaḥ sargo yeṣāṃ sāmye sthitaṃ manaḥc nirdoṣaṃ hi samaṃ brahma tasmād brahmaṇi te sthitāḥa na prahṛṣyet priyaṃ prāpya nodvijet prāpya cāpriyamc sthirabuddhir asaṃmūḍho brahmavid brahmaṇi sthitaḥa bāhyasparśeṣv asaktātmā vindaty ātmani yat sukhamc sa brahmayogayuktātmā sukham akṣayam aśnutea ye hi saṃsparśajā bhogā duḥkhayonaya eva tec ādyantavantaḥ kaunteya na teṣu ramate budhaḥa śaknotīhaiva yaḥ soḍhuṃ prāk śarīravimokṣaṇātc kāmakrodhodbhavaṃ vegaṃ sa yuktaḥ sa sukhī naraḥa yo ntaḥsukho ntarārāmas tathāntarjyotir eva yaḥc sa yogī brahmanirvāṇaṃ brahmabhūto dhigacchatia labhante brahmanirvāṇam ṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥc chinnadvaidhā yatātmānaḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥa kāmakrodhaviyuktānāṃ yatīnāṃ yatacetasāmc abhito brahmanirvāṇaṃ vartate viditātmanāma sparśān kṛtvā bahir bāhyāṃś cakṣuś caivāntare bhruvoḥc prāṇāpānau samau kṛtvā nāsābhyantaracāriṇaua yatendriyamanobuddhir munir mokṣaparāyaṇaḥc vigatecchābhayakrodho yaḥ sadā mukta eva saḥa bhoktāraṃ yajñatapasāṃ sarvalokamaheśvaramc suhṛdaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jñātvā māṃ śāntim ṛcchati śrībhagavān uvācaa anāśritaḥ karmaphalaṃ kāryaṃ karma karoti yaḥc sa saṃnyāsī ca yogī ca na niragnir na cākriyaḥa yaṃ saṃnyāsam iti prāhur yogaṃ taṃ viddhi pāṇḍavac na hy asaṃnyastasaṃkalpo yogī bhavati kaś canaa ārurukṣor muner yogaṃ karma kāraṇam ucyatec yogārūḍhasya tasyaiva śamaḥ kāraṇam ucyatea yadā hi nendriyārtheṣu na karmasv anuṣajjatec sarvasaṃkalpasaṃnyāsī yogārūḍhas tadocyatea uddhared ātmanātmānaṃ nātmānam avasādayetc ātmaiva hy ātmano bandhur ātmaiva ripur ātmanaḥa bandhur ātmātmanas tasya yenātmaivātmanā jitaḥc anātmanas tu śatrutve vartetātmaiva śatruvata jitātmanaḥ praśāntasya paramātmā samāhitaḥc śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkheṣu tathā mānāvamānayoḥa jñānavijñānatṛptātmā kūṭastho vijitendriyaḥc yukta ity ucyate yogī samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥa suhṛnmitrāryudāsīnamadhyasthadveṣyabandhuṣuc sādhuṣv api ca pāpeṣu samabuddhir viśiṣyatea yogī yuñjīta satatam ātmānaṃ rahasi sthitaḥc ekākī yatacittātmā nirāśīr aparigrahaḥa śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya sthiram āsanam ātmanaḥc nātyucchritaṃ nātinīcaṃ cailājinakuśottarama tatraikāgraṃ manaḥ kṛtvā yatacittendriyakriyaḥc upaviśyāsane yuñjyād yogam ātmaviśuddhayea samaṃ kāyaśirogrīvaṃ dhārayann acalaṃ sthiraḥc saṃprekṣya nāsikāgraṃ svaṃ diśaś cānavalokayana praśāntātmā vigatabhīr brahmacārivrate sthitaḥc manaḥ saṃyamya maccitto yukta āsīta matparaḥa yuñjann evaṃ sadātmānaṃ yogī niyatamānasaḥc śāntiṃ nirvāṇaparamāṃ matsaṃsthām adhigacchatia nātyaśnatas tu yogo sti na caikāntam anaśnataḥc na cātisvapnaśīlasya jāgrato naiva cārjunaa yuktāhāravihārasya yuktaceṣṭasya karmasuc yuktasvapnāvabodhasya yogo bhavati duḥkhahāa yadā viniyataṃ cittam ātmany evāvatiṣṭhatec niḥspṛhaḥ sarvakāmebhyo yukta ity ucyate tadāa yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtāc yogino yatacittasya yuñjato yogam ātmanaḥa yatroparamate cittaṃ niruddhaṃ yogasevayāc yatra caivātmanātmānaṃ paśyann ātmani tuṣyatia sukham ātyantikaṃ yat tad buddhigrāhyam atīndriyamc vetti yatra na caivāyaṃ sthitaś calati tattvataḥa yaṃ labdhvā cāparaṃ lābhaṃ manyate nādhikaṃ tataḥc yasmin sthito na duḥkhena guruṇāpi vicālyatea taṃ vidyād duḥkhasaṃyogaviyogaṃ yogasaṃjñitamc sa niścayena yoktavyo yogo nirviṇṇacetasāa saṃkalpaprabhavān kāmāṃs tyaktvā sarvān aśeṣataḥc manasaivendriyagrāmaṃ viniyamya samantataḥa śanaiḥ śanair uparamed buddhyā dhṛtigṛhītayāc ātmasaṃsthaṃ manaḥ kṛtvā na kiṃ cid api cintayeta yato yato niścarati manaś cañcalam asthiramc tatas tato niyamyaitad ātmany eva vaśaṃ nayeta praśāntamanasaṃ hy enaṃ yoginaṃ sukham uttamamc upaiti śāntarajasaṃ brahmabhūtam akalmaṣama yuñjann evaṃ sadātmānaṃ yogī vigatakalmaṣaḥc sukhena brahmasaṃsparśam atyantaṃ sukham aśnutea sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cātmanic īkṣate yogayuktātmā sarvatra samadarśanaḥa yo māṃ paśyati sarvatra sarvaṃ ca mayi paśyatic tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyatia sarvabhūtasthitaṃ yo māṃ bhajaty ekatvam āsthitaḥc sarvathā vartamāno pi sa yogī mayi vartatea ātmaupamyena sarvatra samaṃ paśyati yo rjunac sukhaṃ vā yadi vā duḥkhaṃ sa yogī paramo mataḥ arjuna uvācaa yo yaṃ yogas tvayā proktaḥ sāmyena madhusūdanac etasyāhaṃ na paśyāmi cañcalatvāt sthitiṃ sthirāma cañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa pramāthi balavad dṛḍhamc tasyāhaṃ nigrahaṃ manye vāyor iva suduṣkaram śrībhagavān uvācaa asaṃśayaṃ mahābāho mano durnigrahaṃ calamc abhyāsena tu kaunteya vairāgyeṇa ca gṛhyatea asaṃyatātmanā yogo duṣprāpa iti me matiḥc vaśyātmanā tu yatatā śakyo vāptum upāyataḥ arjuna uvācaa ayatiḥ śraddhayopeto yogāc calitamānasaḥb lipsamānaḥ satāṃ mārgaṃ pramūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathib anekacitto vibhrānto mohasyaiva vaśaṃ gataḥc aprāpya yogasaṃsiddhiṃ kāṃ gatiṃ kṛṣṇa gacchatia kaccin nobhayavibhraṣṭaś chinnābhram iva naśyatic apratiṣṭho mahābāho vimūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathia etan me saṃśayaṃ kṛṣṇa chettum arhasy aśeṣataḥc tvad anyaḥ saṃśayasyāsya chettā na hy upapadyate śrībhagavān uvācaa pārtha naiveha nāmutra vināśas tasya vidyatec na hi kalyāṇakṛt kaś cid durgatiṃ tāta gacchatia prāpya puṇyakṛtāṃl lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥc śucīnāṃ śrīmatāṃ gehe yogabhraṣṭo bhijāyatea atha vā yoginām eva kule bhavati dhīmatāmc etad dhi durlabhataraṃ loke janma yad īdṛśama tatra taṃ buddhisaṃyogaṃ labhate paurvadehikamc yatate ca tato bhūyaḥ saṃsiddhau kurunandanaa pūrvābhyāsena tenaiva hriyate hy avaśo pi saḥc jijñāsur api yogasya śabdabrahmātivartatea prayatnād yatamānas tu yogī saṃśuddhakilbiṣaḥc anekajanmasaṃsiddhas tato yāti parāṃ gatima tapasvibhyo dhiko yogī jñānibhyo pi mato dhikaḥc karmibhyaś cādhiko yogī tasmād yogī bhavārjunaa yoginām api sarveṣāṃ madgatenāntarātmanāc śraddhāvān bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mataḥd bhagavannāmasaṃprāptimātrāt sarvam avāpyated phalitāḥ śālayaḥ samyag vṛṣṭimātre valokite śrībhagavān uvācaa mayy āsaktamanāḥ pārtha yogaṃ yuñjan madāśrayaḥc asaṃśayaṃ samagraṃ māṃ yathā jñāsyasi tac chṛṇua jñānaṃ te haṃ savijñānam idaṃ vakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥc yaj jñātvā neha bhūyo nyaj jñātavyam avaśiṣyatea manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaś cid yatati siddhayec yatatām api siddhānāṃ kaś cin māṃ vetti tattvataḥa bhūmir āpo nalo vāyuḥ khaṃ mano buddhir eva cac ahaṃkāra itīyaṃ me bhinnā prakṛtir aṣṭadhāa apareyam itas tv anyāṃ prakṛtiṃ viddhi me parāmc jīvabhūtāṃ mahābāho yayedaṃ dhāryate jagata etadyonīni bhūtāni sarvāṇīty upadhārayac ahaṃ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayas tathāa mattaḥ parataraṃ nānyat kiṃ cid asti dhanaṃjayac mayi sarvam idaṃ protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā ivaa raso ham apsu kaunteya prabhāsmi śaśisūryayoḥc praṇavaḥ sarvavedeṣu śabdaḥ khe pauruṣaṃ nṛṣua puṇyo gandhaḥ pṛthivyāṃ ca tejaś cāsmi vibhāvasauc jīvanaṃ sarvabhūteṣu tapaś cāsmi tapasviṣua bījaṃ māṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viddhi pārtha sanātanamc buddhir buddhimatām asmi tejas tejasvinām ahama balaṃ balavatāṃ cāhaṃ kāmarāgavivarjitamc dharmāviruddho bhūteṣu kāmo smi bharatarṣabhaa ye caiva sāttvikā bhāvā rājasās tāmasāś ca yec matta eveti tān viddhi na tv ahaṃ teṣu te mayia tribhir guṇamayair bhāvair ebhiḥ sarvam idaṃ jagatc mohitaṃ nābhijānāti mām ebhyaḥ param avyayama daivī hy eṣā guṇamayī mama māyā duratyayāc mām eva ye prapadyante māyām etāṃ taranti tea na māṃ duṣkṛtino mūḍhāḥ prapadyante narādhamāḥc māyayāpahṛtajñānā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥa caturvidhā bhajante māṃ janāḥ sukṛtino rjunac ārto jijñāsur arthārthī jñānī ca bharatarṣabhaa teṣāṃ jñānī nityayukta ekabhaktir viśiṣyatec priyo hi jñānino tyartham ahaṃ sa ca mama priyaḥa udārāḥ sarva evaite jñānī tv ātmaiva me matamc āsthitaḥ sa hi yuktātmā mām evānuttamāṃ gatima bahūnāṃ janmanām ante jñānavān māṃ prapadyatec vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti sa mahātmā sudurlabhaḥa kāmais tais tair hṛtajñānāḥ prapadyante nyadevatāḥc taṃ taṃ niyamam āsthāya prakṛtyā niyatāḥ svayāa yo yo yāṃ yāṃ tanuṃ bhaktaḥ śraddhayārcitum icchatic tasya tasyācalāṃ śraddhāṃ tām eva vidadhāmy jarāmaraṇamokṣāya mām āśritya yatanti yec te brahma tad viduḥ kṛtsnam adhyātmaṃ karma cākhilama sādhibhūtādhidaivaṃ māṃ sādhiyajñaṃ ca ye viduḥc prayāṇakāle pi ca māṃ te vidur yuktacetasaḥd sphuṭaṃ
