adhiyajñaḥ kathaṃ ko tra dehe smin madhusūdanac prayāṇakāle ca kathaṃ jñeyo si niyatātmabhiḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa akṣaraṃ brahma paramaṃ svabhāvo dhyātmam ucyatec bhūtabhāvodbhavakaro visargaḥ karmasaṃjñitaḥa adhibhūtaṃ kṣaro bhāvaḥ puruṣaś cādhidaivatamc adhiyajño ham evātra dehe dehabhṛtāṃ varaa antakāle ca mām eva smaran muktvā kalevaramc yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥa yaṃ yaṃ vāpi smaran bhāvaṃ tyajaty ante kalevaramc taṃ tam evaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥa tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu mām anusmara yudhya cac mayy arpitamanobuddhir mām evaiṣyasy asaṃśayaḥa abhyāsayogayuktena cetasā nānyagāmināc paramaṃ puruṣaṃ divyaṃ yāti pārthānucintayana kaviṃ purāṇam anuśāsitāramaṇor aṇīyāṃsam anusmared yaḥc sarvasya dhātāram acintyarūpamādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāta prayāṇakāle manasācalenabhaktyā yukto yogabalena caivac bhruvor madhye prāṇam āveśya samyaksa taṃ paraṃ puruṣam upaiti divyama yad akṣaraṃ vedavido vadantiviśanti yad yatayo vītarāgāḥc yad icchanto brahmacaryaṃ carantitat te padaṃ saṃgraheṇa pravakṣyed sarve vedā yat padam āmanantid tapāṃsi sarvāṇi ca yad vadantid yad icchanto brahmacaryaṃ carantid tat te padaṃ saṃgraheṇa bravīmia sarvadvārāṇi saṃyamya mano hṛdi nirudhya cac mūrdhny ādhāyātmanaḥ prāṇam āsthito yogadhāraṇāma om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma vyāharan mām anusmaranc yaḥ prayāti tyajan dehaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatima ananyacetāḥ satataṃ yo māṃ smarati nityaśaḥc tasyāhaṃ sulabhaḥ pārtha nityayuktasya yoginaḥa mām upetya punarjanma duḥkhālayam aśāśvatamc nāpnuvanti mahātmānaḥ saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ gatāḥa ā brahmabhuvanāl lokāḥ punarāvartino rjunac mām upetya tu kaunteya punarjanma na vidyatea sahasrayugaparyantam ahar yad brahmaṇo viduḥc rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ te horātravido janāḥa avyaktād vyaktayaḥ sarvāḥ prabhavanty aharāgamec rātryāgame pralīyante tatraivāvyaktasaṃjñakea bhūtagrāmaḥ sa evāyaṃ bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyatec rātryāgame vaśaḥ pārtha prabhavaty aharāgamea paras tasmāt tu bhāvo nyo vyakto vyaktāt sanātanaḥc yaḥ sa sarveṣu bhūteṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyatia avyakto kṣara ity uktas tam āhuḥ paramāṃ gatimc yaṃ prāpya na nivartante tad dhāma paramaṃ mamaa puruṣaḥ sa paraḥ pārtha bhaktyā labhyas tv ananyayāb yaṃ prāpya na punarjanma labhante yogino rjunac yasyāntaḥsthāni bhūtāni yena sarvam idaṃ tatama yatra kāle tv anāvṛttim āvṛttiṃ caiva yoginaḥc prayātā yānti taṃ kālaṃ vakṣyāmi bharatarṣabhaa agnir jyotir ahaḥ śuklaḥ ṣaṇmāsā uttarāyaṇamc tatra prayātā gacchanti brahma brahmavido janāḥa dhūmo rātris tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṇmāsā dakṣiṇāyanamc tatra cāndramasaṃ jyotir yogī prāpya nivartatea śuklakṛṣṇe gatī hy ete jagataḥ śāśvate matec ekayā yāty anāvṛttim anyayāvartate punaḥa naite sṛtī pārtha jānan yogī muhyati kaś canac tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu yogayukto bhavārjunaa vedeṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caivadāneṣu yat puṇyaphalaṃ pradiṣṭamc atyeti tat sarvam idaṃ viditvāyogī paraṃ sthānam upaiti cādyamd sarvatattvagatatvena vijñāte parameśvared antar bahir na sāvasthā na yasyāṃ bhāsate vibhuḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa idaṃ tu te guhyatamaṃ pravakṣyāmy anasūyavec jñānaṃ vijñānasahitaṃ yaj jñātvā mokṣyase śubhāta rājavidyā rājaguhyaṃ pavitram idam uttamamc pratyakṣāvagamaṃ dharmyaṃ susukhaṃ kartum avyayama aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā dharmasyāsya paraṃtapac aprāpya māṃ nivartante mṛtyusaṃsāravartmania mayā tatam idaṃ sarvaṃ jagad avyaktamūrtināc matsthāni sarvabhūtāni na cāhaṃ teṣv avasthitaḥa na ca matsthāni bhūtāni paśya me yogam aiśvaramc bhūtabhṛn na ca bhūtastho mamātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥd sarvagaḥ sarvavaś cādyaḥ sarvakṛt sarvadarśanaḥd sarvajñaḥ sarvadarśī ca sarvātmā sarvatomukhaḥa yathākāśasthito nityaṃ vāyuḥ sarvatrago mahānc tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni matsthānīty upadhārayad evaṃ hi sarvabhūteṣu carāmy anabhilakṣitaḥd bhūtaprakṛtim āsthāya sahaiva ca vinaiva caa sarvabhūtāni kaunteya prakṛtiṃ yānti māmikāmc kalpakṣaye punas tāni kalpādau visṛjāmy ahama prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhya visṛjāmi punaḥ punaḥc bhūtagrāmam imaṃ kṛtsnam avaśaṃ prakṛter vaśāta na ca māṃ tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanaṃjayac udāsīnavad āsīnam asaktaṃ teṣu karmasua mayādhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaramc hetunānena kaunteya jagad viparivartatea avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanum āśritamc paraṃ bhāvam ajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvarama moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥc rākṣasīm āsurīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohinīṃ śritāḥa mahātmānas tu māṃ pārtha daivīṃ prakṛtim āśritāḥc bhajanty ananyamanaso jñātvā bhūtādim avyayama satataṃ kīrtayanto māṃ yatantaś ca dṛḍhavratāḥc namasyantaś ca māṃ bhaktyā nityayuktā upāsatea jñānayajñena cāpy anye yajanto mām upāsatec ekatvena pṛthaktvena bahudhā viśvatomukhama ahaṃ kratur ahaṃ yajñaḥ svadhāham aham auṣadhamc mantro ham aham evājyam aham agnir ahaṃ hutama pitāham asya jagato mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥc vedyaṃ pavitram oṃkāra ṛk sāma yajur eva caa gatir bhartā prabhuḥ sākṣī nivāsaḥ śaraṇaṃ suhṛtc prabhavaḥ pralayaḥ sthānaṃ nidhānaṃ bījam avyayama tapāmy aham ahaṃ varṣaṃ nigṛhṇāmy utsṛjāmi cac amṛtaṃ caiva mṛtyuś ca sad asac cāham arjunaa traividyā māṃ somapāḥ pūtapāpāyajñair iṣṭvā svargatiṃ prārthayantec te puṇyam āsādya surendralokamaśnanti divyān divi devabhogāna te taṃ bhuktvā svargalokaṃ viśālaṃkṣīṇe puṇye martyalokaṃ viśantic evaṃ trayīdharmam anuprapannāgatāgataṃ kāmakāmā labhantea ananyāś cintayanto māṃ ye janāḥ paryupāsatec teṣāṃ nityābhiyuktānāṃ yogakṣemaṃ vahāmy ahama ye py anyadevatā bhaktā yajante śraddhayānvitāḥc te pi mām eva kaunteya yajanty avidhipūrvakama ahaṃ hi sarvayajñānāṃ bhoktā ca prabhur eva cac na tu mām abhijānanti tattvenātaś cyavanti tea yānti devavratā devān pitṝn yānti pitṛvratāḥc bhūtāni yānti bhūtejyā yānti madyājino pi māma patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchatic tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtam aśnāmi prayatātmanaḥa yat karoṣi yad aśnāsi yaj juhoṣi dadāsi yatc yat tapasyasi kaunteya tat kuruṣva madarpaṇama śubhāśubhaphalair evaṃ mokṣyase karmabandhanaiḥc saṃnyāsayogayuktātmā vimukto mām upaiṣyasia samo haṃ sarvabhūteṣu na me dveṣyo sti na priyaḥc ye bhajanti tu māṃ bhaktyā mayi te teṣu cāpy ahama api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhākc sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥa kṣipraṃ bhavati dharmātmā śaśvacchāntiṃ nigacchatic kaunteya pratijānīhi na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyatia māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥc striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te pi yānti parāṃ gatima kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathāc anityam asukhaṃ lokam imaṃ prāpya bhajasva māma manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṃ namaskuruc mām evaiṣyasi yuktvaivam ātmānaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa bhūya eva mahābāho śṛṇu me paramaṃ vacaḥc yat te haṃ prīyamāṇāya vakṣyāmi hitakāmyayāa na me viduḥ suragaṇāḥ prabhavaṃ na maharṣayaḥc aham ādir hi devānāṃ maharṣīṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥa yo mām ajam anādiṃ ca vetti lokamaheśvaramc asaṃmūḍhaḥ sa martyeṣu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyatea buddhir jñānam asaṃmohaḥ kṣamā satyaṃ damaḥ śamaḥc sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhavo bhāvo bhayaṃ cābhayam eva caa ahiṃsā samatā tuṣṭis tapo dānaṃ yaśo yaśaḥc bhavanti bhāvā bhūtānāṃ matta eva pṛthagvidhāḥa maharṣayaḥ sapta pūrve catvāro manavas tathāc madbhāvā mānasā jātā yeṣāṃ loka imāḥ prajāḥa etāṃ vibhūtiṃ yogaṃ ca mama yo vetti tattvataḥc so vikampena yogena yujyate nātra saṃśayaḥa ahaṃ sarvasya prabhavo mattaḥ sarvaṃ pravartatec iti matvā bhajante māṃ budhā bhāvasamanvitāḥa maccittā madgataprāṇā bodhayantaḥ parasparamc kathayantaś ca māṃ nityaṃ tuṣyanti ca ramanti caa teṣāṃ satatayuktānāṃ bhajatāṃ prītipūrvakamc dadāmi buddhiyogaṃ taṃ yena mām upayānti tea teṣām evānukampārtham aham ajñānajaṃ tamaḥc nāśayāmy ātmabhāvastho jñānadīpena bhāsvatā arjuna uvācaa paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma pavitraṃ paramaṃ bhavānc puruṣaṃ śāśvataṃ divyam ādidevam ajaṃ vibhuma āhus tvām ṛṣayaḥ sarve devarṣir nāradas tathāc asito devalo vyāsaḥ svayaṃ caiva bravīṣi mea sarvam etad ṛtaṃ manye yan māṃ vadasi keśavac na hi te bhagavan vyaktiṃ vidur devā na dānavāḥa svayam evātmanātmānaṃ vettha tvaṃ puruṣottamac bhūtabhāvana bhūteśa devadeva jagatpatea vaktum arhasy aśeṣeṇa divyā hy ātmavibhūtayaḥc yābhir vibhūtibhir lokān imāṃs tvaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhasia kathaṃ vidyām ahaṃ yogiṃs tvāṃ sadā paricintayanc keṣu keṣu ca bhāveṣu cintyo si bhagavan mayāa vistareṇātmano yogaṃ vibhūtiṃ ca janārdanac bhūyaḥ kathaya tṛptir hi śṛṇvato nāsti me mṛtam śrībhagavān uvācaa hanta te kathayiṣyāmi divyā hy ātmavibhūtayaḥc prādhānyataḥ kuruśreṣṭha nāsty anto vistarasya mea aham ātmā guḍākeśa sarvabhūtāśayasthitaḥc aham ādiś ca madhyaṃ ca bhūtānām anta eva caa ādityānām ahaṃ viṣṇur jyotiṣāṃ ravir aṃśumānc marīcir marutām asmi nakṣatrāṇām ahaṃ śaśīa vedānāṃ sāmavedo smi devānām asmi vāsavaḥc indriyāṇāṃ manaś cāsmi bhūtānām asmi cetanāa rudrāṇāṃ śaṃkaraś cāsmi vitteśo yakṣarakṣasāmc vasūnāṃ pāvakaś cāsmi meruḥ śikhariṇām ahama purodhasāṃ ca mukhyaṃ māṃ viddhi pārtha bṛhaspatimc senānīnām ahaṃ skandaḥ sarasām asmi sāgaraḥa maharṣīṇāṃ bhṛgur ahaṃ girām asmy ekam akṣaramc yajñānāṃ japayajño smi sthāvarāṇāṃ himālayaḥa aśvatthaḥ sarvavṛkṣāṇāṃ devarṣīṇāṃ ca nāradaḥc gandharvāṇāṃ citrarathaḥ siddhānāṃ kapilo muniḥa uccaiḥśravasam aśvānāṃ viddhi mām amṛtodbhavamc airāvataṃ gajendrāṇāṃ narāṇāṃ ca narādhipama āyudhānām ahaṃ vajraṃ dhenūnām asmi kāmadhukc prajanaś cāsmi kandarpaḥ sarpāṇām asmi vāsukiḥa anantaś cāsmi nāgānāṃ varuṇo yādasām ahamc pitṝṇām aryamā cāsmi yamaḥ saṃyamatām ahama prahlādaś cāsmi daityānāṃ kālaḥ kalayatām ahamc mṛgāṇāṃ ca mṛgendro haṃ vainateyaś ca pakṣiṇāma pavanaḥ pavatām asmi rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtām ahamc jhaṣāṇāṃ makaraś cāsmi srotasām asmi jāhnavīa sargāṇām ādir antaś ca madhyaṃ caivāham arjunac adhyātmavidyā vidyānāṃ vādaḥ pravadatām ahama akṣarāṇām akāro smi dvaṃdvaḥ sāmāsikasya cac aham evākṣayaḥ kālo dhātāhaṃ viśvatomukhaḥa mṛtyuḥ sarvaharaś cāham udbhavaś ca bhaviṣyatāmc kīrtiḥ śrīr vāk ca nārīṇāṃ smṛtir medhā dhṛtiḥ kṣamāa bṛhatsāma tathā sāmnāṃ gāyatrī chandasām ahamc māsānāṃ mārgaśīrṣo ham ṛtūnāṃ kusumākaraḥd oṣadhīnāṃ yavaś cāsmi dhātūnām asmi kāñcanamd saurabheyo gavām asmi snehānāṃ sarpir apy ahamd sarvāsāṃ tṛṇajātīnāṃ darbho haṃ pāṇḍunandanaa dyūtaṃ chalayatām asmi tejas tejasvinām ahamc jayo smi vyavasāyo smi sattvaṃ sattvavatām ahama vṛṣṇīnāṃ vāsudevo smi pāṇḍavānāṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc munīnām apy ahaṃ vyāsaḥ kavīnām uśanā kaviḥa daṇḍo damayatām asmi nītir asmi jigīṣatāmc maunaṃ caivāsmi guhyānāṃ jñānaṃ jñānavatām ahama yac cāpi sarvabhūtānāṃ bījaṃ tad aham arjunac na tad asti vinā yat syān mayā bhūtaṃ carācarama nānto sti mama divyānāṃ vibhūtīnāṃ paraṃtapac eṣa tūddeśataḥ prokto vibhūter vistaro mayāa yad yad vibhūtimat sattvaṃ śrīmad ūrjitam eva vāc tat tad evāvagaccha tvaṃ mama tejoṃśasaṃbhavama atha vā bahunaitena kiṃ jñātena tavārjunac viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ kṛtsnam ekāṃśena sthito jagat arjuna uvācaa madanugrahāya paramaṃ guhyam adhyātmasaṃjñitamc yat tvayoktaṃ vacas tena moho yaṃ vigato mamaa bhavāpyayau hi bhūtānāṃ śrutau vistaraśo mayāc tvattaḥ kamalapatrākṣa māhātmyam api cāvyayama evam etad yathāttha tvam ātmānaṃ parameśvarac draṣṭum icchāmi te rūpam aiśvaraṃ puruṣottamaa manyase yadi tac chakyaṃ mayā draṣṭum iti prabhoc yogeśvara tato me tvaṃ darśayātmānam avyayam śrībhagavān uvācaa paśya me pārtha rūpāṇi śataśo tha sahasraśaḥc nānāvidhāni divyāni nānāvarṇākṛtīni caa paśyādityān vasūn rudrān aśvinau marutas tathāc bahūny adṛṣṭapūrvāṇi paśyāścaryāṇi bhārataa ihaikasthaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ paśyādya sacarācaramc mama dehe guḍākeśa yac cānyad draṣṭum icchasia na tu māṃ śakyase draṣṭum anenaiva svacakṣuṣāc divyaṃ dadāmi te cakṣuḥ paśya me yogam aiśvaram saṃjaya uvācaa evam uktvā tato rājan mahāyogeśvaro hariḥc darśayām āsa pārthāya paramaṃ rūpam aiśvarama anekavaktranayanam anekādbhutadarśanamc anekadivyābharaṇaṃ divyānekodyatāyudhama divyamālyāmbaradharaṃ divyagandhānulepanamc sarvāścaryamayaṃ devam anantaṃ viśvatomukhama divi sūryasahasrasya bhaved yugapad utthitāc yadi bhāḥ sadṛśī sā syād bhāsas tasya mahātmanaḥa tatraikasthaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ pravibhaktam anekadhāc apaśyad devadevasya śarīre pāṇḍavas tadāa tataḥ sa vismayāviṣṭo hṛṣṭaromā dhanaṃjayaḥc praṇamya śirasā devaṃ kṛtāñjalir abhāṣata arjuna uvācaa paśyāmi devāṃs tava deva dehesarvāṃs tathā bhūtaviśeṣasaṃghānc brahmāṇam īśaṃ kamalāsanasthamṛṣīṃś ca sarvān uragāṃś ca divyāna anekabāhūdaravaktranetraṃpaśyāmi tvā sarvato nantarūpamc nāntaṃ na madhyaṃ na punas tavādiṃpaśyāmi viśveśvara viśvarūpaa kirīṭinaṃ gadinaṃ cakriṇaṃ catejorāśiṃ sarvato dīptimantamc paśyāmi tvāṃ durnirīkṣyaṃ samantāddīptānalārkadyutim aprameyama tvam akṣaraṃ paramaṃ veditavyaṃtvam asya viśvasya paraṃ nidhānamc tvam avyayaḥ śāśvatadharmagoptāsanātanas tvaṃ puruṣo mato mea anādimadhyāntam anantavīryamanantabāhuṃ śaśisūryanetramc paśyāmi tvāṃ dīptahutāśavaktraṃsvatejasā viśvam idaṃ tapantama dyāvāpṛthivyor idam antaraṃ hivyāptaṃ tvayaikena diśaś ca sarvāḥc dṛṣṭvādbhutaṃ rūpam idaṃ tavograṃlokatrayaṃ pravyathitaṃ mahātmana amī hi tvā surasaṃghā viśantike cid bhītāḥ prāñjalayo gṛṇantic svastīty uktvā maharṣisiddhasaṃghāḥstuvanti tvāṃ stutibhiḥ puṣkalābhiḥa rudrādityā vasavo ye ca sādhyāviśve śvinau marutaś coṣmapāś cac gandharvayakṣāsurasiddhasaṃghāvīkṣante tvā vismitāś caiva sarvea rūpaṃ mahat te bahuvaktranetraṃmahābāho bahubāhūrupādamc bahūdaraṃ bahudaṃṣṭrākarālaṃdṛṣṭvā lokāḥ pravyathitās tathāhama nabhaḥspṛśaṃ dīptam anekavarṇaṃvyāttānanaṃ dīptaviśālanetramc dṛṣṭvā hi tvāṃ pravyathitāntarātmādhṛtiṃ na vindāmi śamaṃ ca viṣṇoa daṃṣṭrākarālāni ca te mukhānidṛṣṭvaiva kālānalasaṃnibhānic diśo na jāne na labhe ca śarmaprasīda deveśa jagannivāsaa amī ca tvāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāḥsarve sahaivāvanipālasaṃghaiḥc bhīṣmo droṇaḥ sūtaputras tathāsausahāsmadīyair api yodhamukhyaiḥa vaktrāṇi te tvaramāṇā viśantidaṃṣṭrākarālāni bhayānakānib sahasrasūryātasaṃnibhānib tathā jagadgrāsakṛtakṣaṇānib nānārūpaiḥ puruṣair vadhyamānāb viśanti te vaktram acintyarūpamb yaudhiṣṭhirā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca yodhāḥb śastraiḥ kṛttā vividhaiḥ sarva evab tvattejasā nihatā nūnam eteb tathā hīme tvaccharīraṃ praviṣṭāḥc ke cid vilagnā daśanāntareṣusaṃdṛśyante cūrṇitair uttamāṅgaiḥa yathā nadīnāṃ bahavo mbuvegāḥsamudram evābhimukhā dravantic tathā tavāmī naralokavīrāviśanti vaktrāṇy abhivijvalantia yathā pradīptaṃ jvalanaṃ pataṃgāviśanti nāśāya samṛddhavegāḥc tathaiva nāśāya viśanti lokāstavāpi vaktrāṇi samṛddhavegāḥa lelihyase grasamānaḥ samantāllokān samagrān vadanair jvaladbhiḥc tejobhir āpūrya jagat samagraṃbhāsas tavogrāḥ pratapanti viṣṇoa ākhyāhi me ko bhavān ugrarūponamo stu te devavara prasīdac vijñātum icchāmi bhavantam ādyaṃna hi prajānāmi tava pravṛttim śrībhagavān uvācaa kālo smi lokakṣayakṛt pravṛddholokān samāhartum iha pravṛttaḥc ṛte pi tvā na bhaviṣyanti sarveye vasthitāḥ pratyanīkeṣu yodhāḥa tasmāt tvam uttiṣṭha yaśo labhasvajitvā śatrūn bhuṅkṣva rājyaṃ samṛddhamc mayaivaite nihatāḥ pūrvam evanimittamātraṃ bhava savyasācina droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca jayadrathaṃ cakarṇaṃ tathānyān api yodhavīrānc mayā hatāṃs tvaṃ jahi mā vyathiṣṭhāyudhyasva jetāsi raṇe sapatnān saṃjaya uvācaa etac chrutvā vacanaṃ keśavasyakṛtāñjalir vepamānaḥ kirīṭīc namaskṛtvā bhūya evāha kṛṣṇaṃsagadgadaṃ bhītabhītaḥ praṇamya arjuna uvācaa sthāne hṛṣīkeśa tava prakīrtyājagat prahṛṣyaty anurajyate cac rakṣāṃsi bhītāni diśo dravantisarve namasyanti ca siddhasaṃghāḥa kasmāc ca te na nameran mahātmangarīyase brahmaṇo py ādikartrec ananta deveśa jagannivāsatvam akṣaraṃ sad asat tatparaṃ yata tvam ādidevaḥ puruṣaḥ purāṇastvam asya viśvasya paraṃ nidhānamc vettāsi vedyaṃ ca paraṃ ca dhāmatvayā tataṃ viśvam anantarūpaa vāyur yamo gnir varuṇaḥ śaśāṅkaḥprajāpatis tvaṃ prapitāmahaś cac namo namas te stu sahasrakṛtvaḥpunaś ca bhūyo pi namo namas ted anādimān apratimaprabhāvaḥd sarveśvaraḥ sarvamahāvibhūtea namaḥ purastād atha pṛṣṭhatas tenamo stu te sarvata eva sarvab na hi tvad anyaḥ kaś cid apīha devab lokatraye dṛśyate cintyakarmāc anantavīryāmitavikramas tvaṃsarvaṃ samāpnoṣi tato si sarvaḥa sakheti matvā prasabhaṃ yad uktaṃhe kṛṣṇa he yādava he sakhetic ajānatā mahimānaṃ tavedaṃmayā pramādāt praṇayena vāpia yac cāvahāsārtham asatkṛto sivihāraśayyāsanabhojaneṣuc eko tha vāpy acyuta tatsamakṣaṃtat kṣāmaye tvām aham aprameyama pitāsi lokasya carācarasyatvam asya pūjyaś ca gurur garīyānc na tvatsamo sty abhyadhikaḥ kuto nyolokatraye py apratimaprabhāvaa tasmāt praṇamya praṇidhāya kāyaṃprasādaye tvām aham īśam īḍyamc piteva putrasya sakheva sakhyuḥpriyaḥ priyāyārhasi deva soḍhumd divyāni karmāṇi tavādbhutānid pūrvāṇi pūrve py ṛṣayaḥ smarantid nānyo sti kartā jagatas tvam ekod dhātā vidhātā ca vibhur bhavaś cad tavādbhutaṃ kiṃ nu bhaved asahyaṃd kiṃ vāśakyaṃ parataḥ kīrtayiṣyed kartāsi sarvasya yataḥ svayaṃ vaid vibho tataḥ sarvam idaṃ tvam evad aty adbhutaṃ karma na duṣkaraṃ ted karmopamānaṃ na hi vidyate ted na te guṇānāṃ parimāṇam astid na tejaso nāpi balasya narddheḥd imāni karmāṇi tavādbhutānid kṛtāni pūrve munayo vadantid na te guṇānāṃ parimāṇam astid na tejasaś cāpi balasya viṣṇoa adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ hṛṣito smi dṛṣṭvābhayena ca pravyathitaṃ mano mec tad eva me darśaya deva rūpaṃprasīda deveśa jagannivāsaa kirīṭinaṃ gadinaṃ cakrahastamicchāmi tvāṃ draṣṭum ahaṃ tathaivac tenaiva rūpeṇa caturbhujenasahasrabāho bhava viśvamūrte śrībhagavān uvācaa mayā prasannena tavārjunedaṃrūpaṃ paraṃ darśitam ātmayogātc tejomayaṃ viśvam anantam ādyaṃyan me tvad anyena na dṛṣṭapūrvama na vedayajñādhyayanair na dānairna ca kriyābhir na tapobhir ugraiḥc evaṃrūpaḥ śakya ahaṃ nṛlokedraṣṭuṃ tvad anyena kurupravīraa mā te vyathā mā ca vimūḍhabhāvodṛṣṭvā rūpaṃ ghoram īdṛṅ mamedamc vyapetabhīḥ prītamanāḥ punas tvaṃtad eva me rūpam idaṃ prapaśya saṃjaya uvācaa ity arjunaṃ vāsudevas tathoktvāsvakaṃ rūpaṃ darśayām āsa bhūyaḥc āśvāsayām āsa ca bhītam enaṃbhūtvā punaḥ saumyavapur mahātmā arjuna uvācaa dṛṣṭvedaṃ mānuṣaṃ rūpaṃ tava saumyaṃ janārdanac idānīm asmi saṃvṛttaḥ sacetāḥ prakṛtiṃ gataḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa sudurdarśam idaṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭavān asi yan mamac devā apy asya rūpasya nityaṃ darśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥa nāhaṃ vedair na tapasā na dānena na cejyayāc śakya evaṃvidho draṣṭuṃ dṛṣṭavān asi māṃ yathāa bhaktyā tv ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidho rjunac jñātuṃ draṣṭuṃ ca tattvena praveṣṭuṃ ca paraṃtapaa matkarmakṛn matparamo madbhaktaḥ saṅgavarjitaḥc nirvairaḥ sarvabhūteṣu yaḥ sa mām eti pāṇḍava arjuna uvācaa evaṃ satatayuktā ye bhaktās tvāṃ paryupāsatec ye cāpy akṣaram avyaktaṃ teṣāṃ ke yogavittamāḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa mayy āveśya mano ye māṃ nityayuktā upāsatec śraddhayā parayopetās te me yuktatamā matāḥa ye tv akṣaram anirdeśyam avyaktaṃ paryupāsatec sarvatragam acintyaṃ ca kūṭastham acalaṃ dhruvama saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ sarvatra samabuddhayaḥc te prāpnuvanti mām eva sarvabhūtahite ratāḥa kleśo dhikataras teṣām avyaktāsaktacetasāmc avyaktā hi gatir duḥkhaṃ dehavadbhir avāpyatea ye tu sarvāṇi karmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya matparāḥc ananyenaiva yogena māṃ dhyāyanta upāsatea teṣām ahaṃ samuddhartā mṛtyusaṃsārasāgarātc bhavāmi nacirāt pārtha mayy āveśitacetasāma mayy eva mana ādhatsva mayi buddhiṃ niveśayac nivasiṣyasi mayy eva ata ūrdhvaṃ na saṃśayaḥa atha cittaṃ samādhātuṃ na śaknoṣi mayi sthiramc abhyāsayogena tato mām icchāptuṃ dhanaṃjayaa abhyāse py asamartho si matkarmaparamo bhavac madartham api karmāṇi kurvan siddhim avāpsyasia athaitad apy aśakto si kartuṃ madyogam āśritaḥc sarvakarmaphalatyāgaṃ tataḥ kuru yatātmavāna śreyo hi jñānam abhyāsāj jñānād dhyānaṃ viśiṣyatec dhyānāt karmaphalatyāgas tyāgāc chāntir anantarama adveṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ maitraḥ karuṇa eva cac nirmamo nirahaṃkāraḥ samaduḥkhasukhaḥ kṣamīa saṃtuṣṭaḥ satataṃ yogī yatātmā dṛḍhaniścayaḥc mayy arpitamanobuddhir yo madbhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥa yasmān nodvijate loko lokān nodvijate ca yaḥc harṣāmarṣabhayodvegair mukto yaḥ sa ca me priyaḥa anapekṣaḥ śucir dakṣa udāsīno gatavyathaḥc sarvārambhaparityāgī yo madbhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥa yo na hṛṣyati na dveṣṭi na śocati na kāṅkṣatic śubhāśubhaparityāgī bhaktimān yaḥ sa me priyaḥa samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā mānāvamānayoḥc śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkheṣu samaḥ saṅgavivarjitaḥa tulyanindāstutir maunī saṃtuṣṭo yena kena citc aniketaḥ sthiramatir bhaktimān me priyo naraḥa ye tu dharmyāmṛtam idaṃ yathoktaṃ paryupāsatec śraddadhānā matparamā bhaktās te tīva me priyāḥ arjuna uvāca prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva kṣetraṃ kṣetrajñam eva ca etad veditum icchāmi jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ ca keśava śrībhagavān uvāca prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva kṣetraṃ kṣetrajñam eva ca etat te kathayiṣyāmi jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ ca bhārataa idaṃ śarīraṃ kaunteya kṣetram ity abhidhīyatec etad yo vetti taṃ prāhuḥ kṣetrajña iti tadvidaḥa kṣetrajñaṃ cāpi māṃ viddhi sarvakṣetreṣu bhāratac kṣetrakṣetrajñayor jñānaṃ yat taj jñānaṃ mataṃ mamaa tat kṣetraṃ yac ca yādṛk ca yadvikāri yataś ca yatc sa ca yo yatprabhāvaś ca tat samāsena me śṛṇua ṛṣibhir bahudhā gītaṃ chandobhir vividhaiḥ pṛthakc brahmasūtrapadaiś caiva hetumadbhir viniścitaiḥa mahābhūtāny ahaṃkāro buddhir avyaktam eva cac indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca pañca cendriyagocarāḥa icchā dveṣaḥ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ saṃghātaś cetanā dhṛtiḥc etat kṣetraṃ samāsena savikāram udāhṛtama amānitvam adambhitvam ahiṃsā kṣāntir ārjavamc ācāryopāsanaṃ śaucaṃ sthairyam ātmavinigrahaḥa indriyārtheṣu vairāgyam anahaṃkāra eva cac janmamṛtyujarāvyādhiduḥkhadoṣānudarśanama asaktir anabhiṣvaṅgaḥ putradāragṛhādiṣuc nityaṃ ca samacittatvam iṣṭāniṣṭopapattiṣua mayi cānanyayogena bhaktir avyabhicāriṇīc viviktadeśasevitvam aratir janasaṃsadia adhyātmajñānanityatvaṃ tattvajñānārthadarśanamc etaj jñānam iti proktam ajñānaṃ yad ato nyathāa jñeyaṃ yat tat pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvāmṛtam aśnutec anādimat paraṃ brahma na sat tan nāsad ucyatea sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tat sarvatokṣiśiromukhamc sarvataḥśrutimal loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhatia sarvendriyaguṇābhāsaṃ sarvendriyavivarjitamc asaktaṃ sarvabhṛc caiva nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ caa bahir antaś ca bhūtānām acaraṃ caram eva cac sūkṣmatvāt tad avijñeyaṃ dūrasthaṃ cāntike ca tata avibhaktaṃ ca bhūteṣu vibhaktam iva ca sthitamc bhūtabhartṛ ca taj jñeyaṃ grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu caa jyotiṣām api taj jyotis tamasaḥ param ucyatec jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānagamyaṃ hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitama iti kṣetraṃ tathā jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ coktaṃ samāsataḥc madbhakta etad vijñāya madbhāvāyopapadyatea prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva viddhy anādī ubhāv apic vikārāṃś ca guṇāṃś caiva viddhi prakṛtisaṃbhavāna kāryakāraṇakartṛtve hetuḥ prakṛtir ucyatec puruṣaḥ sukhaduḥkhānāṃ bhoktṛtve hetur ucyatea puruṣaḥ prakṛtistho hi bhuṅkte prakṛtijān guṇānc kāraṇaṃ guṇasaṅgo sya sadasadyonijanmasua upadraṣṭānumantā ca bhartā bhoktā maheśvaraḥc paramātmeti cāpy ukto dehe smin puruṣaḥ paraḥa ya evaṃ vetti puruṣaṃ prakṛtiṃ ca guṇaiḥ sahac sarvathā vartamāno pi na sa bhūyo bhijāyatea dhyānenātmani paśyanti ke cid ātmānam ātmanāc anye sāṃkhyena yogena karmayogena cāparea anye tv evam ajānantaḥ śrutvānyebhya upāsatec te pi cātitaranty eva mṛtyuṃ śrutiparāyaṇāḥa yāvat saṃjāyate kiṃ cit sattvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamamc kṣetrakṣetrajñasaṃyogāt tad viddhi bharatarṣabhaa samaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantaṃ parameśvaramc vinaśyatsv avinaśyantaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyatia samaṃ paśyan hi sarvatra samavasthitam īśvaramc na hinasty ātmanātmānaṃ tato yāti parāṃ gatima prakṛtyaiva ca karmāṇi kriyamāṇāni sarvaśaḥc yaḥ paśyati tathātmānam akartāraṃ sa paśyatia yadā bhūtapṛthagbhāvam ekastham anupaśyatic tata eva ca vistāraṃ brahma saṃpadyate tadāa anāditvān nirguṇatvāt paramātmāyam avyayaḥc śarīrastho pi kaunteya na karoti na lipyatea yathā sarvagataṃ saukṣmyād ākāśaṃ nopalipyatec sarvatrāvasthito dehe tathātmā nopalipyatea yathā prakāśayaty ekaḥ kṛtsnaṃ lokam imaṃ raviḥc kṣetraṃ kṣetrī tathā kṛtsnaṃ prakāśayati bhārataa kṣetrakṣetrajñayor evam antaraṃ jñānacakṣuṣāc bhūtaprakṛtimokṣaṃ ca ye vidur yānti te param śrībhagavān uvācaa paraṃ bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi jñānānāṃ jñānam uttamamc yaj jñātvā munayaḥ sarve parāṃ siddhim ito gatāḥa idaṃ jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥc sarge pi nopajāyante pralaye na vyathanti caa mama yonir mahad brahma tasmin garbhaṃ dadhāmy ahamc saṃbhavaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tato bhavati bhārataa sarvayoniṣu kaunteya mūrtayaḥ saṃbhavanti yāḥc tāsāṃ brahma mahad yonir ahaṃ bījapradaḥ pitāa sattvaṃ rajas tama iti guṇāḥ prakṛtisaṃbhavāḥc nibadhnanti mahābāho dehe dehinam avyayama tatra sattvaṃ nirmalatvāt prakāśakam anāmayamc sukhasaṅgena badhnāti jñānasaṅgena cānaghaa rajo rāgātmakaṃ viddhi tṛṣṇāsaṅgasamudbhavamc tan nibadhnāti kaunteya karmasaṅgena dehinama tamas tv ajñānajaṃ viddhi mohanaṃ sarvadehināmc pramādālasyanidrābhis tan nibadhnāti bhārataa sattvaṃ sukhe sañjayati rajaḥ karmaṇi bhāratac jñānam āvṛtya tu tamaḥ pramāde sañjayaty utaa rajas tamaś cābhibhūya sattvaṃ bhavati bhāratac rajaḥ sattvaṃ tamaś caiva tamaḥ sattvaṃ rajas tathāa sarvadvāreṣu dehe smin prakāśa upajāyatec jñānaṃ yadā tadā vidyād vivṛddhaṃ sattvam ity utaa lobhaḥ pravṛttir ārambhaḥ karmaṇām aśamaḥ spṛhāc rajasy etāni jāyante vivṛddhe bharatarṣabhaa aprakāśo pravṛttiś ca pramādo moha eva cac tamasy etāni jāyante vivṛddhe kurunandanaa yadā sattve pravṛddhe tu pralayaṃ yāti dehabhṛtc tadottamavidāṃ lokān amalān pratipadyatea rajasi pralayaṃ gatvā karmasaṅgiṣu jāyatec tathā pralīnas tamasi mūḍhayoniṣu jāyatea karmaṇaḥ sukṛtasyāhuḥ sāttvikaṃ nirmalaṃ phalamc rajasas tu phalaṃ duḥkham ajñānaṃ tamasaḥ phalama sattvāt saṃjāyate jñānaṃ rajaso lobha eva cac pramādamohau tamaso bhavato jñānam eva caa ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti sattvasthā madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥc jaghanyaguṇavṛttasthā adho gacchanti tāmasāḥa nānyaṃ guṇebhyaḥ kartāraṃ yadā draṣṭānupaśyatic guṇebhyaś ca paraṃ vetti madbhāvaṃ so dhigacchatia guṇān etān atītya trīn dehī dehasamudbhavānc janmamṛtyujarāduḥkhair vimukto mṛtam aśnute arjuna uvācaa kair liṅgais trīn guṇān etān atīto bhavati prabhoc kimācāraḥ kathaṃ caitāṃs trīn guṇān ativartate śrībhagavān uvācaa prakāśaṃ ca pravṛttiṃ ca moham eva ca pāṇḍavac na dveṣṭi saṃpravṛttāni na nivṛttāni kāṅkṣatia udāsīnavad āsīno guṇair yo na vicālyatec guṇā vartanta ity eva yo vatiṣṭhati neṅgatea samaduḥkhasukhaḥ svasthaḥ samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥc tulyapriyāpriyo dhīras tulyanindātmasaṃstutiḥa mānāvamānayos tulyas tulyo mitrāripakṣayoḥc sarvārambhaparityāgī guṇātītaḥ sa ucyatea māṃ ca yo vyabhicāreṇa bhaktiyogena sevatec sa guṇān samatītyaitān brahmabhūyāya kalpatea brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāham amṛtasyāvyayasya cac śāśvatasya ca dharmasya sukhasyaikāntikasya ca śrībhagavān uvācaa ūrdhvamūlam adhaḥśākham aśvatthaṃ prāhur avyayamc chandāṃsi yasya parṇāni yas taṃ veda sa vedavita adhaś cordhvaṃ prasṛtās tasya śākhāguṇapravṛddhā viṣayapravālāḥc adhaś ca mūlāny anusaṃtatānikarmānubandhīni manuṣyalokea na rūpam asyeha tathopalabhyatenānto na cādir na ca saṃpratiṣṭhāc aśvattham enaṃ suvirūḍhamūlamasaṅgaśastreṇa dṛḍhena chittvāa tataḥ padaṃ tatparimārgitavyaṃyasmin gatā na nivartanti bhūyaḥc tam eva cādyaṃ puruṣaṃ prapadyeyataḥ pravṛttiḥ prasṛtā purāṇīa nirmānamohā jitasaṅgadoṣāadhyātmanityā vinivṛttakāmāḥc dvaṃdvair vimuktāḥ sukhaduḥkhasaṃjñairgacchanty amūḍhāḥ padam avyayaṃ tata na tad bhāsayate sūryo na śaśāṅko na pāvakaḥc yad gatvā na nivartante tad dhāma paramaṃ mamaa mamaivāṃśo jīvaloke jīvabhūtaḥ sanātanaḥc manaḥṣaṣṭhānīndriyāṇi prakṛtisthāni karṣatia śarīraṃ yad avāpnoti yac cāpy utkrāmatīśvaraḥc gṛhītvaitāni saṃyāti vāyur gandhān ivāśayāta śrotraṃ cakṣuḥ sparśanaṃ ca rasanaṃ ghrāṇam eva cac adhiṣṭhāya manaś cāyaṃ viṣayān upasevatea utkrāmantaṃ sthitaṃ vāpi bhuñjānaṃ vā guṇānvitamc vimūḍhā nānupaśyanti paśyanti jñānacakṣuṣaḥa yatanto yoginaś cainaṃ paśyanty ātmany avasthitamc yatanto py akṛtātmāno nainaṃ paśyanty acetasaḥa yad ādityagataṃ tejo jagad bhāsayate khilamc yac candramasi yac cāgnau tat tejo viddhi māmakama gām āviśya ca bhūtāni dhārayāmy aham ojasāc puṣṇāmi cauṣadhīḥ sarvāḥ somo bhūtvā rasātmakaḥa ahaṃ vaiśvānaro bhūtvā prāṇināṃ deham āśritaḥc prāṇāpānasamāyuktaḥ pacāmy annaṃ caturvidhama sarvasya cāhaṃ hṛdi saṃniviṣṭomattaḥ smṛtir jñānam apohanaṃ cac vedaiś ca sarvair aham eva vedyovedāntakṛd vedavid eva cāhama dvāv imau puruṣau loke kṣaraś cākṣara eva cac kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭastho kṣara ucyatea uttamaḥ puruṣas tv anyaḥ paramātmety udāhṛtaḥc yo lokatrayam āviśya bibharty avyaya īśvaraḥa yasmāt kṣaram atīto ham akṣarād api cottamaḥc ato smi loke vede ca prathitaḥ puruṣottamaḥa yo mām evam asaṃmūḍho jānāti puruṣottamamc sa sarvavid bhajati māṃ sarvabhāvena bhārataa iti guhyatamaṃ śāstram idam uktaṃ mayānaghac etad buddhvā buddhimān syāt kṛtakṛtyaś ca bhārata śrībhagavān uvācaa abhayaṃ sattvasaṃśuddhir jñānayogavyavasthitiḥc dānaṃ damaś ca yajñaś ca svādhyāyas tapa ārjavama ahiṃsā satyam akrodhas tyāgaḥ śāntir apaiśunamc dayā bhūteṣv aloluptvaṃ mārdavaṃ hrīr acāpalama tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucam adroho nātimānitāc bhavanti saṃpadaṃ daivīm abhijātasya bhārataa dambho darpo timānaś ca krodhaḥ pāruṣyam eva cac ajñānaṃ cābhijātasya pārtha saṃpadam āsurīma daivī saṃpad vimokṣāya nibandhāyāsurī matāc mā śucaḥ saṃpadaṃ daivīm abhijāto si pāṇḍavaa dvau bhūtasargau loke smin daiva āsura eva cac daivo vistaraśaḥ prokta āsuraṃ pārtha me śṛṇua pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca janā na vidur āsurāḥc na śaucaṃ nāpi cācāro na satyaṃ teṣu vidyatea asatyam apratiṣṭhaṃ te jagad āhur anīśvaramc aparasparasaṃbhūtaṃ kim anyat kāmahaitukama etāṃ dṛṣṭim avaṣṭabhya naṣṭātmāno lpabuddhayaḥc prabhavanty ugrakarmāṇaḥ kṣayāya jagato hitāḥa kāmam āśritya duṣpūraṃ dambhamānamadānvitāḥc mohād gṛhītvāsadgrāhān pravartante śucivratāḥa cintām aparimeyāṃ ca pralayāntām upāśritāḥc kāmopabhogaparamā etāvad iti niścitāḥa āśāpāśaśatair baddhāḥ kāmakrodhaparāyaṇāḥc īhante kāmabhogārtham anyāyenārthasaṃcayāna idam adya mayā labdham idaṃ prāpsye manorathamc idam astīdam api me bhaviṣyati punar dhanama asau mayā hataḥ śatrur haniṣye cāparān apic īśvaro ham ahaṃ bhogī siddho haṃ balavān sukhīa āḍhyo bhijanavān asmi ko nyo sti sadṛśo mayāc yakṣye dāsyāmi modiṣya ity ajñānavimohitāḥa anekacittavibhrāntā mohajālasamāvṛtāḥc prasaktāḥ kāmabhogeṣu patanti narake śucaua ātmasaṃbhāvitāḥ stabdhā dhanamānamadānvitāḥc yajante nāmayajñais te dambhenāvidhipūrvakama ahaṃkāraṃ balaṃ darpaṃ kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca saṃśritāḥc mām ātmaparadeheṣu pradviṣanto bhyasūyakāḥa tān ahaṃ dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu narādhamānc kṣipāmy ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣv eva yoniṣua āsurīṃ yonim āpannā mūḍhā janmani janmanic mām aprāpyaiva kaunteya tato yānty adhamāṃ gatima trividhaṃ narakasyedaṃ dvāraṃ nāśanam ātmanaḥc kāmaḥ krodhas tathā lobhas tasmād etat trayaṃ tyajeta etair vimuktaḥ kaunteya tamodvārais tribhir naraḥc ācaraty ātmanaḥ śreyas tato yāti parāṃ gatima yaḥ śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥc na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatima tasmāc chāstraṃ pramāṇaṃ te kāryākāryavyavasthitauc jñātvā śāstravidhānoktaṃ karma kartum ihārhasi arjuna uvācaa ye śāstravidhim utsṛjya yajante śraddhayānvitāḥc teṣāṃ niṣṭhā tu kā kṛṣṇa sattvam āho rajas tamaḥ śrībhagavān uvācaa trividhā bhavati śraddhā dehināṃ sā svabhāvajāc sāttvikī rājasī caiva tāmasī ceti tāṃ śṛṇua sattvānurūpā sarvasya śraddhā bhavati bhāratac śraddhāmayo yaṃ puruṣo yo yacchraddhaḥ sa eva saḥa yajante sāttvikā devān yakṣarakṣāṃsi rājasāḥc pretān bhūtagaṇāṃś cānye yajante tāmasā janāḥa aśāstravihitaṃ ghoraṃ tapyante ye tapo janāḥc dambhāhaṃkārasaṃyuktāḥ kāmarāgabalānvitāḥa karśayantaḥ śarīrasthaṃ bhūtagrāmam acetasaḥc māṃ caivāntaḥśarīrasthaṃ tān viddhy āsuraniścayāna āhāras tv api sarvasya trividho bhavati priyaḥc yajñas tapas tathā dānaṃ teṣāṃ bhedam imaṃ śṛṇua āyuḥsattvabalārogyasukhaprītivivardhanāḥc rasyāḥ snigdhāḥ sthirā hṛdyā āhārāḥ sāttvikapriyāḥa kaṭvamlalavaṇātyuṣṇatīkṣṇarūkṣavidāhinaḥc āhārā rājasasyeṣṭā duḥkhaśokāmayapradāḥa yātayāmaṃ gatarasaṃ pūti paryuṣitaṃ ca yatc ucchiṣṭam api cāmedhyaṃ bhojanaṃ tāmasapriyama aphalākāṅkṣibhir yajño vidhidṛṣṭo ya ijyatec yaṣṭavyam eveti manaḥ samādhāya sa sāttvikaḥa abhisaṃdhāya tu phalaṃ dambhārtham api caiva yatc ijyate bharataśreṣṭha taṃ yajñaṃ viddhi rājasama vidhihīnam asṛṣṭānnaṃ mantrahīnam adakṣiṇamc śraddhāvirahitaṃ yajñaṃ tāmasaṃ paricakṣatea devadvijaguruprājñapūjanaṃ śaucam ārjavamc brahmacaryam ahiṃsā ca śārīraṃ tapa ucyatea anudvegakaraṃ vākyaṃ satyaṃ priyahitaṃ ca yatc svādhyāyābhyasanaṃ caiva vāṅmayaṃ tapa ucyatea manaḥprasādaḥ saumyatvaṃ maunam ātmavinigrahaḥc bhāvasaṃśuddhir ity etat tapo mānasam ucyatea śraddhayā parayā taptaṃ tapas tat trividhaṃ naraiḥc aphalākāṅkṣibhir yuktaiḥ sāttvikaṃ paricakṣatea satkāramānapūjārthaṃ tapo dambhena caiva yatc kriyate tad iha proktaṃ rājasaṃ calam adhruvama mūḍhagrāheṇātmano yat pīḍayā kriyate tapaḥc parasyotsādanārthaṃ vā tat tāmasam udāhṛtama dātavyam iti yad dānaṃ dīyate nupakāriṇec deśe kāle ca pātre ca tad dānaṃ sāttvikaṃ smṛtama yat tu pratyupakārārthaṃ phalam uddiśya vā punaḥc dīyate ca parikliṣṭaṃ tad dānaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtama adeśakāle yad dānam apātrebhyaś ca dīyatec asatkṛtam avajñātaṃ tat tāmasam udāhṛtama oṃ tat sad iti nirdeśo brahmaṇas trividhaḥ smṛtaḥc brāhmaṇās tena vedāś ca yajñāś ca vihitāḥ purāa tasmād om ity udāhṛtya yajñadānatapaḥkriyāḥc pravartante vidhānoktāḥ satataṃ brahmavādināma tad ity anabhisaṃdhāya phalaṃ yajñatapaḥkriyāḥc dānakriyāś ca vividhāḥ kriyante mokṣakāṅkṣibhiḥa sadbhāve sādhubhāve ca sad ity etat prayujyatec praśaste karmaṇi tathā sacchabdaḥ pārtha yujyatea yajñe tapasi dāne ca sthitiḥ sad iti cocyatec karma caiva tadarthīyaṃ sad ity evābhidhīyatea aśraddhayā hutaṃ dattaṃ tapas taptaṃ kṛtaṃ ca yatc asad ity ucyate pārtha na ca tat pretya no iha arjuna uvācaa saṃnyāsasya mahābāho tattvam icchāmi veditumc tyāgasya ca hṛṣīkeśa pṛthak keśiniṣūdana śrībhagavān uvācaa kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaṃ saṃnyāsaṃ kavayo viduḥc sarvakarmaphalatyāgaṃ prāhus tyāgaṃ vicakṣaṇāḥa tyājyaṃ doṣavad ity eke karma prāhur manīṣiṇaḥc yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyam iti cāparea niścayaṃ śṛṇu me tatra tyāge bharatasattamac tyāgo hi puruṣavyāghra trividhaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥa yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyaṃ kāryam eva tatc yajño dānaṃ tapaś caiva pāvanāni manīṣiṇāma etāny api tu karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā phalāni cac kartavyānīti me pārtha niścitaṃ matam uttamama niyatasya tu saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇo nopapadyatec mohāt tasya parityāgas tāmasaḥ parikīrtitaḥa duḥkham ity eva yat karma kāyakleśabhayāt tyajetc sa kṛtvā rājasaṃ tyāgaṃ naiva tyāgaphalaṃ labheta kāryam ity eva yat karma niyataṃ kriyate rjunac saṅgaṃ tyaktvā phalaṃ caiva sa tyāgaḥ sāttviko mataḥa na dveṣṭy akuśalaṃ karma kuśale nānuṣajjatec tyāgī sattvasamāviṣṭo medhāvī chinnasaṃśayaḥa na hi dehabhṛtā śakyaṃ tyaktuṃ karmāṇy aśeṣataḥc yas tu karmaphalatyāgī sa tyāgīty abhidhīyatea aniṣṭam iṣṭaṃ miśraṃ ca trividhaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalamc bhavaty atyāgināṃ pretya na tu saṃnyāsināṃ kva cita pañcaitāni mahābāho kāraṇāni nibodha mec sāṃkhye kṛtānte proktāni siddhaye sarvakarmaṇāma adhiṣṭhānaṃ tathā kartā karaṇaṃ ca pṛthagvidhamc vividhāś ca pṛthakceṣṭā daivaṃ caivātra pañcamama śarīravāṅmanobhir yat karma prārabhate naraḥc nyāyyaṃ vā viparītaṃ vā pañcaite tasya hetavaḥa tatraivaṃ sati kartāram ātmānaṃ kevalaṃ tu yaḥc paśyaty akṛtabuddhitvān na sa paśyati durmatiḥa yasya nāhaṃkṛto bhāvo buddhir yasya na lipyatec hatvāpi sa imāṃl lokān na hanti na nibadhyatea jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ parijñātā trividhā karmacodanāc karaṇaṃ karma karteti trividhaḥ karmasaṃgrahaḥa jñānaṃ karma ca kartā ca tridhaiva guṇabhedataḥc procyate guṇasaṃkhyāne yathāvac chṛṇu tāny apia sarvabhūteṣu yenaikaṃ bhāvam avyayam īkṣatec avibhaktaṃ vibhakteṣu taj jñānaṃ viddhi sāttvikama pṛthaktvena tu yaj jñānaṃ nānābhāvān pṛthagvidhānc vetti sarveṣu bhūteṣu taj jñānaṃ viddhi rājasama yat tu kṛtsnavad ekasmin kārye saktam ahaitukamc atattvārthavad alpaṃ ca tat tāmasam udāhṛtama niyataṃ saṅgarahitam arāgadveṣataḥ kṛtamc aphalaprepsunā karma yat tat sāttvikam ucyatea yat tu kāmepsunā karma sāhaṃkāreṇa vā punaḥc kriyate bahulāyāsaṃ tad rājasam udāhṛtama anubandhaṃ kṣayaṃ hiṃsām anapekṣya ca pauruṣamc mohād ārabhyate karma yat tat tāmasam ucyatea muktasaṅgo nahaṃvādī dhṛtyutsāhasamanvitaḥc siddhyasiddhyor nirvikāraḥ kartā sāttvika ucyatea rāgī karmaphalaprepsur lubdho hiṃsātmako śuciḥc harṣaśokānvitaḥ kartā rājasaḥ parikīrtitaḥa ayuktaḥ prākṛtaḥ stabdhaḥ śaṭho naikṛtiko lasaḥc viṣādī dīrghasūtrī ca kartā tāmasa ucyatea buddher bhedaṃ dhṛteś caiva guṇatas trividhaṃ śṛṇuc procyamānam aśeṣeṇa pṛthaktvena dhanaṃjayaa pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca kāryākārye bhayābhayec bandhaṃ mokṣaṃ ca yā vetti buddhiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikīa yayā dharmam adharmaṃ ca kāryaṃ cākāryam eva cac ayathāvat prajānāti buddhiḥ sā pārtha rājasīa adharmaṃ dharmam iti yā manyate tamasāvṛtāc sarvārthān viparītāṃś ca buddhiḥ sā pārtha tāmasīa dhṛtyā yayā dhārayate manaḥprāṇendriyakriyāḥc yogenāvyabhicāriṇyā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha sāttvikīa yayā tu dharmakāmārthān dhṛtyā dhārayate rjunac prasaṅgena phalākāṅkṣī dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha rājasīa yayā svapnaṃ bhayaṃ śokaṃ viṣādaṃ madam eva cac na vimuñcati durmedhā dhṛtiḥ sā pārtha tāmasīa sukhaṃ tv idānīṃ trividhaṃ śṛṇu me bharatarṣabhac abhyāsād ramate yatra duḥkhāntaṃ ca nigacchatia yat tadagre viṣam iva pariṇāme mṛtopamamc tat sukhaṃ sāttvikaṃ proktam ātmabuddhiprasādajama viṣayendriyasaṃyogād yat tadagre mṛtopamamc pariṇāme viṣam iva tat sukhaṃ rājasaṃ smṛtama yad agre cānubandhe ca sukhaṃ mohanam ātmanaḥc nidrālasyapramādotthaṃ tat tāmasam udāhṛtama na tad asti pṛthivyāṃ vā divi deveṣu vā punaḥc sattvaṃ prakṛtijair muktaṃ yad ebhiḥ syāt tribhir guṇaiḥa brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ ca paraṃtapac karmāṇi pravibhaktāni svabhāvaprabhavair guṇaiḥa śamo damas tapaḥ śaucaṃ kṣāntir ārjavam eva cac jñānaṃ vijñānam āstikyaṃ brahmakarma svabhāvajama śauryaṃ tejo dhṛtir dākṣyaṃ yuddhe cāpy apalāyanamc dānam īśvarabhāvaś ca kṣatrakarma svabhāvajama kṛṣigorakṣyavāṇijyaṃ vaiśyakarma svabhāvajamc paricaryātmakaṃ karma śūdrasyāpi svabhāvajama sve sve karmaṇy abhirataḥ saṃsiddhiṃ labhate naraḥc svakarmanirataḥ siddhiṃ yathā vindati tac chṛṇua yataḥ pravṛttir bhūtānāṃ yena sarvam idaṃ tatamc svakarmaṇā tam abhyarcya siddhiṃ vindati mānavaḥa śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitātb svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmodayād apic svabhāvaniyataṃ karma kurvan nāpnoti kilbiṣama sahajaṃ karma kaunteya sadoṣam api na tyajetc sarvārambhā hi doṣeṇa dhūmenāgnir ivāvṛtāḥa asaktabuddhiḥ sarvatra jitātmā vigataspṛhaḥc naiṣkarmyasiddhiṃ paramāṃ saṃnyāsenādhigacchatia siddhiṃ prāpto yathā brahma tathāpnoti nibodha mec samāsenaiva kaunteya niṣṭhā jñānasya yā parāa buddhyā viśuddhayā yukto dhṛtyātmānaṃ niyamya cac śabdādīn viṣayāṃs tyaktvā rāgadveṣau vyudasya caa viviktasevī laghvāśī yatavākkāyamānasaḥc dhyānayogaparo nityaṃ vairāgyaṃ samupāśritaḥa ahaṃkāraṃ balaṃ darpaṃ kāmaṃ krodhaṃ parigrahamc vimucya nirmamaḥ śānto brahmabhūyāya kalpatea brahmabhūtaḥ prasannātmā na śocati na kāṅkṣatic samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu madbhaktiṃ labhate parāma bhaktyā mām abhijānāti yāvān yaś cāsmi tattvataḥc tato māṃ tattvato jñātvā viśate tadanantarama sarvakarmāṇy api sadā kurvāṇo madvyapāśrayaḥc matprasādād avāpnoti śāśvataṃ padam avyayama cetasā sarvakarmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya matparaḥc buddhiyogam upāśritya maccittaḥ satataṃ bhavaa maccittaḥ sarvadurgāṇi matprasādāt tariṣyasic atha cet tvam ahaṃkārān na śroṣyasi vinaṅkṣyasia yad ahaṃkāram āśritya na yotsya iti manyasec mithyaiṣa vyavasāyas te prakṛtis tvāṃ niyokṣyatia svabhāvajena kaunteya nibaddhaḥ svena karmaṇāc kartuṃ necchasi yan mohāt kariṣyasy avaśo pi tata īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛddeśe rjuna tiṣṭhatic bhrāmayan sarvabhūtāni yantrārūḍhāni māyayāa tam eva śaraṇaṃ gaccha sarvabhāvena bhāratac tatprasādāt parāṃ śāntiṃ sthānaṃ prāpsyasi śāśvatama iti te jñānam ākhyātaṃ guhyād guhyataraṃ mayāc vimṛśyaitad aśeṣeṇa yathecchasi tathā kurua sarvaguhyatamaṃ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu me paramaṃ vacaḥc iṣṭo si me dṛḍham iti tato vakṣyāmi te hitama manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṃ namaskuruc mām evaiṣyasi satyaṃ te pratijāne priyo si mea sarvadharmān parityajya mām ekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajac ahaṃ tvā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥa idaṃ te nātapaskāya nābhaktāya kadā canac na cāśuśrūṣave vācyaṃ na ca māṃ yo bhyasūyatia ya idaṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ madbhakteṣv abhidhāsyatic bhaktiṃ mayi parāṃ kṛtvā mām evaiṣyaty asaṃśayaḥa na ca tasmān manuṣyeṣu kaś cin me priyakṛttamaḥc bhavitā na ca me tasmād anyaḥ priyataro bhuvia adhyeṣyate ca ya imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṃvādam āvayoḥc jñānayajñena tenāham iṣṭaḥ syām iti me matiḥa śraddhāvān anasūyaś ca śṛṇuyād api yo naraḥc so pi muktaḥ śubhāṃl lokān prāpnuyāt puṇyakarmaṇāma kaccid etac chrutaṃ pārtha tvayaikāgreṇa cetasāc kaccid ajñānasaṃmohaḥ pranaṣṭas te dhanaṃjaya arjuna uvācaa naṣṭo mohaḥ smṛtir labdhā tvatprasādān mayācyutac sthito smi gatasaṃdehaḥ kariṣye vacanaṃ tava saṃjaya uvācaa ity ahaṃ vāsudevasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥc saṃvādam imam aśrauṣam adbhutaṃ romaharṣaṇama vyāsaprasādāc chrutavān etad guhyam ahaṃ paramc yogaṃ yogeśvarāt kṛṣṇāt sākṣāt kathayataḥ svayama rājan saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya saṃvādam imam adbhutamc keśavārjunayoḥ puṇyaṃ hṛṣyāmi ca muhur muhuḥa tac ca saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya rūpam atyadbhutaṃ hareḥc vismayo me mahān rājan hṛṣyāmi ca punaḥ punaḥa yatra yogeśvaraḥ kṛṣṇo yatra pārtho dhanurdharaḥc tatra śrīr vijayo bhūtir dhruvā nītir matir mamad bhagavadbhaktiyuktasya tatprasādātmabodhataḥd sukhaṃ bandhavimuktiḥ syād iti gītārthasaṃgrahaḥd ṣaṭ śatāni saviṃśāni ślokānāṃ prāha keśavaḥd arjunaḥ saptapañcāśat saptaṣaṣṭis tu saṃjayaḥd dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ślokam ekaṃ gītāyā mānam ucyated vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad gītā sugītā kartavyā kim anyaiḥ śāstravistaraiḥd yā ceyaṃ padmanābhasya mukhapadmād viniḥsṛtād sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadevamayo hariḥd sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvavedamayo manuḥd gaṅgā gītā ca gāyatrī govindeti hṛdi sthited caturgakārasaṃyukte punarjanma na vidyated bhāratāmṛtasarvasvagītāyā mathitasya cad sāram uddhṛtya kṛṣṇena arjunasya mukhe hutamdA jñānayogavinirmuktaṃ taj jñānaṃ brūhi keśava  dA sarvatojyotir ākāśaṃ sarvabhūtaguṇānvitam dA sarvataḥparamātmānam akṣayaṃ paramaṃ padam  dA anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ mahājyotir atidhruvam dA atyantaparamaṃ sthānaṃ śabdādiguṇavarjitam  dA yat tat parataraṃ jyotir dhruvāt parataraṃ sthitam dA ācaturyugam adyāpi kathitaṃ na hi kasya cit  dA ātmadehe mayā sṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ kṣetram eva ca dA sakalaṃ tu bhavet kṣetraṃ niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ padam  dA arjuna tvatprasādena śṛṇvantu munisattamāḥ dA adya muktā mahābāho tvatprasādād dhanaṃjaya  dA pramāṇaṃ vedatattvānāṃ sāṃkhyādīny abhiyoginām dA teṣāṃ na vidyate niṣṭhā sarvaiḥ pāṣaṇḍibhiḥ saha  dA kathitaṃ ca mayā jñānaṃ devānām api durlabham dA viśvarūpamayaṃ divyaṃ bhairavagranthibindunā  dA suṣumṇā dakṣiṇe mārge darśitā viśvarūpiṇā dA aprakāśam idaṃ praśnaṃ yan mayā kathitaṃ tava  dA nāgnir vāyur na cākāśaṃ na kṣitir nāpi vā jalam dA na manobuddhyahaṃkāraṃ gūḍhārthaṃ kathitaṃ tava  dA anityo nityatāṃ yāti yadā bhāvaṃ na paśyati dA śūnyaṃ nirañjanākāraṃ nirvāṇaṃ dhruvam avyayam  dA puruṣaṃ nirguṇaṃ sākṣāt sarvataś caiva tiṣṭhati dA sarvaṃ tat syāt paraṃ brahma buddhiś cāsya na budhyati  dA pratibhāvaprayatnena hariṃ trailokyabāndhavam dA daśamaṃ cāṅgulaṃ vyāpya cāśābāhyaṃ vyavasthitam  dA jīvo yatra pralīyeta sā kalā ṣoḍaśī smṛtā dA tayā sarvam idaṃ vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  dA tac cintyaṃ tena vai jñānaṃ tad atrādyā upāsate dA brahmaṇaiva hi vikhyātaṃ vedānteṣu prakāśitam  dA vedeṣu vedam ity āhur vedadhāma paraṃ matam dA tat paraṃ viditaṃ yasya sa vipro vedapāragaḥ  dA āhutiḥ sā parā jñeyā sā ca saṃdhyā pratiṣṭhitā dA gāyatrī sā parā jñeyā ajapā nāma viśrutā  dA tapasy atha tathā vede munibhiḥ samupāsyate dA tāṃ kalāṃ yo bhijānāti sa kalājño bhidhīyate  dA yāṃ jñātvā mucyate jantur garbhajanmajarādibhiḥ dA parijñānena mucyante narāḥ pātakakilbiṣaiḥ  dA iḍā bhagavatī gaṅgā piṅgalā yamunā nadī dA tayor madhye tṛtīyā tu tat prayāgam anusmaret  dA iḍā vai vaiṣṇavī nāḍī brahmanāḍī tu piṅgalā dA suṣumṇā caiśvarī nāḍī tridhā prāṇavahā smṛtā dA brahmā viṣṇur mahādevo recakaḥ pūrakumbhakaḥ  dA sakrāntiviṣuvac caiva yo bhijānāti vigraham dA nityayuktaḥ sa yogīśo brahmavidyāṃ prapadyate  dA iḍā vai gārhapatyas tu piṅgalāhavanīyakaḥ dA suṣumṇā dakṣiṇāgnis tu hy etad agnitrayaṃ smṛtam  dA tasya madhye sthitaṃ jyotiḥ somamaṇḍalam eva ca dA somamaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ tanmadhye sūryamaṇḍalam  dA sūryamaṇḍalamadhyastho jvalat tejo hutāśanaḥ dA hutāśanasya madhye tu nirdhūmāṅgāravarcasam  dA tatrāsthito mahātmāsau yogibhis tu pragīyate dA sugītaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ mana ekāgracetasā  dA śivo binduḥ śivo devo ghargharāmṛtavarcasā dA nikhilaṃ pūrayed dehaṃ viṣadāhajvarāpaham  dA sarpavatkuṭilākārasuṣumṇāveṣṭitāṃ tanum dA makāraveṣṭitāṃ kṛtvā mātṛvat pariyojayet  dA tristhānaṃ ca trimātraṃ ca tribrahma ca trirakṣaram dA ardhamātraṃ ca yo vetti sa bhaved vedapāragaḥ  dA sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tat sarvatokṣiśiromukham dA arjuna uvācadA nirmalaṃ vimalākāraṃ śuddhasphaṭikasaṃnibham  dA jīvo jīvati jīvena nāsti jīvam ajīvitam dA śrībhagavān uvācadA nirgataḥ saha saṅgena sa jīvaḥ kena jīvati  dA mukhanāsikayor madhye prāṇaḥ saṃcarate sadā dA ākāśaṃ pibate nityaṃ sa jīvas tena jīvati  dA khamadhye ca praveṣṭavyaṃ khaṃ ca brahma sanātanam dA ātmānaṃ khamayaṃ kṛtvā na kiṃ cid api cintayet  dA ūrdhvaśūnyam adhaḥśūnyaṃ madhyeśūnyaṃ nirāmayam dA triśūnyaṃ yo bhijānāti sa bhavet kulanandanaḥ  dA tasya bhāvasya bhāvātmā bhāvanā naiva yujyate dA anāvṛttasya śabdasya tasya śabdasya yo gatiḥ  dA tat padaṃ viditaṃ yena sa yogī chinnasaṃśayaḥ dA puṇyapāpaharāś caiva ye cānye pañcadaivatāḥ  dA jīvinaḥ saha gacchanti yāvat tattvaṃ na vindati dA pāpaṃ dahati jñānāgniḥ puṇyena somasūryayoḥ  dA puṇyapāpavinirmuktir eṣa yogo bhidhīyate dA dhṛtirodhi manodhīti saṃtoṣaṃ samidhāmṛtam  dA indriyāṇi paśuṃ kṛtvā yo yajeta sa dīkṣitaḥ dA paraṃ brahmādhigacchanti śabdabrahmavicintanāt  dA sakale dṛṣṭapāro pi bhāvaṃ yuñjati yuñjati dA niṣkale darśanaṃ nāsti svabhāvo bhāvaṃ yuñjati  dA tālumūle ca lampāyāṃ trikūṭaṃ tripathāntaram dA ekaṃ tattvaṃ vijānīyād vighnasyāyatanaṃ mahat  dA chinnamūlasya vṛkṣasya yathā janma na vidyate dA jñānadagdhaśarīrasya punar deho na vidyate  dA gītāḥ sugītāḥ kartavyāḥ kim anyaiḥ śāstrasaṃgrahaiḥ dA yāḥ purā padmanābhasya mukhapadmād viniḥsṛtāḥ  dA gītāgāṅgodakaṃ pītvā punarjanma na vidyate dA sarvaśāstramayī gītā sarvadharmamayo hariḥ  dA sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī dA sarvabhogamayaś cāyaṃ sarvamokṣamayo hy ayam  dA gītā gaṅgā ca gāyatrī govindo hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ dA caturgakārasmaraṇāt punarjanma na vidyate  dA gītāsāraṃ paṭhed yas tu hy acyutasya ca saṃnidhau dA tasmād guṇasahasreṇa viṣṇor nirvacanaṃ yathā  dA etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam dA paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam
