mahārathāḥa pāṇḍavāḥ somakāś caiva ye caiṣām anuyāyinaḥc dadhmuś ca muditāḥ śaṅkhān vīrāḥ sāgarasaṃbhavāna tato bheryaś ca peśyaś ca krakacā goviṣāṇikāḥc sahasaivābhyahanyanta tataḥ śabdo mahān abhūta atha devāḥ sagandharvāḥ pitaraś ca janeśvarac siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca samīyus te didṛkṣayāa ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgāḥ puraskṛtya śatakratumc samīyus tatra sahitā draṣṭuṃ tad vaiśasaṃ mahatd te sene stimite cāstāṃ vīkṣamāṇe parasparamd gaṅgāyamunayor vegau yathaivaitya parasparamd evaṃ pravṛtte te sene niḥśabde janasaṃsadid citre iva paṭālekhye darśanīyatare śubhea tato yudhiṣṭhiro dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya susamudyatec te sene sāgaraprakhye muhuḥ pracalite nṛpaa vimucya kavacaṃ vīro nikṣipya ca varāyudhamc avaruhya rathāt tūrṇaṃ padbhyām eva kṛtāñjaliḥa pitāmaham abhiprekṣya dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥc vāgyataḥ prayayau yena prāṅmukho ripuvāhinīma taṃ prayāntam abhiprekṣya kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥc avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito nvayātd bhītaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraṃ matvā bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavāna vāsudevaś ca bhagavān pṛṣṭhato nujagāma hab sātyakiś cārjunaś caiva abhimanyuś ca vīryavānc yathāmukhyāś ca rājānas tam anvājagmur utsukāḥ arjuna uvācaa kiṃ te vyavasitaṃ rājan yad asmān apahāya vaic padbhyām eva prayāto si prāṅmukho ripuvāhinīm bhīmasena uvācaa kva gamiṣyasi rājendra nikṣiptakavacāyudhaḥc daṃśiteṣv arisainyeṣu bhrātṝn utsṛjya pārthiva nakula uvācaa evaṃgate tvayi jyeṣṭhe mama bhrātari bhāratac bhīr me dunoti hṛdayaṃ brūhi gantā bhavān kva nud kvaivaṃ gamiṣyasi śreṣṭha tyaktvāsmān durbalo yathād rājā hi tvaṃ mahābāho vāgyato manyumān iva sahadeva uvācaa asmin raṇasamūhe vai vartamāne mahābhayec yoddhavye kva nu gantāsi śatrūn abhimukho nṛpa saṃjaya uvācaa evam ābhāṣyamāṇo pi bhrātṛbhiḥ kurunandanac novāca vāgyataḥ kiṃ cid gacchaty eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥa tān uvāca mahāprājño vāsudevo mahāmanāḥc abhiprāyo sya vijñāto mayeti prahasann ivaa eṣa bhīṣmaṃ tathā droṇaṃ gautamaṃ śalyam eva cac anumānya gurūn sarvān yotsyate pārthivo ribhiḥa śrūyate hi purākalpe gurūn ananumānya yaḥc yudhyate sa bhaved vyaktam apadhyāto mahattaraiḥd yuddhāyāvataraty eva tasya nāsti jayo raṇed yas tu yuddhe samutpanne gurūn dṛṣṭvātha daṃśitāna anumānya yathāśāstraṃ yas tu yudhyen mahattaraiḥc dhruvas tasya jayo yuddhe bhaved iti matir mamaa evaṃ bruvati kṛṣṇe tu dhārtarāṣṭracamūṃ pratib netrair animiṣaiḥ sarve prekṣante sma yudhiṣṭhiramc hāhākāro mahān āsīn niḥśabdās tv apare bhavana dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dūrād dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāḥc mithaḥ saṃkathayāṃ cakrur neśo sti kulapāṃsanaḥa vyaktaṃ bhīta ivābhyeti rājāsau bhīṣmam antikātc yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sasodaryaḥ śaraṇārthaṃ prayācakaḥa dhanaṃjaye kathaṃ nāthe pāṇḍave ca vṛkodarec nakule sahadeve ca bhīto bhyeti ca pāṇḍavaḥa na nūnaṃ kṣatriyakule jātaḥ saṃprathite bhuvic yathāsya hṛdayaṃ bhītam alpasattvasya saṃyugea tatas te kṣatriyāḥ sarve praśaṃsanti sma kauravānc hṛṣṭāḥ sumanaso bhūtvā cailāni dudhuvuḥ pṛthaka vyanindanta tataḥ sarve yodhās tatra viśāṃ patec yudhiṣṭhiraṃ sasodaryaṃ sahitaṃ keśavena haa tatas tat kauravaṃ sainyaṃ dhikkṛtvā tu yudhiṣṭhiramc niḥśabdam abhavat tūrṇaṃ punar eva viśāṃ patea kiṃ nu vakṣyati rājāsau kiṃ bhīṣmaḥ prativakṣyatib kiṃ nu vakṣyati rājāsau dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥb kiṃ nu vakṣyati bhīṣmo sau bharatānāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥc kiṃ bhīmaḥ samaraślāghī kiṃ nu kṛṣṇārjunāv itia vivakṣitaṃ kim asyeti saṃśayaḥ sumahān abhūtc ubhayoḥ senayo rājan yudhiṣṭhirakṛte tadāa sa vigāhya camūṃ śatroḥ śaraśaktisamākulāmc bhīṣmam evābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥa tam uvāca tataḥ pādau karābhyāṃ pīḍya pāṇḍavaḥc bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ rājā yuddhāya samupasthitam yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa āmantraye tvāṃ durdharṣa yotsye tāta tvayā sahac anujānīhi māṃ tāta āśiṣaś ca prayojayad jayeyaṃ ca ripūn sarvān anujñātas tvayānaghad yudhyantaṃ māṃ raṇe vīra tvam anujñātum arhasi bhīṣma uvācaa yady evaṃ nābhigacchethā yudhi māṃ pṛthivīpatec śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya bhārataa prīto smi putra yudhyasva jayam āpnuhi pāṇḍavac yat te bhilaṣitaṃ cānyat tad avāpnuhi saṃyugea vriyatāṃ ca varaḥ pārtha kim asmatto bhikāṅkṣasic evaṃ gate mahārāja na tavāsti parājayaḥa arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya citc iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho smy arthena kauravaiḥa atas tvāṃ klībavad vākyaṃ bravīmi kurunandanac hṛto smy arthena kauravya yuddhād anyat kim icchasi yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa mantrayasva mahāprājña hitaiṣī mama nityaśaḥc yudhyasva kauravasyārthe mamaiṣa satataṃ varaḥ bhīṣma uvācaa rājan kim atra sāhyaṃ te karomi kurunandanab mantrayiṣyāmy ahaṃ rājan yac ca te hitam uttamamc kāmaṃ yotsye parasyārthe brūhi yat te vivakṣitam yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa kathaṃ jayeyaṃ saṃgrāme bhavantam aparājitamc etan me mantraya hitaṃ yadi śreyaḥ prapaśyasi bhīṣma uvācaa na taṃ paśyāmi kaunteya yo māṃ yudhyantam āhavec vijayeta pumān kaś cid api sākṣāc chatakratuḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa hanta pṛcchāmi tasmāt tvāṃ pitāmaha namo stu tec jayopāyaṃ bravīhi tvam ātmanaḥ samare paraiḥ bhīṣma uvācaa na śatruṃ tāta paśyāmi samare yo jayeta māmb ayudhyamānaṃ saṃhatya sauhṛdena pariplutamb nyastaśastraṃ nirudyogaṃ hanyur mā śatravo yudhib nikṣiptaśastre patite vimuktakavace tathāb dravamāṇe ca bhīte ca tavāsmīti ca yo vadetb striyāṃ strīnāmadheye ca vikale caikaputrakeb aprasūte ca hīne ca na yuddhaṃ rocayāmy ahamb idaṃ ca gaditaṃ pārtha paramaṃ vratam āhavec na tāvan mṛtyukālo me punarāgamanaṃ kuru saṃjaya uvācaa tato yudhiṣṭhiro vākyaṃ bhīṣmasya kurunandanac śirasā pratijagrāha bhūyas tam abhivādya caa prāyāt punar mahābāhur ācāryasya rathaṃ pratic paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ madhyena bhrātṛbhiḥ sahaa sa droṇam abhivādyātha kṛtvā caiva pradakṣiṇamc uvāca vācā durdharṣam ātmaniḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥa āmantraye tvāṃ bhagavan yotsye vigatakalmaṣaḥc jayeyaṃ ca ripūn sarvān anujñātas tvayā dvija droṇa uvācaa yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥc śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya sarvaśaḥa tad yudhiṣṭhira tuṣṭo smi pūjitaś ca tvayānaghac anujānāmi yudhyasva vijayaṃ samavāpnuhia karavāṇi ca te kāmaṃ brūhi yat te bhikāṅkṣitamc evaṃ gate mahārāja yuddhād anyat kim icchasia arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya citc iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho smy arthena kauravaiḥa atas tvāṃ klībavad brūmo yuddhād anyat kim icchasic yotsyāmi kauravasyārthe tavāśāsyo jayo mayā yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa jayam āśāssva me brahman mantrayasva ca maddhitamc yudhyasva kauravasyārthe vara eṣa vṛto mayā droṇa uvācaa dhruvas te vijayo rājan yasya mantrī haris tavac ahaṃ ca tvābhijānāmi raṇe śatrūn vijeṣyasia yato dharmas tataḥ kṛṣṇo yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥc yudhyasva gaccha kaunteya pṛccha māṃ kiṃ bravīmi te yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa pṛcchāmi tvāṃ dvijaśreṣṭha śṛṇu me yad vivakṣitamc kathaṃ jayeyaṃ saṃgrāme bhavantam aparājitam droṇa uvācaa na te sti vijayas tāvad yāvad yudhyāmy ahaṃ raṇec mamāśu nidhane rājan yatasva saha sodaraiḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa hanta tasmān mahābāho vadhopāyaṃ vadātmanaḥc ācārya praṇipatyaiṣa pṛcchāmi tvāṃ namo stu te droṇa uvācaa na śatruṃ tāta paśyāmi yo māṃ hanyād raṇe sthitamc yudhyamānaṃ susaṃrabdhaṃ śaravarṣaughavarṣiṇama ṛte prāyagataṃ rājan nyastaśastram acetanamc hanyān māṃ yudhi yodhānāṃ satyam etad bravīmi tea śastraṃ cāhaṃ raṇe jahyāṃ śrutvā sumahad apriyamc śraddheyavākyāt puruṣād etat satyaṃ bravīmi te saṃjaya uvācaa etac chrutvā mahārāja bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥc anumānya tam ācāryaṃ prāyāc chāradvataṃ pratia so bhivādya kṛpaṃ rājā kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇamc uvāca durdharṣatamaṃ vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥa anumānaye tvāṃ yotsyāmi guro vigatakalmaṣaḥc jayeyaṃ ca ripūn sarvān anujñātas tvayānagha kṛpa uvācaa yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥc śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya sarvaśaḥd kiṃ te karomi vai kāmaṃ brūhi pāṇḍavanandanad evaṃ gate mahārāja yuddhād anyat kim icchasia arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya citc iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho smy arthena kauravaiḥa teṣām arthe mahārāja yoddhavyam iti me matiḥc atas tvāṃ klībavad brūmi yuddhād anyat kim icchasi yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa hanta pṛcchāmi te tasmād ācārya śṛṇu me vacaḥb vadhopāyaṃ bravīhi tvam ātmanaḥ samare paraiḥ saṃjaya uvācaa ity uktvā vyathito rājā novāca gatacetanaḥc taṃ gautamaḥ pratyuvāca vijñāyāsya vivakṣitame avadhyo haṃ mahīpāla yudhyasva jayam āpnuhia prītas tv abhigamenāhaṃ jayaṃ tava narādhipac āśāsiṣye sadotthāya satyam etad bravīmi tea etac chrutvā mahārāja gautamasya vacas tadāc anumānya kṛpaṃ rājā prayayau yena madrarāṭa sa śalyam abhivādyātha kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇamc uvāca rājā durdharṣam ātmaniḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥa anumānaye tvāṃ yotsyāmi guro vigatakalmaṣaḥc jayeyaṃ ca mahārāja anujñātas tvayā ripūn śalya uvācaa yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥc śapeyaṃ tvāṃ mahārāja parābhāvāya vai raṇea tuṣṭo smi pūjitaś cāsmi yat kāṅkṣasi tad astu tec anujānāmi caiva tvāṃ yudhyasva jayam āpnuhia brūhi caiva paraṃ vīra kenārthaḥ kiṃ dadāmi tec evaṃ gate mahārāja yuddhād anyat kim icchasia arthasya puruṣo dāso dāsas tv artho na kasya citc iti satyaṃ mahārāja baddho smy arthena kauravaiḥd teṣām arthe mahārāja yoddhavyam iti me matiḥa kariṣyāmi hi te kāmaṃ bhāgineya yathepsitamc bravīmy ataḥ klībavat tvāṃ yuddhād anyat kim icchasi yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa mantrayasva mahārāja nityaṃ maddhitam uttamamc kāmaṃ yudhya parasyārthe varam etad vṛṇomy aham śalya uvācaa brūhi kim atra sāhyaṃ te karomi nṛpasattamac kāmaṃ yotsye parasyārthe vṛto smy arthena kauravaiḥ yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa sa eva me varaḥ satya udyoge yas tvayā kṛtaḥc sūtaputrasya saṃgrāme kāryas tejovadhas tvayād tvāṃ hi yokṣyati sūtatve sūtaputrasya mātulad duryodhano raṇe śūram iti me naiṣṭhikī matiḥ śalya uvācaa saṃpatsyaty eṣa te kāmaḥ kuntīputra yathepsitaḥc gaccha yudhyasva visrabdhaṃ pratijāne jayaṃ tava saṃjaya uvācaa anumānyātha kaunteyo mātulaṃ madrakeśvaramc nirjagāma mahāsainyād bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥa vāsudevas tu rādheyam āhave bhijagāma vaic tata enam uvācedaṃ pāṇḍavārthe gadāgrajaḥa śrutaṃ me karṇa bhīṣmasya dveṣāt kila na yotsyasic asmān varaya rādheya yāvad bhīṣmo na hanyatea hate tu bhīṣme rādheya punar eṣyasi saṃyugec dhārtarāṣṭrasya sāhāyyaṃ yadi paśyasi cet samam karṇa uvācaa na vipriyaṃ kariṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭrasya keśavac tyaktaprāṇaṃ hi māṃ viddhi duryodhanahitaiṣiṇam saṃjaya uvācaa tac chrutvā vacanaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃnyavartata bhāratac yudhiṣṭhirapurogaiś ca pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃgataḥa atha sainyasya madhye tu prākrośat pāṇḍavāgrajaḥc yo smān vṛṇoti tad ahaṃ varaye sāhyakāraṇāta atha tān samabhiprekṣya yuyutsur idam abravītc prītātmā dharmarājānaṃ kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhirama ahaṃ yotsyāmi miṣataḥ saṃyuge dhārtarāṣṭrajānc yuṣmadarthe mahārāja yadi māṃ vṛṇuṣe nagha yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa ehy ehi sarve yotsyāmas tava bhrātṝn apaṇḍitānc yuyutso vāsudevaś ca vayaṃ ca brūma sarvaśaḥd na bhaviṣyanti te bālā dhārtarāṣṭrā na saṃśayaḥa vṛṇomi tvāṃ mahābāho yudhyasva mama kāraṇātc tvayi piṇḍaś ca tantuś ca dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dṛśyated tato jalakriyā caiva tvayā kāryā tathaiva caa bhajasvāsmān rājaputra bhajamānān mahādyutec na bhaviṣyati durbuddhir dhārtarāṣṭro tyamarṣaṇaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa tato yuyutsuḥ kauravyaḥ parityajya sutāṃs tavab sa satyam iti manvāno yudhiṣṭhiravacas tadāc jagāma pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ senāṃ viśrāvya dundubhimd sabalo dhārtarāṣṭrasya kutsayan karma duṣkṛtama tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ sahānujaiḥc jagrāha kavacaṃ bhūyo dīptimat kanakojjvalama pratyapadyanta te sarve rathān svān puruṣarṣabhāḥc tato vyūhaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ pratyavyūhanta te punaḥa avādayan dundubhīṃś ca śataśaś caiva puṣkarānc siṃhanādāṃś ca vividhān vineduḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥa rathasthān puruṣavyāghrān pāṇḍavān prekṣya pārthivāḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnādayaḥ sarve punar jahṛṣire mudāa gauravaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ mānyān mānayatāṃ ca tānc dṛṣṭvā mahīkṣitas tatra pūjayāṃ cakrire bhṛśama sauhṛdaṃ ca kṛpāṃ caiva prāptakālaṃ mahātmanāmc dayāṃ ca jñātiṣu parāṃ kathayāṃ cakrire nṛpāḥa sādhu sādhv iti sarvatra niśceruḥ stutisaṃhitāḥc vācaḥ puṇyāḥ kīrtimatāṃ manohṛdayaharṣiṇīḥa mlecchāś cāryāś ca ye tatra dadṛśuḥ śuśruvus tadāc vṛttaṃ tat pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ rurudus te sagadgadāḥa tato jaghnur mahābherīḥ śataśaś caiva puṣkarānc śaṅkhāṃś ca gokṣīranibhān dadhmur hṛṣṭā manasvinaḥ bhagavān uvāca sic kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanam vāsudevaṃ jagadyoniṃ naumi nārāyaṇaṃ harim dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa evaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu māmakeṣv itareṣu cac ke pūrvaṃ prāharaṃs tatra kuravaḥ pāṇḍavās tathā saṃjaya uvācaa bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito rājan putro duryodhanas tavac bhīṣmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtvā prayayau saha senayāa tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve bhīmasenapurogamāḥc bhīṣmeṇa yuddham icchantaḥ prayayur hṛṣṭamānasāḥa kṣveḍāḥ kilakilāśabdāḥ krakacā goviṣāṇikāḥc bherīmṛdaṅgamurajā hayakuñjaranisvanāḥa ubhayoḥ senayo rājaṃs tatas te smān samādravanc vayaṃ pratinadantaś ca tadāsīt tumulaṃ mahata mahānty anīkāni mahāsamucchrayesamāgame pāṇḍavadhārtarāṣṭrayoḥc cakampire śaṅkhamṛdaṅganisvanaiḥprakampitānīva vanāni vāyunāa narendranāgāśvarathākulānāmabhyāyatīnām aśive muhūrtec babhūva ghoṣas tumulaś camūnāṃvātoddhutānām iva sāgarāṇāma tasmin samutthite śabde tumule lomaharṣaṇec bhīmaseno mahābāhuḥ prāṇadad govṛṣo yathāa śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaṃ vāraṇānāṃ ca bṛṃhitamc siṃhanādaṃ ca sainyānāṃ bhīmasenaravo bhyabhūta hayānāṃ heṣamāṇānām anīkeṣu sahasraśaḥc sarvān abhyabhavac chabdān bhīmasenasya nisvanaḥa taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ tasya sainyās tava vitatrasuḥc jīmūtasyeva nadataḥ śakrāśanisamasvanama vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥc śabdena tasya vīrasya siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥa darśayan ghoram ātmānaṃ mahābhram iva nādayanc vibhīṣayaṃs tava sutāṃs tava senāṃ samabhyayāta tam āyāntaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ sodaryāḥ paryavārayanc chādayantaḥ śaravrātair meghā iva divākarama duryodhanaś ca putras te durmukho duḥsahaḥ śalaḥc duḥśāsanaś cātirathas tathā durmarṣaṇo nṛpaa viviṃśatiś citraseno vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥc purumitro jayo bhojaḥ saumadattiś ca vīryavāna mahācāpāni dhunvanto jaladā iva vidyutaḥc ādadānāś ca nārācān nirmuktāśīviṣopamāna atha tān draupadīputrāḥ saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥa dhārtarāṣṭrān pratiyayur ardayantaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥc vajrair iva mahāvegaiḥ śikharāṇi dharābhṛtāma tasmin prathamasaṃmarde bhīmajyātalanisvanec tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nāsīt kaś cit parāṅmukhaḥa lāghavaṃ droṇaśiṣyāṇām apaśyaṃ bharatarṣabhac nimittavedhināṃ rājañ śarān utsṛjatāṃ bhṛśama nopaśāmyati nirghoṣo dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ tathāc viniśceruḥ śarā dīptā jyotīṃṣīva nabhastalāta sarve tv anye mahīpālāḥ prekṣakā iva bhāratac dadṛśur darśanīyaṃ taṃ bhīmaṃ jñātisamāgamama tatas te jātasaṃrambhāḥ parasparakṛtāgasaḥc anyonyaspardhayā rājan vyāyacchanta mahārathāḥa kurupāṇḍavasene te hastyaśvarathasaṃkulec śuśubhāte raṇe tīva paṭe citragate ivaa tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥc sahasainyāḥ samāpetuḥ putrasya tava śāsanātd teṣām ādhāvatāṃ tatra gajāśvakalilo mahānd siṃhanādaravonmiśraḥ śaṅkhabherīsamākulaḥd sa ghoṣavāñ śaragrāho dhanurnāgo sikacchapaḥd vyāvalgitapurovāta āsīt kṣubdhābdhivat svanaḥa yudhiṣṭhireṇa cādiṣṭāḥ pārthivās te sahasraśaḥc vinadantaḥ samāpetuḥ putrasya tava vāhinīma ubhayoḥ senayos tīvraḥ sainyānāṃ sa samāgamaḥc antardhīyata cādityaḥ sainyena rajasāvṛtaḥa prayuddhānāṃ prabhagnānāṃ punarāvartatām apic nātra sveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ vā viśeṣaḥ samajāyataa tasmiṃs tu tumule yuddhe vartamāne mahābhayec ati sarvāṇy anīkāni pitā te bhivyarocata saṃjaya uvācaa pūrvāhṇe tasya raudrasya yuddham ahno viśāṃ patec prāvartata mahāghoraṃ rājñāṃ dehāvakartanama kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca saṃgrāme vijigīṣatāmc siṃhānām iva saṃhrādo divam urvīṃ ca nādayana āsīt kilakilāśabdas talaśaṅkharavaiḥ sahac jajñire siṃhanādāś ca śūrāṇāṃ pratigarjatāma talatrābhihatāś caiva jyāśabdā bharatarṣabhac pattīnāṃ pādaśabdāś ca vājināṃ ca mahāsvanāḥa tottrāṅkuśanipātāś ca āyudhānāṃ ca nisvanāḥc ghaṇṭāśabdāś ca nāgānām anyonyam abhidhāvatāma tasmin samudite śabde tumule lomaharṣaṇec babhūva rathanirghoṣaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥa te manaḥ krūram ādhāya samabhityaktajīvitāḥc pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta sarva evocchritadhvajāḥa svayaṃ śāṃtanavo rājann abhyadhāvad dhanaṃjayamc pragṛhya kārmukaṃ ghoraṃ kāladaṇḍopamaṃ raṇea arjuno pi dhanur gṛhya gāṇḍīvaṃ lokaviśrutamc abhyadhāvata tejasvī gāṅgeyaṃ raṇamūrdhania tāv ubhau kuruśārdūlau parasparavadhaiṣiṇauc gāṅgeyas tu raṇe pārthaṃ viddhvā nākampayad balīe tathaiva pāṇḍavo rājan bhīṣmaṃ nākampayad yudhia sātyakiś ca maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayātc tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇama sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ kṛtavarmā ca sātyakimc ānarchatuḥ śarair ghorais takṣamāṇau parasparama tau śarācitasarvāṅgau śuśubhāte mahābalauc vasante puṣpaśabalau puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukaua abhimanyur maheṣvāso bṛhadbalam ayodhayatc tataḥ kosalako rājā saubhadrasya viśāṃ patee dhvajaṃ ciccheda samare sārathiṃ ca nyapātayata saubhadras tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ pātite rathasārathauc bṛhadbalaṃ mahārāja vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥa athāparābhyāṃ bhallābhyāṃ pītābhyām arimardanaḥc dhvajam ekena ciccheda pārṣṇim ekena sārathime anyonyaṃ ca śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kruddhau rājaṃs tatakṣatuḥa māninaṃ samare dṛptaṃ kṛtavairaṃ mahārathamc bhīmasenas tava sutaṃ duryodhanam ayodhayata tāv ubhau naraśārdūlau kurumukhyau mahābalauc anyonyaṃ śaravarṣābhyāṃ vavṛṣāte raṇājired tau vīrāv atisaṃrabdhau kṛtinau viṣame sthitaua tau tu vīkṣya mahātmānau kṛtinau citrayodhinauc vismayaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ samapadyata bhārataa duḥśāsanas tu nakulaṃ pratyudyāya mahārathamc avidhyan niśitair bāṇair bahubhir marmabhedibhiḥa tasya mādrīsutaḥ ketuṃ saśaraṃ ca śarāsanamc ciccheda niśitair bāṇaiḥ prahasann iva bhāratae athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samārdayata putras tu tava durdharṣo nakulasya mahāhavec yugeṣāṃ cicchide bāṇair dhvajaṃ caiva nyapātayata durmukhaḥ sahadevaṃ tu pratyudyāya mahābalamc vivyādha śaravarṣeṇa yatamānaṃ mahāhavea sahadevas tato vīro durmukhasya mahāhavec śareṇa bhṛśatīkṣṇena pātayām āsa sārathima tāv anyonyaṃ samāsādya samare yuddhadurmadauc trāsayetāṃ śarair ghoraiḥ kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇaua yudhiṣṭhiraḥ svayaṃ rājā madrarājānam abhyayātb śalyam abhyardayām āsa mahābalaparākramamc tasya madrādhipaś cāpaṃ dvidhā ciccheda māriṣaa tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc anyat kārmukam ādāya vegavad balavattarama tato madreśvaraṃ rājā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc chādayām āsa saṃkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato droṇam abhyadravata bhāratac tasya droṇaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ parāsukaraṇaṃ dṛḍhame tridhā ciccheda samare yatamānasya kārmukama śaraṃ caiva mahāghoraṃ kāladaṇḍam ivāparamc preṣayām āsa samare so sya kāye nyamajjataa athānyad dhanur ādāya sāyakāṃś ca caturdaśac droṇaṃ drupadaputras tu prativivyādha saṃyugee tāv anyonyaṃ susaṃkruddhau cakratuḥ subhṛśaṃ raṇama saumadattiṃ raṇe śaṅkho rabhasaṃ rabhaso yudhic pratyudyayau mahārāja tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta tasya vai dakṣiṇaṃ vīro nirbibheda raṇe bhujamc saumadattis tathā śaṅkhaṃ jatrudeśe samāhanata tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec dṛptayoḥ samare tūrṇaṃ vṛtravāsavayor ivaa bāhlīkaṃ tu raṇe kruddhaṃ kruddharūpo viśāṃ patec abhyadravad ameyātmā dhṛṣṭaketur mahārathaḥa bāhlīkas tu tato rājan dhṛṣṭaketum amarṣaṇamc śarair bahubhir ānarchat siṃhanādam athānadata cedirājas tu saṃkruddho bāhlīkaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha samare tūrṇaṃ matto mattam iva dvipama tau tatra samare kruddhau nardantau ca muhur muhuḥc samīyatuḥ susaṃkruddhāv aṅgārakabudhāv ivaa rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ krūrakarmā ghaṭotkacaḥc alambusaṃ pratyudiyād balaṃ śakra ivāhavea ghaṭotkacas tu saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahābalamc navatyā sāyakais tīkṣṇair dārayām āsa bhārataa alambusas tu samare bhaimaseniṃ mahābalamc bahudhā vārayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa vyabhrājetāṃ tatas tau tu saṃyuge śaravikṣatauc yathā devāsure yuddhe balaśakrau mahābalaua śikhaṇḍī samare rājan drauṇim abhyudyayau balīc aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddhaḥ śikhaṇḍinam avasthitama nārācena sutīkṣṇena bhṛśaṃ viddhvā vyakampayatc śikhaṇḍy api tato rājan droṇaputram atāḍayata sāyakena supītena tīkṣṇena niśitena cac tau jaghnatus tadānyonyaṃ śarair bahuvidhair mṛdhea bhagadattaṃ raṇe śūraṃ virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥc abhyayāt tvarito rājaṃs tato yuddham avartataa virāṭo bhagadattena śaravarṣeṇa tāḍitaḥc abhyavarṣat susaṃkruddho megho vṛṣṭyā ivācalama bhagadattas tatas tūrṇaṃ virāṭaṃ pṛthivīpatimc chādayām āsa samare meghaḥ sūryam ivoditama bṛhatkṣatraṃ tu kaikeyaṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvato yayauc taṃ kṛpaḥ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārataa gautamaṃ kekayaḥ kruddhaḥ śaravṛṣṭyābhyapūrayatc tāv anyonyaṃ hayān hatvā dhanuṣī vinikṛtya vaia virathāv asiyuddhāya samīyatur amarṣaṇauc tayos tad abhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇama drupadas tu tato rājā saindhavaṃ vai jayadrathamc abhyudyayau saṃprahṛṣṭo hṛṣṭarūpaṃ paraṃtapaa tataḥ saindhavako rājā drupadaṃ viśikhais tribhiḥc tāḍayām āsa samare sa ca taṃ pratyavidhyataa tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇamc īkṣitṛprītijananaṃ śukrāṅgārakayor ivaa vikarṇas tu sutas tubhyaṃ sutasomaṃ mahābalamc abhyayāj javanair aśvais tato yuddham avartataa vikarṇaḥ sutasomaṃ tu viddhvā nākampayac charaiḥc sutasomo vikarṇaṃ ca tad adbhutam ivābhavata suśarmāṇaṃ naravyāghraṃ cekitāno mahārathaḥc abhyadravat susaṃkruddhaḥ pāṇḍavārthe parākramīa suśarmā tu mahārāja cekitānaṃ mahārathamc mahatā śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa saṃyugea cekitāno pi saṃrabdhaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ mahāhavec prācchādayat tam iṣubhir mahāmegha ivācalama śakuniḥ prativindhyaṃ tu parākrāntaṃ parākramīc abhyadravata rājendra matto mattam iva dvipama yaudhiṣṭhiras tu saṃkruddhaḥ saubalaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc vyadārayata saṃgrāme maghavān iva dānavama śakuniḥ prativindhyaṃ tu pratividhyantam āhavec vyadārayan mahāprājñaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa sudakṣiṇaṃ tu rājendra kāmbojānāṃ mahārathamc śrutakarmā parākrāntam abhyadravata saṃyugea sudakṣiṇas tu samare sāhadeviṃ mahārathamc viddhvā nākampayata vai mainākam iva parvatama śrutakarmā tataḥ kruddhaḥ kāmbojānāṃ mahārathamc śarair bahubhir ānarchad dārayann iva sarvaśaḥa irāvān atha saṃkruddhaḥ śrutāyuṣam amarṣaṇamc pratyudyayau raṇe yatto yattarūpataraṃ tataḥa ārjunis tasya samare hayān hatvā mahārathaḥc nanāda sumahan nādaṃ tat sainyaṃ pratyapūrayata śrutāyus tv atha saṃkruddhaḥ phālguneḥ samare hayānc nijaghāna gadāgreṇa tato yuddham avartataa vindānuvindāv āvantyau kuntibhojaṃ mahārathamc sasenaṃ sasutaṃ vīraṃ saṃsasajjatur āhavea tatrādbhutam apaśyāma āvantyānāṃ parākramamc yad ayudhyan sthirā bhūtvā mahatyā senayā sahaa anuvindas tu gadayā kuntibhojam atāḍayatc kuntibhojas tatas tūrṇaṃ śaravrātair avākirata kuntibhojasutaś cāpi vindaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥc sa ca taṃ prativivyādha tad adbhutam ivābhavata kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca gāndhārān pañca māriṣac sasainyās te sasainyāṃś ca yodhayām āsur āhavea vīrabāhuś ca te putro vairāṭiṃ rathasattamamc uttaraṃ yodhayām āsa vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd ulūkaṃ tu śatānīkaḥ śarair bahubhir āvṛṇote uttaraś cāpi taṃ dhīraṃ vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa cedirāṭ samare rājann ulūkaṃ samabhidravatb tathaiva śaravarṣeṇa ulūkaṃ samavidhyatac ulūkaś cāpi taṃ bāṇair niśitair lomavāhibhiḥa tayor yuddhaṃ samabhavad ghorarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec dārayetāṃ susaṃkruddhāv anyonyam aparājitaud tathaiva cedirājo pi ulūkaṃ pratyavidhyataa evaṃ dvaṃdvasahasrāṇi rathavāraṇavājināmc padātīnāṃ ca samare tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkulama muhūrtam iva tad yuddham āsīn madhuradarśanamc tata unmattavad rājan na prājñāyata kiṃ canaa gajo gajena samare rathī ca rathinaṃ yayauc aśvo śvaṃ samabhipretya padātiś ca padātinama tato yuddhaṃ sudurdharṣaṃ vyākulaṃ samapadyatac śūrāṇāṃ samare tatra samāsādya parasparama tatra devarṣayaḥ siddhāś cāraṇāś ca samāgatāḥc praikṣanta tad raṇaṃ ghoraṃ devāsuraraṇopamama tato dantisahasrāṇi rathānāṃ cāpi māriṣac aśvaughāḥ puruṣaughāś ca viparītaṃ samāyayuḥa tatra tatraiva dṛśyante rathavāraṇapattayaḥc sādinaś ca naravyāghra yudhyamānā muhur muhuḥ saṃjaya uvācaa rājañ śatasahasrāṇi tatra tatra tadā tadāc nirmaryādaṃ prayuddhāni tat te vakṣyāmi bhārataa na putraḥ pitaraṃ jajñe na pitā putram aurasamc na bhrātā bhrātaraṃ tatra svasrīyaṃ na ca mātulaḥa mātulaṃ na ca svasrīyo na sakhāyaṃ sakhā tathāc āviṣṭā iva yudhyante pāṇḍavāḥ kurubhiḥ sahaa rathānīkaṃ naravyāghrāḥ ke cid abhyapatan rathaiḥc abhajyanta yugair eva yugāni bharatarṣabhaa ratheṣāś ca ratheṣābhiḥ kūbarā rathakūbaraiḥc saṃhatāḥ saṃhataiḥ ke cit parasparajighāṃsavaḥa na śekuś calituṃ ke cit saṃnipatya rathā rathaiḥc prabhinnās tu mahākāyāḥ saṃnipatya gajā gajaiḥa bahudhādārayan kruddhā viṣāṇair itaretaramc satomarapatākaiś ca vāraṇāḥ paravāraṇaiḥa abhisṛtya mahārāja vegavadbhir mahāgajaiḥc dantair abhihatās tatra cukruśuḥ paramāturāḥa abhinītāś ca śikṣābhis tottrāṅkuśasamāhatāḥc suprabhinnāḥ prabhinnānāṃ saṃmukhābhimukhā yayuḥa prabhinnair api saṃsaktāḥ ke cit tatra mahāgajāḥc krauñcavan ninadaṃ muktvā prādravanta tatas tataḥa samyak praṇītā nāgāś ca prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥc ṛṣṭitomaranārācair nirviddhā varavāraṇāḥa vinedur bhinnamarmāṇo nipetuś ca gatāsavaḥc prādravanta diśaḥ ke cin nadanto bhairavān ravāna gajānāṃ pādarakṣās tu vyūḍhoraskāḥ prahāriṇaḥc ṛṣṭibhiś ca dhanurbhiś ca vimalaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥa gadābhir musalaiś caiva bhiṇḍipālaiḥ satomaraiḥc āyasaiḥ parighaiś caiva nistriṃśair vimalaiḥ śitaiḥa pragṛhītaiḥ susaṃrabdhā dhāvamānās tatas tataḥc vyadṛśyanta mahārāja parasparajighāṃsavaḥa rājamānāś ca nistriṃśāḥ saṃsiktā naraśoṇitaiḥc pratyadṛśyanta śūrāṇām anyonyam abhidhāvatāma avakṣiptāvadhūtānām asīnāṃ vīrabāhubhiḥc saṃjajñe tumulaḥ śabdaḥ patatāṃ paramarmasua gadāmusalarugṇānāṃ bhinnānāṃ ca varāsibhiḥc dantidantāv abhinnānāṃ mṛditānāṃ ca dantibhiḥa tatra tatra naraughāṇāṃ krośatām itaretaramc śuśruvur dāruṇā vācaḥ pretānām iva bhārataa hayair api hayārohāś cāmarāpīḍadhāribhiḥc haṃsair iva mahāvegair anyonyam abhidudruvuḥa tair vimuktā mahāprāsā jāmbūnadavibhūṣaṇāḥc āśugā vimalās tīkṣṇāḥ saṃpetur bhujagopamāḥa aśvair agryajavaiḥ ke cid āplutya mahato rathānc śirāṃsy ādadire vīrā rathinām aśvasādinaḥa bahūn api hayārohān bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc rathī jaghāna saṃprāpya bāṇagocaram āgatāna nagameghapratīkāśāś cākṣipya turagān gajāḥc pādair evāvamṛdnanta mattāḥ kanakabhūṣaṇāḥa pāṭyamāneṣu kumbheṣu pārśveṣv api ca vāraṇāḥc prāsair vinihatāḥ ke cid vineduḥ paramāturāḥa sāśvārohān hayān ke cid unmathya varavāraṇāḥc sahasā cikṣipus tatra saṃkule bhairave satia sāśvārohān viṣāṇāgrair utkṣipya turagān dvipāḥc rathaughān avamṛdnantaḥ sadhvajān paricakramuḥa puṃstvād abhimadatvāc ca ke cid atra mahāgajāḥc sāśvārohān hayāñ jaghnuḥ karaiḥ sacaraṇais tathād aśvārohaiś ca samare hastisādibhir eva caa ke cid ākṣipya kariṇaḥ sāśvān api rathān karaiḥc vikarṣanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ samīyuḥ sarvaśabdagāḥd pratimāneṣu gātreṣu pārśveṣv abhi ca vāraṇānd muktās tu rathibhir bāṇā rukmapuṅkhāḥ sutejanāḥd te nipetur akuṇṭhāgrā nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu caa āśugā vimalās tīkṣṇāḥ saṃpetur bhujagopamāḥc narāśvakāyān nirbhidya lauhāni kavacāni caa nipetur vimalāḥ śaktyo vīrabāhubhir arpitāḥc maholkāpratimā ghorās tatra tatra viśāṃ patea dvīpicarmāvanaddhaiś ca vyāghracarmaśayair apic vikośair vimalaiḥ khaḍgair abhijaghnuḥ parān raṇea abhiplutam abhikruddham ekapārśvāvadāritamc vidarśayantaḥ saṃpetuḥ khaḍgacarmaparaśvadhaiḥa śaktibhir dāritāḥ ke cit saṃchinnāś ca paraśvadhaiḥc hastibhir mṛditāḥ ke cit kṣuṇṇāś cānye turaṃgamaiḥa rathaneminikṛttāś ca nikṛttā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc vikrośanti narā rājaṃs tatra tatra sma bāndhavāna putrān anye pitṝn anye bhrātṝṃś ca saha bāndhavaiḥc mātulān bhāgineyāṃś ca parān api ca saṃyugea vikīrṇāntrāḥ subahavo bhagnasakthāś ca bhāratac bāhubhiḥ subhujācchinnaiḥ pārśveṣu ca vidāritāḥe krandantaḥ samadṛśyanta tṛṣitā jīvitepsavaḥa tṛṣṇāparigatāḥ ke cid alpasattvā viśāṃ patec bhūmau nipatitāḥ saṃkhye jalam eva yayācirea rudhiraughapariklinnāḥ kliśyamānāś ca bhāratac vyanindan bhṛśam ātmānaṃ tava putrāṃś ca saṃgatāna apare kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ kṛtavairāḥ parasparamc naiva śastraṃ vimuñcanti naiva krandanti māriṣae tarjayanti ca saṃhṛṣṭās tatra tatra parasparama nirdaśya daśanaiś cāpi krodhāt svadaśanac chadānc bhrukuṭīkuṭilair vaktraiḥ prekṣante ca parasparamd tarjayitvā susaṃhṛṣṭā yāvat prāṇasya dhāraṇama apare kliśyamānās tu vraṇārtāḥ śarapīḍitāḥc niṣkūjāḥ samapadyanta dṛḍhasattvā mahābalāḥa anye tu virathāḥ śūrā ratham anyasya saṃyugec prārthayānā nipatitāḥ saṃkṣuṇṇā varavāraṇaiḥe aśobhanta mahārāja puṣpitā iva kiṃśukāḥa saṃbabhūvur anīkeṣu bahavo bhairavasvanāḥc vartamāne mahābhīme tasmin vīravarakṣayea ahanat tu pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ raṇec svasrīyo mātulaṃ cāpi svasrīyaṃ cāpi mātulaḥa sakhāyaṃ ca sakhā rājan saṃbandhī bāndhavaṃ tathāc evaṃ yuyudhire tatra kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahaa vartamāne bhaye tasmin nirmaryāde mahāhavec bhīṣmam āsādya pārthānāṃ vāhinī samakampataa ketunā pañcatāreṇa tālena bharatarṣabhac rājatena mahābāhur ucchritena mahārathee babhau bhīṣmas tadā rājaṃś candramā iva meruṇā saṃjaya uvācaa gatapūrvāhṇabhūyiṣṭhe tasminn ahani dāruṇec vartamāne mahāraudre mahāvīravarakṣayea durmukhaḥ kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyo viviṃśatiḥc bhīṣmaṃ jugupur āsādya tava putreṇa coditāḥa etair atirathair guptaḥ pañcabhir bharatarṣabhac pāṇḍavānām anīkāni vijagāhe mahārathaḥa cedikāśikarūṣeṣu pāñcāleṣu ca bhāratac bhīṣmasya bahudhā tālaś caran ketur adṛśyataa śirāṃsi ca tadā bhīṣmo bāhūṃś cāpi sahāyudhānb dhanūṃṣi rathināṃ bhīṣmaḥ sotsedhāni śirāṃsi cab bāhūn api tathā corūn rathāṃś ca vipuladhvajānc nicakarta mahāvegair bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥd ekaikena tu mātaṅgā nārācena mahātmanād tāḍitāḥ sahasā jagmuḥ pṛthivīṃ parvatopamāḥa nṛtyato rathamārgeṣu bhīṣmasya bharatarṣabhac ke cid ārtasvaraṃ cakrur nāgā marmaṇi tāḍitāḥd durādharṣas tu śatrūṇāṃ manāṃsi samakampayatd hayāṃś ca sahayārohān pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥd sa rathena maheṣvāso vicaran bahudhā balīd maṇḍalāni ca vīthīś ca gomūtrāṇi ca bhāratad anyāṃś ca subahūn mārgān rathena rathakovidaḥd vismāpayañ śatrusaṃghān vyacaraj jāhnavīsutaḥa abhimanyuḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ piśaṅgais turagottamaiḥc saṃyuktaṃ ratham āsthāya prāyād bhīṣmarathaṃ pratia jāmbūnadavicitreṇa karṇikāreṇa ketunāb abhyavarṣac chalyamukhān rathān satālaketunāc abhyavarṣata bhīṣmaṃ ca tāṃś caiva rathasattamāna sa tālaketos tīkṣṇena ketum āhatya patriṇāc bhīṣmeṇa yuyudhe vīras tasya cānucaraiḥ sahaa kṛtavarmāṇam ekena śalyaṃ pañcabhir āyasaiḥc viddhvā navabhir ānarchac chitāgraiḥ prapitāmahama pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena samyak praṇihitena cac dhvajam ekena vivyādha jāmbūnadavibhūṣitama durmukhasya tu bhallena sarvāvaraṇabhedināc jahāra sāratheḥ kāyāc chiraḥ saṃnataparvaṇād viviṃśatis tribhir bāṇaiḥ sarvāvaraṇabhedibhiḥa dhanuś ciccheda bhallena kārtasvaravibhūṣitamc kṛpasya niśitāgreṇa tāṃś ca tīkṣṇamukhaiḥ śaraiḥa jaghāna paramakruddho nṛtyann iva mahārathaḥc tasya lāghavam udvīkṣya tutuṣur devatā apia labdhalakṣyatayā karṣṇeḥ sarve bhīṣmamukhā rathāḥc sattvavantam amanyanta sākṣād iva dhanaṃjayama tasya lāghavamārgastham alātasadṛśaprabhamc diśaḥ paryapatac cāpaṃ gāṇḍīvam iva ghoṣavata tam āsādya mahāvegair bhīṣmo navabhir āśugaiḥc vivyādha samare tūrṇam ārjuniṃ paravīrahāa dhvajaṃ cāsya tribhir bhallaiś ciccheda paramaujasaḥc sārathiṃ ca tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna yatavrataḥa tathaiva kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyaś ca māriṣab viviṃśatis tathā rājan sarve viddhvā mahārathāḥc viddhvā nākampayat kārṣṇiṃ mainākam iva parvatama sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūro dhārtarāṣṭrair mahārathaiḥc vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi kārṣṇiḥ pañcarathān pratia tatas teṣāṃ mahāstrāṇi saṃvārya śaravṛṣṭibhiḥc nanāda balavān kārṣṇir bhīṣmāya visṛjañ śarāna tatrāsya sumahad rājan bāhvor balam adṛśyatac yatamānasya samare bhīṣmam ardayataḥ śaraiḥa parākrāntasya tasyaiva bhīṣmo pi prāhiṇoc charānc sa tāṃś ciccheda samare bhīṣmacāpacyutāñ śarāna tato dhvajam amogheṣur bhīṣmasya navabhiḥ śaraiḥc ciccheda samare vīras tata uccukruśur janāḥa sa rājato mahāskandhas tālo hemavibhūṣitaḥc saubhadraviśikhaiś chinnaḥ papāta bhuvi bhārataa dhvajaṃ saubhadraviśikhaiḥ patitaṃ bharatarṣabhac dṛṣṭvā bhīmo nadad dhṛṣṭaḥ saubhadram abhiharṣayana atha bhīṣmo mahāstrāṇi divyāni ca bahūni cac prāduścakre mahāraudraḥ kṣaṇe tasmin mahābalaḥa tataḥ śatasahasreṇa saubhadraṃ prapitāmahaḥc avākirad ameyātmā śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇāma tato daśa maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc rakṣārtham abhyadhāvanta saubhadraṃ tvaritā rathaiḥa virāṭaḥ saha putreṇa dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc bhīmaś ca kekayāś caiva sātyakiś ca viśāṃ patea javenāpatatāṃ teṣāṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo raṇec pāñcālyaṃ tribhir ānarchat sātyakiṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena kṣureṇa niśitena cac dhvajam ekena ciccheda bhīmasenasya patriṇāa jāmbūnadamayaḥ ketuḥ kesarī narasattamac papāta bhīmasenasya bhīṣmeṇa mathito rathāta bhīmasenas tribhir viddhvā bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ raṇec kṛpam ekena vivyādha kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥa pragṛhītāgrahastena vairāṭir api dantināc abhyadravata rājānaṃ madrādhipatim uttaraḥa tasya vāraṇarājasya javenāpatato rathīc śalyo nivārayām āsa vegam apratimaṃ raṇea tasya kruddhaḥ sa nāgendro bṛhataḥ sādhuvāhinaḥc padā yugam adhiṣṭhāya jaghāna caturo hayāna sa hatāśve rathe tiṣṭhan madrādhipatir āyasīmc uttarāntakarīṃ śaktiṃ cikṣepa bhujagopamāma tayā bhinnatanutrāṇaḥ praviśya vipulaṃ tamaḥc sa papāta gajaskandhāt pramuktāṅkuśatomaraḥa samādāya ca śalyo sim avaplutya rathottamātc vāraṇendrasya vikramya cicchedātha mahākarama bhinnamarmā śaravrātaiś chinnahastaḥ sa vāraṇaḥc bhīmam ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā papāta ca mamāra caa etad īdṛśakaṃ kṛtvā madrarājo mahārathaḥc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ bhāsvaraṃ kṛtavarmaṇaḥa uttaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā vairāṭir bhrātaraṃ śubhamc kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śalyam avasthitamd śvetaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla haviṣā havyavāḍ ivad sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ śakracāpopamaṃ balīd abhyadhāvaj jighāṃsan vai śalyaṃ madrādhipaṃ balīd mahatā rathavaṃśena samantāt parivāritaḥd muñcan bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ prāyāc chalyarathaṃ pratid tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya mattavāraṇavikramamd tāvakānāṃ rathāḥ sapta samantāt paryavārayand madrarājam abhīpsanto mṛtyor daṃṣṭrāntaraṃ gatamd bṛhadbalaś ca kausalyo jayatsenaś ca māgadhaḥd tathā rukmaratho rājañ śalyaputraḥ pratāpavānd vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥd bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥd nānāvarṇavicitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca mahātmanāmd visphāritāni dṛśyante toyadeṣv iva vidyutaḥd te tu bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ śvetamūrdhany apātayand nidāghānte niloddhūtā meghā iva nage jalamd tataḥ kruddho maheṣvāsaḥ saptabhallaiḥ sutejanaiḥd dhanūṃṣi teṣām ācchidya mamarda pṛtanāpatiḥd nikṛttāny eva tāni sma samadṛśyanta bhāratad tatas te tu nimeṣārdhāt pratyapadyan dhanūṃṣi cad sapta caiva pṛṣatkāṃś ca śvetasyoparyapātayand tataḥ punar ameyātmā bhallaiḥ saptabhir āśugaiḥd nicakarta mahābāhus teṣāṃ cāpāni dhanvināmd te nikṛttamahācāpās tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥd rathaśaktīḥ parāmṛśya vinedur bhairavān ravānd anvayur bharataśreṣṭha sapta śvetarathaṃ pratid tatas tā jvalitāḥ sapta mahendrāśaninisvanāḥd aprāptāḥ saptabhir bhallaiś ciccheda paramāstravitd tataḥ samādāya śaraṃ sarvakāyavidāraṇamd prāhiṇod bharataśreṣṭha śveto rukmarathaṃ pratid tasya dehe nipatito bāṇo vajrātigo mahānd tato rukmaratho rājan sāyakena dṛḍhāhataḥd niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalaṃ cāviśan mahatd taṃ visaṃjñaṃ vimanasaṃ tvaramāṇas tu sārathiḥd apovāha susaṃbhrāntaḥ sarvalokasya paśyataḥd tato nyān ṣaṭ samādāya śveto hemavibhūṣitānd teṣāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ mahābāhur dhvajaśīrṣāṇy apātayatd hayāṃś ca teṣāṃ nirbhidya sārathīṃś ca paraṃtapad śaraiś caitān samākīrya prāyāc chalyarathaṃ pratid tato halahalāśabdas tava sainyeṣu bhāratad dṛṣṭvā senāpatiṃ tūrṇaṃ yāntaṃ śalyarathaṃ pratid tato bhīṣmaṃ puraskṛtya tava putro mahābalaḥd vṛtas tu sarvasainyena prāyāc chvetarathaṃ pratid mṛtyor āsyam anuprāptaṃ madrarājam amocayatd tato yuddhaṃ samabhavat tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamd tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca vyatiṣiktarathadvipamd saubhadre bhīmasene ca sātyakau ca mahārathed kaikeye ca virāṭe ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca pārṣated eteṣu narasiṃheṣu cedimatsyeṣu caiva had dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācad vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥd evaṃ śvete maheṣvāse prāpte śalyarathaṃ pratid kuravaḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca kim akurvata saṃjayad saṃjaya uvācad bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ kiṃ vā tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥd rājañ śatasahasrāṇi tataḥ kṣatriyapuṃgavāḥd śvetaṃ senāpatiṃ śūraṃ puraskṛtya mahārathāḥd rājño balaṃ darśayantas tava putrasya bhāratad śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya trātum aicchan mahārathāḥd abhyavartanta bhīṣmasya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtamd jighāṃsantaṃ yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tadāsīt tumulaṃ mahatd tat te haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāvaiśasam acyutad tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca yathā yuddham avartatad tatrākarod rathopasthāñ śūnyāñ śāṃtanavo bahūnd prākṛntad uttamāṅgāni śarair ārchad rathottamānd samāvṛṇoc charair arkam arkatulyapratāpavānd nudan samantāt samare ravir udyan yathā tamaḥd tenājau preṣitā rājañ śarāḥ śatasahasraśaḥd kṣatriyāntakarāḥ saṃkhye mahāvegā mahābalāḥd śirāṃsi pātayām āsur vīrāṇāṃ śataśo raṇed gajān kaṇṭakasaṃnāhān vajreṇeva śiloccayānd rathā ratheṣu saṃsaktā vyadṛśanta viśāṃ pated eke rathaṃ paryavahaṃs turagāḥ saturaṃgamamd yuvānaṃ nihataṃ vīraṃ lambamānaṃ sakārmukamd udīrṇāś ca hayā rājan vahantas tatra tatra had baddhakhaḍganiṣaṅgāś ca vidhvastaśiraso hatāḥd śataśaḥ patitā bhūmau vīraśayyāsu śerated paraspareṇa dhāvantaḥ patitāḥ punar utthitāḥd utthāya ca pradhāvanto dvaṃdvayuddham avāpnuvand pīḍitāḥ punar anyonyaṃ luṭhanto raṇamūrdhanid sacāpān saniṣaṅgāṃś ca jātarūpapariṣkṛtānd visrabdhahatavīrāś ca śataśaḥ paripīḍitāḥd tena tenābhyadhāvanta visṛjantaś ca bhāratad matto gajaḥ paryavartad dhayāṃś ca hatasādinaḥd sarathā rathinaś cāpi vimṛdnantaḥ samantataḥd syandanād apatat kaś cin nihato nyena sāyakaiḥd hatasārathir apy uccaiḥ papāta kāṣṭhavad rathaḥd yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme vyūḍhe rajasi cotthited dhanuḥkūjitavijñānaṃ tatrāsīt pratiyudhyataḥd gātrasparśena yodhānāṃ vyajñāsta paripanthinamd yudhyamānaṃ śarai rājan siñjinī dhvajinī ravātd anyonyaṃ vīrasaṃśabdo nāśrūyata bhaṭaiḥ kṛtaḥd śabdāyamāne saṃgrāme paṭahe karṇadāriṇid yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme kurvataḥ pauruṣaṃ svakamd nāśrauṣīn nāmagotroktiṃ kīrtanaṃ ca parasparamd bhīṣmacāpacyutair bāṇair ārtānāṃ yudhyatāṃ mṛdhed paraspareṣāṃ vīrāṇāṃ manāṃsi samakampayand tasminn atyākule yuddhe dāruṇe lomaharṣaṇed pitā putraṃ ca samare nābhijānāti kaś canad cakre bhagne yuge chinne eko dhuryo hayo hataḥd ākṣiptaḥ syandanād vīraḥ sasārathir ajihmagaiḥd evaṃ ca samare sarve vīrāś ca virathīkṛtāḥd tena tena sma dṛśyante dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥd gajo hataḥ śiraś chinnaṃ marma bhinnaṃ hayo hataḥd ahataḥ ko pi naivāsīd bhīṣme nighnati śātravānd śvetaḥ kurūṇām akarot svayaṃ tasmin mahāhaved rājaputrān rathodārān avadhīc chatasaṃghaśaḥd ciccheda rathināṃ bāṇaiḥ śirāṃsi bharatarṣabhad sāṅgadā bāhavaś caiva dhanūṃṣi ca samantataḥd ratheṣāṃ rathacakrāṇi tūṇīrāṇi yugāni cad chatrāṇi ca mahārhāṇi patākāś ca viśāṃ pated hayaughāś ca rathaughāś ca naraughāś caiva bhāratad vāraṇāḥ śataśaś caiva hatāḥ śvetena bhāratad vayaṃ śvetabhayād bhītā vihāya rathasattamamd avaśiṣṭās tathā paścād vibhuṃ paśyāma dhṛṣṇavaḥd śarapātam apakramya kuravaḥ kurunandanad bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yuddhe sthitāḥ paśyāma sarvaśaḥd adīno dīnasamaye bhīṣmo smākaṃ mahāhaved ekas tasthau naravyāghro girir merur ivācalaḥd ādadāna iva prāṇān savitā śiśirātyayed gabhastibhir ivādityas tasthau śaramarīcimānd sa mumoca maheṣvāsaḥ śarasaṃghān anekaśaḥd nighnann amitrān samare vajrapāṇir ivāsurānd te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa prajahus taṃ mahābalamd svayūthād iva te yūthān muktaṃ bhūmiṣu dāruṇamd tam ekam upalabhyaiko hṛṣṭaḥ puṣṭaḥ paraṃtapad duryodhanapriye yuktaḥ pāṇḍavān pariśocayand jīvitaṃ dustyajaṃ tyaktvā bhayaṃ ca sumahāhaved pātayām āsa sainyāni pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ pated praharantam anīkāni pitā devavratas tavad dṛṣṭvā senāpatiṃ bhīṣmas tvaritaḥ śvetam abhyayātd sa bhīṣmaṃ śarajālena mahatā samavākiratd śvetaṃ cāpi tathā bhīṣmaḥ śaraughaiḥ samavākiratd tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau mattāv iva mahādvipaud vyāghrāv iva susaṃrabdhāv anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥd astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya tatas tau puruṣarṣabhaud bhīṣmaḥ śvetaś ca yuyudhe parasparavadhaiṣiṇaud ekāhnā nirdahed bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmd śaraiḥ paramasaṃkruddho yadi śveto na pālayetd pitāmahaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā śvetena vimukhīkṛtamd praharṣaṃ pāṇḍavā jagmuḥ putras te vimanābhavatd tato duryodhanaḥ kruddhaḥ pārthivaiḥ parivāritaḥd sasainyaḥ pāṇḍavānīkam abhyadravata saṃyuged durmukhaḥ kṛtavarmā ca kṛpaḥ śalyo viśāṃ pated bhīṣmaṃ jugupur āsādya tava putreṇa coditāḥd dṛṣṭvā tu pārthivaiḥ sarvair duryodhanapurogamaiḥd pāṇḍavānām anīkāni vadhyamānāni saṃyuged śveto gāṅgeyam utsṛjya tava putrasya vāhinīmd nāśayām āsa vegena vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasād drāvayitvā camūṃ rājan vairāṭiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥd āpatat sahasā bhūyo yatra bhīṣmo vyavasthitaḥd tau tatropagatau rājañ śaradīptau mahābalaud ayudhyetāṃ mahātmānau yathobhau vṛtravāsavaud anyonyaṃ tu mahārāja parasparavadhaiṣiṇaud nigṛhya kārmukaṃ śveto bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥd parākramaṃ tatas tasya parākramya parākramīd tarasā vārayām āsa matto mattam iva dvipamd śvetaḥ śāṃtanavaṃ bhūyaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥd vivyādha pañcaviṃśatyā tad adbhutam ivābhavatd taṃ pratyavidhyad daśabhir bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadād sa viddhas tena balavān nākampata yathācalaḥd vairāṭiḥ samare kruddho bhṛśam āyamya kārmukamd ājaghāna tato bhīṣmaṃ śvetaḥ kṣatriyanandanaḥd saṃprahasya tataḥ śvetaḥ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihand dhanuś ciccheda bhīṣmasya navabhir daśadhā śaraiḥd saṃdhāya viśikhaṃ caiva śaraṃ lomapravāhinamd unmamātha tatas tālaṃ dhvajaśīrṣaṃ mahātmanaḥd ketuṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya tanayās tavad hataṃ bhīṣmam amanyanta śvetasya vaśam āgatamd pāṇḍavāś cāpi saṃhṛṣṭā dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yutāḥd bhīṣmasya patitaṃ ketuṃ dṛṣṭvā tālaṃ mahātmanaḥd tato duryodhanaḥ krodhāt svam anīkam acodayatd yatnād bhīṣmaṃ parīpsadhvaṃ rakṣamāṇāḥ samantataḥd mā naḥ prapaśyamānānāṃ śvetān mṛtyum avāpsyatid bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ śūras tathā satyaṃ bravīmi vaḥd rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥd balena caturaṅgeṇa gāṅgeyam anvapālayand bāhlīkaḥ kṛtavarmā ca śalaḥ śalyaś ca bhāratad jalasaṃdho vikarṇaś ca citraseno viviṃśatiḥd tvaramāṇās tvarākāle parivārya samantataḥd śastravṛṣṭiṃ sutumulāṃ śvetasyopary apātayand tān kruddho niśitair bāṇais tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥd avārayad ameyātmā darśayan pāṇilāghavamd sa nivārya tu tān sarvān kesarī kuñjarān ivad mahatā śaravarṣeṇa bhīṣmasya dhanur ācchinatd tato nyad dhanur ādāya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhid śvetaṃ vivyādha rājendra kaṅkapatraiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥd tataḥ senāpatiḥ kruddho bhīṣmaṃ bahubhir āyasaiḥd vivyādha samare rājan sarvalokasya paśyataḥd tataḥ pravyathito rājā bhīṣmaṃ dṛṣṭvā nivāritamd pravīraṃ sarvalokasya śvetena yudhi vai tadād niṣṭhānakaś ca sumahāṃs tava sainyasya cābhavatd taṃ vīraṃ vāritaṃ dṛṣṭvā śvetena śaravikṣatamd hataṃ śvetena manyante śvetasya vaśam āgatamd tataḥ krodhavaśaṃ prāptaḥ pitā devavratas tavad dhvajam unmathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ ca senāṃ nivāritāmd śvetaṃ prati mahārāja vyasṛjat sāyakān bahūnd tān āvārya raṇe śveto bhīṣmasya rathināṃ varaḥd dhanuś ciccheda bhallena punar eva pitus tavad utsṛjya kārmukaṃ rājan gāṅgeyaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥd anyat kārmukam ādāya vipulaṃ balavattaramd tatra saṃdhāya vipulān bhallān sapta śilāśitānd caturbhiś ca jaghānāśvāñ śvetasya pṛtanāpateḥd dhvajaṃ dvābhyāṃ tu ciccheda saptamena ca sāratheḥd śiraś ciccheda bhallena saṃkruddho laghuvikramaḥd hatāśvasūtāt sa rathād avaplutya mahābalaḥd amarṣavaśam āpanno vyākulaḥ samapadyatad virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥd tāḍayām āsa niśitaiḥ śarasaṃghaiḥ samantataḥd sa tāḍyamānaḥ samare bhīṣmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥd svarathe dhanur utsṛjya śaktiṃ jagrāha kāñcanīmd tataḥ śaktiṃ raṇe śveto jagrāhogrāṃ mahābhayāmd kāladaṇḍopamāṃ ghorāṃ mṛtyor iva svasāṃ śvasand abravīc ca tadā śveto bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ raṇed tiṣṭhedānīṃ susaṃrabdhaḥ paśya māṃ puruṣo bhavad evam uktvā maheṣvāso bhīṣmaṃ yudhi parākramīd tataḥ śaktim ameyātmā cikṣepa bhujagopamāmd pāṇḍavārthe parākrāntas tavānarthaṃ cikīrṣatid hāhākāro mahān āsīt putrāṇāṃ te viśāṃ pated dṛṣṭvā śaktiṃ mahāghorāṃ mṛtyor daṇḍasamaprabhāmd śvetasya karanirmuktāṃ nirmuktoragasaṃnibhāmd apatat sahasā rājan maholkeva nabhastalātd jvalantīm antarikṣe tāṃ jvālābhir iva saṃvṛtāmd asaṃbhrāntas tadā rājan pitā devavratas tavad aṣṭabhir navabhir bhīṣmaḥ śaktiṃ ciccheda patribhiḥd utkṛṣṭahemavikṛtāṃ nikṛttāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd uccukruśus tataḥ sarve tāvakā bharatarṣabhad śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā vairāṭiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥd kālopahatacetās tu kartavyaṃ nābhyajānatad krodhasaṃmūrchito rājan vairāṭiḥ prahasann ivad gadāṃ jagrāha saṃhṛṣṭo bhīṣmasya nidhanaṃ pratid krodhena raktanayano daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥd bhīṣmaṃ samabhidudrāva jalaugha iva parvatamd tasya vegam asaṃvārya matvā bhīṣmaḥ pratāpavānd prahāravipramokṣārthaṃ sahasā dharaṇīṃ gataḥd śvetaḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo bhrāmayitvā tu tāṃ gadāmd rathe bhīṣmasya cikṣepa yathā devo dhaneśvaraḥd tayā bhīṣmanipātinyā sa ratho bhasmasāt kṛtaḥd sadhvajaḥ saha sūtena sāśvaḥ sayugabandhuraḥd virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhīṣmaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathottamāḥd abhyadhāvanta sahitāḥ śalyaprabhṛtayo rathāḥd tato nyaṃ ratham āsthāya dhanur visphārya durmanāḥd śanakair abhyayāc chvetaṃ gāṅgeyaḥ prahasann ivad etasminn antare bhīṣmaḥ śuśrāva vipulāṃ giramd ākāśād īritāṃ divyām ātmano hitasaṃbhavāmd bhīṣma bhīṣma mahābāho śīghraṃ yatnaṃ kuruṣva vaid eṣa hy asya jaye kālo nirdiṣṭo viśvayoninād etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ devadūtena bhāṣitamd saṃprahṛṣṭamanā bhūtvā vadhe tasya mano dadhed virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā padātinamd sahitās tv abhyavartanta parīpsanto mahārathāḥd sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥd kaikeyo dhṛṣṭaketuś ca abhimanyuś ca vīryavānd etān āpatataḥ sarvān droṇaśalyakṛpaiḥ sahad avārayad ameyātmā vārivegān ivācalaḥd sa niruddheṣu sarveṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasud śvetaḥ khaḍgam athākṛṣya bhīṣmasya dhanur ācchinatd tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ tvaramāṇaḥ pitāmahaḥd devadūtavacaḥ śrutvā vadhe tasya mano dadhed tataḥ pracāramāṇas tu pitā devavratas tavad anyat kārmukam ādāya tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥd kṣaṇena sajyam akaroc chakracāpasamaprabhamd pitā te bharataśreṣṭha śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahārathaiḥd vṛtaṃ taṃ manujavyāghrair bhīmasenapurogamaiḥd abhyavartata gāṅgeyaḥ śvetaṃ senāpatiṃ drutamd āpatantaṃ tato bhīṣmo bhīmasenaṃ pratāpavānd ājaghne viśikhaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā senānyaṃ sa mahārathaḥd abhimanyuṃ ca samare pitā devavratas tavad ājaghne bharataśreṣṭhas tribhiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥd sātyakiṃ ca śatenājau bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥd dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca viṃśatyā kaikeyaṃ cāpi pañcabhiḥd tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsān pitā devavratas tavad vārayitvā śarair ghoraiḥ śvetam evābhidudruved tataḥ śaraṃ mṛtyusamaṃ bhārasādhanam uttamamd vikṛṣya balavān bhīṣmaḥ samādhatta durāsadamd brahmāstreṇa susaṃyuktaṃ taṃ śaraṃ lomavāhinamd dadṛśur devagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥd sa tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā hṛdayaṃ cāmitaujasaḥd jagāma dharaṇīṃ bāṇo mahāśanir iva jvaland astaṃ gacchan yathādityaḥ prabhām ādāya satvaraḥd evaṃ jīvitam ādāya śvetadehāj jagāma had taṃ bhīṣmeṇa naravyāghraṃ tathā vinihataṃ yudhid prapatantam apaśyāma gireḥ śṛṅgam iva cyutamd aśocan pāṇḍavās tatra kṣatriyāś ca mahārathāḥd prahṛṣṭāś ca sutās tubhyaṃ kuravaś cāpi sarvaśaḥd tato duḥśāsano rājañ śvetaṃ dṛṣṭvā nipātitamd vāditraninadair ghorair nṛtyati sma samantataḥd tasmin hate maheṣvāse bhīṣmeṇāhavaśobhinād prāvepanta maheṣvāsāḥ śikhaṇḍipramukhā rathāḥd tato dhanaṃjayo rājan vārṣṇeyaś cāpi sarvaśaḥd avahāraṃ śanaiś cakrur nihate vāhinīpataud tato vahāraḥ sainyānāṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratad tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nardatāṃ ca muhur muhuḥd pārthā vimanaso bhūtvā nyaviśanta mahārathāḥd dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācad cintayanto vadhaṃ ghoraṃ dvairathena paraṃtapāḥd śvete senāpatau tāta saṃgrāme nihate paraiḥd kim akurvan maheṣvāsāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahad senāpatiṃ samākarṇya śvetaṃ yudhi nipātitamd tadarthaṃ yatatāṃ cāpi pareṣāṃ prapalāyināmd manaḥ prīṇāti me vākyaṃ jayaṃ saṃjaya śṛṇvataḥd pratyupāyaṃ cintayantaḥ sajjanāḥ prasravanti med sa hi vīro nuraktaś ca vṛddhaḥ kurupatis tadād kṛtaṃ vairaṃ sadā tena pituḥ putreṇa dhīmatād tasyodvegabhayāc cāpi saṃśritaḥ pāṇḍavān purād sarvaṃ balaṃ parityajya durgaṃ saṃśritya tiṣṭhatid pāṇḍavānāṃ pratāpena durgaṃ deśaṃ niveśya cad sapatnān satataṃ bādhann āryavṛttim anuṣṭhitaḥd āścaryaṃ vai sadā teṣāṃ purā rājñāṃ sudurmatiḥd tato yudhiṣṭhire bhaktaḥ kathaṃ saṃjaya sūditaḥd prakṣiptaḥ saṃmataḥ kṣudraḥ putro me puruṣādhamaḥd na yuddhaṃ rocayed bhīṣmo na cācāryaḥ kathaṃ canad na kṛpo na ca gāndhārī nāhaṃ saṃjaya rocayed na vāsudevo vārṣṇeyo dharmarājaś ca pāṇḍavaḥd na bhīmo nārjunaś caiva na yamau puruṣarṣabhaud vāryamāṇo mayā nityaṃ gāndhāryā vidureṇa cad jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa vyāsena ca mahātmanād duryodhano yudhyamāno nityam eva hi saṃjayad karṇasya matam āsthāya saubalasya ca pāpakṛtd duḥśāsanasya ca tathā pāṇḍavān anvasūyatad tasyāhaṃ vyasanaṃ ghoraṃ manye prāptaṃ tu saṃjayad śvetasya ca vināśena bhīṣmasya vijayena cad saṃkruddhaḥ kṛṣṇasahitaḥ pārthaḥ kim akarod yudhid arjunād dhi bhayaṃ bhūyas tan me tāta na śāmyatid sa hi śūraś ca kaunteyaḥ kṣiprakārī ca pāṇḍavaḥd manye śaraiḥ śarīrāṇi pramathiṣyati vidviṣāmd aindrir indrānujasamo mahendrasadṛśo baled amoghakrodhasaṃkalpaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaḥ kim abhūn manaḥd tathaiva vedavic chūro jvalanārkasamadyutiḥd aindrāstravid ameyātmā prapatan samitiṃjayaḥd vajrasaṃsparśarūpāṇām astrāṇāṃ nyāsakāritād sa khaḍgākṣepahastas tu ghoṣaṃ cakre mahārathaḥd sa saṃjaya mahāprājño drupadasyātmajo balīd dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ kim akaroc chvete yudhi nipātited purā caivāparādhena vadhena ca camūpateḥd manye manaḥ prajajvāla pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāmd teṣāṃ krodhaṃ cintayaṃs tu ahaḥsu ca niśāsu cad saṃjaya uvācad na śāntim adhigacchāmi sarvam ācakṣva saṃjayad gatapūrvāhṇabhūyiṣṭhe tasminn ahani dāruṇed tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca punar yuddham avartatad śvetaṃ tu nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā virāṭasya camūpatimd kṛtavarmaṇā ca sahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śalyam avasthitame śaṅkhaḥ krodhāt prajajvāla haviṣā havyavāḍ ivaa sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ kārtasvaravibhūṣitamc abhyadhāvaj jighāṃsan vai śalyaṃ madrādhipaṃ balīa mahatā rathavaṃśena samantāt parivāritaḥc sṛjan bāṇamayaṃ puraḥsaraḥc bhīṣmād rakṣyo yam adyeti tato yuddham avartataa hāhākāro mahān āsīd yodhānāṃ yudhi yudhyatāmc tejas tejasi saṃpṛktam ity evaṃ vismayaṃ yayuḥa atha śalyo gadāpāṇir avatīrya mahārathātc antarikṣaṃ bhūmiś ca sarvataḥ samavastṛtamd pāñcālān atha matsyaṃ ca drupadaṃ senayā vṛtama pāñcālān atha matsyāṃś ca kekayāṃś ca prabhadrakānc bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pātayām āsa mārgaṇaiḥa utsṛjya samare tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ savyasācinamc abhyadravata pāñcālyaṃ drupadaṃ senayā vṛtame priyaṃ saṃbandhinaṃ rājañ śarān avakiran bahūna agnineva pradagdhāni vanāni śiśirātyayec śaradagdhāny adṛśyanta sainyāni drupadasya hae atiṣṭhata raṇe bhīṣmo vidhūma iva pāvakaḥa madhyaṃdine yathādityaṃ tapantam iva tejasāc na śekuḥ pāṇḍaveyasya yodhā bhīṣmaṃ nirīkṣituma vīkṣāṃ cakruḥ samantāt te puruṣarṣabhaa sa tvaṃ puruṣaśārdūla vikramya jahi kauravānc ahaṃ ca tvānuyāsyāmi bhīmaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca māriṣaa mādrīputrau ca sahitau draupadeyāś ca daṃśitāḥc ye cānye pṛthivīpālāḥ pradhānāḥ puruṣarṣabhad gāndhāraiḥ pāti gāndhārarājaḥd bhīṣmo grataḥ sarvasainyasya vṛddhaḥd śvetacchatraḥ śvetakacaḥ saśaṅkhaḥd śvetoṣṇīṣaḥ pāṇḍureṇa dhvajenad śveto rathaḥ śailasamaprakāśaḥd tadvat sainyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya sarved bāhlikānāṃ cātiratho mahātmād maheṣvāsā mahābhāgāḥ sthitā yuddhāya daṃśitāḥa teṣām ādityavarṇāni vimalāni mahānti cac śvetacchatrāṇy aśobhanta vāraṇeṣu ratheṣu ca saṃjaya uvācaa krauñcaṃ tato mahāvyūham abhedyaṃ tanayas tavac vyūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāghoraṃ pārthenāmitatejasāa ācāryam upasaṃgamya kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ ca māriṣac saumadattiṃ vikarṇaṃ ca aśvatthāmānam eva caa duḥśāsanādīn bhrātṝṃś ca sa sarvān eva bhāratac anyāṃś ca subahūñ śūrān yuddhāya samupāgatāna prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ kāle harṣayaṃs tanayas tavac nānāśastrapraharaṇāḥ sarve śastrāstravedinaḥa ekaikaśaḥ samarthā hi yūyaṃ sarve mahārathāḥc pāṇḍuputrān raṇe hantuṃ sasainyān kim u saṃhatāḥa aparyāptaṃ tad asmākaṃ balaṃ bhīṣmābhirakṣitamc paryāptaṃ tv idam eteṣāṃ balaṃ pārthivasattamāḥa saṃsthānāḥ śūrasenāś ca veṇikāḥ kukurās tathāc ārevakās trigartāś ca madrakā yavanās tathāa śatruṃjayena sahitās tathā duḥśāsanena cac vikarṇena ca vīreṇa tathā nandopanandakaiḥa citrasenena sahitāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇibhadrakaiḥc bhīṣmam evābhirakṣantu saha sainyapuraskṛtāḥa tato droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca tava putraś ca māriṣac avyūhanta mahāvyūhaṃ pāṇḍūnāṃ pratibādhanea bhīṣmaḥ sainyena mahatā samantāt parivāritaḥc yayau prakarṣan mahatīṃ vāhinīṃ surarāḍ ivaa tam anvayān maheṣvāso bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc kuntalaiś ca daśārṇaiś ca māgadhaiś ca viśāṃ patea vidarbhair mekalaiś caiva karṇaprāvaraṇair apic sahitāḥ sarvasainyena bhīṣmam āhavaśobhinama gāndhārāḥ sindhusauvīrāḥ śibayo tha vasātayaḥc śakuniś ca svasainyena bhāradvājam apālayata tato duryodhano rājā sahitaḥ sarvasodaraiḥc aśvātakair vikarṇaiś ca tathā śarmilakosalaiḥa daradaiś cūcupaiś caiva tathā kṣudrakamālavaiḥc abhyarakṣata saṃhṛṣṭaḥ saubaleyasya vāhinīma bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyo bhagadattaś ca māriṣac vindānuvindāv āvantyau vāmaṃ pārśvam apālayana saumadattiḥ suśarmā ca kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥc śatāyuś ca śrutāyuś ca dakṣiṇaṃ pārśvam āsthitāḥa aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥc mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ senāpṛṣṭhe vyavasthitāḥa pṛṣṭhagopās tu tasyāsan nānādeśyā janeśvarāḥc ketumān vasudānaś ca putraḥ kāśyasya cābhibhūḥa tatas te tāvakāḥ sarve hṛṣṭā yuddhāya bhāratac dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yuktāḥ siṃhanādāṃś ca nādayana teṣāṃ śrutvā tu hṛṣṭānāṃ kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥc siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccaiḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau pratāpavāna tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca peśyaś ca vividhāḥ paraiḥc ānakāś cābhyahanyanta sa śabdas tumulo bhavata tataḥ śvetair hayair yukte mahati syandane sthitauc pradadhmatuḥ śaṅkhavarau hemaratnapariṣkṛtaua pāñcajanyaṃ hṛṣīkeśo devadattaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc pauṇḍraṃ dadhmau mahāśaṅkhaṃ bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥa anantavijayaṃ rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sughoṣamaṇipuṣpakaud yudhiṣṭhiraś ca dharmātmā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaud abhimanyuś ca vikrānta uttamaujāś ca vīryavāna kāśirājaś ca śaibyaś ca śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumno virāṭaś ca sātyakiś ca mahāyaśāḥa pāñcālyaś ca maheṣvāso draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥc sarve dadhmur mahāśaṅkhān siṃhanādāṃś ca nedirea sa ghoṣaḥ sumahāṃs tatra vīrais taiḥ samudīritaḥc nabhaś ca pṛthivīṃ caiva tumulo vyanunādayata evam ete mahārāja prahṛṣṭāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥc punar yuddhāya saṃjagmus tāpayānāḥ parasparam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa evaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu māmakeṣv itareṣu cac kathaṃ praharatāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire saṃjaya uvācaa samaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu saṃnaddhā ruciradhvajāḥb tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ yathāyudhyanta tac chṛṇuc apāram iva saṃdṛśya sāgarapratimaṃ balama teṣāṃ madhye sthito rājā putro duryodhanas tavac abravīt tāvakān sarvān yudhyadhvam iti daṃśitāḥa te manaḥ krūram āsthāya samabhityaktajīvitāḥc pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta sarva evocchritadhvajāḥa tato yuddhaṃ samabhavat tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca vyatiṣaktarathadvipama muktās tu rathibhir bāṇā rukmapuṅkhāḥ sutejanāḥc saṃnipetur akuṇṭhāgrā nāgeṣu ca hayeṣu caa tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme dhanur udyamya daṃśitaḥc abhipatya mahābāhur bhīṣmo bhīmaparākramaḥa saubhadre bhīmasene ca śaineye ca mahārathec kekaye ca virāṭe ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca pārṣatea eteṣu naravīreṣu cedimatsyeṣu cābhitaḥc vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥa prākampata mahāvyūhas tasmin vīrasamāgamec sarveṣām eva sainyānām āsīd vyatikaro mahāna sāditadhvajanāgāś ca hatapravaravājinaḥc viprayātarathānīkāḥ samapadyanta pāṇḍavāḥa arjunas tu naravyāghro dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaṃ mahārathamc vārṣṇeyam abravīt kruddho yāhi yatra pitāmahaḥa eṣa bhīṣmaḥ susaṃkruddho vārṣṇeya mama vāhinīmc nāśayiṣyati suvyaktaṃ duryodhanahite rataḥa eṣa droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyo vikarṇaś ca janārdanac dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca sahitā duryodhanapurogamāḥa pāñcālān nihaniṣyanti rakṣitā dṛḍhadhanvanāc so haṃ bhīṣmaṃ gamiṣyāmi sainyahetor janārdanaa tam abravīd vāsudevo yatto bhava dhanaṃjayac eṣa tvā prāpaye vīra pitāmaharathaṃ pratia evam uktvā tataḥ śaurī rathaṃ taṃ lokaviśrutamc prāpayām āsa bhīṣmāya rathaṃ prati janeśvaraa cañcadbahupatākena balākāvarṇavājināc samucchritamahābhīmanadadvānaraketunād lāṅgūlāsphoṭaśabdena svanayāno nabhastalamd piṅgākṣair dṛṣṭipātaiś ca bhīṣayann arisainikāne mahatā meghanādena rathenādityavarcasāa vinighnan kauravānīkaṃ śūrasenāṃś ca pāṇḍavaḥc āyāc charān nudañ śīghraṃ suhṛcchoṣavināśanaḥa tam āpatantaṃ vegena prabhinnam iva vāraṇamc trāsayānaṃ raṇe śūrān pātayantaṃ ca sāyakaiḥa saindhavapramukhair guptaḥ prācyasauvīrakekayaiḥc sahasā pratyudīyāya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo rjunama ko hi gāṇḍīvadhanvānam anyaḥ kurupitāmahātc droṇavaikartanābhyāṃ vā rathaḥ saṃyātum arhatia tato bhīṣmo mahārāja kauravāṇāṃ pitāmahaḥc arjunaṃ saptasaptatyā nārācānāṃ samāvṛṇota droṇaś ca pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpaḥ pañcāśatā śaraiḥc duryodhanaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā śalyaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥd drauṇiḥ ṣaṣṭyā naravyāghro vikarṇaś ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥa saindhavo navabhiś cāpi śakuniś cāpi pañcabhiḥc vikarṇo daśabhir bhallai rājan vivyādha pāṇḍavama sa tair viddho maheṣvāsaḥ samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc na vivyathe mahābāhur bhidyamāna ivācalaḥa sa bhīṣmaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥc droṇaṃ ṣaṣṭyā naravyāghro vikarṇaṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥd śalyaṃ ca daśabhir bāṇais tāvadbhiś ca jayadrathama ārtāyaniṃ tribhir bāṇai rājānaṃ cāpi pañcabhiḥc pratyavidhyad ameyātmā kirīṭī bharatarṣabhaa taṃ sātyakir virāṭaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc draupadeyābhimanyuś ca parivavrur dhanaṃjayama tato droṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ gāṅgeyasya priye ratamc abhyavarṣata pāñcālyaḥ saṃyuktaḥ saha somakaiḥa bhīṣmas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭhas tūrṇaṃ vivyādha pāṇḍavamc aśītyā niśitair bāṇais tato krośanta tāvakāḥa teṣāṃ tu ninadaṃ śrutvā prahṛṣṭānāṃ prahṛṣṭavatc praviveśa tato madhyaṃ rathasiṃhaḥ pratāpavāna teṣāṃ tu rathasiṃhānāṃ madhyaṃ prāpya dhanaṃjayaḥc cikrīḍa dhanuṣā rājaṃl lakṣyaṃ kṛtvā mahārathānd kṣatriyāṇāṃ śirāṃsy ugraiḥ kṛntañ śastrair mahārathaḥd śūnyān kṛtvā rathopasthān vyacarat phalgunas tadāa tato duryodhano rājā bhīṣmam āha janeśvaraḥc pīḍyamānaṃ svakaṃ sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthena saṃyugea eṣa pāṇḍusutas tāta kṛṣṇena sahito balīc yatatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ mūlaṃ naḥ parikṛntatie tvayi jīvati gāṅgeye droṇe ca rathināṃ varea tvatkṛte hy eṣa karṇo pi nyastaśastro mahārathaḥc na yudhyati raṇe pārthaṃ hitakāmaḥ sadā mamaa sa tathā kuru gāṅgeya yathā hanyeta phalgunaḥc evam uktas tato rājan pitā devavratas tavae dhik kṣatradharmam ity uktvā yayau pārtharathaṃ pratia ubhau śvetahayau rājan saṃsaktau dṛśya pārthivāḥc siṃhanādān bhṛśaṃ cakruḥ śaṅkhaśabdāṃś ca bhārataa drauṇir duryodhanaś caiva vikarṇaś ca tavātmajaḥc parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ sthitā yuddhāya māriṣaa tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parivārya dhanaṃjayamc sthitā yuddhāya mahate tato yuddham avartataa gāṅgeyas tu raṇe pārtham ānarchan navabhiḥ śaraiḥc tam arjunaḥ pratyavidhyad daśabhir marmavedhibhiḥa tataḥ śarasahasreṇa suprayuktena pāṇḍavaḥc arjunaḥ samaraślāghī bhīṣmasyāvārayad diśaḥa śarajālaṃ tatas tat tu śarajālena kauravac vārayām āsa pārthasya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tathāa ubhau paramasaṃhṛṣṭāv ubhau yuddhābhinandinauc nirviśeṣam ayudhyetāṃ kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇaua bhīṣmacāpavimuktāni śarajālāni saṃghaśaḥc śīryamāṇāny adṛśyanta bhinnāny arjunasāyakaiḥa tathaivārjunamuktāni śarajālāni bhāgaśaḥc gāṅgeyaśaranunnāni nyapatanta mahītalea arjunaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā bhīṣmam ārcchac chitaiḥ śaraiḥc bhīṣmo pi samare pārthaṃ vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥa anyonyasya hayān viddhvā dhvajau ca sumahābalauc ratheṣāṃ rathacakre ca cikrīḍatur ariṃdamaua tataḥ kruddho mahārāja bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥc vāsudevaṃ tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntarea bhīṣmacāpacyutair bāṇair nirviddho madhusūdanaḥc virarāja raṇe rājan sapuṣpa iva kiṃśukaḥa tato rjuno bhṛśaṃ kruddho nirviddhaṃ prekṣya mādhavamc gāṅgeyasārathiṃ saṃkhye nirbibheda tribhiḥ śaraiḥa yatamānau tu tau vīrāv anyonyasya vadhaṃ pratic nāśaknutāṃ tadānyonyam abhisaṃdhātum āhavea maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi gatapratyāgatāni cac adarśayetāṃ bahudhā sūtasāmarthyalāghavāta antaraṃ ca prahāreṣu tarkayantau mahārathauc rājann antaramārgasthau sthitāv āstāṃ muhur muhuḥa ubhau siṃharavonmiśraṃ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ pracakratuḥc tathaiva cāpanirghoṣaṃ cakratus tau mahārathaua tayoḥ śaṅkhapraṇādena rathanemisvanena cac dāritā sahasā bhūmiś cakampa ca nanāda caa na tayor antaraṃ kaś cid dadṛśe bharatarṣabhac balinau samare śūrāv anyonyasadṛśāv ubhaua cihnamātreṇa bhīṣmaṃ tu prajajñus tatra kauravāḥc tathā pāṇḍusutāḥ pārthaṃ cihnamātreṇa jajñirea tayor nṛvarayo rājan dṛśya tādṛk parākramamc vismayaṃ sarvabhūtāni jagmur bhārata saṃyugea na tayor vivaraṃ kaś cid raṇe paśyati bhāratac dharme sthitasya hi yathā na kaś cid vṛjinaṃ kva cita ubhau hi śarajālena tāv adṛśyau babhūvatuḥc prakāśau ca punas tūrṇaṃ babhūvatur ubhau raṇea tatra devāḥ sagandharvāś cāraṇāś ca saharṣibhiḥc anyonyaṃ pratyabhāṣanta tayor dṛṣṭvā parākramama na śakyau yudhi saṃrabdhau jetum etau mahārathauc sadevāsuragandharvair lokair api kathaṃ canaa āścaryabhūtaṃ lokeṣu yuddham etan mahādbhutamc naitādṛśāni yuddhāni bhaviṣyanti kathaṃ canaa nāpi śakyo raṇe jetuṃ bhīṣmaḥ pārthena dhīmatāc sadhanuś ca rathasthaś ca pravapan sāyakān raṇea tathaiva pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe devair api durāsadamc na vijetuṃ raṇe bhīṣma utsaheta dhanurdharamd ālokād api yuddhaṃ tu samam etad bhaviṣyatia iti sma vācaḥ śrūyante proccarantyas tatas tataḥc gāṅgeyārjunayoḥ saṃkhye stavayuktā viśāṃ patea tvadīyās tu tato yodhāḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca bhāratac anyonyaṃ samare jaghnus tayos tatra parākramea śitadhārais tathā khaḍgair vimalaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥc śarair anyaiś ca bahubhiḥ śastrair nānāvidhair yudhie ubhayoḥ senayor vīrā nyakṛntanta parasparama vartamāne tathā ghore tasmin yuddhe sudāruṇec droṇapāñcālyayo rājan mahān āsīt samāgamaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālyaś cāpi pārṣataḥc raṇe samīyatur yattau tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa diṣṭam eva paraṃ manye pauruṣād api saṃjayac yatra śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo nātarad yudhi pāṇḍavama bhīṣmo hi samare kruddho hanyāl lokāṃś carācarānc sa kathaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhe nātarat saṃjayaujasā saṃjaya uvācaa śṛṇu rājan sthiro bhūtvā yuddham etat sudāruṇamc na śakyaḥ pāṇḍavo jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥa droṇas tu niśitair bāṇair dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayatc sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apātayata tasyātha caturo vāhāṃś caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥc pīḍayām āsa saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnasya māriṣaa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato droṇaṃ navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha prahasan vīras tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta tataḥ punar ameyātmā bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa dhṛṣṭadyumnam amarṣaṇama ādade ca śaraṃ ghoraṃ pārṣatasya vadhaṃ pratic śakrāśanisamasparśaṃ mṛtyudaṇḍam ivāparama hāhākāro mahān āsīt sarvasainyasya bhāratac tam iṣuṃ saṃdhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāradvājena saṃyugea tatrādbhutam apaśyāma dhṛṣṭadyumnasya pauruṣamc yad ekaḥ samare vīras tasthau girir ivācalaḥa taṃ ca dīptaṃ śaraṃ ghoram āyāntaṃ mṛtyum ātmanaḥc ciccheda śaravṛṣṭiṃ ca bhāradvāje mumoca haa tata uccukruśuḥ sarve pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac dhṛṣṭadyumnena tat karma kṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā suduṣkarama tataḥ śaktiṃ mahāvegāṃ svarṇavaiḍūryabhūṣitāmc droṇasya nidhanākāṅkṣī cikṣepa sa parākramīa tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śaktiṃ kanakabhūṣaṇāmc tridhā cikṣepa samare bhāradvājo hasann ivaa śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavānc vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi droṇaṃ prati janeśvaraa śaravarṣaṃ tatas taṃ tu saṃnivārya mahāyaśāḥc droṇo drupadaputrasya madhye ciccheda kārmukama sa cchinnadhanvā samare gadāṃ gurvīṃ mahāyaśāḥc droṇāya preṣayām āsa girisāramayīṃ balīa sā gadā vegavan muktā prāyād droṇajighāṃsayāc tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bhāradvājasya vikramama lāghavād vyaṃsayām āsa gadāṃ hemavibhūṣitāmc vyaṃsayitvā gadāṃ tāṃ ca preṣayām āsa pārṣatea bhallān suniśitān pītān svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitānc te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhavea athānyad dhanur ādāya dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāmanāḥc droṇaṃ yudhi parākramya śarair vivyādha pañcabhiḥa rudhirāktau tatas tau tu śuśubhāte nararṣabhauc vasantasamaye rājan puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukaua amarṣitas tato rājan parākramya camūmukhec droṇo drupadaputrasya punaś ciccheda kārmukama athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc avākirad ameyātmā vṛṣṭyā megha ivācalamd tad apy asya raṇe droṇaś ciccheda saśaraṃ dhanuḥa sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apātayatc athāsya caturo vāhāṃś caturbhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa pātayām āsa samare siṃhanādaṃ nanāda cac tato pareṇa bhallena hastāc cāpam athācchinata sa cchinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥc gadāpāṇir avārohat khyāpayan pauruṣaṃ mahata tām asya viśikhais tūrṇaṃ pātayām āsa bhāratac rathād anavarūḍhasya tad adbhutam ivābhavata tataḥ sa vipulaṃ carma śatacandraṃ ca bhānumatc khaḍgaṃ ca vipulaṃ divyaṃ pragṛhya subhujo balīa abhidudrāva vegena droṇasya vadhakāṅkṣayāc āmiṣārthī yathā siṃho vane mattam iva dvipama tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bhāradvājasya pauruṣamc lāghavaṃ cāstrayogaṃ ca balaṃ bāhvoś ca bhārataa yad enaṃ śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa pārṣatamc na śaśāka tato gantuṃ balavān api saṃyugea tatra sthitam apaśyāma dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahārathamc vārayāṇaṃ śaraughāṃś ca carmaṇā kṛtahastavata tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ sahasābhyapatad balīc sāhāyyakārī samare pārṣatasya mahātmanaḥa sa droṇaṃ niśitair bāṇai rājan vivyādha saptabhiḥc pārṣataṃ ca tadā tūrṇam anyam āropayad rathama tato duryodhano rājā kaliṅgaṃ samacodayatc sainyena mahatā yuktaṃ bhāradvājasya rakṣaṇea tataḥ sā mahatī senā kaliṅgānāṃ janeśvarac bhīmam abhyudyayau tūrṇaṃ tava putrasya śāsanāta pāñcālyam abhisaṃtyajya droṇo pi rathināṃ varaḥc virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau yodhayām āsa saṃgataue dhṛṣṭadyumno pi samare dharmarājaṃ samabhyayāta tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc kaliṅgānāṃ ca samare bhīmasya ca mahātmanaḥe jagataḥ prakṣayakaraṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa tathā pratisamādiṣṭaḥ kaliṅgo vāhinīpatiḥc katham adbhutakarmāṇaṃ bhīmasenaṃ mahābalama carantaṃ gadayā vīraṃ daṇḍapāṇim ivāntakamc yodhayām āsa samare kaliṅgaḥ saha senayā saṃjaya uvācaa putreṇa tava rājendra sa tathokto mahābalaḥc mahatyā senayā guptaḥ prāyād bhīmarathaṃ pratia tām āpatantīṃ sahasā kaliṅgānāṃ mahācamūmc rathanāgāśvakalilāṃ pragṛhītamahāyudhāma bhīmasenaḥ kaliṅgānām ārchad bhārata vāhinīmc ketumantaṃ ca naiṣādim āyāntaṃ saha cedibhiḥa tataḥ śrutāyuḥ saṃkruddho rājñā ketumatā sahac āsasāda raṇe bhīmaṃ vyūḍhānīkeṣu cediṣua rathair anekasāhasraiḥ kaliṅgānāṃ janādhipaḥc ayutena gajānāṃ ca niṣādaiḥ saha ketumāne bhīmasenaṃ raṇe rājan samantāt paryavārayata cedimatsyakarūṣāś ca bhīmasenapurogamāḥc abhyavartanta sahasā niṣādān saha rājabhiḥa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakamb sarve kaliṅgakāś caiva saṃnivṛtteṣu cediṣub svabāhubalam āsthāya abhyavartanta pāṇḍavamc prajānan na ca yodhān svān parasparajighāṃsayāa ghoram āsīt tato yuddhaṃ bhīmasya sahasā paraiḥc yathendrasya mahārāja mahatyā daityasenayāa tasya sainyasya saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya bhāratac babhūva sumahāñ śabdaḥ sāgarasyeva garjataḥa anyonyasya tadā yodhā nikṛntanto viśāṃ patec mahīṃ cakruś citāṃ sarvāṃ śaśaśoṇitasaṃnibhāma yodhāṃś ca svān parān vāpi nābhyajānañ jighāṃsayāc svān apy ādadate svāś ca śūrāḥ samaradurjayāḥa vimardaḥ sumahān āsīd alpānāṃ bahubhiḥ sahac kaliṅgaiḥ saha cedīnāṃ niṣādaiś ca viśāṃ patea kṛtvā puruṣakāraṃ tu yathāśakti mahābalāḥc bhīmasenaṃ parityajya saṃnyavartanta cedayaḥa sarvaiḥ kaliṅgair āsannaḥ saṃnivṛtteṣu cediṣuc svabāhubalam āsthāya na nyavartata pāṇḍavaḥa na cacāla rathopasthād bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc śitair avākiran bāṇaiḥ kaliṅgānāṃ varūthinīma kaliṅgas tu maheṣvāsaḥ putraś cāsya mahārathaḥc śakradeva iti khyāto jaghnatuḥ pāṇḍavaṃ śaraiḥa tato bhīmo mahābāhur vidhunvan ruciraṃ dhanuḥc yodhayām āsa kāliṅgān svabāhubalam āśritaḥa śakradevas tu samare visṛjan sāyakān bahūnc aśvāñ jaghāna samare bhīmasenasya sāyakaiḥd taṃ dṛṣṭvā virathaṃ tatra bhīmasenam ariṃdamamd śakradevo bhidudrāva śitair avakirañ śaraiḥd bhīmasyopari rājendra śakradevo mahābalaḥe vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi tapānte jalado yathāa hatāśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc śakradevāya cikṣepa sarvaśaikyāyasīṃ gadāma sa tayā nihato rājan kaliṅgasya suto rathātc sadhvajaḥ saha sūtena jagāma dharaṇītalama hatam ātmasutaṃ dṛṣṭvā kaliṅgānāṃ janādhipaḥc rathair anekasāhasrair bhimasyāvārayad diśaḥd ayutena gajānāṃ ca niṣādaiḥ parivāritaḥa tato bhīmo mahābāhur gurvīṃ tyaktvā mahāgadāmc udbabarhātha nistriṃśaṃ cikīrṣuḥ karma dāruṇama carma cāpratimaṃ rājann ārṣabhaṃ puruṣarṣabhac nakṣatrair ardhacandraiś ca śātakumbhamayaiś citama kaliṅgas tu tataḥ kruddho dhanurjyām avamṛjya hac pragṛhya ca śaraṃ ghoram ekaṃ sarpaviṣopamame prāhiṇod bhīmasenāya vadhākāṅkṣī janeśvaraḥa tam āpatantaṃ vegena preritaṃ niśitaṃ śaramc bhīmaseno dvidhā rājaṃś ciccheda vipulāsināe udakrośac ca saṃhṛṣṭas trāsayāno varūthinīma kaliṅgas tu tataḥ kruddho bhīmasenāya saṃyugec tomarān prāhiṇoc chīghraṃ caturdaśa śilāśitāna tān aprāptān mahābāhuḥ khagatān eva pāṇḍavaḥc ciccheda sahasā rājann asaṃbhrānto varāsināa nikṛtya tu raṇe bhīmas tomarān vai caturdaśac bhānumantam abhiprekṣya prādravat puruṣarṣabhaḥa bhānumāṃs tu tato bhīmaṃ śaravarṣeṇa chādayanc nanāda balavan nādaṃ nādayāno nabhastalama na taṃ sa mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ siṃhanādaṃ mahāraṇec tataḥ svareṇa mahatā vinanāda mahāsvanama tena śabdena vitrastā kaliṅgānāṃ varūthinīc na bhīmaṃ samare mene mānuṣaṃ bharatarṣabhaa tato bhīmo mahārāja naditvā vipulaṃ svanamc sāsir vegād avaplutya dantābhyāṃ vāraṇottamama āruroha tato madhyaṃ nāgarājasya māriṣab tato mumoca kāliṅgaḥ śaktiṃ tām akarod dvidhāc khaḍgena pṛthunā madhye bhānumantam athācchinata so ntarāyudhinaṃ hatvā rājaputram ariṃdamaḥc gurubhārasahaskandhe nāgasyāsim apātayata chinnaskandhaḥ sa vinadan papāta gajayūthapaḥc ārugṇaḥ sindhuvegena sānumān iva parvataḥa tatas tasmād avaplutya gajād bhārata bhārataḥc khaḍgapāṇir adīnātmā atiṣṭhad bhuvi daṃśitaḥa sa cacāra bahūn mārgān abhītaḥ pātayan gajānc agnicakram ivāviddhaṃ sarvataḥ pratyadṛśyataa aśvavṛndeṣu nāgeṣu rathānīkeṣu cābhibhūḥc padātīnāṃ ca saṃgheṣu vinighnañ śoṇitokṣitaḥe śyenavad vyacarad bhīmo raṇe ripubalotkaṭaḥa chindaṃs teṣāṃ śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca mahājavaḥc khaḍgena śitadhāreṇa saṃyuge gajayodhināma padātir ekaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śatrūṇāṃ bhayavardhanaḥc mohayām āsa ca tadā kālāntakayamopamaḥd padātibhiḥ padātīṃś ca aśvān aśvair gajān gajaiḥd rathān rathaiś ca bahudhā jaghāna samare balīa mūḍhāś ca te tam evājau vinadantaḥ samādravanb vibhujya kṣudhitā nādaṃ vidravanti diśo daśab bhramantaṃ kālarūpeṇa bhīmasenaṃ mahābalamc sāsim uttamavegena vicarantaṃ mahāraṇea nikṛtya rathinām ājau ratheṣāś ca yugāni cac jaghāna rathinaś cāpi balavān arimardanaḥa bhīmasenaś caran mārgān subahūn pratyadṛśyatac bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutaṃ prasṛtaṃ sṛtame saṃpātaṃ samudīryaṃ ca darśayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥa ke cid agrāsinā chinnāḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanāc vinedur bhinnamarmāṇo nipetuś ca gatāsavaḥa chinnadantāgrahastāś ca bhinnakumbhās tathāparec viyodhāḥ svāny anīkāni jaghnur bhārata vāraṇāḥe nipetur urvyāṃ ca tathā vinadanto mahāravānf gajāṃś ca gajayantṝṃś ca gajahastāṃś ca bhārataa chinnāṃś ca tomarāṃś cāpān mahāmātraśirāṃsi cac paristomāni citrāṇi kakṣyāś ca kanakojjvalāḥa graiveyāṇy atha śaktīś ca patākāḥ kaṇapāṃs tathāc tūṇīrāṇy atha yantrāṇi vicitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi caa agnikuṇḍāni śubhrāṇi tottrāṃś caivāṅkuśaiḥ sahac ghaṇṭāś ca vividhā rājan hemagarbhāṃs tsarūn apie patataḥ patitāṃś caiva paśyāmaḥ saha sādibhiḥa chinnagātrāvarakarair nihataiś cāpi vāraṇaiḥc āsīt tasmin samāstīrṇā patitair bhūr nagair ivaa vimṛdyaivaṃ mahānāgān mamardāśvān nararṣabhaḥc aśvārohavarāṃś cāpi pātayām āsa bhāratae tad ghoram abhavad yuddhaṃ tasya teṣāṃ ca bhārataa khalīnāny atha yoktrāṇi kaśāś ca kanakojjvalāḥc paristomāś ca prāsāś ca ṛṣṭayaś ca mahādhanāḥa kavacāny atha carmāṇi citrāṇy āstaraṇāni cac tatra tatrāpaviddhāni vyadṛśyanta mahāhavea prothayantrair vicitraiś ca śastraiś ca vimalais tathāc sa cakre vasudhāṃ kīrṇāṃ śabalaiḥ kusumair ivaa āplutya rathinaḥ kāṃś cit parāmṛśya mahābalaḥa         ākṣipyānyāny apātayata khaḍgenānyāṃś ca ciccheda        c pātayām āsa khaḍgena sadhvajān api pāṇḍavaḥa muhur utpatato dikṣu dhāvataś ca yaśasvinaḥc mārgāṃś ca carataś citrān vyasmayanta raṇe janāḥa nijaghāna padā kāṃś cid ākṣipyānyān apothayatc khaḍgenānyāṃś ca ciccheda nādenānyāṃś ca bhīṣayana ūruvegena cāpy anyān pātayām āsa bhūtalec apare cainam ālokya bhayāt pañcatvam āgatāḥa evaṃ sā bahulā senā kaliṅgānāṃ tarasvināmc parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ bhīmasenam upādravata tataḥ kaliṅgasainyānāṃ pramukhe bharatarṣabhac śrutāyuṣam abhiprekṣya bhīmasenaḥ samabhyayāta tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya kaliṅgo navabhiḥ śaraiḥc bhīmasenam ameyātmā pratyavidhyat stanāntarea kaliṅgabāṇābhihatas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥc bhīmasenaḥ prajajvāla krodhenāgnir ivendhanaiḥa athāśokaḥ samādāya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtamc bhīmaṃ saṃpādayām āsa rathena rathasārathiḥa tam āruhya rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ kaunteyaḥ śatrusūdanaḥc kaliṅgam abhidudrāva tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta tataḥ śrutāyur balavān bhīmāya niśitāñ śarānc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho darśayan pāṇilāghavama sa kārmukavarotsṛṣṭair navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc samāhato bhṛśaṃ rājan kaliṅgena mahāyaśāḥe saṃcukrudhe bhṛśaṃ bhīmo daṇḍāhata ivoragaḥa kruddhaś ca cāpam āyamya balavad balināṃ varaḥc kaliṅgam avadhīt pārtho bhīmaḥ saptabhir āyasaiḥa kṣurābhyāṃ cakrarakṣau ca kaliṅgasya mahābalauc satyadevaṃ ca satyaṃ ca prāhiṇod yamasādanama tataḥ punar ameyātmā nārācair niśitais tribhiḥc ketumantaṃ raṇe bhīmo gamayad yamasādanama tataḥ kaliṅgāḥ saṃkruddhā bhīmasenam amarṣaṇamc anīkair bahusāhasraiḥ kṣatriyāḥ samavārayana tataḥ śaktigadākhaḍgatomararṣṭiparaśvadhaiḥc kaliṅgāś ca tato rājan bhīmasenam avākirana saṃnivārya sa tāṃ ghorāṃ śaravṛṣṭiṃ samutthitāmc gadām ādāya tarasā pariplutya mahābalaḥd papāta śatrusainyeṣu kesarīva mahābalaḥe bhīmaḥ saptaśatān vīrān anayad yamasādanama punaś caiva dvisāhasrān kaliṅgān arimardanaḥc prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya tad adbhutam ivābhavatd gadayā muktayā rājan pātayām āsa dantinaḥd tathā gajaṃ gajenaiva prāhiṇod yamasādanamd rathaṃ rathena saṃcūrṇya turaṅgaṃ turageṇa tud padātinaṃ padātena preṣayām āsa mṛtyaved punar aśveṣu patati gajeṣu ca punaḥ punaḥd ratheṣu sa padāteṣu vāyuneva mahānalaḥd yathā mṛgāṇāṃ madhye tu kesarīva nakhagrahaḥd evaṃ bhramati sainyeṣu bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥa evaṃ sa tāny anīkāni kaliṅgānāṃ punaḥ punaḥc bibheda samare vīraḥ prekṣya bhīṣmaṃ mahāvratama hatārohāś ca mātaṅgāḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanāc viprajagmur anīkeṣu meghā vātahatā ivae mṛdnantaḥ svāny anīkāni vinadantaḥ śarāturāḥf bhramanti tatra tatraiva kālyamānā mahātmanāa tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ śaṅkhaṃ prādhmāpayad balīa         khaḍgāsaktamahābhujaḥa saṃprahṛṣṭo mahāghoṣaṃ        c sarvakāliṅgasainyānāṃ manāṃsi samakampayatd bhīmena sahasā rājan bhramamāṇena saṃyugea mohaś cāpi kaliṅgānām āviveśa paraṃtapac prākampanta ca sainyāni vāhanāni ca sarvaśaḥa bhīmena samare rājan gajendreṇeva sarvataḥc mārgān bahūn vicaratā dhāvatā ca tatas tataḥe muhur utpatatā caiva saṃmohaḥ samajāyataf dhāvatā hastimārgeṣu muhur āpatatā punaḥf kaliṅgānāṃ sasainyānāṃ saṃmohaḥ samajāyataa bhīmasenabhayatrastaṃ sainyaṃ ca samakampatac kṣobhyamāṇam asaṃbādhaṃ grāheṇeva mahat saraḥa trāsiteṣu ca vīreṣu bhīmenādbhutakarmaṇāc punarāvartamāneṣu vidravatsu ca saṃghaśaḥa sarvakāliṅgayodheṣu pāṇḍūnāṃ dhvajinīpatiḥc abravīt svāny anīkāni yudhyadhvam iti pārṣataḥa senāpativacaḥ śrutvā śikhaṇḍipramukhā gaṇāḥc bhīmam evābhyavartanta rathānīkaiḥ prahāribhiḥa dharmarājaś ca tān sarvān upajagrāha pāṇḍavaḥc mahatā meghavarṇena nāgānīkena pṛṣṭhataḥa evaṃ saṃcodya sarvāṇi svāny anīkāni pārṣataḥc bhīmasenasya jagrāha pārṣṇiṃ satpuruṣocitāma na hi pāñcālarājasya loke kaś cana vidyatec bhīmasātyakayor anyaḥ prāṇebhyaḥ priyakṛttamaḥa so paśyat taṃ kaliṅgeṣu carantam arisūdanamc bhīmasenaṃ mahābāhuṃ pārṣataḥ paravīrahāa nanarda bahudhā rājan hṛṣṭaś cāsīt paraṃtapaḥc śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau ca samare siṃhanādaṃ nanāda caa sa ca pārāvatāśvasya rathe hemapariṣkṛtec kovidāradhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaḥ samāśvasata dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā kaliṅgaiḥ samabhidrutamc bhīmasenam ameyātmā trāṇāyājau samabhyayāta tau dūrāt sātyakir dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarauc kaliṅgān samare vīrau yodhayantau manasvinaua sa tatra gatvā śaineyo javena jayatāṃ varaḥc pārthapārṣatayoḥ pārṣṇiṃ jagrāha puruṣarṣabhaḥd etac caturdaśe varṣe bhīmo dṛṣṭvā raṇājiramd viśeṣeṇa gajān rājan paraṃ toṣam upāgamata sa kṛtvā kadanaṃ tatra pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥc āsthito raudram ātmānaṃ jaghāna samare parāna kaliṅgaprabhavāṃ caiva māṃsaśoṇitakardamāmc rudhirasyandinīṃ tatra bhīmaḥ prāvartayan nadīma antareṇa kaliṅgānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca vāhinīmc saṃtatāra sudustārāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥa bhīmasenaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā prākrośaṃs tāvakā nṛpac kālo yaṃ bhīmarūpeṇa kaliṅgaiḥ saha yudhyatea tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ śrutvā taṃ ninadaṃ raṇec abhyayāt tvarito bhīmaṃ vyūḍhānīkaḥ samantataḥa taṃ sātyakir bhīmaseno dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc abhyadravanta bhīṣmasya rathaṃ hemapariṣkṛtama parivārya ca te sarve gāṅgeyaṃ rabhasaṃ raṇec tribhis tribhiḥ śarair ghorair bhīṣmam ānarchur añjasāa pratyavidhyata tān sarvān pitā devavratas tavac yatamānān maheṣvāsāṃs tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥa tataḥ śarasahasreṇa saṃnivārya mahārathānc hayān kāñcanasaṃnāhān bhīmasya nyahanac charaiḥa hatāśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānc śaktiṃ cikṣepa tarasā gāṅgeyasya rathaṃ pratia aprāptām eva tāṃ śaktiṃ pitā devavratas tavac tridhā ciccheda samare sā pṛthivyām aśīryataa tataḥ śaikyāyasīṃ gurvīṃ pragṛhya balavad gadāmc bhīmaseno rathāt tūrṇaṃ pupluve manujarṣabhad bhīṣmam evābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥa sātyako pi tatas tūrṇaṃ bhīmasya priyakāmyayāb āplutyāplutya vegena carma bhrāmya punaḥ punaḥb asinā tīkṣṇadhāreṇa yodhāñ chittvā mahāhavec sārathiṃ kuruvṛddhasya pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥa bhīṣmas tu nihate tasmin sārathau rathināṃ varaḥc vātāyamānais tair aśvair apanīto raṇājirāta bhīmasenas tato rājann apanīte mahāvratec prajajvāla yathā vahnir dahan kakṣam ivaidhitaḥa sa hatvā sarvakāliṅgān senāmadhye vyatiṣṭhatac nainam abhyutsahan ke cit tāvakā bharatarṣabhaa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tam āropya svarathe rathināṃ varaḥc paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānām apovāha yaśasvinama saṃpūjyamānaḥ pāñcālyair matsyaiś ca bharatarṣabhac dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ pariṣvajya sameyād atha sātyakima athābravīd bhīmasenaṃ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥc praharṣayan yaduvyāghro dhṛṣṭadyumnasya paśyataḥa diṣṭyā kaliṅgarājaś ca rājaputraś ca ketumānc śakradevaś samasajjata pāñcālyas tribhir etair mahārathaiḥa sa lokaviditān aśvān nijaghāna mahābalaḥc drauṇeḥ pāñcāladāyādaḥ śitair daśabhir āśugaiḥa tataḥ śalyarathaṃ tūrṇam āsthāya hatavāhanaḥc drauṇiḥ pāñcāladāyādam abhyavarṣad atheṣubhiḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tu saṃsaktaṃ drauṇinā dṛśya bhāratac saubhadro bhyapatat tūrṇaṃ vikiran niśitāñ śarāna sa śalyaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṛpaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥc aśvatthāmānam aṣṭābhir vivyādha puruṣarṣabhaa ārjuniṃ tu tatas tūrṇaṃ drauṇir vivyādha patriṇāc śalyo dvādaśabhiś caiva kṛpaś ca niśitais tribhiḥa lakṣmaṇas tava pautras tu tava pautram avasthitamc abhyavartata saṃhṛṣṭas tato yuddham avartataa dauryodhanis tu saṃkruddhaḥ saubhadraṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha samare rājaṃs tad adbhutam ivābhavata abhimanyus tu saṃkruddho bhrātaraṃ bharatarṣabhac śaraiḥ pañcāśatā rājan kṣiprahasto bhyavidhyataa lakṣmaṇo pi tatas tasya dhanuś ciccheda patriṇāc muṣṭideśe mahārāja tata uccukruśur janāḥa tad vihāya dhanuś chinnaṃ saubhadraḥ paravīrahāc anyad ādattavāṃś citraṃ kārmukaṃ vegavattarama tau tatra samare hṛṣṭau kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇauc anyonyaṃ viśikhais tīkṣṇair jaghnatuḥ puruṣarṣabhaua tato duryodhano rājā dṛṣṭvā putraṃ mahārathamc pīḍitaṃ tava pautreṇa prāyāt tatra janeśvaraḥa saṃnivṛtte tava sute sarva eva janādhipāḥc ārjuniṃ rathavaṃśena samantāt paryavārayana sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ śūraiḥ śūro yudhi sudurjayaiḥc na sma vivyathate rājan kṛṣṇatulyaparākramaḥa saubhadram atha saṃsaktaṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā dhanaṃjayaḥc abhidudrāva saṃkruddhas trātukāmaḥ svam ātmajama tataḥ sarathanāgāśvā bhīṣmadroṇapurogamāḥc abhyavartanta rājānaḥ sahitāḥ praṇeduḥ sarvabhūtāni babhūvus timirā diśaḥc kurūṇām anayas tīvraḥ samadṛśyata dāruṇaḥa nāpy antarikṣaṃ na diśo na bhūmir na ca bhāskaraḥc prajajñe bharataśreṣṭha śarasaṃghaiḥ kirīṭinaḥa rjunaṃ samare śūraṃ pratyudyāyāt kathaṃ canaa yo yo hi samare pārthaṃ patyudyāti viśāṃ patec sa sa vai viśikhais tīkṣṇaiḥ paralokāya nīyatea teṣu vidravamāṇeṣu tava yodheṣu sarvaśaḥc arjuno vāsudevaś pradṛśyanta pannagābhāḥ samantataḥd diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva vyāptā hy ārjunasāyakaiḥa eṣa cāstaṃ giriśreṣṭhaṃ bhānumān pratipadyatec vapūṃṣi sarvalokasya saṃharann iva sarvathāa tatrāvahāraṃ saṃprāptaṃ sasomakāḥd pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva praṇeduś ca punaḥ punaḥd prayayuḥ śibirāyaiva dhanaṃjayapuraskṛtāḥd vāditraghoṣaiḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pranṛtyanto mahārathāḥa tato vahāraḥ sainyānāṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratac putrāṇāṃ te jayākāṅkṣī bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥa garuḍasya svayaṃ tuṇḍe pitā devavratas tavac cakṣuṣī ca bharadvājaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥa aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva śīrṣam āstāṃ yaśasvinauc trigartair tad anv eva virāṭaś ca drupadaś ca mahārathaḥc tadanantaram evāsīn nīlo nīlāyudhaiḥ sahaa nīlād anantaraṃ caiva dhṛṣṭaketur mahārathaḥc cedikāśikarūṣaiś ca pauravaiś cābhisaṃvṛtaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca pāñcālāś ca prabhadrakāḥc madhye sainyasya mahataḥ sthitā yuddhāya bhārataa tathaiva dharmarājo pi gajānīkena saṃvṛtaḥc tatas tu sātyakī rājan draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥa abhimanyus tatas caiva na prajñāyata kiṃ canaa udatiṣṭhad rajo bhaumaṃ chādayānaṃ divākaramc diśaḥ pratidiśo vāpi tatra jajñuḥ kathaṃ canaa anumānena saṃjñābhir nāmagotraiś ca saṃyugec vartate sma tadā yuddhaṃ tatra samadṛśyanta taiś cāpi gajayodhinaḥa pattisaṃghā hayārohaiḥ sādisaṃghāś ca pattibhiḥc pātyamānā vyadṛśyanta śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa dhvajais tatrāpaviddhaiś ca kārmukais tomarais tathāc prāsais tathā
