saṃbabhūvur janeśvaraa utthitāny agaṇeyāni kabandhāni samantataḥc cihnabhūtāni jagato vināśārthāya bhārataa tasmin yuddhe mahāraudre vartamāne sudāruṇec pratyadṛśyanta rathino dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥa tato droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥc purumitro vikarṇaś ca śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥa ete samaradurdharṣāḥ siṃhatulyaparākramāḥc pāṇḍavānām anīkāni babhañjuḥ sma punaḥ punaḥa tathaiva saṃyugec rathair anekasāhasraiḥ samantāt paryavārayana athainaṃ rathavṛndena koṣṭakīkṛtya bhāratac śaraiḥ subahusāhasraiḥ samantād abhyavārayana śaktīś ca vimalās tīkṣṇā gadāś ca parighaiḥ sahac prāsān paraśvadhāṃś caiva mudgarān musalān apie cikṣipuḥ samare kruddhāḥ phalgunasya rathaṃ pratia śastrāṇām atha tāṃ vṛṣṭiṃ śalabhānām ivāyatimc rurodha sarvataḥ pārthaḥ śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥa tatra tal lāghavaṃ dṛṣṭvā bībhatsor atimānuṣamc devadānavagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥe sādhu sādhv iti rājendra phalgunaṃ pratyapūjayana sātyakiṃ cābhimanyuṃ ca mahatyā senayā sahac gāndhārāḥ samare śūrā āruroha paraṃtapaḥa tāv ekarathasaṃyuktau saubaleyasya vāhinīmc vyadhametāṃ śitais tūrṇaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa droṇabhīṣmau raṇe yattau dharmarājasya vāhinīmc nāśayetāṃ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ sudāruṇama kurvāṇau tu mahat karma bhīmasenaghaṭotkacaub pitā putraś ca samare kurvāṇau karma duṣkaramb rājānaṃ pratyudīyetāṃ bhīmasenaghaṭotkacauc duryodhanas tato bhyetya tāv ubhāv abhyavārayata duryodhano rājā prahāravaramohitaḥc niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalaṃ ca jagāma haa taṃ visaṃjñam atho jñātvā tvaramāṇo sya sārathiḥc apovāha raṇād rājaṃs tataḥ sainyam abhidyataa tatas tāṃ kauravīṃ senāṃ dravamāṇāṃ samantataḥc nighnan bhīmaḥ śarais tīkṣṇair anuvavrāja pṛṣṭhataḥa pārṣataś ca rathaśreṣṭho dharmaputraś ca pāṇḍavaḥc droṇasya paśyataḥ sainyaṃ gāṅgeyasya ca paśyataḥe jaghnatur viśikhais tīkṣṇaiḥ parānīkaviśātanaiḥa dravamāṇaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ tava putrasya saṃyugec nāśaknutāṃ vārayituṃ bhīṣmadroṇau mahārathaua vāryamāṇaṃ hi bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca viśāṃ patec vidravaty eva tat sainyaṃ paśyator droṇabhīṣmayoḥa tato rathasahasreṣu vidravatsu tatas tataḥc tāv āsthitāv ekarathaṃ saubhadraśinipuṃgavaue saubalīṃ samare senāṃ śātayetāṃ samantataḥa śuśubhāte tadā tau tu śaineyakurupuṃgavauc amāvāsyāṃ gatau yadvat somasūryau nabhastalea arjunas tu tataḥ kruddhas tava sainyaṃ viśāṃ patec vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa dhārābhir iva toyadaḥa vadhyamānaṃ tatas tat tu śaraiḥ pārthasya saṃyugec dudrāva kauravaṃ sainyaṃ viṣādabhayakampitamd vāryamāṇaṃ mahārāja bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādibhiḥa dravatas tān samālokya bhīṣmadroṇau mahārathauc nyavārayetāṃ saṃrabdhau duryodhanahitaiṣiṇaua tato duryodhano rājā samāśvasya viśāṃ patec nyavartayata tat sainyaṃ dravamāṇaṃ samantataḥa yatra yatra sutaṃ tubhyaṃ yo yaḥ paśyati bhāratac tatra tatra nyavartanta kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahārathāḥa tān nivṛttān samīkṣyaiva tato nye pītare janāḥc anyonyaspardhayā rājaṃl lajjayānye vatasthirea punarāvartatāṃ teṣāṃ vega āsīd viśāṃ patec pūryataḥ sāgarasyeva candrasyodayanaṃ pratia saṃnivṛttāṃs tatas tāṃs tu dṛṣṭvā rājā suyodhanaḥc abravīt tvarito gatvā bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ vacaḥa pitāmaha nibodhedaṃ yat tvā vakṣyāmi bhāratac nānurūpam ahaṃ manye tvayi jīvati kauravaa droṇe cāstravidāṃ śreṣṭhe saputre sasuhṛjjanec kṛpe caiva maheṣvāse dravatīyaṃ varūthinīa na pāṇḍavāḥ pratibalās tava rājan kathaṃ canac tathā droṇasya saṃgrāme drauṇeś caiva kṛpasya caa anugrāhyāḥ pāṇḍusutā nūnaṃ tava pitāmahac yathemāṃ kṣamase vīra vadhyamānāṃ varūthinīma so smi vācyas tvayā rājan pūrvam eva samāgamec na yotsye pāṇḍavān saṃkhye nāpi pārṣatasātyakīa śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tubhyam ācāryasya kṛpasya cac karṇena sahitaḥ kṛtyaṃ cintayānas tadaiva hia yadi nāhaṃ parityājyo yuvābhyām iha saṃyugec vikrameṇānurūpeṇa yudhyetāṃ puruṣarṣabhaua etac chrutvā vaco bhīṣmaḥ prahasan vai muhur muhuḥc abravīt tanayaṃ tubhyaṃ krodhād udvṛtya cakṣuṣīa bahuśo hi mayā rājaṃs tathyam uktaṃ hitaṃ vacaḥc ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavā yuddhe devair api savāsavaiḥa yat tu śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ vṛddhenādya nṛpottamac kariṣyāmi yathāśakti prekṣedānīṃ sabāndhavaḥa adya pāṇḍusutān sarvān sasainyān saha bandhubhiḥc miṣato vārayiṣyāmi sarvalokasya paśyataḥa evam ukte tu bhīṣmeṇa putrās tava janeśvarac dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mudā yuktā bherīś ca jaghnire bhṛśama pāṇḍavāpi tato rājañ śrutvā taṃ ninadaṃ mahatc dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca bherīś ca murajāṃś ca vyanādayan dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa pratijñāte tu bhīṣmeṇa tasmin yuddhe sudāruṇeb pāṇḍūn āvārayiṣyeti kathaṃ yuyudhire nṛpāḥc krodhito mama putreṇa duḥkhitena viśeṣataḥa bhīṣmaḥ kim akarot tatra pāṇḍaveyeṣu saṃjayac pitāmahe vā pāñcālās tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa gatapūrvāhṇabhūyiṣṭhe tasminn ahani bhāratab paścimāṃ diśam āsthāya sthite cāpi divākarec jayaṃ prāpteṣu hṛṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasua sarvadharmaviśeṣajñaḥ pitā devavratas tavac abhyayāj javanair aśvaiḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīme mahatyā senayā guptas tava putraiś ca sarvaśaḥa prāvartata tato yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc asmākaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham anayāt tava bhārataa dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ tatra talānāṃ cābhihanyatāmc mahān samabhavac chabdo girīṇām iva dīryatāma tiṣṭha sthito smi viddhy enaṃ nivartasva sthiro bhavac sthito smi praharasveti śabdāḥ śrūyanta sarvaśaḥa kāñcaneṣu tanutreṣu kirīṭeṣu dhvajeṣu cac śilānām iva śaileṣu patitānām abhūt svanaḥa patitāny uttamāṅgāni bāhavaś ca vibhūṣitāḥc vyaceṣṭanta mahīṃ prāpya śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa hṛtottamāṅgāḥ ke cit tu tathaivodyatakārmukāḥc pragṛhītāyudhāś cāpi tasthuḥ puruṣasattamāḥa prāvartata mahāvegā nadī rudhiravāhinīc mātaṅgāṅgaśilāraudrā māṃsaśoṇitakardamāa varāśvanaranāgānāṃ śarīraprabhavā tadāc paralokārṇavamukhī gṛdhragomāyumodinīa na dṛṣṭaṃ na śrutaṃ cāpi yuddham etādṛśaṃ nṛpac yathā tava sutānāṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārataa nāsīd rathapathas tatra yodhair yudhi nipātitaiḥc gajaiś ca patitair nīlair giriśṛṅgair ivāvṛtama vikīrṇaiḥ kavacaiś citrair dhvajaiś chatraiś ca māriṣac śuśubhe tad raṇasthānaṃ śaradīva nabhastalama vinirbhinnāḥ śaraiḥ ke cid antapīḍāvikarṣiṇaḥc abhītāḥ samare śatrūn abhyadhāvanta daṃśitāḥa tāta bhrātaḥ sakhe bandho vayasya mama mātulac mā māṃ parityajety anye cukruśuḥ patitā raṇea ādhāvābhyehi mā gaccha kiṃ bhīto si kva yāsyasic sthito haṃ samare mā bhair iti cānye vicukruśuḥa tatra bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo nityaṃ maṇḍalakārmukaḥc mumoca bāṇān dīptāgrān ahīn āśīviṣān ivaa śarair ekāyanīkurvan diśaḥ sarvā yatavrataḥc jaghāna pāṇḍavarathān ādiśyādiśya bhārataa sa nṛtyan vai rathopasthe darśayan pāṇilāghavamc alātacakravad rājaṃs tatra tatra sma dṛśyatea tam ekaṃ samare śūraṃ pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayās tathāc anekaśatasāhasraṃ samapaśyanta lāghavāta māyākṛtātmānam iva bhīṣmaṃ tatra sma menirec pūrvasyāṃ diśi taṃ dṛṣṭvā pratīcyāṃ dadṛśur janāḥa udīcyāṃ cainam ālokya dakṣiṇasyāṃ punaḥ prabhoc evaṃ sa samare vīro gāṅgeyaḥ pratyadṛśyataa na cainaṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ kaś cic chaknoti vīkṣitumc viśikhān eva paśyanti bhīṣmacāpacyutān bahūna kurvāṇaṃ samare karma sūdayānaṃ ca vāhinīmc vyākrośanta raṇe tatra vīrā bahuvidhaṃ bahue amānuṣeṇa rūpeṇa carantaṃ pitaraṃ tavaa śalabhā iva rājānaḥ patanti vidhicoditāḥc bhīṣmāgnim abhi saṃkruddhaṃ vināśāya sahasraśaḥa na hi moghaḥ śaraḥ kaś cid āsīd bhīṣmasya saṃyugec naranāgāśvakāyeṣu bahutvāl laghuvedhinaḥa bhinatty ekena bāṇena sumuktena patatriṇāc gajakaṅkaṭasaṃnāhaṃ vajreṇevācalottamama dvau trīn api gajārohān piṇḍitān varmitān apic nārācena sutīkṣṇena nijaghāna pitā tavaa yo yo bhīṣmaṃ naravyāghram abhyeti yudhi kaś canac muhūrtadṛṣṭaḥ sa mayā pātito bhuvi dṛśyatea evaṃ sā dharmarājasya vadhyamānā mahācamūḥc bhīṣmeṇātulavīryeṇa vyaśīryata sahasradhāa prakīryata mahāsenā śaravarṣābhitāpitāc paśyato vāsudevasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥa yatamānāpi te vīrā dravamāṇān mahārathānc nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ bhīṣmabāṇaprapīḍitāḥa mahendrasamavīryeṇa vadhyamānā mahācamūḥc abhajyata mahārāja na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥa āviddhanaranāgāśvaṃ patitadhvajakūbaramc anīkaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ hāhābhūtam acetanama jaghānātra pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ tathāc priyaṃ sakhāyaṃ cākrande sakhā daivabalātkṛtaḥa vimucya kavacān anye pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥc prakīrya keśān dhāvantaḥ pratyadṛśyanta bhārataa tad gokulam ivodbhrāntam udbhrāntarathayūthapamc dadṛśe pāṇḍuputrasya sainyam ārtasvaraṃ tadāa prabhajyamānaṃ tat sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvā devakinandanaḥc uvāca pārthaṃ bībhatsuṃ nigṛhya ratham uttamama ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pārtha yaḥ kāṅkṣitas tvayāc praharāsmai naravyāghra na cen mohād vimuhyasea yat tvayā kathitaṃ vīra purā rājñāṃ samāgamec bhīṣmadroṇamukhān sarvān dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāna sānubandhān haniṣyāmi ye māṃ yotsyanti saṃyugec iti tat kuru kaunteya satyaṃ vākyam ariṃdamaa bībhatso paśya sainyaṃ svaṃ bhajyamānaṃ samantataḥc dravataś ca mahīpālān sarvān yaudhiṣṭhire balea dṛṣṭvā hi samare bhīṣmaṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakamc bhayārtāḥ saṃpraṇaśyanti siṃhaṃ kṣudramṛgā ivaa evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca vāsudevaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc codayāśvān yato bhīṣmo vigāhyaitad balārṇavamd pātayiṣyāmi durdharṣaṃ kuruvṛddhaṃ pitāmahama tato śvān rajataprakhyāṃś codayām āsa mādhavaḥc yato bhīṣmaratho rājan duṣprekṣyo raśmimān ivaa tatas tat punar āvṛttaṃ yudhiṣṭhirabalaṃ mahatc dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ mahābāhuṃ bhīṣmāyodyantam āhavea tato bhīṣmaḥ kuruśreṣṭhaḥ siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥc dhanaṃjayarathaṃ tūrṇaṃ śaravarṣair avākirata kṣaṇena sa rathas tasya sahayaḥ sahasārathiḥc śaravarṣeṇa mahatā saṃchanno na prakāśatea vāsudevas tv asaṃbhrānto dhairyam āsthāya sattvavānc codayām āsa tān aśvān vitunnān bhīṣmasāyakaiḥa tataḥ pārtho dhanur gṛhya divyaṃ jaladanisvanamc pātayām āsa bhīṣmasya dhanuś chittvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥa sa cchinnadhanvā kauravyaḥ punar anyan mahad dhanuḥc nimeṣāntaramātreṇa sajyaṃ cakre pitā tavaa vicakarṣa tato dorbhyāṃ dhanur jaladanisvanamc athāsya tad api kruddhaś ciccheda dhanur arjunaḥa tasya tat pūjayām āsa lāghavaṃ śaṃtanoḥ sutaḥc sādhu pārtha mahābāho sādhu bho pāṇḍunandanaa tvayy evaitad yuktarūpaṃ mahat karma dhanaṃjayac prīto smi sudṛḍhaṃ putra kuru yuddhaṃ mayā sahaa iti pārthaṃ praśasyātha pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥc mumoca samare vīraḥ śarān pārtharathaṃ pratia adarśayad vāsudevo hayayāne paraṃ balamc moghān kurvañ śarāṃs tasya maṇḍalāny acaral laghua tathāpi bhīṣmaḥ sudṛḍhaṃ vāsudevadhanaṃjayauc vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiḥ sarvagātreṣu māriṣaa śuśubhāte naravyāghrau tau bhīṣmaśaravikṣatauc govṛṣāv iva nardantau viṣāṇollikhitāṅkitaua punaś cāpi susaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc kṛṣṇayor yudhi saṃrabdho bhīṣmo vyāvārayad diśaḥd pārtho pi samare kruddho bhīṣmasyāvārayad diśaḥd bhīṣmo pi rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pārthasyāvārayad diśaḥa vārṣṇeyaṃ ca śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ kampayām āsa roṣitaḥc muhur abhyutsmayan bhīṣmaḥ prahasya svanavat tadāa tataḥ kṛṣṇas tu samare dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaparākramamc saṃprekṣya ca mahābāhuḥ pārthasya mṛduyuddhatāma bhīṣmaṃ ca śaravarṣāṇi sṛjantam aniśaṃ yudhic pratapantam ivādityaṃ madhyam āsādya senayoḥa varān varān vinighnantaṃ pāṇḍuputrasya sainikānc yugāntam iva kurvāṇaṃ bhīṣmaṃ yaudhiṣṭhire balea amṛṣyamāṇo bhagavān keśavaḥ paravīrahāc acintayad ameyātmā nāsti yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ balama ekāhnā hi raṇe bhīṣmo nāśayed devadānavānc kim u pāṇḍusutān yuddhe sabalān sapadānugāna dravate ca mahat sainyaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥc ete ca kauravās tūrṇaṃ prabhagnān dṛśya somakāne ādravanti raṇe hṛṣṭā harṣayantaḥ pitāmahama so haṃ bhīṣmaṃ nihanmy adya pāṇḍavārthāya daṃśitaḥc bhāram etaṃ vineṣyāmi pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāma arjuno pi śarais tīkṣṇair vadhyamāno hi saṃyugec kartavyaṃ nābhijānāti raṇe bhīṣmasya gauravāta tathā cintayatas tasya bhūya eva pitāmahaḥc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ śarān pārtharathaṃ pratia teṣāṃ bahutvād dhi bhṛśaṃ śarāṇāṃdiśo tha sarvāḥ pihitā babhūvuḥc na cāntarikṣaṃ na diśo na bhūmirna bhāskaro dṛśyata raśmimālīe vavuś ca vātās tumulāḥ sadhūmādiśaś ca sarvāḥ kṣubhitā babhūvuḥa droṇo vikarṇo tha jayadrathaś cabhūriśravāḥ kṛtavarmā kṛpaś cac śrutāyur ambaṣṭhapatiś ca rājāvindānuvindau ca hṛṣṭaḥd itīdam uktvā sa mahānubhāvaḥd sasmāra cakraṃ niśitaṃ purāṇamd sudarśanaṃ cintitamātram evad tasyāgrahastaṃ svayam ārurohaa tataḥ sunābhaṃ vasudevaputraḥsūryaprabhaṃ vajrasamaprabhāvamc dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥa tasya pāñcālaputras tu pratīpam abhidhāvataḥc śitanistriṃśahastasya śarāvaraṇadhāriṇaḥa bāṇavegam atītasya rathābhyāśam upeyuṣaḥc tvaran senāpatiḥ kruddho bibheda gadayā śiraḥa tasya rājan sanistriṃśaṃ suprabhaṃ ca śarāvaramc hatasya patato hastād vegena nyapatad bhuvia taṃ nihatya gadāgreṇa lebhe sa paramaṃ yaśaḥc putraḥ pāñcālarājasya mahātmā bhīmavikramaḥa tasmin hate maheṣvāse rājaputre mahārathec hāhākāro mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣaa tataḥ sāṃyamaniḥ kruddho dṛṣṭvā nihatam ātmajamc abhidudrāva vegena pāñcālyaṃ yuddhadurmadama tau tatra samare vīrau sametau rathināṃ varauc dadṛśuḥ sarvarājānaḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍavās tathāa tataḥ sāṃyamaniḥ kruddhaḥ pārṣataṃ paravīrahāc ājaghāna tribhir bāṇais tottrair iva mahādvipama tathaiva pārṣataṃ śūraṃ śalyaḥ samitiśobhanaḥc ājaghānorasi kruddhas tato yuddham avartata dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa daivam eva paraṃ manye pauruṣād api saṃjayac yat sainyaṃ mama putrasya pāṇḍusainyena vadhyatea nityaṃ hi māmakāṃs tāta hatān eva hi śaṃsasic avyagrāṃś ca prahṛṣṭāṃś ca nityaṃ śaṃsasi pāṇḍavānd vibhagnāṃś ca praṇaṣṭāṃś ca nityaṃ śaṃsasi māmakāna hīnān puruṣakāreṇa māmakān adya saṃjayac patitān pātyamānāṃś ca hatān eva ca śaṃsasia yudhyamānān yathāśakti ghaṭamānāñ jayaṃ pratic pāṇḍavā vijayanty eva jīyante caiva māmakāḥa so haṃ tīvrāṇi duḥkhāni duryodhanakṛtāni cac aśrauṣaṃ satataṃ tāta duḥsahāni bahūni caa tam upāyaṃ na paśyāmi jīyeran yena pāṇḍavāḥc māmakā vā jayaṃ yuddhe prāpnuyur yena saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa kṣayaṃ manuṣyadehānāṃ gajavājirathakṣayamc śṛṇu rājan sthiro bhūtvā tavaivāpanayo mahāna dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu śalyena pīḍito navabhiḥ śaraiḥc pīḍayām āsa saṃkruddho madrādhipatim āyasaiḥa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma pārṣatasya parākramamc nyavārayata yat tūrṇaṃ śalyaṃ samitiśobhanama nāntaraṃ dadṛśe kaś cit tayoḥ saṃrabdhayo raṇec muhūrtam iva tad yuddhaṃ tayoḥ samam ivābhavata tataḥ śalyo mahārāja dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyugec dhanuś ciccheda bhallena pītena niśitena caa athainaṃ śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhāratac giriṃ jalāgame yadvaj jaladā jaladhāriṇaḥa abhimanyus tu saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumne nipīḍitec abhidudrāva vegena madrarājarathaṃ pratia tato madrādhiparathaṃ kārṣṇiḥ prāpyātikopanaḥc ārtāyanim ameyātmā vivyādha viśikhais tribhiḥa tatas tu tāvakā rājan parīpsanto rjuniṃ raṇec madrarājarathaṃ tūrṇaṃ parivāryāvatasthirea duryodhano vikarṇaś ca duḥśāsanaviviṃśatīc durmarṣaṇo duḥsahaś ca citrasenaś ca durmukhaḥa satyavrataś ca bhadraṃ te purumitraś ca bhāratac ete madrādhiparathaṃ pālayantaḥ sthitā raṇea tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc draupadeyābhimanyuś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaud dhārtarāṣṭrān daśa rathān daśaiva pratyavārayana nānārūpāṇi śastrāṇi visṛjanto viśāṃ patec abhyavartanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥe te vai samīyuḥ saṃgrāme rājan durmantrite tavaa tasmin dāśarathe yuddhe vartamāne bhayāvahec tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca prekṣakā rathino bhavana śastrāṇy anekarūpāṇi visṛjanto mahārathāḥc anyonyam abhinardantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrirea te yattā jātasaṃrambhāḥ sarve nyonyaṃ jighāṃsavaḥb anyonyam abhinardantaḥ spardhamānāḥ parasparamb anyonyaspardhayā rājañ jñātayaḥ saṃgatā mithaḥb samāgatā mahārāja jñātayaḥ śastrapāṇayaḥc mahāstrāṇi vimuñcantaḥ samāpetur amarṣaṇāḥa duryodhanas tu saṃkruddho dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāraṇec vivyādha niśitair bāṇaiś caturbhis tvarito bhṛśama durmarṣaṇaś ca viṃśatyā citrasenaś ca pañcabhiḥc durmukho navabhir bāṇair duḥsahaś cāpi saptabhiḥe viviṃśatiḥ pañcabhiś ca tribhir duḥśāsanas tathāf vikarṇo daśabhir bāṇaiḥ purumitraś ca pañcabhiḥf satyavrataḥ saptabhiś ca pārṣataṃ samare hanatf madrādhipas tribhiś caiva vikarṇaḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥa tān pratyavidhyad rājendra pārṣataḥ śatrutāpanaḥc ekaikaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā darśayan pāṇilāghavama satyavrataṃ tu samare purumitraṃ ca bhāratac abhimanyur avidhyat tau daśabhir daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa mādrīputrau tu samare mātulaṃ mātṛnandanauc chādayetāṃ śaravrātais tad adbhutam ivābhavata tataḥ śalyo mahārāja svasrīyau rathināṃ varauc śarair bahubhir ānarchat kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇaue chādyamānau tatas tau tu mādrīputrau na celatuḥa atha duryodhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc vidhitsuḥ kalahasyāntaṃ gadāṃ jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥa tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā kailāsam iva śṛṅgiṇamc bhīmasenaṃ mahābāhuṃ putrās te prādravan bhayāta duryodhanas tu saṃkruddho māgadhaṃ samacodayatc anīkaṃ daśasāhasraṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvināmd gajānīkena sahitas tena rājā suyodhanaḥe māgadhaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā bhīmasenaṃ samabhyayāta āpatantaṃ ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā gajānīkaṃ vṛkodaraḥc gadāpāṇir avārohad rathāt siṃha ivonnadand ghoraḥ pratibhayaś cāsīt pinākīva pinākadhṛkd nirmathyamānāṃ kruddhena pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāma adrisāramayīṃ gurvīṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmc abhyadhāvad gajānīkaṃ vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥa sa gajān gadayā nighnan vyacarat samare balīc bhīmaseno mahābāhuḥ savajra iva vāsavaḥa tasya nādena mahatā manohṛdayakampināb vipradhvastā gajā rājan madaṃ tyaktvā bhayaṃ gatāḥc vyatyaceṣṭanta saṃhatya gajā bhīmasya nardataḥa tatas tu draupadīputrāḥ saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥa pṛṣṭhaṃ bhīmasya rakṣantaḥ śaravarṣeṇa vāraṇānc abhyadhāvanta varṣanto meghā iva girīn yathād nākulis tu śatānīkaḥ samare śatrupūgahāa kṣuraiḥ kṣuraprair bhallaiś ca pītair añjalikair apic pātayantottamāṅgāni pāṇḍavā gajayodhināma śirobhiḥ prapatadbhiś ca bāhubhiś ca vibhūṣitaiḥc aśmavṛṣṭir ivābhāti pāṇibhiś ca sahāṅkuśaiḥa hṛtottamāṅgāḥ skandheṣu gajānāṃ gajayodhinaḥc adṛśyantācalāgreṣu drumā bhagnaśikhā ivaa dhṛṣṭadyumnahatān anyān apaśyāma mahāgajānc patitān pātyamānāṃś ca pārṣatena mahātmanāa māgadho tha mahīpālo gajam airāvatopamamc preṣayām āsa samare saubhadrasya rathaṃ pratia tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya māgadhasya gajottamamc jaghānaikeṣuṇā vīraḥ saubhadraḥ paravīrahāa tasyāvarjitanāgasya kārṣṇiḥ parapuraṃjayaḥc rājño rajatapuṅkhena bhallenāpaharac chiraḥa vigāhya tad gajānīkaṃ bhīmaseno pi pāṇḍavaḥc vyacarat samare mṛdnan gajān indro girīn ivaa ekaprahārābhihatān bhīmasenena kuñjarānc apaśyāma raṇe tasmin girīn vajrahatān ivaa bhagnadantān bhagnakaṭān bhagnasakthāṃś ca vāraṇānc bhagnapṛṣṭhān bhagnakumbhān nihatān parvatopamāna nadataḥ sīdataś cānyān vimukhān samare gajānc vimūtrān bhagnasaṃvignāṃs tathā viśakṛto parāna bhīmasenasya mārgeṣu gatāsūn parvatopamānc apaśyāma hatān nāgān niṣṭanantas tathāparea vamanto rudhiraṃ cānye bhinnakumbhā mahāgajāḥc vihvalanto gatā bhūmiṃ śailā iva dharātaled mārgeṇa gacchamānasya bhīmasyobhayapārśvataḥd dṛśyante patitā nāgā vajreṇeva śiloccayāḥa medorudhiradigdhāṅgo vasāmajjāsamukṣitaḥc vyacarat samare bhīmo daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥa gajānāṃ rudhirāktāṃ tāṃ gadāṃ bibhrad vṛkodaraḥc ghoraḥ pratibhayaś cāsīt pinākīva pinākadhṛka nirmathyamānāḥ kruddhena bhīmasenena dantinaḥc sahasā prādravañ śiṣṭā mṛdnantas tava vāhinīma taṃ hi vīraṃ maheṣvāsāḥ saubhadrapramukhā rathāḥc paryarakṣanta yudhyantaṃ vajrāyudham ivāmarāḥa śoṇitāktāṃ gadāṃ bibhrad ukṣito gajaśoṇitaiḥc kṛtānta iva raudrātmā bhīmaseno vyadṛśyataa vyāyacchamānaṃ gadayā dikṣu sarvāsu bhāratac nṛtyamānam apaśyāma nṛtyantam iva śaṃkarama yamadaṇḍopamāṃ gurvīm indrāśanisamasvanāmc apaśyāma mahārāja raudrāṃ viśasanīṃ gadāma vimiśrāṃ keśamajjābhiḥ pradigdhāṃ rudhireṇa cac pinākam iva rudrasya kruddhasyābhighnataḥ paśūnd keśamajjāsṛgabhyakto raudraṃ bibhrat tadā vapuḥd mārutiḥ śūlahastasya purevābhighnataḥ paśūna yathā paśūnāṃ saṃghātaṃ yaṣṭyā pālaḥ prakālayetc tathā bhīmo gajānīkaṃ gadayā paryakālayata gadayā vadhyamānās te mārgaṇaiś ca samantataḥc svāny anīkāni mṛdnantaḥ prādravan kuñjarās tavaa mahāvāta ivābhrāṇi vidhamitvā sa vāraṇānc atiṣṭhat tumule bhīmaḥ śmaśāna iva śūlabhṛt saṃjaya uvācaa tasmin hate gajānīke putro duryodhanas tavac bhīmasenaṃ ghnatety evaṃ sarvasainyāny acodayata tataḥ sarvāṇy anīkāni tava putrasya śāsanātc abhyadravan bhīmasenaṃ nadantaṃ bhairavān ravāna taṃ balaugham aparyantaṃ devair api durutsahamc āpatantaṃ suduṣpāraṃ samudram iva parvaṇia rathanāgāśvakalilaṃ śaṅkhadundubhināditamc athānantam apāraṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāmc avadhīt tāvakān yodhān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥe pothayan rathavṛndāni vājivṛndāni cābhibhūḥa vyacarat samare bhīmo yugānte pāvako yathāc vinighnan samare sarvān yugānte kālavad vibhuḥa ūruvegena saṃkarṣan rathajālāni pāṇḍavaḥc pramardayan gajān sarvān naḍvalānīva kuñjaraḥa mṛdnan rathebhyo rathino gajebhyo gajayodhinaḥc sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyo bhūmau caiva padātinaḥd gadayā vyadhamat sarvān vāto vṛkṣān ivaujasād bhīmaseno mahābāhus tava putrasya vai baled sā vai majjāvasāmāṃsaiḥ pradigdhā rudhireṇa cad adṛśyata mahāraudrā gadā nāgāśvaghātinīa tatra tatra hataiś cāpi manuṣyagajavājibhiḥc raṇāṅgaṇaṃ tad abhavan mṛtyor āghātasaṃnibhama pinākam iva rudrasya kruddhasyābhighnataḥ paśūnc yamadaṇḍopamām ugrām indrāśanisamasvanāme dadṛśur bhīmasenasya raudrāṃ viśasanīṃ gadāma āvidhyato gadāṃ tasya kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥb gadāmārutavego bhūd viṣphūrjitam ivāśaneḥc babhau rūpaṃ mahāghoraṃ kālasyeva yugakṣayea taṃ tathā mahatīṃ senāṃ drāvayantaṃ punaḥ punaḥc dṛṣṭvā mṛtyum ivāyāntaṃ sarve vimanaso bhavana yato yataḥ prekṣate sma gadām udyamya pāṇḍavaḥc tena tena sma dīryante sarvasainyāni bhārataa pradārayantaṃ sainyāni balaughenāparājitamc grasamānam anīkāni vyāditāsyam ivāntakama taṃ tathā bhīmakarmāṇaṃ pragṛhītamahāgadamc dṛṣṭvā vṛkodaraṃ bhīṣmaḥ sahasaiva samabhyayāta mahatā meghaghoṣeṇa rathenādityavarcasāc chādayañ śaravarṣeṇa parjanya iva vṛṣṭimāna tam āyāntaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā vyāttānanam ivāntakamc bhīṣmaṃ bhīmo mahābāhuḥ pratyudīyād amarṣaṇaḥa tasmin kṣaṇe sātyakiḥ satyasaṃdhaḥśinipravīro bhyapatat pitāmahamc nighnann amitrān dhanuṣā dṛḍhenasa kampayaṃs tava putrasya senāma taṃ yāntam aśvai rajataprakāśaiḥśarān dhamantaṃ dhanuṣā dṛḍhenac nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ tadānīṃsarve gaṇā bhārata ye tvadīyāḥa avidhyad enaṃ niśitaiḥ śarāgrairalambuso rājavarārśyaśṛṅgiḥc taṃ vai caturbhiḥ pratividhya vīronaptā śiner abhyapatad rathenaa anvāgataṃ vṛṣṇivaraṃ niśamyamadhye ripūṇāṃ parivartamānamc prāvartayantaṃ kurupuṃgavāṃś capunaḥ punaś ca
