saṃjaya uvācaa tato bhūriśravā rājan sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc avidhyad bhṛśasaṃkruddhas tottrair iva mahādvipama kauravaṃ sātyakiś caiva śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc avākirad ameyātmā sarvalokasya paśyataḥa tato duryodhano rājā sodaryaiḥ parivāritaḥc saumadattiṃ raṇe yattaḥ samantāt paryavārayata tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve sātyakiṃ rabhasaṃ raṇec parivārya sthitāḥ saṃkhye samantāt sumahaujasaḥa bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddho gadām udyamya bhāratac duryodhanamukhān sarvān putrāṃs te paryavārayatd tathaiva ca sutās tubhyaṃ bhīmasenaṃ mahārathamd duryodhanamukhāḥ sarve samantāt paryavārayana rathair anekasāhasraiḥ krodhāmarṣasamanvitaḥc nandakas tava putras tu bhīmasenaṃ mahābalame vivyādha niśitaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥa duryodhanas tu samare bhīmasenaṃ mahābalamc ājaghānorasi kruddho mārgaṇair niśitais tribhiḥa tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ svarathaṃ sumahābalaḥc āruroha rathaśreṣṭhaṃ viśokaṃ cedam abravīta ete mahārathāḥ śūrā dhārtarāṣṭrā mahābalāḥc mām eva bhṛśasaṃkruddhā hantum abhyudyatā yudhid manorathadrumo smākaṃ cintito bahuvārṣikaḥd saphalaḥ sūta adyeha yo haṃ paśyāmi sodarānd yatrāśoka samutkṣiptā reṇavo rathanemibhiḥd na prayāsyantyantarikṣaṃ hi śaravṛndair digantared tatra tiṣṭhati saṃnaddhaḥ svayaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥd bhrātaraś cāsya saṃnaddhāḥ kulaputrā madotkaṭāḥa etān adya haniṣyāmi paśyatas te na saṃśayaḥc tasmān mamāśvān saṃgrāme yattaḥ saṃyaccha sārathea evam uktvā tataḥ pārthaḥ putraṃ duryodhanaṃ tavac vivyādha daśabhis tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥe nandakaṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntarea taṃ tu duryodhanaḥ ṣaṣṭyā viddhvā bhīmaṃ mahābalamc tribhir anyaiḥ suniśitair viśokaṃ pratyavidhyataa bhīmasya ca raṇe rājan dhanuś ciccheda bhāsvaramc muṣṭideśe śarais tīkṣṇais tribhī rājā hasann ivad ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ putras te prahasann iva bhārataa bhīmas tu prekṣya yantāraṃ viśokaṃ saṃyuge tadāc pīḍitaṃ viśikhais tīkṣṇais tava putreṇa dhanvināa amṛṣyamāṇaḥ saṃkruddho dhanur divyaṃ parāmṛśatc putrasya te mahārāja vadhārthaṃ bharatarṣabhaa samādatta ca saṃrabdhaḥ kṣurapraṃ lomavāhinamc tena ciccheda nṛpater bhīmaḥ kārmukam uttamama so pavidhya dhanuś chinnaṃ krodhena prajvalann ivac anyat kārmukam ādatta satvaraṃ vegavattarama saṃdhatta viśikhaṃ ghoraṃ kālamṛtyusamaprabhamc tenājaghāna saṃkruddho bhīmasenaṃ stanāntarea sa gāḍhaviddho vyathitaḥ syandanopastha āviśatc sa niṣaṇṇo rathopasthe mūrchām abhijagāma haa taṃ dṛṣṭvā vyathitaṃ bhīmam abhimanyupurogamāḥc nāmṛṣyanta maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥa tatas tu tumulāṃ vṛṣṭiṃ śastrāṇāṃ tigmatejasāmc pātayām āsur avyagrāḥ putrasya tava mūrdhania pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc duryodhanaṃ tribhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥa śalyaṃ ca pañcaviṃśatyā śarair vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥc rukmapuṅkhair maheṣvāsaḥ sa viddho vyapayād raṇāta pratyudyayus tato bhīmaṃ tava putrāś caturdaśac senāpatiḥ suṣeṇaś ca jalasaṃdhaḥ sulocanaḥa ugro bhīmaratho bhīmo bhīmabāhur alolupaḥc durmukho duṣpradharṣaś ca vivitsur vikaṭaḥ samaḥa visṛjanto bahūn bāṇān krodhasaṃraktalocanāḥc bhīmasenam abhidrutya vivyadhuḥ sahitā bhṛśama putrāṃs tu tava saṃprekṣya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc sṛkkiṇī vilihan vīraḥ paśumadhye vṛko yathād abhipatya mahābāhur garutmān iva vegitaḥe senāpateḥ kṣurapreṇa śiraś ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥf saṃprahṛṣya ca hṛṣṭātmā tribhir bāṇair mahābhujaḥa jalasaṃdhaṃ vinirbhidya so nayad yamasādanamc suṣeṇaṃ ca tato hatvā preṣayām āsa mṛtyaved vicitraṃ ca tathā hatvā preṣayām āsa mṛtyavea ugrasya saśirastrāṇaṃ śiraś candropamaṃ bhuvic pātayām āsa bhallena kuṇḍalābhyāṃ vibhūṣitama bhīmabāhuṃ ca saptatyā sāśvaketuṃ sasārathimc nināya samare bhīmaḥ paralokāya māriṣaa bhīmaṃ bhīmarathaṃ cobhau bhīmaseno hasann ivac bhrātarau rabhasau rājann anayad yamasādanama tataḥ sulocanaṃ bhīmaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahāmṛdhec miṣatāṃ sarvasainyānām anayad yamasādanama putrās tu tava taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaparākramamc śeṣā ye nye bhavaṃs tatra te bhīmasya bhayārditāḥe vipradrutā diśo rājan vadhyamānā mahātmanāa tato bravīc chāṃtanavaḥ sarvān eva mahārathānc eṣa bhīmo raṇe kruddho dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathāna yathāprāgryān yathājyeṣṭhān yathāśūrāṃś ca saṃgatānc nipātayaty ugradhanvā taṃ pramathnīta pārthivāḥa evam uktās tataḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikāḥc abhyadravanta saṃkruddhā bhīmasenaṃ mahābalama bhagadattaḥ prabhinnena kuñjareṇa viśāṃ patec apatat sahasā tatra yatra bhīmo vyavasthitaḥa āpatann eva ca raṇe bhīmasenaṃ śilāśitaiḥc adṛśyaṃ samare cakre jīmūta iva bhāskarama abhimanyumukhās tatra nāmṛṣyanta mahārathāḥc bhīmasyācchādanaṃ saṃkhye svabāhubalam āśritāḥa ta enaṃ śaravarṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayanc gajaṃ ca śaravṛṣṭyā taṃ bibhidus te samantataḥa sa śastravṛṣṭyābhihataḥ prādravad dviguṇaṃ padamc prāgjyotiṣagajo rājan nānāliṅgaiḥ sutejanaiḥa saṃjātarudhirotpīḍaḥ prekṣaṇīyo bhavad raṇec gabhastibhir ivārkasya saṃsyūto jalado mahāna sa codito madasrāvī bhagadattena vāraṇaḥc abhyadhāvata tān sarvān kālotsṛṣṭa ivāntakaḥe dviguṇaṃ javam āsthāya kampayaṃś caraṇair mahīma tasya tat sumahad rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve mahārathāḥc asahyaṃ manyamānās te nātipramanaso bhavana tatas tu nṛpatiḥ kruddho bhīmasenaṃ stanāntarec ājaghāna naravyāghra śareṇa nataparvaṇāa so tividdho maheṣvāsas tena rājñā mahārathaḥc mūrchayābhiparītāṅgo dhvajayaṣṭim upāśritaḥa tāṃs tu bhītān samālakṣya bhīmasenaṃ ca mūrchitamc nanāda balavan nādaṃ bhagadattaḥ pratāpavānd bhīmo pi labdhasaṃjñas tu adravat sa tato raṇea tato ghaṭotkaco rājan prekṣya bhīmaṃ tathāgatamc saṃkruddho rākṣaso ghoras tatraivāntaradhīyataa sa kṛtvā dāruṇāṃ māyāṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinīmc adṛśyata nimeṣārdhād ghorarūpaṃ samāśritaḥa airāvataṃ samāruhya svayaṃ māyāmayaṃ kṛtamb kailāsagirisaṃkāśaṃ vajrapāṇir ivābhyayātc tasya cānye pi diṅnāgā babhūvur anuyāyinaḥa añjano vāmanaś caiva mahāpadmaś ca suprabhaḥc traya ete mahānāgā rākṣasaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥd madhye trigartāsicn rākṣasyo labhante prasravanti cad kāmarūpadharāś caiva bhavanti bahurūpakāḥd praṇamya vikacaḥ pādāv agṛhṇāt pitaraṃ tadād mātuś ca parameṣvāsas tau ca nāmāsya cakratuḥd ghaṭotkacasyoktapūrvaṃ mātā taṃ pratyabhāṣatad abravīt tena nāmāsya ghaṭotkaca iti sma had sa hi sṛṣṭo maghavatā karṇahetor mahātmanād karṇasyāprativīryasya pratiyoddhā mahārathaḥa mahākāyās tridhā rājan prasravanto madaṃ bahuc tejovīryabalopetā mahābalaparākramāḥd preṣitāś ca mahārāja rākṣasaiś ca caturdiśama ghaṭotkacas tu svaṃ nāgaṃ codayām āsa taṃ tataḥc sagajaṃ bhagadattaṃ tu hantukāmaḥ paraṃtapaḥa te cānye coditā nāgā rākṣasais tair mahābalaiḥc paripetuḥ susaṃrabdhāś caturdaṃṣṭrāś caturdiśame bhagadattasya taṃ nāgaṃ viṣāṇais te bhyapīḍayana saṃpīḍyamānas tair nāgair vedanārtaḥ śarāturaḥc so nadat sumahānādam indrāśanisamasvanamd nyavartata mahāghoṣo bhīmasenaśarārditaḥd mṛditvā sarvasainyāni tava putrasya bhārataa tasya taṃ nadato nādaṃ sughoraṃ bhīmanisvanamc śrutvā bhīṣmo bravīd droṇaṃ rājānaṃ ca suyodhanama eṣa yudhyati saṃgrāme haiḍimbena durātmanāc bhagadatto maheṣvāsaḥ kṛcchreṇa parivartatea rākṣasaś ca mahāmāyaḥ sa ca rājātikopanaḥc tau sametau mahāvīryau kālamṛtyusamāv ubhaua śrūyate hy eṣa hṛṣṭānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahāsvanaḥc hastinaś caiva sumahān bhītasya ruvato dhvaniḥa tatra gacchāma bhadraṃ vo rājānaṃ parirakṣitumc arakṣyamāṇaḥ samare kṣipraṃ prāṇān vimokṣyatea te tvaradhvaṃ mahāvīryāḥ kiṃ cireṇa prayāmahec mahān hi vartate raudraḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥa bhaktaś ca kulaputraś ca śūraś ca pṛtanāpatiḥc yuktaṃ tasya paritrāṇaṃ kartum asmābhir acyutāḥa bhīṣmasya tad vacaḥ śrutvā bhāradvājapurogamāḥc sahitāḥ sarvarājāno bhagadattaparīpsayāe uttamaṃ javam āsthāya prayayur yatra so bhavata tān prayātān samālokya yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥc pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ pṛṣṭhato nuyayuḥ parāna tāny anīkāny athālokya rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavānc nanāda sumahānādaṃ visphoṭam aśaner ivaa tasya taṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā nāgāṃś ca yudhyataḥc bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bhūyo bhāradvājam abhāṣataa na rocate me saṃgrāmo haiḍimbena durātmanāc balavīryasamāviṣṭaḥ sasahāyaś ca sāṃpratama naiṣa śakyo yudhā jetum api vajrabhṛtā svayamc labdhalakṣyaḥ prahārī ca vayaṃ ca śrāntavāhanāḥe pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiś ca divasaṃ kṣatavikṣatāḥf idānīṃ yudhi nirjetuṃ na śakyo sau sa rākṣasaḥf astam abhyeti savitā rātrau yoddhuṃ na śakyatea tan na me rocate yuddhaṃ pāṇḍavair jitakāśibhiḥc ghuṣyatām avahāro dya śvo yotsyāmaḥ paraiḥ sahaa pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā tathā cakruḥ sma kauravāḥc upāyenāpayānaṃ te ghaṭotkacabhayārditāḥa kauraveṣu nivṛtteṣu pāṇḍavā jitakāśinaḥc siṃhanādam akurvanta śaṅkhaveṇusvanaiḥ sahaa evaṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ divasaṃ bharatarṣabhac pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca puraskṛtya ghaṭotkacama kauravās tu tato rājan prayayuḥ śibiraṃ svakamc vrīḍamānā niśākāle pāṇḍaveyaiḥ parājitāḥa śaravikṣatagātrāś ca pāṇḍuputrā mahārathāḥc yuddhe sumanaso bhūtvā śibirāyaiva jagmirea puraskṛtya mahārāja bhīmasenaghaṭotkacauc pūjayantas tadānyonyaṃ mudā paramayā yutāḥa nadanto vividhān nādāṃs tūryasvanavimiśritānc siṃhanādāṃś ca kurvāṇā vimiśrāñ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥa vinadanto mahātmānaḥ kampayantaś ca medinīmc ghaṭṭayantaś ca marmāṇi tava putrasya māriṣad kampayantaś ca putrāṇāṃ tava cetāṃsi bhūmipad putrāś ca tava rājendra tathaiva śaravikṣatāḥe prayātāḥ śibirāyaiva niśākāle paraṃtapāḥa duryodhanas tu nṛpatir dīno bhrātṛvadhena cac muhūrtaṃ cintayām āsa bāṣpaśokasamākulaḥa tataḥ kṛtvā vidhiṃ sarvaṃ śibirasya yathāvidhic pradadhyau śokasaṃtapto bhrātṛvyasanakarśitaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa bhayaṃ me sumahaj jātaṃ vismayaś caiva saṃjayac śrutvā pāṇḍukumārāṇāṃ karma devaiḥ suduṣkarama putrāṇāṃ ca parābhavaṃ śrutvā saṃjaya sarvaśaḥc cintā me mahatī sūta bhaviṣyati kathaṃ tv itia dhruvaṃ viduravākyāni dhakṣyanti hṛdayaṃ mamac yathā hi dṛśyate sarvaṃ daivayogena saṃjayaa yatra bhīṣmamukhāñ śūrān astrajñān yodhasattamānc pāṇḍavānām anīkāni yodhayanti prahāriṇaḥa kenāvadhyā mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍuputrā mahābalāḥc kena dattavarās tāta kiṃ vā jñānaṃ vidanti tee yena kṣayaṃ na gacchanti divi tārāgaṇā ivaa punaḥ punar na mṛṣyāmi hataṃ sainyaṃ sma pāṇḍavaiḥc mayy eva daṇḍaḥ patati daivāt paramadāruṇaḥa yathāvadhyāḥ pāṇḍusutā yathā vadhyāś ca me sutāḥc etan me sarvam ācakṣva yathātattvena saṃjayaa na hi pāraṃ prapaśyāmi duḥkhasyāsya kathaṃ canac samudrasyeva mahato bhujābhyāṃ prataran naraḥa putrāṇāṃ vyasanaṃ manye dhruvaṃ prāptaṃ sudāruṇamc ghātayiṣyati me putrān sarvān bhīmo na saṃśayaḥa na hi paśyāmi taṃ vīraṃ yo me rakṣet sutān raṇec dhruvaṃ vināśaḥ samare putrāṇāṃ mama saṃjayaa tasmān me kāraṇaṃ sūta yuktiṃ caiva viśeṣataḥc pṛcchato dya yathātattvaṃ sarvam ākhyātum arhasia duryodhano pi yac cakre dṛṣṭvā svān vimukhān raṇec bhīṣmadroṇau kṛpaś caiva saubaleyo jayadrathaḥe drauṇir vāpi maheṣvāso vikarṇo vā mahābalaḥa niścayo vāpi kas teṣāṃ tadā hy āsīn mahātmanāmc vimukheṣu mahāprājña mama putreṣu saṃjayad yad vṛttaṃ tatra saṃgrāme tad bhavān vaktum arhati saṃjaya uvācaa śṛṇu rājann avahitaḥ śrutvā caivāvadhārayac naiva mantrakṛtaṃ kiṃ cin naiva māyāṃ tathāvidhāme na vai vibhīṣikāṃ kāṃ cid rājan kurvanti pāṇḍavāḥa yudhyanti te yathānyāyaṃ śaktimantaś ca saṃyugec dharmeṇa sarvakāryāṇi kīrtitānīti bhāratae ārabhante sadā pārthāḥ prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥa na te yuddhān nivartante dharmopetā mahābalāḥc śriyā paramayā yuktā yato dharmas tato jayaḥe tenāvadhyā raṇe pārthā jayayuktāś ca pārthivaa tava putrā durātmānaḥ pāpeṣv abhiratāḥ sadāc niṣṭhurā hīnakarmāṇas tena hīyanti saṃyugea subahūni nṛśaṃsāni putrais tava janeśvarac nikṛtānīha pāṇḍūnāṃ nīcair iva yathā naraiḥa sarvaṃ ca tad anādṛtya putrāṇāṃ tava kilbiṣamc sāpahnavāḥ sadaivāsan pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajae na cainān bahu manyante putrās tava viśāṃ patea tasya pāpasya satataṃ kriyamāṇasya karmaṇaḥc saṃprāptaṃ sumahad ghoraṃ phalaṃ kiṃpākasaṃnibhame sa tad bhuṅkṣva mahārāja saputraḥ sasuhṛjjanaḥa nāvabudhyasi yad rājan vāryamāṇaḥ suhṛjjanaiḥc vidureṇātha bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanāa tathā mayā cāpy asakṛd vāryamāṇo na gṛhṇasic vākyaṃ hitaṃ ca pathyaṃ ca martyaḥ pathyam ivauṣadhame putrāṇāṃ matam āsthāya jitān manyasi pāṇḍavāna śṛṇu bhūyo yathātattvaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasic kāraṇaṃ bharataśreṣṭha pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaṃ pratie tat te haṃ kathayiṣyāmi yathāśrutam ariṃdamaa duryodhanena saṃpṛṣṭa etam arthaṃ pitāmahaḥc dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn raṇe sarvān nirjitān sumahārathāna śokasaṃmūḍhahṛdayo niśākāle sma kauravaḥc pitāmahaṃ mahāprājñaṃ vinayenopagamya hae yad abravīt sutas te sau tan me śṛṇu janeśvara duryodhana uvācaa tvaṃ ca droṇaś ca śalyaś ca kṛpo drauṇis tathaiva cac kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥa bhūriśravā vikarṇaś ca bhagadattaś ca vīryavānc mahārathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥa trayāṇām api lokānāṃ paryāptā iti me matiḥc pāṇḍavānāṃ samastāś ca na tiṣṭhanti parākramea tatra me saṃśayo jātas tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥc yaṃ samāśritya kaunteyā jayanty asmān pade pade bhīṣma uvācaa śṛṇu rājan vaco mahyaṃ yat tvāṃ vakṣyāmi kauravac bahuśaś ca mamokto si na ca me tattvayā kṛtama kriyatāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ śamo bharatasattamac etat kṣamam ahaṃ manye pṛthivyās tava cābhibhoa bhuñjemāṃ pṛthivīṃ rājan bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sukhīc durhṛdas tāpayan sarvān nandayaṃś cāpi bāndhavāna na ca me krośatas tāta śrutavān asi vai purāc tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ yat pāṇḍūn avamanyasea yaś ca hetur avadhyatve teṣām akliṣṭakarmaṇāmc taṃ śṛṇuṣva mahārāja mama kīrtayataḥ prabhoa nāsti lokeṣu tad bhūtaṃ bhavitā no bhaviṣyatic yo jayet pāṇḍavān saṃkhye pālitāñ śārṅgadhanvanāa yat tu me kathitaṃ tāta munibhir bhāvitātmabhiḥc purāṇagītaṃ dharmajña tac chṛṇuṣva yathātathama purā kila surāḥ sarve ṛṣayaś ca samāgatāḥc pitāmaham upāseduḥ parvate gandhamādanea madhye teṣāṃ samāsīnaḥ prajāpatir apaśyatac vimānaṃ jājvalad bhāsā sthitaṃ pravaram ambarea dhyānenāvedya taṃ brahmā kṛtvā ca niyato ñjalimc namaścakāra hṛṣṭātmā paramaṃ parameśvarama ṛṣayas tv atha devāś ca dṛṣṭvā brahmāṇam utthitamc sthitāḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve paśyanto mahad adbhutama yathāvac ca tam abhyarcya brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥc jagāda jagataḥ sraṣṭā paraṃ paramadharmavita viśvāvasur viśvamūrtir viśveśoviṣvakseno viśvakarmā vaśī cac viśveśvaro vāsudevo si tasmādyogātmānaṃ daivataṃ tvām upaimid viśvāvāso viśvamūrtir viṣvakseno janārdanaḥd viśvakartā viśvapatir devadeva jagatpated yogeśvara namaste stu saṃsārārṇavatāraṇaa jaya viśva mahādeva jaya lokahite ratac jaya yogīśvara vibho jaya yogaparāvaraa padmagarbha viśālākṣa jaya lokeśvareśvarac bhūtabhavyabhavan nātha jaya saumyātmajātmajaa asaṃkhyeyaguṇājeya jaya sarvaparāyaṇac nārāyaṇa suduṣpāra jaya śārṅgadhanurdharaa sarvaguhyaguṇopeta viśvamūrte nirāmayac viśveśvara mahābāho jaya lokārthatatparaa mahoraga varāhādya harikeśa vibho jayac harivāsa viśāmīśa viśvāvāsāmitāvyayaa vyaktāvyaktāmitasthāna niyatendriya sendriyac asaṃkhyeyātmabhāvajña jaya gambhīra kāmadaa ananta viditaprajña nityaṃ bhūtavibhāvanac kṛtakārya kṛtaprajña dharmajña vijayājayaa guhyātman sarvabhūtātman sphuṭasaṃbhūtasaṃbhavac bhūtārthatattva lokeśa jaya bhūtavibhāvanaa ātmayone mahābhāga kalpasaṃkṣepatatparac udbhāvana manodbhāva jaya brahmajanapriyaa nisargasargābhirata kāmeśa parameśvarac amṛtodbhava sadbhāva yugāgne vijayapradaa prajāpatipate deva padmanābha mahābalac ātmabhūta mahābhūta karmātmañ jaya karmadaa pādau tava dharā devī diśo bāhur divaṃ śiraḥc mūrtis te haṃ surāḥ kāyaś candrādityau ca cakṣuṣīa balaṃ tapaś ca satyaṃ ca dharmaḥ kāmātmajaḥ prabhoc tejo gniḥ pavanaḥ śvāsa āpas te svedasaṃbhavāḥa aśvinau śravaṇau nityaṃ devī jihvā sarasvatīc vedāḥ saṃskāraniṣṭhā hi tvayīdaṃ jagad āśritama na saṃkhyāṃ na parīmāṇaṃ na tejo na parākramamc na balaṃ yogayogīśa jānīmas te na saṃbhavama tvadbhaktiniratā deva niyamais tvā samāhitāḥc arcayāmaḥ sadā viṣṇo parameśaṃ maheśvarama ṛṣayo devagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥc piśācā mānuṣāś caiva mṛgapakṣisarīsṛpāḥa evamādi mayā sṛṣṭaṃ pṛthivyāṃ tvatprasādajamc padmanābha viśālākṣa kṛṣṇa duḥsvapnanāśanaa tvaṃ gatiḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tvaṃ netā tvaṃ jaganmukhamc tvatprasādena deveśa sukhino vibudhāḥ sadāa pṛthivī nirbhayā deva tvatprasādāt sadābhavatc tasmād bhava viśālākṣa yaduvaṃśavivardhanaḥa dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya daiteyānāṃ vadhāya cac jagato dhāraṇārthāya vijñāpyaṃ kuru me prabhoa yad etat paramaṃ guhyaṃ tvatprasādamayaṃ vibhoc vāsudeva tad etat te mayodgītaṃ yathātathama sṛṣṭvā saṃkarṣaṇaṃ devaṃ svayam ātmānam ātmanāc kṛṣṇa tvam ātmanāsrākṣīḥ pradyumnaṃ cātmasaṃbhavama pradyumnāc cāniruddhaṃ tvaṃ yaṃ vidur viṣṇum avyayamc aniruddho sṛjan māṃ vai brahmāṇaṃ lokadhāriṇama vāsudevamayaḥ so haṃ tvayaivāsmi vinirmitaḥb vāsudeveti taṃ vidyād yenāhaṃ nirmitaḥ prabhob tasmād yācāmi lokeśa caturātmānam ātmanāc vibhajya bhāgaśo tmānaṃ vraja mānuṣatāṃ vibhoa tatrāsuravadhaṃ kṛtvā sarvalokasukhāya vaic dharmaṃ sthāpya yaśaḥ prāpya yogaṃ prāpsyasi tattvataḥa tvāṃ hi brahmarṣayo loke devāś cāmitavikramac tais taiś ca nāmabhir bhaktā gāyanti paramātmakamd sarvabhūteśvaraṃ devaṃ yogaṃ yogeśvaraṃ prabhuma sthitāś ca sarve tvayi bhūtasaṃghāḥkṛtvāśrayaṃ tvāṃ varadaṃ subāhoc anādimadhyāntam apārayogaṃlokasya setuṃ pravadanti viprāḥ bhīṣma uvācaa tataḥ sa bhagavān devo lokānāṃ parameśvaraḥc brahmāṇaṃ pratyuvācedaṃ snigdhagambhīrayā girāa viditaṃ tāta yogān me sarvam etat tavepsitamc tathā tad bhavitety uktvā tatraivāntaradhīyataa tato devarṣigandharvā vismayaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥc kautūhalaparāḥ sarve pitāmaham athābruvana ko nv ayaṃ yo bhagavatā praṇamya vinayād vibhoc vāgbhiḥ stuto variṣṭhābhiḥ śrotum icchāma taṃ vayama evam uktas tu bhagavān pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥc devabrahmarṣigandharvān sarvān madhurayā girāa yat tatparaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca bhavitavyaṃ ca yat paramc bhūtātmā yaḥ prabhuś caiva brahma yac ca paraṃ padama tenāsmi kṛtasaṃvādaḥ prasannena surarṣabhāḥc jagato nugrahārthāya yācito me jagatpatiḥa mānuṣaṃ lokam ātiṣṭha vāsudeva iti śrutaḥc asurāṇāṃ vadhārthāya saṃbhavasva mahītalec   vāsudeva iti śrutaḥc vāsudevagṛhe sākṣāt  a saṃgrāme nihatā ye te daityadānavarākṣasāḥc ta ime nṛṣu saṃbhūtā ghorarūpā mahābalāḥa teṣāṃ vadhārthaṃ bhagavān nareṇa sahito vaśīc mānuṣīṃ yonim āsthāya cariṣyati mahītalea naranārāyaṇau yau tau purāṇāv ṛṣisattamauc sahitau mānuṣe loke saṃbhūtāv amitadyutīa ajeyau samare yattau sahitāv amarair apic mūḍhās tv etau na jānanti naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣīd jagataś cāgrajau vidmas tato devau surarṣabhāḥa tasyāham ātmajo brahmā sarvasya jagataḥ patiḥc vāsudevo rcanīyo vaḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥa tathā manuṣyo yam iti kadā cit surasattamāḥc nāvajñeyo mahāvīryaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥd etat puruṣasaṃjñaṃ vai purāṇaṃ rūpam uttamama etat paramakaṃ guhyam etat paramakaṃ padamc etat paramakaṃ brahma etat paramakaṃ yaśaḥa etad akṣaram avyaktam etat tac chāśvataṃ mahatc etat puruṣasaṃjñaṃ vai gīyate jñāyate na caa etat paramakaṃ teja etat paramakaṃ sukhamc etat paramakaṃ satyaṃ kīrtitaṃ viśvakarmaṇāa tasmāt sarvaiḥ suraiḥ sendrair lokaiś cāmitavikramaḥc nāvajñeyo vāsudevo mānuṣo yam iti prabhuḥa yaś ca mānuṣamātro yam iti brūyāt sumandadhīḥc hṛṣīkeśam avajñānāt tam āhuḥ puruṣādhamama yoginaṃ taṃ mahātmānaṃ praviṣṭaṃ mānuṣīṃ tanumc avamanyed vāsudevaṃ tam āhus tāmasaṃ janāḥa devaṃ carācarātmānaṃ śrīvatsāṅkaṃ suvarcasamc padmanābhaṃ na jānāti tam āhus tāmasaṃ janāḥa kirīṭakaustubhadharaṃ mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaramc avajānan mahātmānaṃ ghore tamasi majjatia evaṃ viditvā tattvārthaṃ lokānām īśvareśvaraḥc vāsudevo namaskāryaḥ sarvalokaiḥ surottamāḥa evam uktvā sa bhagavān sarvān devagaṇān purāc visṛjya sarvalokātmā jagāma bhavanaṃ svakama tato devāḥ sagandharvā munayo psaraso pi cac kathāṃ tāṃ brahmaṇā gītāṃ śrutvā prītā divaṃ yayuḥa etac chrutaṃ mayā tāta ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanāmc vāsudevaṃ kathayatāṃ samavāye purātanama jāmadagnyasya rāmasya mārkaṇḍeyasya dhīmataḥc vyāsanāradayoś cāpi śrutaṃ śrutaviśāradaa etam arthaṃ ca vijñāya śrutvā ca prabhum avyayamc vāsudevaṃ mahātmānaṃ lokānām īśvareśvarama yasyāsāv ātmajo brahmā sarvasya jagataḥ pitāc kathaṃ na vāsudevo yam arcyaś cejyaś ca mānavaiḥa vārito si purā tāta munibhir vedapāragaiḥc mā gaccha saṃyugaṃ tena vāsudevena dhīmatāe mā pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham iti tac ca mohān na budhyasea manye tvāṃ rākṣasaṃ krūraṃ tathā cāsi tamovṛtaḥc yasmād dviṣasi govindaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayame naranārāyaṇau devau nānyo dviṣyād dhi mānavaḥa tasmād bravīmi te rājann eṣa vai śāśvato vyayaḥc sarvalokamayo nityaḥ śāstā dhātā dharo dhruvaḥa lokān dhārayate yas trīṃś carācaraguruḥ prabhuḥc yoddhā jayaś ca jetā ca sarvaprakṛtir īśvaraḥa rājan sattvamayo hy eṣa tamorāgavivarjitaḥc yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato dharmo yato dharmas tato jayaḥa tasya māhātmyayogena yogenātmana eva cac dhṛtāḥ pāṇḍusutā rājañ jayaś caiṣāṃ bhaviṣyatia śreyoyuktāṃ sadā buddhiṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ dadhāti yaḥc balaṃ caiva raṇe nityaṃ bhayebhyaś caiva rakṣatia sa eṣa śāśvato devaḥ sarvaguhyamayaḥ śivaḥc vāsudeva iti jñeyo yan māṃ pṛcchasi bhārataa brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaiḥc sevyate bhyarcyate caiva nityayuktaiḥ svakarmabhiḥa dvāparasya yugasyānte ādau kaliyugasya cac sātvataṃ vidhim āsthāya gītaḥ saṃkarṣaṇena yaḥa sa eṣa sarvāsuramartyalokaṃsamudrakakṣyāntaritāḥ purīś cac yuge yuge mānuṣaṃ caiva vāsaṃpunaḥ punaḥ sṛjate vāsudevaḥ duryodhana uvācaa vāsudevo mahad bhūtaṃ sarvalokeṣu kathyatec tasyāgamaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ ca jñātum icche pitāmaha bhīṣma uvācaa vāsudevo mahad bhūtaṃ saṃbhūtaṃ saha daivataiḥc na paraṃ puṇḍarīkākṣād dṛśyate bharatarṣabhad śrutaṃ me tāta rāmasya jāmadagnyasya jalpataḥd nāradasya ca devarṣeḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya cad asito devalaś cāpi vālakhilyās tapodhanāḥe mārkaṇḍeyaś ca govindaṃ kathayaty adbhutaṃ mahata sarvabhūtāni bhūtātmā mahātmā puruṣottamaḥc āpo vāyuś ca tejaś ca trayam etad akalpayata sa sṛṣṭvā pṛthivīṃ devaḥ sarvalokeśvaraḥ prabhuḥc apsu vai śayanaṃ cakre mahātmā puruṣottamaḥe sarvatoyamayo devo yogāt suṣvāpa tatra haa mukhataḥ so gnim asṛjat prāṇād vāyum athāpi cac sarasvatīṃ ca vedāṃś ca manasaḥ sasṛje cyutaḥa eṣa lokān sasarjādau devāṃś carṣigaṇaiḥ sahac nidhanaṃ caiva mṛtyuṃ ca prajānāṃ prabhavo vyayaḥa eṣa dharmaś ca dharmajño varadaḥ sarvakāmadaḥc eṣa kartā ca kāryaṃ ca pūrvadevaḥ svayaṃprabhuḥa bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca pūrvam etad akalpayatc ubhe saṃdhye diśaḥ khaṃ ca niyamaṃ ca janārdanaḥa ṛṣīṃś caiva hi govindas tapaś caivānu kalpayatc sraṣṭāraṃ jagataś cāpi mahātmā prabhur avyayaḥa agrajaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃkarṣaṇam akalpayatb tasmān nārāyaṇo jajñe devadevaḥ sanātanaḥb nābhau padmaṃ babhūvāsya sarvalokasya saṃbhavaḥb tasmāt pitāmaho jātas tasmāj jātās tv imāḥ prajāḥc śeṣaṃ cākalpayad devam anantam iti yaṃ viduḥa yo dhārayati bhūtāni dharāṃ cemāṃ saparvatāmc dhyānayogena viprāś ca taṃ vadanti mahaujasama karṇasrotodbhavaṃ cāpi madhuṃ nāma mahāsuramc tam ugram ugrakarmāṇam ugrāṃ buddhiṃ samāsthitamd harantaṃ brahmaṇo vedāñ jaghāna brahmaṇaḥ pitāe brahmaṇo pacitiṃ kurvañ jaghāna puruṣottamaḥa tasya tāta vadhād eva devadānavamānavāḥc madhusūdanam ity āhur ṛṣayaś ca janārdaname varāhaś caiva siṃhaś ca trivikramagatiḥ prabhuḥa eṣa mātā pitā caiva sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ hariḥc paraṃ hi puṇḍarīkākṣān na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyatia mukhato sṛjad brāhmaṇān bāhubhyāṃ kṣatriyāṃs tathāc vaiśyāṃś cāpy ūruto rājañ śūdrān padbhyāṃ tathaiva cae tapasā niyato devo nidhānaṃ sarvadehināma brahmabhūtam amāvāsyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tathaiva cac yogabhūtaṃ paricaran keśavaṃ mahad āpnuyāta keśavaḥ paramaṃ tejaḥ sarvalokapitāmahaḥc evam āhur hṛṣīkeśaṃ munayo vai narādhipaa evam enaṃ vijānīhi ācāryaṃ pitaraṃ gurumc kṛṣṇo yasya prasīdeta lokās tenākṣayā jitāḥa yaś caivainaṃ bhayasthāne keśavaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajetc sadā naraḥ paṭhaṃś cedaṃ svastimān sa sukhī bhaveta ye ca kṛṣṇaṃ prapadyante te na muhyanti mānavāḥc bhaye mahati ye magnāḥ pāti nityaṃ janārdanaḥa etad yudhiṣṭhiro jñātvā yāthātathyena bhāratac sarvātmanā mahātmānaṃ keśavaṃ jagadīśvarame prapannaḥ śaraṇaṃ rājan yogānām īśvaraṃ prabhum bhīṣma uvācaa śṛṇu cedaṃ mahārāja brahmabhūtastavaṃ mamac brahmarṣibhiś ca devaiś ca yaḥ purā kathito bhuvia sādhyānām api devānāṃ devadeveśvaraḥ prabhuḥc lokabhāvanabhāvajña iti tvāṃ nārado bravīte bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyo bhyuvāca haa yajñānāṃ caiva yajñaṃ tvāṃ tapaś ca tapasām apic devānām api devaṃ ca tvām āha bhagavān bhṛguḥe purāṇe bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ viṣṇo bhūtapateti vaia vāsudevo vasūnāṃ tvaṃ śakraṃ sthāpayitā tathāc devadevo si devānām iti dvaipāyano bravīta pūrve prajānisargeṣu dakṣam āhuḥ prajāpatimc sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānām aṅgirās tvāṃ tato bravīta avyaktaṃ te śarīrotthaṃ vyaktaṃ te manasi sthitamc devā vāksaṃbhavāś ceti devalas tv asito bravīta śirasā te divaṃ vyāptaṃ bāhubhyāṃ pṛthivī dhṛtāc jaṭharaṃ te trayo lokāḥ puruṣo si sanātanaḥa evaṃ tvām abhijānanti tapasā bhāvitā narāḥc ātmadarśanatṛptānām ṛṣīṇāṃ cāpi sattamaḥa rājarṣīṇām udārāṇām āhaveṣv anivartināmc sarvadharmapradhānānāṃ tvaṃ gatir madhusūdanad iti nityaṃ yogavidbhir bhagavān puruṣottamaḥd sanatkumārapramukhaiḥ stūyate bhyarcyate hariḥd etad dvaipāyanaḥ prāha stutvā vai puruṣottamama eṣa te vistaras tāta saṃkṣepaś ca prakīrtitaḥc keśavasya yathātattvaṃ suprīto bhava keśaved purāṇapuruṣasyeha yadarthaṃ nṛṣu saṃbhavaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa puṇyaṃ śrutvaitad ākhyānaṃ mahārāja sutas tavac keśavaṃ bahu mene sa pāṇḍavāṃś ca mahārathāna tam abravīn mahārāja bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punaḥc māhātmyaṃ te śrutaṃ rājan keśavasya mahātmanaḥd arjunasya māhātmyaṃ hi kathitaṃ tattvato mayād na jeṣyāmi mahāyuddhe vicarantaṃ naraṃ kva citd nārāyaṇaṃ ca saṃgrāme avadhyau tau yataḥ smṛtaud dharmarājaś ca bhīmaś ca mādrīputraś ca pāṃḍavaud ete py avadhyāḥ kathitāḥ purāṇe paramarṣiṇāa narasya ca yathātattvaṃ yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasic yadarthaṃ nṛṣu saṃbhūtau naranārāyaṇāv ubhaua avadhyau ca yathā vīrau saṃyugeṣv aparājitauc yathā ca pāṇḍavā rājann agamyā yudhi kasya cita prītimān hi dṛḍhaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍaveṣu yaśasviṣuc tasmād bravīmi rājendra śamo bhavatu pāṇḍavaiḥa pṛthivīṃ bhuṅkṣva sahito bhrātṛbhir balibhir vaśīc naranārāyaṇau devāv avajñāya naśiṣyasid na cet kartāsi vacanaṃ saṃdigdhaṃ na tariṣyasia evam uktvā tava pitā tūṣṇīm āsīd viśāṃ patec vyasarjayac ca rājānaṃ śayanaṃ ca viveśa haa rājāpi śibiraṃ prāyāt praṇipatya mahātmanec śiśye ca śayane śubhre tāṃ rātriṃ bharatarṣabha saṃjaya uvācaa vyuṣitāyāṃ ca śarvaryām udite ca divākarec ubhe sene mahārāja yuddhāyaiva samīyatuḥd tasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ niryayuḥ kurupuṃgavāḥd puraskṛtya mahātmānaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yudhia abhyadhāvaṃś ca saṃkruddhāḥ parasparajigīṣavaḥc te sarve sahitā yuddhe samālokya parasparama pāṇḍavā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca rājan durmantrite tavac vyūhau ca vyūhya saṃrabdhāḥ saṃprayuddhāḥ prahāriṇaḥa arakṣan makaravyūhaṃ bhīṣmo rājan samantataḥc tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājann arakṣan vyūham ātmanaḥd ajātaśatruḥ śatrūṇāṃ manāṃsi samakampayatd śyenavad vyūhya taṃ vyūhaṃ dhaumyasya vacanāt svayamd sa hi tasya suvijñāta agnicityeṣu bhāratad makaras tu mahāvyūhas tava putrasya dhīmataḥd svayaṃ sarveṇa sainyena droṇenānumatas tadād yathāvyūhaṃ śāṃtanavaḥ so nvavartata tat punaḥa sa niryayau rathānīkaṃ pitā devavratas tavac mahatā rathavaṃśena saṃvṛto rathināṃ varaḥa itaretaram anvīyur yathābhāgam avasthitāḥc rathinaḥ pattayaś caiva dantinaḥ sādinas tathāa tān dṛṣṭvā prodyatān saṃkhye pāṇḍavāś ca yaśasvinaḥc śyenena vyūharājena tenājayyena saṃyugea aśobhata mukhe tasya bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc netre śikhaṇḍī durdharṣo dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥa śīrṣaṃ tasyābhavad vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥc vidhunvan gāṇḍivaṃ pārtho grīvāyām abhavat tadāa akṣauhiṇyā samagrā yā vāmapakṣo bhavat tadāc mahātmā drupadaḥ śrīmān saha putreṇa saṃyugea dakṣiṇaś cābhavat pakṣaḥ kaikeyo kṣauhiṇīpatiḥc pṛṣṭhato draupadeyāś ca saubhadraś cāpi vīryavāna pṛṣṭhe samabhavac chrīmān svayaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc bhrātṛbhyāṃ sahito dhīmān yamābhyāṃ cāruvikramaḥa praviśya tu raṇe bhīmo makaraṃ mukhatas tadāc bhīṣmam āsādya saṃgrāme chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥa tato bhīṣmo mahāstrāṇi pātayām āsa bhāratac mohayan pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ vyūḍhaṃ sainyaṃ mahāhavea saṃmuhyati tadā sainye tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥc bhīṣmaṃ śarasahasreṇa vivyādha raṇamūrdhania parisaṃvārya cāstrāṇi bhīṣmamuktāni saṃyugec svenānīkena hṛṣṭena yuddhāya samavasthitaḥa tato duryodhano rājā bhāradvājam abhāṣatac pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭvā vadhaṃ ghoraṃ balasya balināṃ varaḥe bhrātṝṇāṃ ca vadhaṃ yuddhe smaramāṇo mahārathaḥa ācārya satataṃ tvaṃ hi hitakāmo mamānaghac vayaṃ hi tvāṃ samāśritya bhīṣmaṃ caiva pitāmahama devān api raṇe jetuṃ prārthayāmo na saṃśayaḥc kim u pāṇḍusutān yuddhe hīnavīryaparākramānd sa tathā kuru bhadraṃ te yathā vadhyanti pāṇḍavāḥa evam uktas tato droṇas tava putreṇa māriṣab uvāca tatra rājānaṃ saṃkruddha iva niḥśvasanb bāliśas tvaṃ na jānīṣe pāṇḍavānāṃ parākramamb na śakyā hi yathā jetuṃ pāṇḍavā hi mahābalāḥb yathābalaṃ yathāvīryaṃ karma kuryām ahaṃ hi teb ity uktvā te sutaṃ rājann abhyapadyata vāhinīmc abhinat pāṇḍavānīkaṃ prekṣamāṇasya sātyakeḥa sātyakis tu tadā droṇaṃ vārayām āsa bhāratac tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇama śaineyaṃ tu raṇe kruddho bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc avidhyan niśitair bāṇair jatrudeśe hasann ivaa bhīmasenas tataḥ kruddho bhāradvājam avidhyatac saṃrakṣan sātyakiṃ rājan droṇāc chastrabhṛtāṃ varāta tato droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca tathā śalyaś ca māriṣac bhīmasenaṃ raṇe kruddhāś chādayāṃ cakrire śaraiḥa tatrābhimanyuḥ saṃkruddho draupadeyāś ca māriṣac vivyadhur niśitair bāṇaiḥ sarvāṃs tān udyatāyudhāna bhīṣmadroṇau ca saṃkruddhāv āpatantau mahābalauc pratyudyayau śikhaṇḍī tu maheṣvāso mahāhavea pragṛhya balavad vīro dhanur jaladanisvanamc abhyavarṣac charais tūrṇaṃ chādayāno divākarama śikhaṇḍinaṃ samāsādya bharatānāṃ pitāmahaḥc avarjayata saṃgrāme strītvaṃ tasyānusaṃsmarana tato droṇo mahārāja abhyadravata taṃ raṇec rakṣamāṇas tato bhīṣmaṃ tava putreṇa coditaḥa śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya droṇaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varamc avarjayata saṃgrāme yugāntāgnim ivolbaṇama tato balena mahatā putras tava viśāṃ patec jugopa bhīṣmam āsādya prārthayāno mahad yaśaḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan puraskṛtya dhanaṃjayamc bhīṣmam evābhyavartanta jaye kṛtvā dṛḍhāṃ matima tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ devānāṃ dānavair ivac jayaṃ ca kāṅkṣatāṃ nityaṃ yaśaś ca paramādbhutam saṃjaya uvācaa akarot tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadāc bhīmasenabhayād icchan putrāṃs tārayituṃ tavaa pūrvāhṇe tan mahāraudraṃ rājñāṃ yuddham avartatac kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca mukhyaśūravināśanama tasminn ākulasaṃgrāme vartamāne mahābhayec abhavat tumulaḥ śabdaḥ saṃspṛśan gaganaṃ mahata nadadbhiś ca mahānāgair heṣamāṇaiś ca vājibhiḥc bherīśaṅkhaninādaiś ca tumulaḥ samapadyataa yuyutsavas te vikrāntā vijayāya mahābalāḥc anyonyam abhigarjanto goṣṭheṣv iva maharṣabhāḥa śirasāṃ pātyamānānāṃ samare niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc aśmavṛṣṭir ivākāśe babhūva bharatarṣabhaa kuṇḍaloṣṇīṣadhārīṇi jātarūpojjvalāni cac patitāni sma dṛśyante śirāṃsi bharatarṣabhaa viśikhonmathitair gātrair bāhubhiś ca sakārmukaiḥc sahastābharaṇaiś cānyair abhavac chāditā mahīa kavacopahitair gātrair hastaiś ca samalaṃkṛtaiḥc mukhaiś ca candrasaṃkāśai raktāntanayanaiḥ śubhaiḥa gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ sarvagātraiś ca bhūpatec āsīt sarvā samākīrṇā muhūrtena vasuṃdharāa rajomeghaiś ca tumulaiḥ śastravidyutprakāśitaiḥc āyudhānāṃ ca nirghoṣaḥ stanayitnusamo bhavata sa saṃprahāras tumulaḥ kaṭukaḥ śoṇitodakaḥc prāvartata kurūṇāṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārataa tasmin mahābhaye ghore tumule lomaharṣaṇec vavarṣuḥ śaravarṣāṇi kṣatriyā yuddhadurmadāḥa krośanti kuñjarās tatra śaravarṣapratāpitāḥc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca saṃyuge bharatottamad saṃrabdhānāṃ ca vīrāṇāṃ dhīrāṇām amitaujasāmd dhanurjyātalaśabdena na prājñāyata kiṃ canad utthiteṣu kabandheṣu sarvataḥ śoṇitodaked samare paryadhāvanta nṛpā ripuvadhodyatāḥd śaraśaktigadābhis te khaḍgaiś cāmitatejasaḥd nijaghnuḥ samare śūrās te nyonyaṃ ca paraṃtapad babhramuḥ kuñjarāś cātra śarair viddhā niraṅkuśāḥe aśvāś ca paryadhāvanta hatārohā diśo daśaa utpatya nipatanty anye śaraghātaprapīḍitāḥc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca yodhānāṃ bharatarṣabhad bahūnām uttamāṅgānāṃ kārmukāṇāṃ tathaiva cad gadānāṃ parighāṇāṃ ca hastānāṃ corubhiḥ sahad pādānāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca keyūrāṇāṃ ca saṃghaśaḥd rāśayaḥ sma pradṛśyante bhīṣmabhīmaparākramea aśvānāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca rathānāṃ cātivartatāmc saṃghātāḥ sma pradṛśyante tatra tatra viśāṃ patea gadābhir asibhiḥ prāsair bāṇaiś ca nataparvabhiḥc jaghnuḥ parasparaṃ tatra kṣatriyāḥ kālacoditāḥa apare bāhubhir vīrā niyuddhakuśalā yudhic bahudhā samasajjanta āyasaiḥ parighair ivaa muṣṭibhir jānubhiś caiva talaiś caiva viśāṃ patec anyonyaṃ jaghnire vīrās tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahad patitaiḥ pātyamānaiś ca viceṣṭadbhiś ca bhūtaled ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe tatra tatra janeśvarad duryodhanamate ghore akṣadyūtābhidevaned bhīṣme yudhi parākrānte bhīmasenena bhāratad prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīd madhye ca mahatī senā keśaśaivalaśādvalād hatārohā hayā rājan rathino virathā apid vicerus tatra saṃgrāme nistriṃśavaradhāriṇaḥa virathā rathinaś cātra nistriṃśavaradhāriṇaḥc anyonyam abhidhāvanta parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥa tato duryodhano rājā kaliṅgair bahubhir vṛtaḥc puraskṛtya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ pāṇḍavān abhyavartataa tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parivārya vṛkodaramc bhīṣmam abhyadravan kruddhā raṇe rabhasavāhanāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmeṇa saṃsaktān bhrātṝn anyāṃś ca pārthivānc tam abhyadhāvad gāṅgeyam udyatāstro dhanaṃjayaḥa pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaṃ dhanuṣo gāṇḍivasya cac dhvajaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā pārthasya sarvān no bhayam āviśatd siṃhalāṅgūlam ākāśe jvalantam iva parvatama asajjamānaṃ vṛkṣeṣu dhūmaketum ivotthitamc bahuvarṇaṃ ca citraṃ ca divyaṃ vānaralakṣaṇame apaśyāma mahārāja dhvajaṃ gāṇḍivadhanvanaḥa vidyutaṃ meghamadhyasthāṃ bhrājamānām ivāmbarec dadṛśur gāṇḍivaṃ yodhā rukmapṛṣṭhaṃ mahārathea aśuśruma bhṛśaṃ cāsya śakrasyevābhigarjataḥc sughoraṃ talayoḥ śabdaṃ nighnatas tava vāhinīma caṇḍavāto yathā meghaḥ savidyutstanayitnumānc diśaḥ saṃplāvayan sarvāḥ śaravarṣaiḥ samantataḥa abhyadhāvata gāṅgeyaṃ bhairavāstro dhanaṃjayaḥc diśaṃ prācīṃ pratīcīṃ ca na jānīmo stramohitāḥa kāṃdigbhūtāḥ śrāntapatrā hatāstrā hatacetasaḥc anyonyam abhisaṃśliṣya yodhās te bharatarṣabhaa bhīṣmam evābhilīyanta saha sarvais tavātmajaiḥc teṣām ārtāyanam abhūd bhīṣmaḥ śaṃtanavo raṇea samutpatanta vitrastā rathebhyo rathinas tadāc sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyo bhūmau cāpi padātayaḥd gajebhyo gajayodhāś ca vitrastā bhayamohitāḥd vihvalāḥ pratyadṛśyanta na jānanti diśo nṛpaa śrutvā gāṇḍīvanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥc sarvasainyāni bhītāni vyavalīyanta bhārataa atha kāmbojamukhyais tu bṛhadbhiḥ śīghragāmibhiḥc gopānāṃ bahusāhasrair balair govāsano vṛtaḥd tataḥ kāmbojamukhyāś ca te haṃsapathakarṇikāḥd gopāsanabalaughāś ca gopāsanapatis tathāa madrasauvīragāndhārais trigartaiś ca viśāṃ patec sarvakāliṅgamukhyaiś ca kaliṅgādhipatir vṛtaḥa nāgā naragaṇaughāś ca duḥśāsanapuraḥsarāḥc jayadrathaś ca nṛpatiḥ sahitaḥ sarvarājabhiḥa hayārohavarāś caiva tava putreṇa coditāḥc caturdaśa sahasrāṇi saubalaṃ paryavārayana tatas te sahitāḥ sarve vibhaktarathavāhanāḥc pāṇḍavān samare jagmus tāvakā bharatarṣabhad cedikāśipadātaiś ca rathaiḥ pāñcālasṛñjayaiḥd pāṇḍavāḥ sahitāḥ sarve dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥd tāvakān samare jagmur dharmaputreṇa coditāḥa rathibhir vāraṇair aśvaiḥ padātaiś ca samīritamc ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe mahābhrasadṛśaṃ rajaḥa tomaraprāsanārācagajāśvarathayodhināmc balena mahatā bhīṣmaḥ samasajjat kirīṭināa āvantyaḥ kāśirājena bhīmasenena saindhavaḥc ajātaśatrur madrāṇām ṛṣabheṇa yaśasvināe sahaputraḥ sahāmātyaḥ śalyena samasajjataa vikarṇaḥ sahadevena citrasenaḥ śikhaṇḍināc matsyā duryodhanaṃ jagmuḥ śakuniṃ ca viśāṃ patea drupadaś cekitānaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc droṇena samasajjanta saputreṇa mahātmanāe kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca dhṛṣṭaketum abhidrutaua evaṃ prajavitāśvāni bhrāntanāgarathāni cac sainyāni samasajjanta prayuddhāni samantataḥa nirabhre vidyutas tīvrā diśaś ca rajasāvṛtāḥc prādurāsan maholkāś ca sanirghātā viśāṃ patea pravavau ca mahāvātaḥ pāṃsuvarṣaṃ papāta cac nabhasy antardadhe sūryaḥ sainyena rajasāvṛtaḥa pramohaḥ sarvasattvānām atīva samapadyatab prakāśaṃ cakrur ākāśa udyatāsibhir uttamaiḥc rajasā cābhibhūtānām astrajālaiś ca tudyatāma vīrabāhuvisṛṣṭānāṃ sarvāvaraṇabhedināmc saṃghātaḥ śarajālānāṃ tumulaḥ samapadyataa prakāśaṃ cakrur ākāśam udyatāni bhujottamaiḥc nakṣatravimalābhāni śastrāṇi bharatarṣabhaa ārṣabhāṇi vicitrāṇi rukmajālāvṛtāni cac saṃpetur dikṣu sarvāsu carmāṇi bharatarṣabhaa sūryavarṇaiś ca nistriṃśaiḥ pātyamānāni sarvaśaḥc dikṣu sarvāsv adṛśyanta śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi caa bhagnacakrākṣanīḍāś ca nipātitamahādhvajāḥc hatāśvāḥ pṛthivīṃ jagmus tatra tatra mahārathāḥa paripetur hayāś cātra ke cic chastrakṛtavraṇāḥc rathān viparikarṣanto hateṣu rathayodhiṣua śarāhatā bhinnadehā baddhayoktrā hayottamāḥc yugāni paryakarṣanta tatra tatra sma bhārataa adṛśyanta sasūtāś ca sāśvāḥ sarathayodhinaḥc ekena balinā rājan vāraṇena hatā rathāḥa gandhahastimadasrāvam āghrāya bahavo raṇec saṃnipāte balaughānāṃ vītam ādadire gajāḥa satomaramahāmātrair nipatadbhir gatāsubhiḥc babhūvāyodhanaṃ channaṃ nārācābhihatair gajaiḥa saṃnipāte balaughānāṃ preṣitair varavāraṇaiḥc nipetur yudhi saṃbhagnāḥ sayodhāḥ sadhvajā rathāḥa nāgarājopamair hastair nāgair ākṣipya saṃyugec vyadṛśyanta mahārāja saṃbhagnā rathakūbarāḥa viśīrṇarathajālāś ca keśeṣv ākṣipya dantibhiḥc drumaśākhā ivāvidhya niṣpiṣṭā rathino raṇea ratheṣu ca rathān yuddhe saṃsaktān varavāraṇāḥc vikarṣanto diśaḥ sarvāḥ saṃpetuḥ sarvaśabdagāḥa teṣāṃ tathā karṣatāṃ ca gajānāṃ rūpam ābabhauc saraḥsu nalinījālaṃ viṣaktam iva karṣatāma evaṃ saṃchāditaṃ tatra babhūvāyodhanaṃ mahatc sādibhiś ca padātaiś ca sadhvajaiś ca mahārathaiḥ saṃjaya uvācaa śikhaṇḍī saha matsyena virāṭena viśāṃ patec bhīṣmam āśu maheṣvāsam āsasāda sudurjayama droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca maheṣvāsān mahābalānc rājñaś cānyān raṇe śūrān bahūn ārchad dhanaṃjayaḥa saindhavaṃ ca maheṣvāsaṃ sāmātyaṃ saha bandhubhiḥc prācyāṃś ca dākṣiṇātyāṃś ca bhūmipān bhūmiparṣabhaa putraṃ ca te maheṣvāsaṃ duryodhanam amarṣaṇamc duḥsahaṃ caiva samare bhīmaseno bhyavartataa sahadevas tu śakunim ulūkaṃ ca mahārathamc pitāputrau maheṣvāsāv abhyavartata durjayaua yudhiṣṭhiro mahārāja gajānīkaṃ mahārathaḥc samavartata saṃgrāme putreṇa nikṛtas tavaa mādrīputras tu nakulaḥ śūraḥ saṃkrandano yudhic trigartānāṃ rathodāraiḥ samasajjata pāṇḍavaḥa abhyavartanta durdharṣāḥ samare śālvakekayānb nākuliś ca śatānīkaḥ samare rathapuṃgavaḥc sātyakiś cekitānaś ca saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥa dhṛṣṭaketuś ca samare rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥc putrāṇāṃ te rathānīkaṃ pratyudyātāḥ sudurjayāḥa senāpatir ameyātmā dhṛṣṭadyumno mahābalaḥc droṇena samare rājan samiyāyendrakarmaṇāa evam ete maheṣvāsās tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac sametya samare śūrāḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrirea madhyaṃdinagate sūrye nabhasy ākulatāṃ gatec kuravaḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca nijaghnur itaretarama dhvajino hemacitrāṅgā vicaranto raṇājirec sapatākā rathā rejur vaiyāghraparivāraṇāḥa sametānāṃ ca samare jigīṣūṇāṃ parasparamc babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ siṃhānām iva nardatāma tatrādbhutam apaśyāma saṃprahāraṃ sudāruṇamc yam akurvan raṇe vīrāḥ sṛñjayāḥ kurubhiḥ sahaa naiva khaṃ na diśo rājan na sūryaṃ śatrutāpanac vidiśo vāpy apaśyāma śarair muktaiḥ samantataḥa śaktīnāṃ vimalāgrāṇāṃ tomarāṇāṃ tathāsyatāmc nistriṃśānāṃ ca pītānāṃ nīlotpalanibhāḥ prabhāḥa kavacānāṃ vicitrāṇāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ prabhās tathāc khaṃ diśaḥ pradiśaś caiva bhāsayām āsur ojasād vapurbhiś ca narendrāṇāṃ candrasūryasamaprabhaiḥe virarāja tadā rājaṃs tatra tatra raṇāṅgaṇama rathasiṃhāsanavyāghrāḥ samāyāntaś ca saṃyugec virejuḥ samare rājan grahā iva nabhastalea bhīṣmas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭho bhīmasenaṃ mahābalamc avārayata saṃkruddhaḥ sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa tato bhīṣmavinirmuktā rukmapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥc abhyaghnan samare bhīmaṃ tailadhautāḥ sutejanāḥa tasya śaktiṃ mahāvegāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc kruddhāśīviṣasaṃkāśāṃ preṣayām āsa bhārataa tām āpatantīṃ sahasā rukmadaṇḍāṃ durāsadāmc ciccheda samare bhīṣmaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa tato pareṇa bhallena pītena niśitena cac kārmukaṃ bhīmasenasya dvidhā ciccheda bhāratad apāsya tu dhanuś chinnaṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥd śarair bahubhir ānarchad bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yudhia sātyakis tu tatas tūrṇaṃ bhīṣmam āsādya saṃyugeb ākarṇaprahitais tīkṣṇair niśitais tigmatejanaiḥc śarair bahubhir ānarchat pitaraṃ te janeśvaraa tataḥ saṃdhāya vai tīkṣṇaṃ śaraṃ paramadāruṇamc vārṣṇeyasya rathād bhīṣmaḥ pātayām āsa sārathima tasyāśvāḥ pradrutā rājan nihate rathasārathauc tena tenaiva dhāvanti manomārutaraṃhasaḥa tataḥ sarvasya sainyasya nisvanas tumulo bhavatc hāhākāraś ca saṃjajñe pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāma abhidravata gṛhṇīta hayān yacchata dhāvatac ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdo yuyudhānarathaṃ pratia etasminn eva kāle tu bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punaḥc vyahanat pāṇḍavīṃ senām āsurīm iva vṛtrahāa te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ sahac āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā bhīṣmam evābhidudruvuḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhāś cāpi pārthāḥ śāṃtanavaṃ raṇec abhyadhāvañ jigīṣantas tava putrasya vāhinīma tathaiva tāvakā rājan bhīṣmadroṇamukhāḥ parānc abhyadhāvanta vegena tato yuddham avartata saṃjaya uvācaa virāṭo tha tribhir bāṇair bhīṣmam ārchan mahārathamc vivyādha turagāṃś cāsya tribhir bāṇair mahārathaḥa taṃ pratyavidhyad daśabhir bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ śaraiḥc rukmapuṅkhair maheṣvāsaḥ kṛtahasto mahābalaḥa drauṇir gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ bhīmadhanvā mahārathaḥc avidhyad iṣubhiḥ ṣaḍbhir dṛḍhahastaḥ stanāntarea kārmukaṃ tasya ciccheda phalgunaḥ paravīrahāc avidhyac ca bhṛśaṃ tīkṣṇaiḥ patribhiḥ śatrukarśanaḥa so nyat kārmukam ādāya vegavat krodhamūrchitaḥc amṛṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena kārmukacchedam āhavea avidhyat phalgunaṃ rājan navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc vāsudevaṃ ca saptatyā vivyādha parameṣubhiḥa tataḥ krodhābhitāmrākṣaḥ saha kṛṣṇena phalgunaḥc dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya cintayitvā muhur muhuḥa dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇāmitrakarśanaḥc gāṇḍīvadhanvā saṃkruddhaḥ śitān saṃnataparvaṇaḥe jīvitāntakarān ghorān samādatta śilīmukhāna tais tūrṇaṃ samare vidhyad drauṇiṃ balavatāṃ varamc tasya te kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhavea na vivyathe ca nirbhinno drauṇir gāṇḍīvadhanvanāc tathaiva śaravarṣāṇi pratimuñcann avihvalaḥe tasthau sa samare rājaṃs trātum icchan mahāvratama tasya tat sumahat karma śaśaṃsuḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥc yat kṛṣṇābhyāṃ sametābhyāṃ nāpatrapata saṃyuged sa viddhaḥ phālgunenājau na papāta mahītalea sa hi nityam anīkeṣu yudhyate bhayam āsthitaḥc astragrāmaṃ sasaṃhāraṃ droṇāt prāpya sudurlabhama mamāyam ācāryasuto droṇasyātipriyaḥ sutaḥc brāhmaṇaś ca viśeṣeṇa mānanīyo mameti caa samāsthāya matiṃ vīro bībhatsuḥ śatrutāpanaḥc kṛpāṃ cakre rathaśreṣṭho bhāradvājasutaṃ pratia drauṇiṃ tyaktvā tato yuddhe kaunteyaḥ śatrutāpanaḥc yuyudhe tāvakān nighnaṃs tvaramāṇaḥ parākramīa duryodhanas tu daśabhir gārdhrapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥc bhīmasenaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ rukmapuṅkhaiḥ samarpayata bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddhaḥ parāsukaraṇaṃ dṛḍhamc citraṃ kārmukam ādatta śarāṃś ca niśitān daśaa ākarṇaprahitais tīkṣṇair vegitais tigmatejanaiḥc avidhyat tūrṇam avyagraḥ kururājaṃ mahorasia tasya kāñcanasūtras tu śaraiḥ parivṛto maṇiḥc rarājorasi vai sūryo grahair iva samāvṛtaḥa putras tu tava tejasvī bhīmasenena tāḍitaḥc nāmṛṣyata yathā nāgas talaśabdaṃ samīritama tataḥ śarair mahārāja rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥc bhīmaṃ vivyādha saṃkruddhas trāsayāno varūthinīma tau yudhyamānau samare bhṛśam anyonyavikṣatauc putrau te devasaṃkāśau vyarocetāṃ mahābalaua citrasenaṃ naravyāghraṃ saubhadraḥ paravīrahāc avidhyad daśabhir bāṇaiḥ purumitraṃ ca saptabhiḥa satyavrataṃ ca saptatyā viddhvā śakrasamo yudhic nṛtyann iva raṇe vīra ārtiṃ naḥ samajījanata taṃ pratyavidyad daśabhiś citrasenaḥ śilīmukhaiḥc satyavrataś ca navabhiḥ purumitraś ca saptabhiḥa sa viddho vikṣaran raktaṃ śatrusaṃvāraṇaṃ mahatc ciccheda citrasenasya citraṃ kārmukam ārjuniḥe bhittvā cāsya tanutrāṇaṃ śareṇorasy atāḍayata tatas te tāvakā vīrā rājaputrā mahārathāḥc sametya yudhi saṃrabdhā vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥe tāṃś ca sarvāñ śarais tīkṣṇair jaghāna paramāstravita tasya dṛṣṭvā tu tat karma parivavruḥ sutās tavac dahantaṃ samare sainyaṃ tava kakṣaṃ yatholbaṇama apetaśiśire kāle samiddham iva pāvakaḥc atyarocata saubhadras tava sainyāni śātayana tat tasya caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā pautras tava viśāṃ patec lakṣmaṇo bhyapatat tūrṇaṃ sātvatīputram āhavea abhimanyus tu saṃkruddho lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇamc vivyādha viśikhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥa tathaiva lakṣmaṇo rājan saubhadraṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc avidhyata mahārāja tad adbhutam ivābhavata tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sārathiṃ ca mahābalaḥc abhyadravata saubhadro lakṣmaṇaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa hatāśve tu rathe tuṣṭhaṃl lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahāc śaktiṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddhaḥ saubhadrasya rathaṃ pratia tām āpatantīṃ sahasā ghorarūpāṃ durāsadāmc abhimanyuḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiś ciccheda bhujagopamāma tataḥ svaratham āropya lakṣmaṇaṃ gautamas tadāc apovāha rathenājau sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa tataḥ samākule tasmin vartamāne mahābhayeb hayo hayaṃ gajo nāgaṃ vīro vīraṃ viśāṃ patec abhyadravañ jighāṃsantaḥ parasparavadhaiṣiṇaḥa tāvakāś ca maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavāś ca mahārathāḥc juhvantaḥ samare prāṇān nijaghnur itaretarama muktakeśā vikavacā virathāś chinnakārmukāḥc bāhubhiḥ samayudhyanta sṛñjayāḥ kurubhiḥ sahaa tato bhīṣmo mahābāhuḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāmc senāṃ jaghāna saṃkruddho divyair astrair mahābalaḥa hateśvarair gajais tatra narair aśvaiś ca pātitaiḥc rathibhiḥ sādibhiś caiva samāstīryata medinī saṃjaya uvācaa atha rājan mahābāhuḥ sātyakir yuddhadurmadaḥc vikṛṣya cāpaṃ samare bhārasādhanam uttamamd yat tat sakhyus tu pūrveṇa arjunād upaśikṣitama prāmuñcat puṅkhasaṃyuktāñ śarān āśīviṣopamānc prakāśaṃ laghu citraṃ ca darśayann astralāghavama tasya vikṣipataś cāpaṃ śarān anyāṃś ca muñcataḥc ādadānasya bhūyaś ca saṃdadhānasya cāparāna kṣipataś ca śarān asya raṇe śatrūn vinighnataḥc dadṛśe rūpam atyarthaṃ meghasyeva pravarṣataḥa tam udīryantam ālokya rājā duryodhanas tataḥc rathānām ayutaṃ tasya preṣayām āsa bhārataa tāṃs tu sarvān maheṣvāsān sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥc jaghāna parameṣvāso divyenāstreṇa vīryavāna sa kṛtvā dāruṇaṃ karma pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥc āsasāda tato vīro bhūriśravasam āhavea sa hi saṃdṛśya senāṃ tāṃ yuyudhānena pātitāmc abhyadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ kurūṇāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥa indrāyudhasavarṇaṃ tat sa visphārya mahad dhanuḥc vyasṛjad vajrasaṃkāśāñ śarān āśīviṣopamāne sahasraśo mahārāja darśayan pāṇilāghavama śarāṃs tān mṛtyusaṃsparśān sātyakes tu padānugāḥc na viṣehus tadā rājan dudruvus te samantataḥe vihāya samare rājan sātyakiṃ yuddhadurmadama taṃ dṛṣṭvā yuyudhānasya sutā daśa mahābalāḥc mahārathāḥ samākhyātāś citravarmāyudhadhvajāḥa samāsādya maheṣvāsaṃ bhūriśravasam āhavec ūcuḥ sarve susaṃrabdhā yūpaketuṃ mahāraṇed yudhyasva samare cādya paśyāmas tava pauruṣama bho bho kauravadāyāda sahāsmābhir mahābalac ehi yudhyasva saṃgrāme samastaiḥ pṛthag eva vāa asmān vā tvaṃ parājitya yaśaḥ prāpnuhi saṃyugec vayaṃ vā tvāṃ parājitya prītiṃ dāsyāmahe pituḥa evam uktas tadā śūrais tān uvāca mahābalaḥc vīryaślāghī naraśreṣṭhas tān dṛṣṭvā samupasthitāna sādhv idaṃ kathyate vīrā yad evaṃ matir adya vaḥc yudhyadhvaṃ sahitā yattā nihaniṣyāmi vo raṇea evam uktā maheṣvāsās te vīrāḥ kṣiprakāriṇaḥc mahatā śaravarṣeṇa abhyavarṣann ariṃdamama aparāhṇe mahārāja saṃgrāmas tumulo bhavatc ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca sametānāṃ raṇājirea tam ekaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śaravarṣair avākiranc prāvṛṣīva mahāśailaṃ siṣicur jaladā nṛpaa tais tu muktāñ śaraughāṃs tān yamadaṇḍāśaniprabhānc asaṃprāptān asaṃprāptāṃś cicchedāśu mahārathaḥa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma saumadatteḥ parākramamc yad eko bahubhir yuddhe samasajjad abhītavata visṛjya śaravṛṣṭiṃ tāṃ daśa rājan mahārathāḥc parivārya mahābāhuṃ nihantum upacakramuḥa saumadattis tataḥ kruddhas teṣāṃ cāpāni bhāratac ciccheda daśabhir bāṇair nimeṣeṇa mahārathaḥa athaiṣāṃ chinnadhanuṣāṃ bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc ciccheda samare rājañ śirāṃsi niśitaiḥ śaraiḥe te hatā nyapatan bhūmau vajrabhagnā iva drumāḥa tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān vīrān raṇe putrān mahābalānc vārṣṇeyo vinadan rājan bhūriśravasam abhyayāta rathaṃ rathena samare pīḍayitvā mahābalauc tāv anyonyasya samare nihatya rathavājinaḥe virathāv abhivalgantau sameyātāṃ mahārathaua pragṛhītamahākhaḍgau tau carmavaradhāriṇauc śuśubhāte naravyāghrau yuddhāya samavasthitaud asahyam asiyuddhāya bhūriśravasam āhaved matvā vṛkodaras tūrṇam abhiplutya mahārathaḥa tataḥ sātyakim abhyetya nistriṃśavaradhāriṇamc bhīmasenas tvaran rājan ratham āropayat tadāa tavāpi tanayo rājan bhūriśravasam āhavec āropayad rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvināma tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne raṇe bhīṣmaṃ mahārathamc ayodhayanta saṃrabdhāḥ pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabhaa lohitāyati cāditye tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥc pañcaviṃśatisāhasrān nijaghāna mahārathāna te hi duryodhanādiṣṭās tadā pārthanibarhaṇec saṃprāpyaiva gatā nāśaṃ śalabhā iva pāvakama tato matsyāḥ kekayāś ca dhanurvedaviśāradāḥc parivavrus tadā pārthaṃ sahaputraṃ mahārathama etasminn eva kāle tu sūrye stam upagacchatic sarveṣām eva sainyānāṃ pramohaḥ samajāyataa avahāraṃ tataś cakre pitā devavratas tavac saṃdhyākāle mahārāja sainyānāṃ śrāntavāhanaḥa pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca parasparasamāgamec te sene bhṛśasaṃvigne yayatuḥ svaṃ niveśanama tataḥ svaśibiraṃ gatvā nyaviśaṃs tatra bhāratac pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ sārdhaṃ kuravaś ca yathāvidhi saṃjaya uvācaa vihṛtya ca tato rājan sahitāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥc vyatītāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ punar yuddhāya niryayuḥa tatra śabdo mahān āsīt tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratac yujyatāṃ rathamukhyānāṃ kalpyatāṃ caiva dantināma saṃnahyatāṃ padātīnāṃ hayānāṃ caiva bhāratac śaṅkhadundubhinādaś ca tumulaḥ sarvato bhavata tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā dhṛṣṭadyumnam abhāṣatac vyūhaṃ vyūha mahābāho makaraṃ śatrutāpanama evam uktas tu pārthena dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārathaḥc vyādideśa mahārāja rathino rathināṃ varaḥa śiro bhūd drupadas tasya pāṇḍavaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥc cakṣuṣī sahadevaś ca nakulaś ca mahārathaḥe tuṇḍam āsīn mahārāja bhīmaseno mahābalaḥa saubhadro draupadeyāś ca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥc sātyakir dharmarājaś ca vyūhagrīvāṃ samāsthitāḥa pṛṣṭham āsīn mahārāja virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahito mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥa kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca vāmaṃ pārśvaṃ samāśritāḥc dhṛṣṭaketur naravyāghraḥ karakarṣaś ca vīryavāne dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā vyūhasya rakṣaṇea pādayos tu mahārāja sthitaḥ śrīmān mahārathaḥc kuntibhojaḥ śatānīko mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥa śikhaṇḍī tu maheṣvāsaḥ somakaiḥ saṃvṛto balīc irāvāṃś ca tataḥ pucche makarasya vyavasthitaua evam etan mahāvyūhaṃ vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥc sūryodaye mahārāja punar yuddhāya daṃśitāḥa kauravān abhyayus tūrṇaṃ hastyaśvarathapattibhiḥc samucchritair dhvajaiś citraiḥ śastraiś ca vimalaiḥ śitaiḥa vyūhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu tat sainyaṃ pitā devavratas tavac krauñcena mahatā rājan pratyavyūhata vāhinīma tasya tuṇḍe maheṣvāso bhāradvājo vyarocatac aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva cakṣur āstāṃ nareśvaraa kṛtavarmā tu sahitaḥ kāmbojāraṭṭabāhlikaiḥc śirasy āsīn naraśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatāma grīvāyāṃ śūrasenas tu tava putraś ca māriṣac duryodhano mahārāja rājabhir bahubhir vṛtaḥa prāgjyotiṣas tu sahitaḥ madrasauvīrakekayaiḥc urasy abhūn naraśreṣṭha mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥd pṛṣṭhe cāstāṃ maheṣvāsāv āvantyau sapadānugaua svasenayā ca sahitaḥ suśarmā prasthalādhipaḥc vāmaṃ pakṣaṃ samāśritya daṃśitaḥ samavasthitaḥa tuṣārā yavanāś caiva śakāś ca saha cūcupaiḥc dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā vyūhasya bhārataa śrutāyuś ca śatāyuś ca saumadattiś ca māriṣac vyūhasya jaghane tasthū rakṣamāṇāḥ parasparama tato yuddhāya saṃjagmuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kauravaiḥ sahac sūryodaye mahārāja tato yuddham abhūn mahata pratīyū rathino nāgān nāgāś ca rathino yayuḥc hayārohā hayārohān rathinaś cāpi sādinaḥa sārathiṃ ca rathī rājan kuñjarāṃś ca mahāraṇec hastyārohā rathārohān rathinaś cāpi sādinaḥa rathinaḥ pattibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sādinaś cāpi pattibhiḥc anyonyaṃ samare rājan pratyadhāvann amarṣitāḥa bhīmasenārjunayamair guptā cānyair mahārathaiḥc śuśubhe pāṇḍavī senā nakṣatrair iva śarvarīa tathā bhīṣmakṛpadroṇaśalyaduryodhanādibhiḥc tavāpi vibabhau senā grahair dyaur iva saṃvṛtāa bhīmasenas tu kaunteyo droṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā parākramīc abhyayāj javanair aśvair bhāradvājasya vāhinīma droṇas tu samare kruddho bhīmaṃ navabhir āyasaiḥc vivyādha samare rājan marmāṇy uddiśya vīryavāna dṛḍhāhatas tato bhīmo bhāradvājasya saṃyugec sārathiṃ preṣayām āsa yamasya sadanaṃ pratia sa saṃgṛhya svayaṃ vāhān bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc vyadhamat pāṇḍavīṃ senāṃ tūlarāśim ivānalaḥa te vadhyamānā droṇena bhīṣmeṇa ca narottamac sṛñjayāḥ kekayaiḥ sārdhaṃ palāyanaparābhavana tathaiva tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ bhīmārjunaparikṣatamc muhyate tatra tatraiva samadeva varāṅganāa abhidyetāṃ tato vyūhau tasmin vīravarakṣayec āsīd vyatikaro ghoras tava teṣāṃ ca bhārataa tad adbhutam apaśyāma tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sahac ekāyanagatāḥ sarve yad ayudhyanta bhārataa pratisaṃvārya cāstrāṇi te nyonyasya viśāṃ patec yuyudhuḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva kauravāś ca mahārathāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa evaṃ bahuguṇaṃ sainyam evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ paramc vyūḍham evaṃ yathāśāstram amoghaṃ caiva saṃjayaa puṣṭam asmākam atyantam abhikāmaṃ ca naḥ sadāc prahvam avyasanopetaṃ purastād dṛṣṭavikramama nātivṛddham abālaṃ ca na kṛśaṃ na ca pīvaramc laghuvṛttāyataprāyaṃ sāragātram anāmayama āttasaṃnāhaśastraṃ ca bahuśastraparigrahamc asiyuddhe niyuddhe ca gadāyuddhe ca kovidama prāsarṣṭitomareṣv ājau parigheṣv āyaseṣu cac bhiṇḍipāleṣu śaktīṣu musaleṣu ca sarvaśaḥa kampaneṣu ca cāpeṣu kaṇapeṣu ca sarvaśaḥc kṣepaṇīṣu ca citrāsu muṣṭiyuddheṣu kovidama aparokṣaṃ ca vidyāsu vyāyāmeṣu kṛtaśramamc śastragrahaṇavidyāsu sarvāsu pariniṣṭhitama ārohe paryavaskande saraṇe sāntaraplutec samyakpraharaṇe yāne vyapayāne ca kovidama nāgāśvarathayāneṣu bahuśaḥ suparīkṣitamc parīkṣya ca yathānyāyaṃ vetanenopapāditama na goṣṭhyā nopacāreṇa na ca bandhunimittataḥc na sauhṛdabalaiś cāpi nākulīnaparigrahaiḥa samṛddhajanam āryaṃ ca tuṣṭasatkṛtabāndhavamc kṛtopakārabhūyiṣṭhaṃ yaśasvi ca manasvi caa sajayaiś ca narair mukhyair bahuśo mukhyakarmabhiḥc lokapālopamais tāta pālitaṃ lokaviśrutaiḥa bahubhiḥ kṣatriyair guptaṃ pṛthivyāṃ lokasaṃmataiḥc asmān abhigataiḥ kāmāt sabalaiḥ sapadānugaiḥa mahodadhim ivāpūrṇam āpagābhiḥ samantataḥc apakṣaiḥ pakṣasaṃkāśai rathair nāgaiś ca saṃvṛtama nānāyodhajalaṃ bhīmaṃ vāhanormitaraṅgiṇamc kṣepaṇyasigadāśaktiśaraprāsasamākulama dhvajabhūṣaṇasaṃbādhaṃ ratnapaṭṭena saṃcitamc vāhanaiḥ parisarpadbhir vāyuvegavikampitama apāram iva garjantaṃ sāgarapratimaṃ mahatc droṇabhīṣmābhisaṃguptaṃ guptaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇāa kṛpaduḥśāsanābhyāṃ ca jayadrathamukhais tathāc bhagadattavikarṇābhyāṃ drauṇisaubalabāhlikaiḥa guptaṃ pravīrair lokasya sāravadbhir mahātmabhiḥc yad ahanyata saṃgrāme diṣṭam etat purātanama naitādṛśaṃ samudyogaṃ dṛṣṭavanto tha mānuṣāḥc ṛṣayo vā mahābhāgāḥ purāṇā bhuvi saṃjayaa īdṛśo hi balaughas tu yuktaḥ śastrāstrasaṃpadāc vadhyate yatra saṃgrāme kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa viparītam idaṃ sarvaṃ pratibhāti sma saṃjayac yatredṛśaṃ balaṃ ghoraṃ nātarad yudhi pāṇḍavāna atha vā pāṇḍavārthāya devās tatra samāgatāḥc yudhyante māmakaṃ sainyaṃ yad avadhyanta saṃjayaa ukto hi vidureṇeha hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca saṃjayac na ca gṛhṇāti tan mandaḥ putro duryodhano mamaa tasya manye matiḥ pūrvaṃ sarvajñasya mahātmanaḥc āsīd yathāgataṃ tāta yena dṛṣṭam idaṃ purāa atha vā bhāvyam evaṃ hi saṃjayaitena sarvathāc purā dhātrā yathā sṛṣṭaṃ tat tathā na tad anyathā saṃjaya uvācaa ātmadoṣāt tvayā rājan prāptaṃ vyasanam īdṛśamc na hi duryodhanas tāni paśyate bharatarṣabhae yāni tvaṃ dṛṣṭavān rājan dharmasaṃkarakāritea tava doṣāt purā vṛttaṃ dyūtam etad viśāṃ patec tava doṣeṇa yuddhaṃ ca pravṛttaṃ saha pāṇḍavaiḥe tvam evādya phalaṃ bhuṅkṣva kṛtvā kilbiṣam ātmanāa ātmanā hi kṛtaṃ karma ātmanaivopabhujyatec iha vā pretya vā rājaṃs tvayā prāptaṃ yathātathama tasmād rājan sthiro bhūtvā prāpyedaṃ vyasanaṃ mahatc śṛṇu yuddhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ śaṃsato mama māriṣaa bhīmasenas tu niśitair bāṇair bhittvā mahācamūmc āsasāda tato vīraḥ sarvān duryodhanānujāna duḥśāsanaṃ durviṣahaṃ duḥsahaṃ durmadaṃ jayamc jayatsenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca citrasenaṃ sudarśanama cārucitraṃ suvarmāṇaṃ duṣkarṇaṃ karṇam eva cac etān anyāṃś ca subahūn samīpasthān mahārathāna dhārtarāṣṭrān susaṃkruddhān dṛṣṭvā bhīmo mahābalaḥc bhīṣmeṇa samare guptāṃ praviveśa mahācamūma athāhvayanta te nyonyam ayaṃ prāpto vṛkodaraḥb athālokya praviṣṭaṃ tam ūcus te sarva eva tuc jīvagrāhaṃ nigṛhṇīmo vayam enaṃ narādhipāḥa sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ pārtho bhrātṛbhiḥ kṛtaniścayaiḥc prajāsaṃharaṇe sūryaḥ krūrair iva mahāgrahaiḥa saṃprāpya madhyaṃ vyūhasya na bhīḥ pāṇḍavam āviśatc yathā devāsure yuddhe mahendraḥ prāpya dānavāna tataḥ śatasahasrāṇi rathināṃ sarvaśaḥ prabhoc chādayānaṃ śarair ghorais tam ekam anuvavrirea sa teṣāṃ pravarān yodhān hastyaśvarathasādinaḥc jaghāna samare śūro dhārtarāṣṭrān acintayana teṣāṃ vyavasitaṃ jñātvā bhīmaseno jighṛkṣatāmc samastānāṃ vadhe rājan matiṃ cakre mahāmanāḥa tato rathaṃ samutsṛjya gadām ādāya pāṇḍavaḥb uvāca sārathiṃ bhīmaḥ sthīyatām iti bhāratab yāvad enān haniṣyāmi dhārtarāṣṭrān sahānugānb ity uktvā bhīmasenas tu praviśya mahatīṃ camūmc jaghāna dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ taṃ balaughamahārṇavamd gadayā bhīmasenena tāḍitā vāraṇottamāḥd bhinnakumbhā mahākāyā bhinnapṛṣṭhās tathaiva cad bhinnagātrāḥ sahārohāḥ śerate parvatā ivad rathāś ca bhagnās tilaśaḥ sayodhāḥ śataśo raṇed aśvāś ca sādinaś caiva pādātaiḥ saha bhāratad tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bhīmasenasya vikramamd yad ekaḥ samare rājan bahubhiḥ samayodhayatd antakāle prajāḥ sarvā daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥa bhīmasene praviṣṭe tu dhṛṣṭadyumno pi pārṣataḥc droṇam utsṛjya tarasā prayayau yatra saubalaḥa vidārya mahatīṃ senāṃ tāvakānāṃ nararṣabhaḥc āsasāda rathaṃ śūnyaṃ bhīmasenasya saṃyuged rathaṃ ca śūnyaṃ saṃprekṣya bhīmaṃ prati vicetanaḥa dṛṣṭvā viśokaṃ samare bhīmasenasya sārathimc dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja durmanā gatacetanaḥa apṛcchad bāṣpasaṃruddho nisvanāṃ vācam īrayanc mama prāṇaiḥ priyatamaḥ kva bhīma iti duḥkhitaḥa viśokas tam uvācedaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥc saṃsthāpya mām iha balī pāṇḍaveyaḥ pratāpavāna praviṣṭo dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām etad balamahārṇavamc mām uktvā puruṣavyāghra prītiyuktam idaṃ vacaḥa pratipālaya māṃ sūta niyamyāśvān muhūrtakamc yāvad etān nihanmy āśu ya ime madvadhodyatāḥd abhyadhāvad gadāpāṇis tad balaṃ sa mahābalaḥa tato dṛṣṭvā gadāhastaṃ pradhāvantaṃ mahābalamc sarveṣām eva sainyānāṃ saṃgharṣaḥ samajāyataa tasmiṃs tu tumule yuddhe vartamāne bhayānakec bhittvā rājan mahāvyūhaṃ praviveśa sakhā tavaa viśokasya vacaḥ śrutvā dhṛṣṭadyumno pi pārṣataḥc pratyuvāca tataḥ sūtaṃ raṇamadhye mahābalaḥa na hi me vidyate sūta jīvite dya prayojanamc bhīmasenaṃ raṇe hitvā sneham utsṛjya pāṇḍavaiḥa yadi yāmi vinā bhīmaṃ kiṃ māṃ kṣatraṃ vadiṣyatic ekāyanagate bhīme mayi cāvasthite yudhia asvasti tasya kurvanti devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥc yaḥ sahāyān parityajya svastimān āvrajed gṛhānd dhikkṛtasya ca kṣatreṇa nirarthaṃ jīvitaṃ bhavetd raurave narake majjed aplave dustare nṛbhiḥa mama bhīmaḥ sakhā caiva saṃbandhī ca mahābalaḥc bhakto smān bhaktimāṃś cāhaṃ tam apy ariniṣūdanama so haṃ tatra gamiṣyāmi yatra yāto vṛkodaraḥc nighnantaṃ mām arīn paśya dānavān iva vāsavama evam uktvā tato vīro yayau madhyena bhāratīmc bhīmasenasya mārgeṣu gadāpramathitair gajaiḥa sa dadarśa tato bhīmaṃ dahantaṃ ripuvāhinīmc vātaṃ vṛkṣān iva balāt prabhañjantaṃ raṇe nṛpāna te hanyamānāḥ samare rathinaḥ sādinas tathāc pādātā dantinaś caiva cakrur ārtasvaraṃ mahata hāhākāraś ca saṃjajñe tava sainyasya māriṣac vadhyato bhīmasenena kṛtinā citrayodhināa tataḥ kṛtāstrās te sarve parivārya vṛkodaramc abhītāḥ samavartanta śastravṛṣṭyā samantataḥa abhidrutaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃsamantataḥ pāṇḍavaṃ lokavīraiḥb abhidrutaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃ ca samantataḥb lokapālasamaṃ vīra lokavīraiś ca pāṇḍavamc sainyena ghoreṇa susaṃgatenadṛṣṭvā balī pārṣato bhīmasenama athopagacchac charavikṣatāṅgaṃpadātinaṃ krodhaviṣaṃ vamantamc āśvāsayan pārṣato bhīmasenaṃgadāhastaṃ kālam ivāntakālea niḥśalyam enaṃ ca cakāra tūrṇamāropayac cātmarathaṃ mahātmāc bhṛśaṃ pariṣvajya ca bhīmasenamāśvāsayām āsa ca śatrumadhyed tathā tasmin vartamāne tivegaṃd bhīmo tatho pretya ca yājñasenam sica bhrātṝn athopetya tavāpi putrastasmin vimarde mahati pravṛtteb dṛṣṭvā raṇe vākyam idaṃ babhāṣec ayaṃ durātmā drupadasya putraḥsamāgato bhīmasenena sārdhame taṃ yāta sarve sahitā nihantuṃmā vo ripuḥ prārthayatām anīkamf ārchann etaṃ kṣudrakarmātihīnaṃf sainyaṃ ca vidhvaṃsayate pṛṣatkaiḥa śrutvā tu vākyaṃ tam amṛṣyamāṇājyeṣṭhājñayā coditā dhārtarāṣṭrāḥc vadhāya niṣpetur udāyudhās teyugakṣaye ketavo yadvad ugrāḥa pragṛhya citrāṇi dhanūṃṣi vīrājyānemighoṣaiḥ pravikampayantaḥc śarair avarṣan drupadasya putraṃyathāmbudā bhūdharaṃ vārijālaiḥe nihatya tāṃś cāpi śaraiḥ sutīkṣṇairna vivyathe samare citrayodhīa samabhyudīrṇāṃś ca tavātmajāṃs tathāniśāmya vīrān abhitaḥ sthitān raṇec jighāṃsur ugraṃ drupadātmajo yuvāpramohanāstraṃ yuyuje mahārathaḥe kruddho bhṛśaṃ tava putreṣu rājandaityeṣu yadvat samare mahendraḥf sa vai tato straṃ sumahāprabhāvaṃf pramohanaṃ droṇadattaṃ mahātmāf prayojayām āsa udārakarmāf tasmin raṇe tava sainyasya rājana tato vyamuhyanta raṇe nṛvīrāḥpramohanāstrāhatabuddhisattvāḥc pradudruvuḥ kuravaś caiva sarvesavājināgāḥ sarathāḥ samantāte parītakālān iva naṣṭasaṃjñānmohopetāṃs tava putrān niśamyaf etasminn eva kāle tu bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥf viśramya ca tadā rājan pītvāmṛtarasaṃ jalamf punaḥ saṃnahya sahasā yodhayām āsa saṃyugef dhṛṣṭadyumnena sahitaḥ kālayām āsa bhārataa etasminn eva kāle tu droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥc drupadaṃ tribhir āsādya śarair vivyādha dāruṇaiḥa so tividdhas tadā rājan raṇe droṇena pārthivaḥc apāyād drupado rājan pūrvavairam anusmarana jitvā tu drupadaṃ droṇaḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau pratāpavānc tasya śaṅkhasvanaṃ śrutvā vitresuḥ sarvasomakāḥa atha śuśrāva tejasvī droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥc pramohanāstreṇa raṇe mohitān ātmajāṃs tavaa tato droṇo rājagṛddhī tvarito bhiyayau raṇātc tatrāpaśyan maheṣvāso bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavāne dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca vicarantau mahāraṇea mohāviṣṭāṃś ca te putrān apaśyat sa mahārathaḥc tataḥ prajñāstram ādāya mohanāstraṃ vyaśātayata atha pratyāgataprāṇās tava putrā mahārathāḥc punar yuddhāya samare prayayur bhīmapārṣataua tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ prāha samāhūya svasainikānc gacchantu padavīṃ śaktyā bhīmapārṣatayor yudhia saubhadrapramukhā vīrā rathā dvādaśa daṃśitāḥc pravṛttim adhigacchantu na hi śudhyati me manaḥd pravṛttiṃ bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca saṃyuged vijñāya samare śīghraṃ praviśadhvaṃ rathārṇavamd gacchantu parayā śaktyā bhavanta iti me matiḥa ta evaṃ samanujñātāḥ śūrā vikrāntayodhinaḥc bāḍham ity evam uktvā tu sarve puruṣamāninaḥe madhyaṃdinagate sūrye prayayuḥ sarva eva hia kekayā draupadeyāś ca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavānc abhimanyuṃ puraskṛtya mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥa te kṛtvā samare vyūhaṃ sūcīmukham ariṃdamāḥc bibhidur dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ tad rathānīkam āhavea tān prayātān maheṣvāsān abhimanyupurogamānc bhīmasenabhayāviṣṭā dhṛṣṭadyumnavimohitāa na saṃdhārayituṃ śaktā tava senā janādhipac madamūrchānvitātmānaṃ pramadevādhvani sthitāa te bhiyātā maheṣvāsāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥc parīpsanto bhyadhāvanta dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodaraua tau ca dṛṣṭvā maheṣvāsān abhimanyupurogamānc babhūvatur mudā yuktau nighnantau tava vāhinīmd droṇam iṣvastrakuśalaṃ sarvavidyāsu pāragama dṛṣṭvā ca sahasāyāntaṃ pāñcālyo gurum ātmanaḥc nāśaṃsata vadhaṃ vīraḥ putrāṇāṃ tava pārṣataḥa tato rathaṃ samāropya kekayasya vṛkodaramc abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddho droṇam iṣvastrapāragama tasyābhipatatas tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc kruddhaś ciccheda bhallena dhanuḥ śatruniṣūdanaḥa anyāṃś ca śataśo bāṇān preṣayām āsa pārṣatec duryodhanahitārthāya bhartṛpiṇḍam anusmarana athānyad dhanur ādāya pārṣataḥ paravīrahāc droṇaṃ vivyādha saptatyā rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥa tasya droṇaḥ punaś cāpaṃ cicchedāmitrakarśanaḥc hayāṃś ca caturas tūrṇaṃ caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥa vaivasvatakṣayaṃ ghoraṃ preṣayām āsa vīryavānc sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena preṣayām āsa mṛtyaved dharmarājapuraṃ rājan preṣayām āsa vai dvijaḥa hatāśvāt sa rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥc āruroha mahābāhur abhimanyor mahārathama tataḥ sarathanāgāśvā samakampata vāhinīc paśyato bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca paśyataḥa tat prabhagnaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā droṇenāmitatejasāc nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ samastās te mahārathāḥa vadhyamānaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ droṇena niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc vyabhramat tatra tatraiva kṣobhyamāṇa ivārṇavaḥa tathā dṛṣṭvā ca tat sainyaṃ jahṛṣe ca balaṃ tavac dṛṣṭvācāryaṃ ca saṃkruddhaṃ dahantaṃ ripuvāhinīme cukruśuḥ sarvato yodhāḥ sādhu sādhv iti bhārata saṃjaya uvācaa tato duryodhano rājā mohāt pratyāgatas tadāc śaravarṣaiḥ punar bhīmaṃ pratyavārayad acyutama ekībhūtāḥ punaś caiva tava putrā mahārathāḥc sametya samare bhīmaṃ yodhayām āsur udyatāḥa bhīmaseno pi samare saṃprāpya svarathaṃ punaḥc samāruhya mahābāhur yayau yena tavātmajaḥa pragṛhya ca mahāvegaṃ parāsukaraṇaṃ dṛḍhamc citraṃ śarāsanaṃ saṃkhye śarair vivyādha te sutāna tato duryodhano rājā bhīmasenaṃ mahābalamc nārācena sutīkṣṇena bhṛśaṃ marmaṇy atāḍayata so tividdho maheṣvāsas tava putreṇa dhanvināc krodhasaṃraktanayano vegenotkṣipya kārmukama duryodhanaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayatc sa tathābhihato rājā nācalad girirāḍ ivaa tau dṛṣṭvā samare kruddhau vinighnantau parasparamc duryodhanānujāḥ sarve śūrāḥ saṃtyaktajīvitāḥa saṃsmṛtya mantritaṃ pūrvaṃ nigrahe bhīmakarmaṇaḥc niścayaṃ manasā kṛtvā nigrahītuṃ pracakramuḥa tān āpatata evājau bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc pratyudyayau mahārāja gajaḥ pratigajān ivaa bhṛśaṃ kruddhaś ca tejasvī nārācena samarpayatc citrasenaṃ mahārāja tava putraṃ mahāyaśāḥa tathetarāṃs tava sutāṃs tāḍayām āsa bhāratac śarair bahuvidhaiḥ saṃkhye rukmapuṅkhaiḥ suvegitaiḥa tataḥ saṃsthāpya samare svāny anīkāni sarvaśaḥc abhimanyuprabhṛtayas te dvādaśa mahārathāḥa preṣitā dharmarājena bhīmasenapadānugāḥc pratyudyayur mahārāja tava putrān mahābalāna dṛṣṭvā rathasthāṃs tāñ śūrān sūryāgnisamatejasaḥc sarvān eva maheṣvāsān bhrājamānāñ śriyā vṛtāna mahāhave dīpyamānān suvarṇakavacojjvalānc tatyajuḥ samare bhīmaṃ tava putrā mahābalāḥa tān nāmṛṣyata kaunteyo jīvamānā gatā itic anvīya ca punaḥ sarvāṃs tava putrān apīḍayata athābhimanyuṃ samare bhīmasenena saṃgatamc pārṣatena ca saṃprekṣya tava sainye mahārathāḥc   kekayā draupadīsutāḥc tān dṛṣṭvā samare kruddhāsa duryodhanaprabhṛtayaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥc bhṛśam aśvaiḥ prajavitaiḥ prayayur yatra te rathāḥa aparāhṇe tato rājan prāvartata mahān raṇaḥc tāvakānāṃ ca balināṃ pareṣāṃ caiva bhārataa abhimanyur vikarṇasya hayān hatvā mahājavānc athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samācinota hatāśvaṃ ratham utsṛjya vikarṇas tu mahārathaḥc āruroha rathaṃ rājaṃś citrasenasya bhāsvarama sthitāv ekarathe tau tu bhrātarau kuruvardhanauc ārjuniḥ śarajālena chādayām āsa bhārataa durjayo tha vikarṇaś ca kārṣṇiṃ pañcabhir āyasaiḥc vivyadhāte na cākampat kārṣṇir merur ivācalaḥa duḥśāsanas tu samare kekayān pañca māriṣac yodhayām āsa rājendra tad adbhutam ivābhavata draupadeyā raṇe kruddhā duryodhanam avārayanc ekaikas tribhir ānarchat putraṃ tava viśāṃ patea putro pi tava durdharṣo draupadyās tanayān raṇec sāyakair niśitai rājann ājaghāna pṛthak pṛthaka taiś cāpi viddhaḥ śuśubhe rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥc giriprasravaṇair yadvad girir dhātuvimiśritaiḥa bhīṣmo pi samare rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc kālayām āsa balavān pālaḥ paśugaṇān ivaa tato gāṇḍīvanirghoṣaḥ prādurāsīd viśāṃ patec dakṣiṇena varūthinyāḥ pārthasyārīn vinighnataḥa uttasthuḥ samare tatra kabandhāni samantataḥc kurūṇāṃ cāpi sainyeṣu pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārataa śoṇitodaṃ rathāvartaṃ gajadvīpaṃ hayormiṇamc rathanaubhir naravyāghrāḥ prateruḥ sainyasāgarama chinnahastā vikavacā videhāś ca narottamāḥc patitās tatra dṛśyante śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa nihatair mattamātaṅgaiḥ śoṇitaughapariplutaiḥc bhūr bhāti bharataśreṣṭha parvatair ācitā yathāa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratac na tatrāsīt pumān kaś cid yo yoddhuṃ nābhikāṅkṣatia evaṃ yuyudhire vīrāḥ prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥc tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ kāṅkṣamāṇā jayaṃ yudhi saṃjaya uvācaa tato duryodhano rājā lohitāyati bhāskarec saṃgrāmarabhaso bhīmaṃ hantukāmo bhyadhāvataa tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya nṛvīraṃ dṛḍhavairiṇamc bhīmasenaḥ susaṃkruddha idaṃ vacanam abravīta ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto varṣapūgābhikāṅkṣitaḥc adya tvāṃ nihaniṣyāmi yadi notsṛjase raṇama adya kuntyāḥ parikleśaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥc draupadyāś ca parikleśaṃ praṇotsyāmi hate tvayia yat tvaṃ durodaro bhūtvā pāṇḍavān avamanyasec tasya pāpasya gāndhāre paśya vyasanam āgatama karṇasya matam ājñāya saubalasya ca yat purāc acintya pāṇḍavān kāmād yatheṣṭaṃ kṛtavān asia yācamānaṃ ca yan mohād dāśārham avamanyasec ulūkasya samādeśaṃ yad dadāsi ca hṛṣṭavata adya tvā nihaniṣyāmi sānubandhaṃ sabāndhavamc samīkariṣye tat pāpaṃ yat purā kṛtavān asia evam uktvā dhanur ghoraṃ vikṛṣyodbhrāmya cāsakṛtc samādāya śarān ghorān mahāśanisamaprabhāna ṣaḍviṃśat tarasā kruddho mumocāśu suyodhanec jvalitāgniśikhākārān vajrakalpān ajihmagāna tato sya kārmukaṃ dvābhyāṃ sūtaṃ dvābhyāṃ ca vivyadhec caturbhir aśvāñ javanān anayad yamasādanama dvābhyāṃ ca suvikṛṣṭābhyāṃ śarābhyām arimardanaḥc chatraṃ ciccheda samare rājñas tasya rathottamāta tribhiś ca tasya ciccheda jvalantaṃ dhvajam uttamamb tribhir anyair maheṣvāsaś cicchedāsya dhvajaṃ tathāc chittvā taṃ ca nanādoccais tava putrasya paśyataḥa rathāc ca sa dhvajaḥ śrīmān nānāratnavibhūṣitaḥc papāta sahasā bhūmiṃ vidyuj jaladharād ivaa jvalantaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ nāgaṃ maṇimayaṃ śubhamc dhvajaṃ kurupateś chinnaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥa athainaṃ daśabhir bāṇais tottrair iva mahāgajamc ājaghāna raṇe bhīmaḥ smayann iva mahārathaḥd sa tathābhihato rājā smayann iva mahārathaḥa tatas tu rājā sindhūnāṃ rathaśreṣṭho jayadrathaḥc duryodhanasya jagrāha pārṣṇiṃ satpuruṣocitāma kṛpaś ca rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ kauravyam amitaujasamc āropayad rathaṃ rājan duryodhanam amarṣaṇama sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito bhīmasenena saṃyugec niṣasāda rathopasthe rājā duryodhanas tadāa parivārya tato bhīmaṃ hantukāmo jayadrathaḥc rathair anekasāhasrair bhīmasyāvārayad diśaḥa dhṛṣṭaketus tato rājann abhimanyuś ca vīryavānc kekayā draupadeyāś ca tava putrān ayodhayana citrasenaḥ sucitraś ca citrāśvaś citradarśanaḥc cārucitraḥ sucāruś ca tathā nandopanandakaua aṣṭāv ete maheṣvāsāḥ sukumārā yaśasvinaḥc abhimanyurathaṃ rājan samantāt paryavārayana ājaghāna tatas tūrṇam abhimanyur mahāmanāḥc ekaikaṃ pañcabhir viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥe vajramṛtyupratīkāśair vicitrāyudhaniḥsṛtaiḥa amṛṣyamāṇās te sarve saubhadraṃ rathasattamamc vavarṣur mārgaṇais tīkṣṇair giriṃ merum ivāmbudāḥa sa pīḍyamānaḥ samare kṛtāstro yuddhadurmadaḥc abhimanyur mahārāja tāvakān samakampayate yathā devāsure yuddhe vajrapāṇir mahāsurāna vikarṇasya tato bhallān preṣayām āsa bhāratac caturdaśa rathaśreṣṭho ghorān āśīviṣopamānd sa tair vikarṇasya rathāt pātayām āsa vīryavāne dhvajaṃ sūtaṃ hayāṃś cāsya chittvā nṛtyann ivāhavea punaś cānyāñ śarān pītān akuṇṭhāgrāñ śilāśitānc preṣayām āsa saubhadro vikarṇāya mahābalaḥa te vikarṇaṃ samāsādya kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasaḥc bhittvā dehaṃ gatā bhūmiṃ jvalanta iva pannagāḥa te śarā hemapuṅkhāgrā vyadṛśyanta mahītalec vikarṇarudhiraklinnā vamanta iva śoṇitama vikarṇaṃ vīkṣya nirbhinnaṃ tasyaivānye sahodarāḥc abhyadravanta samare saubhadrapramukhān rathāna abhiyātvā tathaivāśu rathasthān sūryavarcasaḥc avidhyan samare nyonyaṃ saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥa durmukhaḥ śrutakarmāṇaṃ viddhvā saptabhir āśugaiḥc dhvajam ekena ciccheda sārathiṃ cāsya saptabhiḥa aśvāñ jāmbūnadair jālaiḥ pracchannān vātaraṃhasaḥc jaghāna ṣaḍbhir āsādya sārathiṃ cābhyapātayata sa hatāśve rathe tiṣṭhañ śrutakarmā mahārathaḥc śaktiṃ cikṣepa saṃkruddho maholkāṃ jvalitām ivaa sā durmukhasya vipulaṃ varma bhittvā yaśasvinaḥc vidārya prāviśad bhūmiṃ dīpyamānā sutejanād durmukho vihvalas tatra niṣasāda rathe vibhod visaṃjñaṃ prekṣya te sarve bhrātaraḥ paryavārayana taṃ dṛṣṭvā virathaṃ tatra sutasomo mahābalaḥc paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ ratham āropayat svakama śrutakīrtis tathā vīro jayatsenaṃ sutaṃ tavac abhyayāt samare rājan hantukāmo yaśasvinama tasya vikṣipataś cāpaṃ śrutakīrter mahātmanaḥc ciccheda samare rājañ jayatsenaḥ sutas tavae kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena prahasann iva bhārataa taṃ dṛṣṭvā chinnadhanvānaṃ śatānīkaḥ sahodaramc abhyapadyata tejasvī siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥa śatānīkas tu samare dṛḍhaṃ visphārya kārmukamb nanāda sumahānādaṃ prabhinna iva vāraṇaḥc vivyādha daśabhis tūrṇaṃ jayatsenaṃ śilīmukhaiḥa athānyena sutīkṣṇena sarvāvaraṇabhedināc śatānīko jayatsenaṃ vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśama tathā tasmin vartamāne duṣkarṇo bhrātur antikeb mumocāsmai śitān bāṇāṃs tīkṣṇān āśīviṣopamānc ciccheda samare cāpaṃ nākuleḥ krodhamūrchitaḥa athānyad dhanur ādāya bhārasādhanam uttamamc samādatta śitān bāṇāñ śatānīko mahābalaḥa tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cāmantrya duṣkarṇaṃ bhrātur agrataḥc mumoca niśitān bāṇāñ jvalitān pannagān ivaa tato sya dhanur ekena dvābhyāṃ sūtaṃ ca māriṣac ciccheda samare tūrṇaṃ taṃ ca vivyādha saptabhiḥa aśvān manojavāṃś cāsya kalmāṣān vītakalmaṣaḥc jaghāna niśitais tūrṇaṃ sarvān dvādaśabhiḥ śaraiḥa athāpareṇa bhallena sumuktena nipātināc duṣkarṇaṃ samare kruddho vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśamd sa papāta tato bhūmau vajrarugṇa iva drumaḥd sa vihvalo rathopasthe niṣasāda sutas tavaa duṣkarṇaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā pañca rājan mahārathāḥc jighāṃsantaḥ śatānīkaṃ sarvataḥ paryavārayana chādyamānaṃ śaravrātaiḥ śatānīkaṃ yaśasvinamc abhyadhāvanta saṃrabdhāḥ kekayāḥ pañca sodarāḥa tān abhyāpatataḥ prekṣya tava putrā mahārathāḥc pratyudyayur mahārāja gajā iva mahāgajāna durmukho durjayaś caiva tathā durmarṣaṇo yuvāc śatruṃjayaḥ śatrusahaḥ sarve kruddhā yaśasvinaḥe pratyudyātā mahārāja kekayān bhrātaraḥ samama rathair nagarasaṃkāśair hayair yuktair manojavaiḥc nānāvarṇavicitrābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtaiḥa varacāpadharā vīrā vicitrakavacadhvajāḥc viviśus te paraṃ sainyaṃ siṃhā iva vanād vanama teṣāṃ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ vyatiṣaktarathadvipamc avartata mahāraudraṃ nighnatām itaretarame anyonyāgaskṛtāṃ rājan yamarāṣṭravivardhanama muhūrtāstamite sūrye cakrur yuddhaṃ sudāruṇamc rathinaḥ sādinaś caiva vyakīryanta sahasraśaḥa tataḥ śāṃtanavaḥ kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc nāśayām āsa senāṃ vai bhīṣmas teṣāṃ mahātmanāme pāñcālānāṃ ca sainyāni śarair ninye yamakṣayama evaṃ bhittvā maheṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc kṛtvāvahāraṃ sainyānāṃ yayau svaśibiraṃ nṛpad nāśayām āsatur vīrau dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodaraud kauravāṇām anīkāni śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa dharmarājo pi saṃprekṣya dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarauc mūrdhni caitāv upāghrāya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śibiraṃ yayaud arjuno vāsudevaś ca kauravāṇām anīkinīmd hatvā vidrāvya ca śaraiḥ śibirāyaiva jagmatuḥ saṃjaya uvācaa atha śūrā mahārāja parasparakṛtāgasaḥc jagmuḥ svaśibirāṇy eva rudhireṇa samukṣitāḥa viśramya ca yathānyāyaṃ pūjayitvā parasparamc saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta bhūyo yuddhacikīrṣayāa tatas tava suto rājaṃś cintayābhipariplutaḥc visravac choṇitāktāṅgaḥ papracchedaṃ pitāmahama sainyāni raudrāṇi bhayānakānivyūḍhāni samyag bahuladhvajānic vidārya hatvā ca nipīḍya śūrāste pāṇḍavānāṃ tvaritā rathaughāḥa saṃmohya sarvān yudhi kīrtimantovyūhaṃ ca taṃ makaraṃ vajrakalpamc praviśya bhīmena nibarhito smighoraiḥ śarair mṛtyudaṇḍaprakāśaiḥa kruddhaṃ tam udvīkṣya bhayena rājansaṃmūrchito nālabhaṃ śāntim adyac icche prasādāt tava satyasaṃdhaprāptuṃ jayaṃ pāṇḍaveyāṃś ca hantuma tenaivam uktaḥ prahasan mahātmāduryodhanaṃ jātamanyuṃ viditvāc taṃ pratyuvācāvimanā manasvīgaṅgāsutaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥa pareṇa yatnena vigāhya senāṃsarvātmanāhaṃ tava rājaputrac icchāmi dātuṃ vijayaṃ sukhaṃ cana cātmānaṃ chādaye haṃ tvadarthea ete tu raudrā bahavo mahārathāyaśasvinaḥ śūratamāḥ kṛtāstrāḥc ye pāṇḍavānāṃ samare sahāyājitaklamāḥ krodhaviṣaṃ vamantia te neha śakyāḥ sahasā vijetuṃvīryonnaddhāḥ kṛtavairās tvayā cac ahaṃ hy etān pratiyotsyāmi rājansarvātmanā jīvitaṃ tyajya vīraa raṇe tavārthāya mahānubhāvana jīvitaṃ rakṣyatamaṃ mamādyac sarvāṃs tavārthāya sadevadaityāṃllokān daheyaṃ kim u śatrūṃs tavehaa tat pāṇḍavān yodhayiṣyāmi rājanpriyaṃ ca te sarvam ahaṃ kariṣyec śrutvaiva caitat paramapratītoduryodhanaḥ prītamanā babhūvaa sarvāṇi sainyāni tataḥ prahṛṣṭonirgacchatety āha nṛpāṃś ca sarvānc tadājñayā tāni viniryayur drutaṃrathāśvapādātagajāyutānia rathadantisaṃsthāvāteritā bhrāmyamāṇāḥ samantātc nānāraṅgāḥ samare tatra rājanmeghair yuktā vidyutaḥ khe yathaivaa dhanūṃṣi visphārayatāṃ nṛpāṇāṃbabhūva śabdas tumulo tighoraḥc vimathyato bāhlikaḥ saha bāhlikaiḥc trigartarājaś ca balī māgadhaś ca sudurjayaḥa bṛhadbalaś ca kausalyaś citraseno viviṃśatiḥb kṛpaś ca saha sodaryais tava rājan padānugaiḥc rathāś ca bahusāhasrāḥ śobhamānā mahādhvajāḥa deśajāś ca hayā rājan svārūḍhā hayasādibhiḥc gajendrāś ca madodvṛttāḥ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥa padātāś ca tathā śūrā nānāpraharaṇāyudhāḥc nānādeśasamutpannās tvadarthe yoddhum udyatāḥa ete cānye ca bahavas tvadarthe tyaktajīvitāḥc devān api raṇe jetuṃ samarthā iti me matiḥa avaśyaṃ tu mayā rājaṃs tava vācyaṃ hitaṃ sadāc aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥe vāsudevasahāyāś ca mahendrasamavikramāḥa sarvathāhaṃ tu rājendra kariṣye vacanaṃ tavac pāṇḍavān vā raṇe jeṣye māṃ vā jeṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥa evam uktvā dadau cāsmai viśalyakaraṇīṃ śubhāmc oṣadhīṃ vīryasaṃpannāṃ viśalyaś cābhavat tadāa tataḥ prabhāte vimale svenānīkena vīryavānc avyūhata svayaṃ vyūhaṃ bhīṣmo vyūhaviśāradaḥa maṇḍalaṃ manujaśreṣṭha nānāśastrasamākulamc saṃpūrṇaṃ yodhamukhyaiś ca tathā dantipadātibhiḥa rathair anekasāhasraiḥ samantāt parivāritamc aśvavṛndair mahadbhiś ca ṛṣṭitomaradhāribhiḥa nāge nāge rathāḥ sapta sapta cāśvā rathe rathec anv aśvaṃ daśa dhānuṣkā dhānuṣke sapta carmiṇaḥa evaṃvyūhaṃ mahārāja tava sainyaṃ mahārathaiḥc sthitaṃ raṇāya mahate bhīṣmeṇa yudhi pālitama daśāśvānāṃ sahasrāṇi dantināṃ ca tathaiva cac rathānām ayutaṃ cāpi putrāś ca tava daṃśitāḥe citrasenādayaḥ śūrā abhyarakṣan pitāmahama rakṣyamāṇaś ca taiḥ śūrair gopyamānāś ca tena tec saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta rājānaś ca mahābalāḥa duryodhanas tu samare daṃśito ratham āsthitaḥc vyabhrājata śriyā juṣṭo yathā śakras triviṣṭapea tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīt putrāṇāṃ tava bhāratac rathaghoṣaś ca tumulo vāditrāṇāṃ ca nisvanaḥa bhīṣmeṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ vyūḍhaḥ pratyaṅmukho yudhic maṇḍalaḥ sumahāvyūho durbhedyo mitraghātināme sarvataḥ śuśubhe rājan raṇe rīṇāṃ durāsadaḥa maṇḍalaṃ tu samālokya vyūhaṃ paramadāruṇamc svayaṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā vyūhaṃ vajram athākarota tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu yathāsthānam avasthitāḥc rathinaḥ sādinaś caiva siṃhanādam athānadana bibhitsavas tato vyūhaṃ niryayur yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥc itaretarataḥ śūrāḥ sahasainyāḥ prahāriṇaḥa bhāradvājo yayau matsyaṃ drauṇiś cāpi śikhaṇḍinamc svayaṃ duryodhano rājā pārṣataṃ samupādravata nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca rājan madreśam īyatuḥc vindānuvindāv āvantyāv irāvantam abhidrutaua sarve nṛpās tu samare dhanaṃjayam ayodhayanc bhīmaseno raṇe yatto hārdikyaṃ samavārayata citrasenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca tathā durmarṣaṇaṃ vibhoc ārjuniḥ samare rājaṃs tava putrān ayodhayata prāgjyotiṣaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ haiḍimbo rākṣasottamaḥc abhidudrāva vegena matto mattam iva dvipama alambusas tato rājan sātyakiṃ yuddhadurmadamc sasainyaṃ samare kruddho rākṣasaḥ samabhidravata bhūriśravā raṇe yatto dhṛṣṭaketum ayodhayatc śrutāyuṣaṃ tu rājānaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥa cekitānas tu samare kṛpam evānvayodhayatc śeṣāḥ pratiyayur yattā bhīmam eva mahārathama tato rājasahasrāṇi parivavrur dhanaṃjayamc śaktitomaranārācagadāparighapāṇayaḥa arjuno tha bhṛśaṃ kruddho vārṣṇeyam idam abravītc paśya mādhava sainyāni dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃyugee vyūḍhāni vyūhaviduṣā gāṅgeyena mahātmanāa yuddhābhikāmāñ śūrāṃś ca paśya mādhava daṃśitānc trigartarājaṃ sahitaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ paśya keśavaa adyaitān pātayiṣyāmi paśyatas te janārdanac ya ime māṃ yaduśreṣṭha yoddhukāmā raṇājirea evam uktvā tu kaunteyo dhanurjyām avamṛjya cac vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi narādhipagaṇān pratia te pi taṃ parameṣvāsāḥ śaravarṣair apūrayanc taḍāgam iva dhārābhir yathā prāvṛṣi toyadāa hāhākāro mahān āsīt tava sainye viśāṃ patec chādyamānau bhṛśaṃ kṛṣṇau śarair dṛṣṭvā mahāraṇea devā devarṣayaś caiva gandharvāś ca mahoragāḥc vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmur dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇau tathāgataua tataḥ kruddho rjuno rājann aindram astram udīrayatc tatrādbhutam apaśyāma vijayasya parākramama śastravṛṣṭiṃ parair muktāṃ śaraughair yad avārayatc na ca tatrāpy anirbhinnaḥ kaś cid āsīd viśāṃ patea teṣāṃ rājasahasrāṇāṃ hayānāṃ dantināṃ tathāc dvābhyāṃ tribhiḥ śaraiś cānyān pārtho vivyādha māriṣaa te hanyamānāḥ pārthena bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yayuḥc agādhe majjamānānāṃ bhīṣmas trātābhavat tadāa āpatadbhis tu tais tatra prabhagnaṃ tāvakaṃ balamc saṃcukṣubhe mahārāja vātair iva mahārṇavaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa tathā pravṛtte saṃgrāme nivṛtte ca suśarmaṇic prabhagneṣu ca vīreṣu pāṇḍavena mahātmanāa kṣubhyamāṇe bale tūrṇaṃ sāgarapratime tavac pratyudyāte ca gāṅgeye tvaritaṃ vijayaṃ pratia dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājan raṇe pārthasya vikramamc tvaramāṇaḥ samabhyetya sarvāṃs tān abravīn nṛpāna teṣāṃ ca pramukhe śūraṃ suśarmāṇaṃ mahābalamc madhye sarvasya sainyasya bhṛśaṃ saṃharṣayan vacaḥa eṣa bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yoddhukāmo dhanaṃjayamc sarvātmanā kuruśreṣṭhas tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥa taṃ prayāntaṃ parānīkaṃ sarvasainyena bhāratamc saṃyattāḥ samare sarve pālayadhvaṃ pitāmahama bāḍham ity evam uktvā tu tāny anīkāni sarvaśaḥc narendrāṇāṃ mahārāja samājagmuḥ pitāmahama tataḥ prayātaḥ sahasā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo rjunamc raṇe bhāratam āyāntam āsasāda mahābalama mahāśvetāśvayuktena bhīmavānaraketunāc mahatā meghanādena rathenāti virājataa samare sarvasainyānām upayātaṃ dhanaṃjayamc abhavat tumulo nādo bhayād dṛṣṭvā kirīṭinama abhīśuhastaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca dṛṣṭvādityam ivāparamc madhyaṃdinagataṃ saṃkhye na śekuḥ prativīkṣituma tathā śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śvetāśvaṃ śvetakārmukamc na śekuḥ pāṇḍavā draṣṭuṃ śvetagraham ivoditama sa sarvataḥ parivṛtas trigartaiḥ sumahātmabhiḥc bhrātṛbhis tava putraiś ca tathānyaiś ca mahārathaiḥa bhāradvājas tu samare matsyaṃ vivyādha patriṇāc dhvajaṃ cāsya śareṇājau dhanuś caikena cicchidea tad apāsya dhanuś chinnaṃ virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥc anyad ādatta vegena dhanur bhārasahaṃ dṛḍhame śarāṃś cāśīviṣākārāñ jvalitān pannagān ivaa droṇaṃ tribhiḥ pravivyādha caturbhiś cāsya vājinaḥc dhvajam ekena vivyādha sārathiṃ cāsya pañcabhiḥe dhanur ekeṣuṇāvidhyat tatrākrudhyad
