dvijarṣabhaḥa tasya droṇo vadhīd aśvāñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc aṣṭābhir bharataśreṣṭha sūtam ekena patriṇāa sa hatāśvād avaplutya syandanād dhatasārathiḥc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ śaṅkhasya rathināṃ varaḥa tatas tu tau pitāputrau bhāradvājaṃ rathe sthitauc mahatā śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsatur balāta bhāradvājas tataḥ kruddhaḥ śaram āśīviṣopamamc cikṣepa samare tūrṇaṃ śaṅkhaṃ prati janeśvaraa sa tasya hṛdayaṃ bhittvā pītvā śoṇitam āhavec jagāma dharaṇiṃ bāṇo lohitārdrīkṛtacchaviḥa sa papāta rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājaśarāhataḥc dhanus tyaktvā śarāṃś caiva pitur eva samīpataḥa hataṃ svam ātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā virāṭaḥ prādravad bhayātc utsṛjya samare droṇaṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakama bhāradvājas tatas tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūmc dārayām āsa samare śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa śikhaṇḍy api mahārāja drauṇim āsādya saṃyugec ājaghāna bhruvor madhye nārācais tribhir āśugaiḥa sa babhau naraśārdūlo lalāṭe saṃsthitais tribhiḥc śikharaiḥ kāñcanamayair merus tribhir ivocchritaiḥa aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddho nimeṣārdhāc chikhaṇḍinaḥc sūtaṃ dhvajam atho rājaṃs turagān āyudhaṃ tathāe śarair bahubhir uddiśya pātayām āsa saṃyugea sa hatāśvād avaplutya rathād vai rathināṃ varaḥc khaḍgam ādāya niśitaṃ vimalaṃ ca śarāvarame śyenavad vyacarat kruddhaḥ śikhaṇḍī śatrutāpanaḥa sakhaḍgasya mahārāja caratas tasya saṃyugec nāntaraṃ dadṛśe drauṇis tad adbhutam ivābhavata tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi bahūni bharatarṣabhac preṣayām āsa samare drauṇiḥ paramakopanaḥa tām āpatantīṃ samare śaravṛṣṭiṃ sudāruṇāmc asinā tīkṣṇadhāreṇa ciccheda balināṃ varaḥa tato sya vimalaṃ drauṇiḥ śatacandraṃ manoramamc carmācchinad asiṃ cāsya khaṇḍayām āsa saṃyugee śitaiḥ subahuśo rājaṃs taṃ ca vivyādha patribhiḥa śikhaṇḍī tu tataḥ khaḍgaṃ khaṇḍitaṃ tena sāyakaiḥc āvidhya vyasṛjat tūrṇaṃ jvalantam iva pannagama tam āpatantaṃ sahasā kālānalasamaprabhamc ciccheda samare drauṇir darśayan pāṇilāghavame śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca vivyādha śarair bahubhir āyasaiḥa śikhaṇḍī tu bhṛśaṃ rājaṃs tāḍyamānaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ mādhavasya mahātmanaḥa sātyakis tu tataḥ kruddho rākṣasaṃ krūram āhavec alambusaṃ śarair ghorair vivyādha balinaṃ balīa rākṣasendras tatas tasya dhanuś ciccheda bhāratac ardhacandreṇa samare taṃ ca vivyādha sāyakaiḥe māyāṃ ca rākṣasīṃ kṛtvā śaravarṣair avākiratf athānyad dhanur ādāya bhārasādhanam uttamama tatrādbhutam apaśyāma śaineyasya parākramamc nāsaṃbhramad yat samare vadhyamānaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa aindram astraṃ ca vārṣṇeyo yojayām āsa bhāratac vijayād yad anuprāptaṃ mādhavena yaśasvināa tad astraṃ bhasmasāt kṛtvā māyāṃ tāṃ rākṣasīṃ tadāc alambusaṃ śarair ghorair abhyākirata sarvaśaḥe parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥa tat tathā pīḍitaṃ tena mādhavena mahātmanāc pradudrāva bhayād rakṣo hitvā sātyakim āhavea tam ajeyaṃ rākṣasendraṃ saṃkhye maghavatā apic śaineyaḥ prāṇadaj jitvā yodhānāṃ tava paśyatāma nyahanat tāvakāṃś cāpi sātyakiḥ satyavikramaḥc niśitair bahubhir bāṇais te dravanta bhayārditāḥa etasminn eva kāle tu drupadasyātmajo balīc dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja tava putraṃ janeśvarame chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa saṃchādyamāno viśikhair dhṛṣṭadyumnena bhāratac vivyathe na ca rājendra tava putro janeśvaraḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca samare tūrṇaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥc ṣaṣṭyā ca triṃśatā caiva tad adbhutam ivābhavata tasya senāpatiḥ kruddho dhanuś ciccheda māriṣac hayāṃś ca caturaḥ śīghraṃ nijaghāna mahārathaḥe śaraiś cainaṃ suniśitaiḥ kṣipraṃ vivyādha saptabhiḥa sa hatāśvān mahābāhur avaplutya rathād balīc padātir asim udyamya prādravat pārṣataṃ pratia śakunis taṃ samabhyetya rājagṛddhī mahābalaḥc rājānaṃ sarvalokasya ratham āropayat svakama tato nṛpaṃ parājitya pārṣataḥ paravīrahāc nyahanat tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vajrapāṇir ivāsurama kṛtavarmā raṇe bhīmaṃ śarair ārchan mahārathamc pracchādayām āsa ca taṃ mahāmegho raviṃ yathāa tataḥ prahasya samare bhīmasenaḥ paraṃtapaḥc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ sāyakān kṛtavarmaṇea tair ardyamāno tirathaḥ sātvataḥ śastrakovidaḥc nākampata mahārāja bhīmaṃ cārchac chitaiḥ śaraiḥa tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc sārathiṃ pātayām āsa dhvajaṃ ca supariṣkṛtama śarair bahuvidhaiś cainam ācinot paravīrahāc śakalīkṛtasarvāṅgaḥ śvāvidvat samadṛśyataa hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇaṃ vṛṣakasya rathaṃ yayauc syālasya te mahārāja tava putrasya paśyataḥa bhīmaseno pi saṃkruddhas tava sainyam upādravatc nijaghāna ca saṃkruddho daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa bahūnīha vicitrāṇi dvairathāni sma saṃjayac pāṇḍūnāṃ māmakaiḥ sārdham aśrauṣaṃ tava jalpataḥa na caiva māmakaṃ kaṃ cid dhṛṣṭaṃ śaṃsasi saṃjayac nityaṃ pāṇḍusutān hṛṣṭān abhagnāṃś caiva śaṃsasia jīyamānān vimanaso māmakān vigataujasaḥc vadase saṃyuge sūta diṣṭam etad asaṃśayam saṃjaya uvācaa yathāśakti yathotsāhaṃ yuddhe ceṣṭanti tāvakāḥc darśayānāḥ paraṃ śaktyā pauruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabhaa gaṅgāyāḥ suranadyā vai svādubhūtaṃ yathodakamc mahodadhiguṇābhyāsāl lavaṇatvaṃ nigacchatia tathā tat pauruṣaṃ rājaṃs tāvakānāṃ mahātmanāmc prāpya pāṇḍusutān vīrān vyarthaṃ bhavati saṃyugea ghaṭamānān yathāśakti kurvāṇān karma duṣkaramc na doṣeṇa kuruśreṣṭha kauravān gantum arhasia tavāparādhāt sumahān saputrasya viśāṃ patec pṛthivyāḥ prakṣayo ghoro yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥa ātmadoṣāt samutpannaṃ śocituṃ nārhase nṛpac na hi rakṣanti rājānaḥ sarvārthān nāpi jīvitama yuddhe sukṛtināṃ lokān icchanto vasudhādhipāḥc camūṃ vigāhya yudhyante nityaṃ svargaparāyaṇāḥa pūrvāhṇe tu mahārāja prāvartata janakṣayaḥc tan mamaikamanā bhūtvā śṛṇu devāsuropamama āvantyau tu maheṣvāsau mahātmānau mahābalauc irāvantam abhiprekṣya sameyātāṃ raṇotkaṭaue teṣāṃ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇama irāvāṃs tu susaṃkruddho bhrātarau devarūpiṇauc vivyādha niśitais tūrṇaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥe tāv enaṃ pratyavidhyetāṃ samare citrayodhinaua yudhyatāṃ hi tathā rājan viśeṣo na vyadṛśyatac yatatāṃ śatrunāśāya kṛtapratikṛtaiṣiṇāma irāvāṃs tu tato rājann anuvindasya sāyakaiḥc caturbhiś caturo vāhān anayad yamasādanama bhallābhyāṃ ca sutīkṣṇābhyāṃ dhanuḥ ketuṃ ca māriṣac ciccheda samare rājaṃs tad adbhutam ivābhavata tyaktvānuvindo tha rathaṃ vindasya ratham āsthitaḥc dhanur gṛhītvā navamaṃ bhārasādhanam uttamama tāv ekasthau raṇe vīrāv āvantyau rathināṃ varauc śarān mumucatus tūrṇam irāvati mahātmania tābhyāṃ muktā mahāvegāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥc divākarapathaṃ prāpya chādayām āsur ambarama irāvāṃs tu tataḥ kruddho bhrātarau tau mahārathauc vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa sārathiṃ cāpy apātayata tasmin nipatite bhūmau gatasattve tha sārathauc rathaḥ pradudrāva diśaḥ samudbhrāntahayas tataḥa tau sa jitvā mahārāja nāgarājasutāsutaḥc pauruṣaṃ khyāpayaṃs tūrṇaṃ vyadhamat tava vāhinīma sā vadhyamānā samare dhārtarāṣṭrī mahācamūḥc vegān bahuvidhāṃś cakre viṣaṃ pītveva mānavaḥa haiḍimbo rākṣasendras tu bhagadattaṃ samādravatc rathenādityavarṇena sadhvajena mahābalaḥa tataḥ prāgjyotiṣo rājā nāgarājaṃ samāsthitaḥc yathā vajradharaḥ pūrvaṃ saṃgrāme tārakāmayea tatra devāḥ sagandharvā ṛṣayaś ca samāgatāḥc viśeṣaṃ na sma vividur haiḍimbabhagadattayoḥa yathā surapatiḥ śakras trāsayām āsa dānavānc tathaiva samare rājaṃs trāsayām āsa pāṇḍavāna tena vidrāvyamāṇās te pāṇḍavāḥ sarvatodiśamc trātāraṃ nābhyavindanta sveṣv anīkeṣu bhārataa bhaimaseniṃ rathasthaṃ tu tatrāpaśyāma bhāratac śeṣā vimanaso bhūtvā prādravanta mahārathāḥa nivṛtteṣu tu pāṇḍūnāṃ punaḥ sainyeṣu bhāratab naiṣṭhikīṃ buddhim āsthāya svargāya bharatottamāḥc āsīn niṣṭānako ghoras tava sainyeṣu saṃyugea ghaṭotkacas tato rājan bhagadattaṃ mahāraṇec śaraiḥ pracchādayām āsa meruṃ girim ivāmbudaḥa nihatya tāñ śarān rājā rākṣasasya dhanuścyutānc bhaimaseniṃ raṇe tūrṇaṃ sarvamarmasv atāḍayata sa tāḍyamāno bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc na vivyathe rākṣasendro bhidyamāna ivācalaḥa tasya prāgjyotiṣaḥ kruddhas tomarān sa caturdaśac preṣayām āsa samare tāṃś ca ciccheda rākṣasaḥa sa tāṃś chittvā mahābāhus tomarān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc bhagadattaṃ ca vivyādha saptatyā kaṅkapatribhiḥa tataḥ prāgjyotiṣo rājan prahasann iva bhāratac tasyāśvāṃś caturaḥ saṃkhye pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥa sa hatāśve rathe tiṣṭhan rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavānc śaktiṃ cikṣepa vegena prāgjyotiṣagajaṃ pratia tām āpatantīṃ sahasā hemadaṇḍāṃ suvegitāmc tridhā ciccheda nṛpatiḥ sā vyakīryata medinīma śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā haiḍimbaḥ prādravad bhayātc yathendrasya raṇāt pūrvaṃ namucir daityasattamaḥa taṃ vijitya raṇe śūraṃ vikrāntaṃ khyātapauruṣamc ajeyaṃ samare rājan yamena varuṇena caa pāṇḍavīṃ samare senāṃ saṃmamarda sakuñjaraḥc yathā vanagajo rājan mṛdnaṃś carati padminīma madreśvaras tu samare yamābhyāṃ saha saṃgataḥc svasrīyau chādayāṃ cakre śaraughaiḥ pāṇḍunandanaua sahadevas tu samare mātulaṃ vīkṣya saṃgatamc avārayac charaugheṇa megho yadvad divākarama chādyamānaḥ śaraugheṇa hṛṣṭarūpataro bhavatc tayoś cāpy abhavat prītir atulā mātṛkāraṇāta tataḥ prahasya samare nakulasya mahārathaḥb dhvajaṃ ciccheda bāṇena dhanuś caikena māriṣab athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ chādayann iva bhāratab nijaghāna raṇe taṃ tu sūtaṃ cāsya nyapātayatc aśvān vai caturo rājaṃś caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥe preṣayām āsa samare yamasya sadanaṃ pratia hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥc āruroha tato yānaṃ bhrātur eva yaśasvinaḥa ekasthau tu raṇe śūrau dṛḍhe vikṣipya kārmukec madrarājarathaṃ kruddhau chādayām āsatuḥ kṣaṇāta sa cchādyamāno bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc svasrīyābhyāṃ naravyāghro nākampata yathācalaḥe prahasann iva tāṃ cāpi śaravṛṣṭiṃ jaghāna haf pṛṣatkānāṃ sahasrāṇi prahasann iva tāv apif sṛjan rurodha samare megho vṛṣṭyā yathācalama sahadevas tataḥ kruddhaḥ śaram udyamya vīryavānc madrarājam abhiprekṣya preṣayām āsa bhārataa sa śaraḥ preṣitas tena garutmān iva vegavānc madrarājaṃ vinirbhidya nipapāta mahītalea sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopasthe mahārathaḥc niṣasāda mahārāja kaśmalaṃ ca jagāma haa taṃ visaṃjñaṃ nipatitaṃ sūtaḥ saṃprekṣya saṃyugec apovāha rathenājau yamābhyām abhipīḍitama dṛṣṭvā madreśvararathaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ parāṅmukhamc sarve vimanaso bhūtvā nedam astīty acintayana nirjitya mātulaṃ saṃkhye mādrīputrau mahārathauc dadhmatur muditau śaṅkhau siṃhanādaṃ vinedatuḥa abhidudruvatur hṛṣṭau tava sainyaṃ viśāṃ patec yathā daityacamūṃ rājann indropendrāv ivāmarau saṃjaya uvācaa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā madhyaṃ prāpte divākarec śrutāyuṣam abhiprekṣya codayām āsa vājinaḥa abhyadhāvat tato rājā śrutāyuṣam ariṃdamamc vinighnan sāyakais tīkṣṇair navabhir nataparvabhiḥa sa saṃvārya raṇe rājā preṣitān dharmasūnunāc śarān sapta maheṣvāsaḥ kaunteyāya samarpayata te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhavec asūn iva vicinvanto dehe tasya mahātmanaḥa pāṇḍavas tu bhṛśaṃ viddhas tena rājñā mahātmanāc raṇe varāhakarṇena rājānaṃ hṛdi vivyadhea athāpareṇa bhallena ketuṃ tasya mahātmanaḥc rathaśreṣṭho rathāt tūrṇaṃ bhūmau pārtho nyapātayata ketuṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutāyuḥ sa tu pārthivaḥc pāṇḍavaṃ viśikhais tīkṣṇai rājan vivyādha saptabhiḥa tataḥ krodhāt prajajvāla dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc yathā yugānte bhūtāni dhakṣyann iva hutāśanaḥa kruddhaṃ tu pāṇḍavaṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvarākṣasāḥc pravivyathur mahārāja vyākulaṃ cāpy abhūj jagata sarveṣāṃ caiva bhūtānām idam āsīn manogatamc trīṃl lokān adya saṃkruddho nṛpo yaṃ dhakṣyatīti vaia ṛṣayaś caiva devāś ca cakruḥ svastyayanaṃ mahatc lokānāṃ nṛpa śāntyarthaṃ krodhite pāṇḍave tadāa sa ca krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ sṛkkiṇī parilelihanc dadhārātmavapur ghoraṃ yugāntādityasaṃnibhama tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni tāvakāni viśāṃ patec nirāśāny abhavaṃs tatra jīvitaṃ prati bhārataa sa tu dhairyeṇa taṃ kopaṃ saṃnivārya mahāyaśāḥc śrutāyuṣaḥ praciccheda muṣṭideśe mahad dhanuḥa athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ nārācena stanāntarec nirbibheda raṇe rājā sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa satvaraṃ caraṇe rājaṃs tasya vāhān mahātmanaḥc nijaghāna śaraiḥ kṣipraṃ sūtaṃ ca sumahābalaḥa hatāśvaṃ tu rathaṃ tyaktvā dṛṣṭvā rājñas tu pauruṣamc vipradudrāva vegena śrutāyuḥ samare tadāa tasmiñ jite maheṣvāse dharmaputreṇa saṃyugec duryodhanabalaṃ rājan sarvam āsīt parāṅmukhama etat kṛtvā mahārāja dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc vyāttānano yathā kālas tava sainyaṃ jaghāna haa cekitānas tu vārṣṇeyo gautamaṃ rathināṃ varamc prekṣatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥa saṃnivārya śarāṃs tāṃs tu kṛpaḥ śāradvato yudhic cekitānaṃ raṇe yattaṃ rājan vivyādha patribhiḥa athāpareṇa bhallena dhanuś ciccheda māriṣac sārathiṃ cāsya samare kṣiprahasto nyapātayate hayāṃś cāsyāvadhīd rājann ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathīa so vaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ gadāṃ jagrāha sātvataḥc sa tayā vīraghātinyā gadayā gadināṃ varaḥe gautamasya hayān hatvā sārathiṃ ca nyapātayata bhūmiṣṭho gautamas tasya śarāṃś cikṣepa ṣoḍaśac te śarāḥ sātvataṃ bhittvā prāviśanta dharātalama cekitānas tataḥ kruddhaḥ punaś cikṣepa tāṃ gadāmc gautamasya vadhākāṅkṣī vṛtrasyeva puraṃdaraḥa tām āpatantīṃ vimalām aśmagarbhāṃ mahāgadāmc śarair anekasāhasrair vārayām āsa gautamaḥa cekitānas tataḥ khaḍgaṃ kośād uddhṛtya bhāratac lāghavaṃ param āsthāya gautamaṃ samupādravata gautamo pi dhanus tyaktvā pragṛhyāsiṃ susaṃśitamc vegena mahatā rājaṃś cekitānam upādravata tāv ubhau balasaṃpannau nistriṃśavaradhāriṇauc nistriṃśābhyāṃ sutīkṣṇābhyām anyonyaṃ saṃtatakṣatuḥa nistriṃśavegābhihatau tatas tau puruṣarṣabhauc dharaṇīṃ samanuprāptau sarvabhūtaniṣevitāme mūrchayābhiparītāṅgau vyāyāmena ca mohitaua tato bhyadhāvad vegena karakarṣaḥ suhṛt tayāc cekitānaṃ tathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā samaradurmadame ratham āropayac cainaṃ sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa tathaiva śakuniḥ śūraḥ syālas tava viśāṃ patec āropayad rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ gautamaṃ rathināṃ varama saumadattiṃ tathā kruddho dhṛṣṭaketur mahābalaḥc navatyā sāyakaiḥ kṣipraṃ rājan vivyādha vakṣasia saumadattir uraḥsthais tair bhṛśaṃ bāṇair aśobhatac madhyaṃdine mahārāja raśmibhis tapano yathāa bhūriśravās tu samare dhṛṣṭaketuṃ mahārathamc hatasūtahayaṃ cakre virathaṃ sāyakottamaiḥa virathaṃ cainam ālokya hatāśvaṃ hatasārathimc mahatā śaravarṣeṇa chādayām āsa saṃyugea sa ca taṃ ratham utsṛjya dhṛṣṭaketur mahāmanāḥc āruroha tato yānaṃ śatānīkasya māriṣaa citraseno vikarṇaś ca rājan durmarṣaṇas tathāc rathino hemasaṃnāhāḥ saubhadram abhidudruvuḥa abhimanyos tatas tais tu ghoraṃ yuddham avartatac śarīrasya yathā rājan vātapittakaphais tribhiḥa virathāṃs tava putrāṃs tu kṛtvā rājan mahāhavec na jaghāna naravyāghraḥ smaran bhīmavacas tadāa tato rājñāṃ bahuśatair gajāśvarathayāyibhiḥc saṃvṛtaṃ samare bhīṣmaṃ devair api durāsadama prayāntaṃ śīghram udvīkṣya paritrātuṃ sutāṃs tavac abhimanyuṃ samuddiśya bālam ekaṃ mahārathame vāsudevam uvācedaṃ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥa codayāśvān hṛṣīkeśa yatraite bahulā rathāḥc ete hi bahavaḥ śūrāḥ kṛtāstrā yuddhadurmadāḥe yathā na hanyur naḥ senāṃ tathā mādhava codayaa evam uktaḥ sa vārṣṇeyaḥ kaunteyenāmitaujasāb satvaraṃ bālarakṣārthaṃ gacchāv eti dhanaṃjayaḥc rathaṃ śvetahayair yuktaṃ preṣayām āsa saṃyugea niṣṭānako mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣac yad arjuno raṇe kruddhaḥ saṃyātas tāvakān pratia samāsādya tu kaunteyo rājñas tān bhīṣmarakṣiṇaḥc suśarmāṇam atho rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīta jānāmi tvāṃ yudhi śreṣṭham atyantaṃ pūrvavairiṇamb tatas tvaṃ samare yoddhuṃ rājabhir bahubhir vṛtaḥc paryāyasyādya saṃprāptaṃ phalaṃ paśya sudāruṇame adya te darśayiṣyāmi pūrvapretān pitāmahāna evaṃ saṃjalpatas tasya bībhatsoḥ śatrughātinaḥc śrutvāpi paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ suśarmā rathayūthapaḥe na cainam abravīt kiṃ cic chubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubhama abhi gatvārjunaṃ vīraṃ rājabhir bahubhir vṛtaḥc purastāt pṛṣṭhataś caiva pārśvataś caiva sarvataḥa parivāryārjunaṃ saṃkhye tava putraiḥ sahānaghac śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa meghair iva divākarama tataḥ pravṛttaḥ sumahān saṃgrāmaḥ śoṇitodakaḥc tāvakānāṃ ca samare pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārata saṃjaya uvācaa sa tudyamānas tu śarair dhanaṃjayaḥpadā hato nāga iva śvasan balīc bāṇena bāṇena mahārathānāṃciccheda cāpāni raṇe prasahyaa saṃchidya cāpāni ca tāni rājñāṃteṣāṃ raṇe vīryavatāṃ kṣaṇenac vivyādha bāṇair yugapan mahātmāniḥśeṣatāṃ teṣv atha manyamānaḥa nipetur ājau rudhirapradigdhāste tāḍitāḥ śakrasutena rājanc vibhinnagātrāḥ patitottamāṅgāgatāsavaś chinnatanutrakāyāḥa mahīṃ gatāḥ pārthabalābhibhūtāvicitrarūpā yugapad vineśuḥc dṛṣṭvā hatāṃs tān yudhi rājaputrāṃstrigartarājaḥ prayayau kṣaṇenaa teṣāṃ rathānām atha pṛṣṭhagopādvātriṃśad anye byapatanta pārthamc tathaiva te saṃparivārya pārthaṃvikṛṣya cāpāni mahāravāṇie avīvṛṣan bāṇamahaughavṛṣṭyāyathā giriṃ toyadharā jalaughaiḥa saṃpīḍyamānas tu śaraughavṛṣṭyādhanaṃjayas tān yudhi jātaroṣaḥc ṣaṣṭyā śaraiḥ saṃyati tailadhautairjaghāna tān apy atha pṛṣṭhagopāna ṣaṣṭiṃ rathāṃs tān avajitya saṃkhyedhanaṃjayaḥ prītamanā yaśasvīc athātvarad bhīṣmavadhāya jiṣṇurbalāni rājñāṃ samare nihatyaa trigartarājo nihatān samīkṣyamahārathāṃs tān atha bandhuvargānc raṇe puraskṛtya narādhipāṃs tāñjagāma pārthaṃ tvarito vadhāyaa abhidrutaṃ cāstrabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaṃdhanaṃjayaṃ vīkṣya śikhaṇḍimukhyāḥc abhyudyayus te śitaśastrahastārirakṣiṣanto ratham arjunasyaa pārtho pi tān āpatataḥ samīkṣyatrigartarājñā sahitān nṛvīrānc vidhvaṃsayitvā samare dhanuṣmāngāṇḍīvamuktair niśitaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥe bhīṣmaṃ yiyāsur yudhi saṃdadarśaduryodhanaṃ saindhavādīṃś ca rājñaḥa āvārayiṣṇūn abhisaṃprayāyamuhūrtam āyodhya balena vīraḥc utsṛjya rājānam anantavīryojayadrathādīṃś ca nṛpān mahaujāḥe yayau tato bhīmabalo manasvīgāṅgeyam ājau śaracāpapāṇiḥf bhīṣmo pi dṛṣṭvā samare kṛtāstrānf sa pāṇḍavānāṃ rathino bhyudārānf vihāya saṃgrāmamukhe dhanaṃjayaṃf javena pārthaṃ punar ājagāmaa yudhiṣṭhiraś cograbalo mahātmāsamāyayau tvarito jātakopaḥc madrādhipaṃ samabhityajya saṃkhyesvabhāgam āptaṃ tam anantakīrtiḥe sārdhaṃ sa mādrīsutabhīmasenairbhīṣmaṃ yayau śāṃtanavaṃ raṇāyaa taiḥ saṃprayuktaḥ sa mahārathāgryairgaṅgāsutaḥ samare citrayodhīc na vivyathe śāṃtanavo mahātmāsamāgataiḥ pāṇḍusutaiḥ samastaiḥa athaitya rājā yudhi satyasaṃdhojayadratho tyugrabalo manasvīc ciccheda cāpāni mahārathānāṃprasahya teṣāṃ dhanuṣā vareṇaa yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhīmasenaṃ yamau capārthaṃ tathā yudhi saṃjātakopaḥc duryodhanaḥ krodhaviṣo mahātmājaghāna bāṇair analaprakāśaiḥa kṛpeṇa śalyena śalena caivatathā vibho citrasenena cājaub te vāridhārāś ca yathādrirājaṃb tathā ca varṣanti mahānubhāvāḥc viddhāḥ śarais te tivivṛddhakopairdevā yathā daityagaṇaiḥ sametaiḥa chinnāyudhaṃ śāṃtanavena rājāśikhaṇḍinaṃ prekṣya ca jātakopaḥc ajātaśatruḥ samare mahātmāśikhaṇḍinaṃ kruddha uvāca vākyama uktvā tathā tvaṃ pitur agrato māmahaṃ haniṣyāmi mahāvrataṃ tamc bhīṣmaṃ śaraughair vimalārkavarṇaiḥsatyaṃ vadāmīti kṛtā pratijñāa tvayā na caināṃ saphalāṃ karoṣidevavrataṃ yan na nihaṃsi yuddhec mithyāpratijño bhava mā nṛvīrarakṣasva dharmaṃ ca kulaṃ yaśaś caa prekṣasva bhīṣmaṃ yudhi bhīmavegaṃsarvāṃs tapantaṃ mama sainyasaṃghānc śaraughajālair atitigmatejaiḥkālaṃ yathā mṛtyukṛtaṃ kṣaṇenaa nikṛttacāpaḥ samarānapekṣaḥparājitaḥ śāṃtanavena rājñāc vihāya bandhūn atha sodarāṃś cakva yāsyase nānurūpaṃ tavedama dṛṣṭvā hi bhīṣmaṃ tam anantavīryaṃbhagnaṃ ca sainyaṃ dravamāṇam evamc bhīto si nūnaṃ drupadasya putratathā hi te mukhavarṇo prahṛṣṭaḥa ājñāyamāne pi dhanaṃjayenamahāhave saṃprasakte nṛvīrac kathaṃ hi bhīṣmāt prathitaḥ pṛthivyāṃbhayaṃ tvam adya prakaroṣi vīraa sa dharmarājasya vaco niśamyarūkṣākṣaraṃ vipralāpānubaddhamc pratyādeśaṃ manyamāno mahātmāpratatvare bhīṣmavadhāya rājana tam āpatantaṃ mahatā javenaśikhaṇḍinaṃ bhīṣmam abhidravantamc āvārayām āsa hi śalya enaṃśastreṇa ghoreṇa sudurjayenaa sa cāpi dṛṣṭvā samudīryamāṇamastraṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabhāvamc nāsau vyamuhyad drupadasya putrorājan mahendrapratimaprabhāvaḥa tasthau ca tatraiva mahādhanuṣmāñśarais tad astraṃ pratibādhamānaḥc athādade vāruṇam anyad astraṃśikhaṇḍy athograṃ pratighātāya tasyae tad astram astreṇa vidāryamāṇaṃkhasthāḥ surā dadṛśuḥ pārthivāś caa bhīṣmas tu rājan samare mahātmādhanuḥ sucitraṃ dhvajam eva cāpic chittvānadat pāṇḍusutasya vīroyudhiṣṭhirasyājamīḍhasya rājñaḥa tataḥ samutsṛjya dhanuḥ sabāṇaṃyudhiṣṭhiraṃ vīkṣya bhayābhibhūtamc gadāṃ pragṛhyābhipapāta saṃkhyejayadrathaṃ bhīmasenaḥ padātiḥa tam āpatantaṃ mahatā javenajayadrathaḥ sagadaṃ bhīmasenamc vivyādha ghorair yamadaṇḍakalpaiḥśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pañcaśataiḥ samantāta acintayitvā sa śarāṃs tarasvīvṛkodaraḥ krodhaparītacetāḥc jaghāna vāhān samare samastānāraṭṭajān sindhurājasya saṃkhyea tato bhivīkṣyāpratimaprabhāvastavātmajas tvaramāṇo rathenac abhyāyayau bhīmasenaṃ nihantuṃsamudyatāstraḥ surarājakalpaḥd jayadratho bhagnavāhaṃ rathaṃ taṃd tyaktvā yayau yatra rājā kurūṇāmd bhayena bhīmasya sa mūḍhacetāḥd sasaubalas tatra yuddhasya bhītaḥa bhīmo py athainaṃ sahasā vinadyapratyudyayau gadayā tarjamānaḥc samudyatāṃ tāṃ yamadaṇḍakalpāṃdṛṣṭvā gadāṃ te kuravaḥ samantāta vihāya sarve tava putram ugraṃpātaṃ gadāyāḥ parihartukāmāḥc apakrāntās tumule saṃvimardesudāruṇe bhārata mohanīyea amūḍhacetās tv atha citrasenomahāgadām āpatantīṃ nirīkṣyac rathaṃ samutsṛjya padātir ājaupragṛhya khaḍgaṃ vimalaṃ ca carmae avaplutaḥ siṃha ivācalāgrājjagāma cānyaṃ bhuvi bhūmideśama gadāpi sā prāpya rathaṃ sucitraṃsāśvaṃ sasūtaṃ vinihatya saṃkhyec jagāma bhūmiṃ jvalitā maholkābhraṣṭāmbarād gām iva saṃpatantīa āścaryabhūtaṃ sumahat tvadīyādṛṣṭvaiva tad bhārata saṃprahṛṣṭāḥc sarve vineduḥ sahitāḥ samantātpupūjire tava putraṃ sasainyāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa virathaṃ taṃ samāsādya citrasenaṃ manasvinamc ratham āropayām āsa vikarṇas tanayas tavaa tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne tumule saṃkule bhṛśamc bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tūrṇaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram upādravata tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ samakampanta sṛñjayāḥc mṛtyor āsyam anuprāptaṃ menire ca yudhiṣṭhirama yidhiṣṭhiro pi kauravyo yamābhyāṃ sahitaḥ prabhuḥc maheṣvāsaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ yayaua tataḥ śarasahasrāṇi pramuñcan pāṇḍavo yudhic bhīṣmaṃ saṃchādayām āsa yathā megho divākarama tena samyak praṇītāni śarajālāni bhāratac patijagrāha gāṅgeyaḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa tathaiva śarajālāni bhīṣmeṇāstāni māriṣac ākāśe samadṛśyanta khagamānāṃ vrajā ivaa nimeṣārdhāc ca kaunteyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhic adṛśyaṃ samare cakre śarajālena bhāgaśaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā kauravyasya mahātmanaḥc nārācaṃ preṣayām āsa kruddha āśīviṣopamama asaṃprāptaṃ tatas taṃ tu kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥc ciccheda samare rājan bhīṣmas tasya dhanuścyutama taṃ tu chittvā raṇe bhīṣmo nārācaṃ kālasaṃmitamc nijaghne kauravendrasya hayān kāñcanabhūṣaṇānd hatāśve tu rathe tiṣṭhañ śaktiṃ cikṣepa dharmarāṭd tām āpatantīṃ sahasā kālapāśopamāṃ śitāmd ciccheda samare bhīṣmaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa hatāśvaṃ tu rathaṃ tyaktvā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ nakulasya mahātmanaḥa yamāv api susaṃkruddhaḥ samāsādya raṇe tadāc śaraiḥ saṃchādayām āsa bhīṣmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥd bhīṣmo pi rathināṃ śreṣṭho vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥd bhrātarau tau mahāvīryau śatrusainyabhayaṃkaraua tau tu dṛṣṭvā mahārāja bhīṣmabāṇaprapīḍitauc jagāmātha parāṃ cintāṃ bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣayāa tato yudhiṣṭhiro vaśyān rājñas tān samacodayatc bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ sarve nihateti suhṛdgaṇāna tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitamc mahatā rathavaṃśena parivavruḥ pitāmahama sa samantāt parivṛtaḥ pitā devavratas tavac cikrīda dhanuṣā rājan pātayāno mahārathāna taṃ carantaṃ raṇe pārthā dadṛśuḥ kauravaṃ yudhic mṛgamadhyaṃ praviśyeva yathā siṃhaśiśuṃ vanea tarjayānaṃ raṇe śūrāṃs trāsayānaṃ ca sāyakaiḥc dṛṣṭvā tresur mahārāja siṃhaṃ mṛgagaṇā ivaa raṇe bharatasiṃhasya dadṛśuḥ kṣatriyā gatimc agner vāyusahāyasya yathā kakṣaṃ didhakṣataḥa śirāṃsi rathināṃ bhīṣmaḥ pātayām āsa saṃyugec tālebhya iva pakvāni phalāni kuśalo naraḥa patadbhiś ca mahārāja śirobhir dharaṇītalec babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ patatām aśmanām ivaa tasmiṃs tu tumule yuddhe vartamāne sudāruṇec sarveṣām eva sainyānām āsīd vyatikaro mahāna bhinneṣu teṣu vyūheṣu kṣatriyā itaretaramc ekam ekaṃ samāhūya yuddhāyaivopatasthirea śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bharatānāṃ pitāmahamc abhidudrāva vegena tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta anādṛtya tato bhīṣmas taṃ śikhaṇḍinam āhavec prayayau sṛñjayān kruddhaḥ strītvaṃ cintya śikhaṇḍinaḥa sṛñjayās tu tato hṛṣṭā dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaṃ mahārathamc siṃhanādān bahuvidhāṃś cakruḥ śaṅkhavimiśritāna tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ vyatiṣaktarathadvipamc aparāṃ diśam āsthāya sthite savitari prabhoa dhṛṣṭadyumno tha pāñcālyaḥ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc pīḍayantau bhṛśaṃ sainyaṃ śaktitomaravṛṣṭibhiḥe śastraiś ca bahubhī rājañ jaghnatus tāvakān raṇea te hanyamānāḥ samare tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabhac āryāṃ yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā na tyajanti sma saṃyugame yathotsāhaṃ ca samare jaghnur lokaṃ mahārathāḥa tatrākrando mahān āsīt tāvakānāṃ mahātmanāmc vadhyatāṃ samare rājan pārṣatena mahātmanāa taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ tāvakānāṃ mahārathauc vindānuvindāv āvantyau pārṣataṃ patyupasthitaua tau tasya turagān hatvā tvaramāṇau mahārathauc chādayām āsatur ubhau śaravarṣeṇa pārṣatama avaplutyātha pāñcālyo rathāt tūrṇaṃ mahābalaḥc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ sātyakeḥ sumahātmanaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥc āvantyau samare kruddhāv abhyayāt sa paraṃtapaua tathaiva tava putro pi sarvodyogena māriṣac vindānuvindāv āvantyau parivāryopatasthivāna arjunaś cāpi saṃkruddhaḥ kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabhac ayodhayata saṃgrāme vajrapāṇir ivāsurāna droṇaś ca samare kruddhaḥ putrasya priyakṛt tavac vyadhamat sarvapāñcālāṃs tūlarāśim ivānalaḥa duryodhanapurogās tu putrās tava viśāṃ patec parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ yuyudhuḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahaa tato duryodhano rājā lohitāyati bhāskarec abravīt tāvakān sarvāṃs tvaradhvam iti bhārataa yudhyatāṃ tu tathā teṣāṃ kurvatāṃ karma duṣkaramc astaṃ girim athārūḍhe naprakāśati bhāskarea prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitaughataraṅgiṇīc gomāyugaṇasaṃkīrṇā kṣaṇena rajanīmukhea śivābhir aśivābhiś ca ruvadbhir bhairavaṃ ravamc ghoram āyodhanaṃ jajñe bhūtasaṃghasamākulama rākṣasāś ca piśācāś ca tathānye piśitāśanāḥc samantato vyadṛśyanta śataśo tha sahasraśaḥd mattā rudhiragandhena piśitena ca te nṛpāḥd āsvādyāsvādya nṛtyante nādaṃ muñcanti bhīṣaṇamd kabandhāni ca nṛtyanti dhanur hastāni saṃyuged prāsam ālambya niśitaṃ nistriṃśaṃ nirmalaṃ mahata arjuno tha suśarmādīn rājñas tān sapadānugānc vijitya pṛtanāmadhye yayau svaśibiraṃ pratia yudhiṣṭhiro pi kauravyo bhrātṛbhyāṃ sahitas tadāc yayau svaśibiraṃ rājā niśāyāṃ senayā vṛtaḥa bhīmaseno pi rājendra duryodhanamukhān rathānc avajitya tataḥ saṃkhye yayau svaśibiraṃ pratia duryodhano pi nṛpatiḥ parivārya mahāraṇec bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ tūrṇaṃ prayātaḥ śibiraṃ pratia droṇo drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥc parivārya camūṃ sarvāṃ prayayuḥ śibiraṃ pratia tathaiva sātyakī rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc parivārya raṇe yodhān yayatuḥ śibiraṃ pratia evam ete mahārāja tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac paryavartanta sahitā niśākāle paraṃtapāḥa tataḥ svaśibiraṃ gatvā pāṇḍavāḥ kuravas tathāc nyaviśanta mahārāja pūjayantaḥ parasparama rakṣāṃ kṛtvātmanaḥ śūrā nyasya gulmān yathāvidhic apanīya ca śalyāṃs te snātvā ca vividhair jalaiḥa kṛtasvastyayanāḥ sarve saṃstūyantaś ca bandibhiḥc gītavāditraśabdena vyakrīḍanta yaśasvinaḥa muhūrtam iva tat sarvam abhavat svargasaṃnibhamc na hi yuddhakathāṃ kāṃ cit tatra cakrur mahārathāḥa te prasupte bale tatra pariśrāntajane nṛpac hastyaśvabahule rājan prekṣaṇīye babhūvatuḥ saṃjaya uvācaa pariṇāmya niśāṃ tāṃ tu sukhasuptā janeśvarāḥc kuravaḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva punar yuddhāya niryayuḥa tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīt senayor ubhayor apic nirgacchamānayoḥ saṃkhye sāgarapratimo mahāna tato duryodhano rājā citraseno viviṃśatiḥc bhīṣmaś ca rathināṃ śreṣṭho bhāradvājaś ca vai dvijaḥa ekībhūtāḥ susaṃyattāḥ kauravāṇāṃ mahācamūḥc vyūhāya vidadhū rājan pāṇḍavān prati daṃśitāḥa bhīṣmaḥ kṛtvā mahāvyūhaṃ pitā tava viśāṃ patec sāgarapratimaṃ ghoraṃ vāhanormitaraṅgiṇama agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yayauc mālavair dākṣiṇātyaiś ca āvantyaiś ca samanvitaḥa tato nantaram evāsīd bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc pulindaiḥ pāradaiś caiva tathā kṣudrakamālavaiḥa droṇād anantaraṃ yatto bhagadattaḥ pratāpavānc māgadhaiś ca kaliṅgaiś ca piśācaiś ca viśāṃ patea prāgjyotiṣād anu nṛpaḥ kausalyo tha bṛhadbalaḥc mekalais traipuraiś caiva cicchilaiś ca samanvitaḥa bṛhadbalāt tataḥ śūras trigartaḥ prasthalādhipaḥc kāmbojair bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ yavanaiś ca sahasraśaḥa drauṇis tu rabhasaḥ śūras trigartād anu bhāratac prayayau siṃhanādena nādayāno dharātalama tathā sarveṇa sainyena rājā duryodhanas tadāc drauṇer anantaraṃ prāyāt sodaryaiḥ parivāritaḥa duryodhanād anu kṛpas tataḥ śāradvato yayauc evam eṣa mahāvyūhaḥ prayayau sāgaropamaḥa rejus tatra patākāś ca śvetacchatrāṇi cābhibhoc aṅgadāny atha citrāṇi mahārhāṇi dhanūṃṣi caa taṃ tu dṛṣṭvā mahāvyūhaṃ tāvakānāṃ mahārathaḥc yudhiṣṭhiro bravīt tūrṇaṃ pārṣataṃ pṛtanāpatima paśya vyūhaṃ maheṣvāsa nirmitaṃ sāgaropamamc prativyūhaṃ tvam api hi kuru pārṣata mācirama tataḥ sa pārṣataḥ śūro vyūhaṃ cakre sudāruṇamc śṛṅgāṭakaṃ mahārāja paravyūhavināśanama śṛṅgebhyo bhīmasenaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc rathair anekasāhasrais tathā hayapadātibhiḥa nābhyām abhūn naraśreṣṭhaḥ śvetāśvo vānaradhvajaḥc madhye yudhiṣṭhiro rājā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaua athetare maheṣvāsāḥ sahasainyā narādhipāḥc vyūhaṃ taṃ pūrayām āsur vyūhaśāstraviśāradāḥa abhimanyus tataḥ paścād virāṭaś ca mahārathaḥc draupadeyāś ca saṃhṛṣṭā rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥa evam etaṃ mahāvyūhaṃ vyūhya bhārata pāṇḍavāḥc atiṣṭhan samare śūrā yoddhukāmā jayaiṣiṇaḥa bherīśabdāś ca tumulā vimiśrāḥ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥc kṣveḍitāsphoṭitotkruṣṭaiḥ subhīmāḥ sarvatodiśama tataḥ śūrāḥ samāsādya samare te parasparamc netrair animiṣai rājann avaikṣanta prakopitāḥa manobhis te manuṣyendra pūrvaṃ yodhāḥ parasparamc yuddhāya samavartanta samāhūyetaretarama tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvahamc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca nighnatām itaretarama nārācā niśitāḥ saṃkhye saṃpatanti sma bhāratac vyāttānanā bhayakarā uragā iva saṃghaśaḥa niṣpetur vimalāḥ śaktyas tailadhautāḥ sutejanāḥc ambudebhyo yathā rājan bhrājamānāḥ śatahradāḥa gadāś ca vimalaiḥ paṭṭaiḥ pinaddhāḥ svarṇabhūṣitāḥc patantyas tatra dṛśyante giriśṛṅgopamāḥ śubhāḥe nistriṃśāś ca vyarājanta vimalāmbarasaṃnibhāḥa ārṣabhāṇi ca carmāṇi śatacandrāṇi bhāratac aśobhanta raṇe rājan patamānāni sarvaśaḥd meghāntare yathā vidyuj jvalamāneva dṛśyatea te nyonyaṃ samare sene yudhyamāne narādhipac aśobhetāṃ yathā daityadevasene samudyatee abhyadravanta samare te nyonyaṃ vai samantataḥa rathās tu rathibhis tūrṇaṃ preṣitāḥ paramāhavec yugair yugāni saṃśliṣya yuyudhuḥ pārthivarṣabhāḥa dantināṃ yudhyamānānāṃ saṃgharṣāt pāvako bhavatc danteṣu bharataśreṣṭha sadhūmaḥ sarvatodiśama prāsair abhihatāḥ ke cid gajayodhāḥ samantataḥc patamānāḥ sma dṛśyante giriśṛṅgān nagā ivaa pādātāś cāpy adṛśyanta nighnanto hi parasparamc citrarūpadharāḥ śūrā nakharaprāsayodhinaḥa anyonyaṃ te samāsādya kurupāṇḍavasainikāḥc śastrair nānāvidhair ghorai raṇe ninyur yamakṣayama tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo rathaghoṣeṇa nādayanc abhyāgamad raṇe pāṇḍūn dhanuḥśabdena mohayana pāṇḍavānāṃ rathāś cāpi nadanto bhairavasvanamc abhyadravanta saṃyattā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratac narāśvarathanāgānāṃ vyatiṣaktaṃ parasparam saṃjaya uvācaa bhīṣmaṃ tu samare kruddhaṃ pratapantaṃ samantataḥc na śekuḥ pāṇḍavā draṣṭuṃ tapantam iva bhāskarama tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni dharmaputrasya śāsanātc abhyadravanta gāṅgeyaṃ mardayantaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa sa tu bhīṣmo raṇaślāghī somakān sahasṛñjayānc pāñcālāṃś ca maheṣvāsān pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥa te vadhyamānā bhīṣmeṇa pāñcālāḥ somakaiḥ sahac bhīṣmam evābhyayus tūrṇaṃ tyaktvā mṛtyukṛtaṃ bhayama sa teṣāṃ rathināṃ vīro bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhic ciccheda sahasā rājan bāhūn atha śirāṃsi caa virathān rathinaś cakre pitā devavratas tavac patitāny uttamāṅgāni hayebhyo hayasādināma nirmanuṣyāṃś ca mātaṅgāñ śayānān parvatopamānc apaśyāma mahārāja bhīṣmāstreṇa pramohitāna na tatrāsīt pumān kaś cit pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ patec anyatra rathināṃ śreṣṭhād bhīmasenān mahābalāta sa hi bhīṣmaṃ samāsādya tāḍayām āsa saṃyugec tato niṣṭānako ghoro bhīṣmabhīmasamāgamea babhūva sarvasainyānāṃ ghorarūpo bhayānakaḥc tathaiva pāṇḍavā hṛṣṭāḥ siṃhanādam athānadana tato duryodhano rājā sodaryaiḥ parivāritaḥc bhīṣmaṃ jugopa samare vartamāne janakṣayea bhīmas tu sārathiṃ hatvā bhīṣmasya rathināṃ varaḥc vidrutāśve rathe tasmin dravamāṇe samantataḥe sunābhasya śareṇāśu śiraś ciccheda cārihāa kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena sa hato nyapatad bhuvic hate tasmin mahārāja tava putre mahārathee nāmṛṣyanta raṇe śūrāḥ sodaryāḥ sapta saṃyugea ādityaketur bahvāśī kuṇḍadhāro mahodaraḥc aparājitaḥ paṇḍitako viśālākṣaḥ sudurjayaḥa pāṇḍavaṃ citrasaṃnāhā vicitrakavacadhvajāḥc abhyadravanta saṃgrāme yoddhukāmārimardanāḥa mahodaras tu samare bhīmaṃ vivyādha patribhiḥc navabhir vajrasaṃkāśair namuciṃ vṛtrahā yathāa ādityaketuḥ saptatyā bahvāśī cāpi pañcabhiḥc navatyā kuṇḍadhāras tu viśālākṣaś ca saptabhiḥa aparājito mahārāja parājiṣṇur mahārathaḥc śarair bahubhir ānarchad bhīmasenaṃ mahābalama raṇe paṇḍitakaś cainaṃ tribhir bāṇaiḥ samardayatc sa tan na mamṛṣe bhīmaḥ śatrubhir vadham āhavea dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇāmitrakarśanaḥb aparājitasya rājendra bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc śiraś ciccheda samare śareṇa nataparvaṇāa aparājitasya sunasaṃ tava putrasya saṃyugec parājitasya bhīmena nipapāta śiro mahīma athāpareṇa bhallena kuṇḍadhāraṃ mahārathamc prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya sarvalokasya paśyataḥa tataḥ punar ameyātmā prasaṃdhāya śilīmukhamc preṣayām āsa samare paṇḍitaṃ prati bhārataa sa śaraḥ paṇḍitaṃ hatvā viveśa dharaṇītalamc yathā naraṃ nihatyāśu bhujagaḥ kālacoditaḥa viśālākṣaśiraś chittvā pātayām āsa bhūtalec tribhiḥ śarair adīnātmā smaran kleśaṃ purātanama mahodaraṃ maheṣvāsaṃ nārācena stanāntarec vivyādha samare rājan sa hato nyapatad bhuvia ādityaketoḥ ketuṃ ca chittvā bāṇena saṃyugec bhallena bhṛśatīkṣṇena śiraś ciccheda cārihāa bahvāśinaṃ tato bhīmaḥ śareṇa nataparvaṇāc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho yamasya sadanaṃ pratia pradudruvus tatas te nye putrās tava viśāṃ patec manyamānā hi tat satyaṃ sabhāyāṃ tasya bhāṣitama tato duryodhano rājā bhrātṛvyasanakarśitaḥc abravīt tāvakān yodhān bhīmo yaṃ yudhi vadhyatāma evam ete maheṣvāsāḥ putrās tava viśāṃ pateb nihatā bhīmasenena mahāvīryeṇa saṃyugec bhrātṝn saṃdṛśya nihatān prāsmaraṃs te hi tad vacaḥa yad uktavān mahāprājñaḥ kṣattā hitam anāmayamc tad idaṃ samanuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ divyadarśinaḥa lobhamohasamāviṣṭaḥ putraprītyā janādhipac na budhyase purā yat tat tathyam uktaṃ vaco mahata tathaiva hi vadhārthāya putrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavo balīc nūnaṃ jāto mahābāhur yathā hanti sma kauravāna tato duryodhano rājā bhīṣmam āsādya māriṣac duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo vilalāpātikarśitaḥa nihatā bhrātaraḥ śūrā bhīmasenena me yudhic yatamānās tathānye pi hanyante sarvasainikāḥa bhavāṃś ca madhyasthatayā nityam asmān upekṣatec so haṃ kāpatham ārūḍhaḥ paśya daivam idaṃ mamaa etac chrutvā vacaḥ krūraṃ pitā devavratas tavac duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam abravīt sāśrulocanama uktam etan mayā pūrvaṃ droṇena vidureṇa cac gāndhāryā ca yaśasvinyā tattvaṃ tāta na buddhavāna samayaś ca mayā pūrvaṃ kṛto vaḥ śatrukarśanac nāhaṃ yudhi vimoktavyo nāpy ācāryaḥ kathaṃ canaa yaṃ yaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ bhīmo drakṣyati saṃyugec haniṣyati raṇe taṃ taṃ satyam etad bravīmi tea sa tvaṃ rājan sthiro bhūtvā dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā raṇe matimc yodhayasva raṇe pārthān svargaṃ kṛtvā parāyaṇama na śakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ sendrair api surāsuraiḥc tasmād yuddhe matiṃ kṛtvā sthirāṃ yudhyasva bhārata dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa dṛṣṭvā mama hatān putrān bahūn ekena saṃjayac bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaś caiva kim akurvata saṃyugea ahany ahani me putrāḥ kṣayaṃ gacchanti saṃjayac manye haṃ sarvathā sūta daivenopahatā bhṛśama yatra me tanayāḥ sarve jīyante na jayanty utac yatra bhīṣmasya droṇasya kṛpasya ca mahātmanaḥa saumadatteś ca vīrasya bhagadattasya cobhayoḥc aśvatthāmnas tathā tāta śūrāṇāṃ sumahātmanāma anyeṣāṃ caiva vīrāṇāṃ madhyagās tanayā mamac yad ahanyanta saṃgrāme kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥa na hi duryodhano mandaḥ purā proktam abudhyatac vāryamāṇo mayā tāta bhīṣmeṇa vidureṇa caa gāndhāryā caiva durmedhāḥ satataṃ hitakāmyayāc nāvabudhyat purā mohāt tasya prāptam idaṃ phalama yad bhīmasenaḥ samare putrān mama vicetasaḥc ahany ahani saṃkruddho nayate yamasādanam saṃjaya uvācaa idaṃ tat samanuprāptaṃ kṣattur vacanam uttamamc na buddhavān asi vibho procyamānaṃ hitaṃ tadāa nivāraya sutān dyūtāt pāṇḍavān mā druheti cac suhṛdāṃ hitakāmānāṃ bruvatāṃ tat tad eva caa na śuśrūṣasi yad vākyaṃ martyaḥ pathyam ivauṣadhamc tad eva tvām anuprāptaṃ vacanaṃ sādhu bhāṣitama viduradroṇabhīṣmāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ hitaiṣiṇāmc akṛtvā vacanaṃ pathyaṃ kṣayaṃ gacchanti kauravāḥa tad etat samatikrāntaṃ pūrvam eva viśāṃ patec tasmān me śṛṇu tattvena yathā yuddham avartataa madhyāhne sumahāraudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyatac lokakṣayakaro rājaṃs tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇua tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni dharmaputrasya śāsanātc saṃrabdhāny abhyadhāvanta bhīṣmam eva jighāṃsayāa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc yuktānīkā mahārāja bhīṣmam eva samabhyayuḥd virāṭo drupadaś caiva sahitāḥ sarvasomakaiḥd abhyadravanta saṃgrāme bhīṣmam eva mahārathāḥd kekayā dhṛṣṭaketuś ca kuntibhojaś ca daṃśitaḥd yuktānīkā mahārāja bhīṣmam eva samabhyayuḥa arjuno draupadeyāś ca cekitānaś ca saṃyugec duryodhanasamādiṣṭān rājñaḥ sarvān samabhyayuḥa abhimanyus tathā vīro haiḍimbaś ca mahārathaḥc bhīmasenaś ca saṃkruddhas te bhyadhāvanta kauravāna tridhābhūtair avadhyanta pāṇḍavaiḥ kauravā yudhic tathaiva kaurave rājann avadhyanta pare raṇea droṇas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ somakān sṛñjayaiḥ sahac abhyadravata saṃkruddhaḥ preṣayiṣyan yamakṣayama tatrākrando mahān āsīt sṛñjayānāṃ mahātmanāmc vadhyatāṃ samare rājan bhāradvājena dhanvināa droṇena nihatās tatra kṣatriyā bahavo raṇec viveṣṭantaḥ sma dṛśyante vyādhikliṣṭā narā ivaa kūjatāṃ krandatāṃ caiva stanatāṃ caiva saṃyugec aniśaṃ śrūyate śabdaḥ kṣutkṛśānāṃ nṛṇām ivaa tathaiva kauraveyāṇāṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥc cakāra kadanaṃ ghoraṃ kruddhaḥ kāla ivāparaḥa vadhyatāṃ tatra sainyānām anyonyena mahāraṇec prāvartata nadī ghorā rudhiraughapravāhinīa sa saṃgrāmo mahārāja ghorarūpo bhavan mahānc kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥa tato bhīmo raṇe kruddho rabhasaś ca viśeṣataḥc gajānīkaṃ samāsādya preṣayām āsa mṛtyavea tatra bhārata bhīmena nārācābhihatā gajāḥc petuḥ seduś ca neduś ca diśaś ca paribabhramuḥa chinnahastā mahānāgāś chinnapādāś ca māriṣac krauñcavad vyanadan bhītāḥ pṛthivīm adhiśiśyirea nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca hayānīkam abhidrutauc te hayāḥ kāñcanāpīḍā rukmabhāṇḍaparicchadāḥe vadhyamānā vyadṛśyanta śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa patadbhiś ca hayai rājan samāstīryata medinīc nirjihvaiś ca śvasadbhiś ca kūjadbhiś ca gatāsubhiḥe hayair babhau naraśreṣṭha nānārūpadharair dharāa arjunena hataiḥ saṃkhye tathā bhārata vājibhiḥc prababhau vasudhā ghorā tatra tatra viśāṃ patea rathair bhagnair dhvajaiś chinnaiś chatraiś ca sumahāprabhaiḥc hārair niṣkaiḥ sakeyūraiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥd cāmaravyajanaiś chinnair nikṛttaiś ca mahāyudhaiḥd pratodaiś ca tathā chinnair vikṛtaiś ca mahāyudhaiḥa uṣṇīṣair apaviddhaiś ca patākābhiś ca sarvaṣaḥc anukarṣaiḥ śubhai rājan yoktraiś cavyasuraśmibhiḥe saṃchannā vasudhā bhāti vasante kusumair ivaa evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ pāṇḍūnām api bhāratac kruddhe śāṃtanave bhīṣme droṇe ca rathasattamea aśvatthāmni kṛpe caiva tathaiva kṛtavarmaṇic tathetareṣu kruddheṣu tāvakānām api kṣayaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa vartamāne tathā raudre rājan vīravarakṣayec śakuniḥ saubalaḥ śrīmān pāṇḍavān samupādravata tathaiva sātvato rājan hārdikyaḥ paravīrahāc abhyadravata saṃgrāme pāṇḍavānām anīkinīma tataḥ kāmbojamukhyānāṃ nadījānāṃ ca vājināmc āraṭṭānāṃ mahījānāṃ sindhujānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥa vanāyujānāṃ śubhrāṇāṃ tathā parvatavāsināmb vājināṃ bahubhiḥ saṃkhye samantāt paryavārayanc ye cāpare tittirajā javanā vātaraṃhasaḥa suvarṇālaṃkṛtair etair varmavadbhiḥ sukalpitaiḥc hayair vātajavair mukhyaiḥ pāṇḍavasya suto balīe abhyavartata tat sainyaṃ hṛṣṭarūpaḥ paraṃtapaḥa arjunasyātha dāyāda irāvān nāma vīryavānc sutāyāṃ nāgarājasya jātaḥ pārthena dhīmatāa airāvatena sā dattā anapatyā mahātmanāc patyau hate suparṇena kṛpaṇā dīnacetanāa bhāryārthaṃ tāṃ ca jagrāha pārthaḥ kāmavaśānugāmc evam eṣa samutpannaḥ parakṣetre rjunātmajaḥa sa nāgaloke saṃvṛddho mātrā ca parirakṣitaḥc pitṛvyeṇa parityaktaḥ pārthadveṣād durātmanāa rūpavān vīryasaṃpanno guṇavān satyavikramaḥc indralokaṃ jagāmāśu śrutvā tatrārjunaṃ gatama so bhigamya mahātmānaṃ pitaraṃ satyavikramamb uvāca vacanaṃ rājann ulūpītanayas tadāc abhyavādayad avyagro vinayena kṛtāñjaliḥd nyavedayata cātmānam arjunasya mahātmanaḥe irāvān asmi bhadraṃ te putraś cāhaṃ tavābhibhoa mātuḥ samāgamo yaś ca tat sarvaṃ pratyavedayatc tac ca sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam anusasmāra pāṇḍavaḥa pariṣvajya sutaṃ cāpi so tmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ guṇaiḥc prītimān abhavat pārtho devarājaniveśanea so rjunena samājñapto devaloke tadā nṛpac prītipūrvaṃ mahābāhuḥ svakāryaṃ prati bhāratad sa cāpi naraśārdūlaḥ śārdūlasamavikramaḥd abravīc ca tadā pārtham ayam asmi tadā vibhod sthitaḥ preṣyaś ca putraś ca sarvathā hy anuśādhi māmd kiṃ karomi ca te kāmaṃ kaṃ vā kāmaṃ tvam icchasid pariṣvajya sutaṃ premṇā vāsaviḥ pratyuvāca tamd prītipūrvaṃ ca kāryaṃ ca kāryaṃ prati ca mānadae yuddhakāle tvayāsmākaṃ sāhyaṃ deyam iti prabhoa bāḍham ity evam uktvā ca yuddhakāla upāgataḥc kāmavarṇajavair aśvaiḥ saṃvṛto bahubhir nṛpaa te hayāḥ kāñcanāpīḍā nānāvarṇā manojavāḥc utpetuḥ sahasā rājan haṃsā iva mahodadhaua te tvadīyān samāsādya hayasaṃghān mahājavānc kroḍaiḥ kroḍān abhighnanto ghoṇābhiś ca parasparame nipetuḥ sahasā rājan suvegābhihatā bhuvia nipatadbhis tathā taiś ca hayasaṃghaiḥ parasparamc śuśruve dāruṇaḥ śabdaḥ suparṇapatane yathāa tathaiva ca mahārāja sametyānyonyam āhavec parasparavadhaṃ ghoraṃ cakrus te hayasādinaḥa tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃkule tumule bhṛśamc ubhayor api saṃśāntā hayasaṃghāḥ samantataḥa prakṣīṇasāyakāḥ śūrā nihatāśvāḥ śramāturāḥc vilayaṃ samanuprāptās takṣamāṇāḥ parasparama tataḥ kṣīṇe hayānīke kiṃciccheṣe ca bhāratac saubalasyātmajāḥ śūrā nirgatā raṇamūrdhania vāyuvegasamasparśā jave vāyusamāṃs tathāc āruhya śīlasaṃpannān vayaḥsthāṃs turagottamāna gajo gavākṣo vṛṣakaś carmavān ārjavaḥ śukaḥc ṣaḍ ete balasaṃpannā niryayur mahato balāta vāryamāṇāḥ śakuninā svaiś ca yodhair mahābalaiḥc saṃnaddhā yuddhakuśalā raudrarūpā mahābalāḥa tad anīkaṃ mahābāho bhittvā paramadurjayamc balena mahatā yuktāḥ svargāya vijayaiṣiṇaḥe viviśus te tadā hṛṣṭā gāndhārā yuddhadurmadāḥa tān praviṣṭāṃs tadā dṛṣṭvā irāvān api vīryavānc abravīt samare yodhān vicitrābharaṇāyudhāna yathaite dhārtarāṣṭrasya yodhāḥ sānugavāhanāḥc hanyante samare sarve tathā nītir vidhīyatāma bāḍham ity evam uktvā te sarve yodhā irāvataḥc jaghnus te vai parānīkaṃ durjayaṃ samare paraiḥa tad anīkam anīkena samare vīkṣya pātitamc amṛṣyamāṇās te sarve subalasyātmajā raṇee irāvantam abhidrutya sarvataḥ paryavārayana tāḍayantaḥ śitaiḥ prāsaiś codayantaḥ parasparamc te śūrāḥ paryadhāvanta kurvanto mahad ākulama irāvān atha nirbhinnaḥ prāsais tīkṣṇair mahātmabhiḥc sravatā rudhireṇāktas tottrair viddha iva dvipaḥa urasy api ca pṛṣṭhe ca pārśvayoś ca bhṛśāhataḥc eko bahubhir atyarthaṃ dhairyād rājan na vivyathea irāvān atha saṃkruddhaḥ sarvāṃs tān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc mohayām āsa samare viddhvā parapuraṃjayaḥa prāsān uddhṛtya sarvāṃś ca svaśarīrād ariṃdamaḥc tair eva tāḍayām āsa subalasyātmajān raṇea nikṛṣya niśitaṃ khaḍgaṃ gṛhītvā ca śarāvaramc padātis tūrṇam āgacchaj jighāṃsuḥ saubalān yudhia tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇāḥ sarve te subalātmajāḥc bhūyaḥ krodhasamāviṣṭā irāvantam athādravana irāvān api khaḍgena darśayan pāṇilāghavamc abhyavartata tān sarvān saubalān baladarpitaḥa lāghavenātha carataḥ sarve te subalātmajāḥc antaraṃ nādhyagacchanta carantaḥ śīghragāminaḥa bhūmiṣṭham atha taṃ saṃkhye saṃpradṛśya tataḥ punaḥc parivārya bhṛśaṃ sarve grahītum upacakramuḥa athābhyāśagatānāṃ sa khaḍgenāmitrakarśanaḥc upahastāvahastābhyāṃ teṣāṃ gātrāṇy akṛntataa āyudhāni ca sarveṣāṃ bāhūn api ca bhūṣitānc apatanta nikṛttāṅgā gatā bhūmiṃ gatāsavaḥa vṛṣakas tu mahārāja bahudhā parivikṣataḥc amucyata mahāraudrāt tasmād vīrāvakartanāta tān sarvān patitān dṛṣṭvā bhīto duryodhanas tataḥc abhyabhāṣata saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ ghoradarśanama ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ māyāvinam ariṃdamamc vairiṇaṃ bhīmasenasya pūrvaṃ bakavadhena vaia paśya vīra yathā hy eṣa phalgunasya suto balīc māyāvī vipriyaṃ ghoram akārṣīn me balakṣayama tvaṃ ca kāmagamas tāta māyāstre ca viśāradaḥc kṛtavairaś ca pārthena tasmād enaṃ raṇe jahia bāḍham ity evam uktvā tu rākṣaso ghoradarśanaḥc prayayau siṃhanādena yatrārjunasuto yuvāa svārūḍhair yuddhakuśalair vimalaprāsayodhibhiḥc vīraiḥ prahāribhir yuktaḥ svair anīkaiḥ samāvṛtaḥd hataśeṣair mahārāja dvisāhasrair hayottamaiḥe nihantukāmaḥ samare irāvantaṃ mahābalama irāvān api saṃkruddhas tvaramāṇaḥ parākramīc hantukāmam amitraghno rākṣasaṃ pratyavārayata tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya rākṣasaḥ sumahābalaḥc tvaramāṇas tato māyāṃ prayoktum upacakramea tena māyāmayāḥ kḷptā hayās tāvanta eva hic svārūḍhā rākṣasair ghoraiḥ śūlapaṭṭiśapāṇibhiḥa te saṃrabdhāḥ samāgamya dvisāhasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥc acirād gamayām āsuḥ pretalokaṃ parasparama tasmiṃs tu nihate sainye tāv ubhau yuddhadurmadauc saṃgrāme vyavatiṣṭhetāṃ yathā vai vṛtravāsavaua ādravantam abhiprekṣya rākṣasaṃ yuddhadurmadamc irāvān krodhasaṃrabdhaḥ pratyadhāvan mahābalaḥa samabhyāśagatasyājau tasya khaḍgena durmateḥc ciccheda kārmukaṃ dīptaṃ śarāvāpaṃ ca pañcakama sa nikṛttaṃ dhanur dṛṣṭvā khaṃ javena samāviśatc irāvantam abhikruddhaṃ mohayann iva māyayāa tato ntarikṣam utpatya irāvān api rākṣasamc vimohayitvā māyābhis tasya gātrāṇi sāyakaiḥe ciccheda sarvamarmajñaḥ kāmarūpo durāsadaḥa tathā sa rākṣasaśreṣṭhaḥ śaraiḥ kṛttaḥ punaḥ punaḥc saṃbabhūva mahārāja samavāpa ca yauvanama māyā hi sahajā teṣāṃ vayo rūpaṃ ca kāmajamc evaṃ tad rākṣasasyāṅgaṃ chinnaṃ chinnaṃ vyarohataa irāvān api saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahābalamc paraśvadhena tīkṣṇena ciccheda ca punaḥ punaḥa sa tena balinā vīraś chidyamāna iva drumaḥc rākṣaso vyanadad ghoraṃ sa śabdas tumulo bhavata paraśvadhakṣataṃ rakṣaḥ susrāva rudhiraṃ bahuc tataś cukrodha balavāṃś cakre vegaṃ ca saṃyugea ārśyaśṛṅgis tato dṛṣṭvā samare śatrum ūrjitamc kṛtvā ghoraṃ mahad rūpaṃ grahītum upacakramed arjunasya sutaṃ vīram irāvantaṃ yaśasviname saṃgrāmaśiraso madhye sarveṣāṃ tatra paśyatāma tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛśīṃ māyāṃ rākṣasasya mahātmanaḥc irāvān api saṃkruddho māyāṃ sraṣṭuṃ pracakramea tasya krodhābhibhūtasya saṃyugeṣv anivartinaḥc yo nvayo mātṛkas tasya sa enam abhipedivāna sa nāgair bahuśo rājan sarvataḥ saṃvṛto raṇec dadhāra sumahad rūpam ananta iva bhogavāne tato bahuvidhair nāgaiś chādayām āsa rākṣasama chādyamānas tu nāgaiḥ sa dhyātvā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥc sauparṇaṃ rūpam āsthāya bhakṣayām āsa pannagāna māyayā bhakṣite tasminn anvaye tasya mātṛkec vimohitam irāvantam asinā rākṣaso vadhīta sakuṇḍalaṃ samukuṭaṃ padmendusadṛśaprabhamc irāvataḥ śiro rakṣaḥ pātayām āsa bhūtalea tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre rākṣasenārjunātmajec viśokāḥ samapadyanta dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ sarājakāḥa tasmin mahati saṃgrāme tādṛśe bhairave punaḥc mahān vyatikaro ghoraḥ senayoḥ samapadyataa hayā gajāḥ padātāś ca vimiśrā dantibhir hatāḥc rathāś ca dantinaś caiva pattibhis tatra sūditāḥa tathā pattirathaughāś ca hayāś ca bahavo raṇec rathibhir nihatā rājaṃs tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkulea ajānann arjunaś cāpi nihataṃ putram aurasamc jaghāna samare śūrān rājñas tān bhīṣmarakṣiṇaḥa tathaiva tāvakā rājan sṛñjayāś ca mahābalāḥc juhvataḥ samare prāṇān nijaghnur itaretarama muktakeśā vikavacā virathāś chinnakārmukāḥc bāhubhiḥ samayudhyanta samavetāḥ parasparama tathā marmātigair bhīṣmo nijaghāna mahārathānc kampayan samare senāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahābalaḥa tena yaudhiṣṭhire sainye bahavo mānavā hatāḥc dantinaḥ sādinaś caiva rathino tha hayās tathāa tatra bhārata bhīṣmasya raṇe dṛṣṭvā parākramamc atyadbhutam apaśyāma śakrasyeva parākramama tathaiva bhīmasenasya pārṣatasya ca bhāratac raudram āsīt tadā yuddhaṃ sātvatasya ca dhanvinaḥa dṛṣṭvā droṇasya vikrāntaṃ pāṇḍavān bhayam āviśatc eka eva raṇe śakto hantum asmān sasainikāna kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivīśūrair yodhavrātaiḥ samāvṛtaḥc ity abruvan mahārāja raṇe droṇena pīḍitāḥa vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme bharatarṣabhac ubhayoḥ senayoḥ śūrā nāmṛṣyanta parasparama āviṣṭā iva yudhyante rakṣobhūtā mahābalāḥc tāvakāḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca saṃrabdhās tāta dhanvinaḥa na sma paśyāmahe kaṃ cid yaḥ prāṇān parirakṣatic saṃgrāme daityasaṃkāśe tasmin yoddhā narādhipa dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa irāvantaṃ tu nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthā mahārathāḥc saṃgrāme kim akurvanta tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa irāvantaṃ tu nihataṃ saṃgrāme vīkṣya rākṣasaḥc vyanadat sumahānādaṃ bhaimasenir ghaṭotkacaḥa nadatas tasya śabdena pṛthivī sāgarāmbarāc saparvatavanā rājaṃś cacāla subhṛśaṃ tadāe antarikṣaṃ diśaś caiva sarvāś ca pradiśas tathāf celuś ca sahasā tatra tena nādena nāditāḥa taṃ śrutvā sumahānādaṃ tava sainyasya bhāratac ūrustambhaḥ samabhavad vepathuḥ sveda eva caa sarva eva ca rājendra tāvakā dīnacetasaḥc sarpavat samaveṣṭanta siṃhabhītā gajā ivaa ninadat sumahānādaṃ nirghātam iva rākṣasaḥc jvalitaṃ śūlam udyamya rūpaṃ kṛtvā vibhīṣaṇama nānāpraharaṇair ghorair vṛto rākṣasapuṃgavaiḥc ājagāma susaṃkruddhaḥ kālāntakayamopamaḥa tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya saṃkruddhaṃ bhīmadarśanamc svabalaṃ ca bhayāt tasya prāyaśo vimukhīkṛtama tato duryodhano rājā ghaṭotkacam upādravatc pragṛhya vipulaṃ cāpaṃ siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥa pṛṣṭhato nuyayau cainaṃ sravadbhiḥ parvatopamaiḥc kuñjarair daśasāhasrair vaṅgānām adhipaḥ svayama tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya gajānīkena saṃvṛtamc putraṃ tava mahārāja cukopa sa niśācaraḥa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc rākṣasānāṃ ca rājendra duryodhanabalasya caa gajānīkaṃ ca saṃprekṣya meghavṛndam ivodyatamc abhyadhāvanta saṃkruddhā rākṣasāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥa nadanto vividhān nādān meghā iva savidyutaḥc śaraśaktyṛṣṭinārācair nighnanto gajayodhinaḥa bhiṇḍipālais tathā śūlair mudgaraiḥ saparaśvadhaiḥc parvatāgraiś ca vṛkṣaiś ca nijaghnus te mahāgajāna bhinnakumbhān virudhirān bhinnagātrāṃś ca vāraṇānc apaśyāma mahārāja vadhyamānān niśācaraiḥa teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu bhagneṣu gajayodhiṣuc duryodhano mahārāja rākṣasān samupādravata amarṣavaśam āpannas tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥc mumoca niśitān bāṇān rākṣaseṣu mahābalaḥa jaghāna ca maheṣvāsaḥ pradhānāṃs tatra rākṣasānc saṃkruddho bharataśreṣṭha putro duryodhanas tavaa vegavantaṃ mahāraudraṃ vidyujjihvaṃ pramāthinamc śaraiś caturbhiś caturo nijaghāna mahārathaḥa tataḥ punar ameyātmā śaravarṣaṃ durāsadamc mumoca bharataśreṣṭha niśācarabalaṃ pratia tat tu dṛṣṭvā mahat karma putrasya tava māriṣac krodhenābhiprajajvāla bhaimasenir mahābalaḥa visphārya ca mahac cāpam indrāśanisamasvanamc abhidudrāva vegena duryodhanam ariṃdamama tam āpatantam udvīkṣya kālasṛṣṭam ivāntakamc na vivyathe mahārāja putro duryodhanas tavaa athainam abravīt kruddhaḥ krūraḥ saṃraktalocanaḥb adyānṛṇyaṃ gamiṣyāmi pitṝṇāṃ mātur eva cac ye tvayā sunṛśaṃsena dīrghakālaṃ pravāsitāḥe yac ca te pāṇḍavā rājaṃś chaladyūte parājitāḥa yac caiva draupadī kṛṣṇā ekavastrā rajasvalāc sabhām ānīya durbuddhe bahudhā kleśitā tvayād asya pāpasya durbuddhe phalaṃ prāpnuhi durmatea tava ca priyakāmena āśramasthā durātmanāc saindhavena parikliṣṭā paribhūya pitṝn mamaa eteṣām avamānānām anyeṣāṃ ca kulādhamac antam adya gamiṣyāmi yadi notsṛjase raṇama evam uktvā tu haiḍimbo mahad visphārya kārmukamc saṃdaśya daśanair oṣṭhaṃ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihana śaravarṣeṇa mahatā duryodhanam avākiratc parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa tatas tad bāṇavarṣaṃ tu duḥsahaṃ dānavair apic dadhāra yudhi rājendro yathā varṣaṃ mahādvipaḥa tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo niḥśvasann iva pannagaḥc saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ prāptaḥ putras te bharatarṣabhaa mumoca niśitāṃs tīkṣṇān nārācān pañcaviṃśatimc te patan sahasā rājaṃs tasmin rākṣasapuṃgavee āśīviṣā iva kruddhāḥ parvate gandhamādanea sa tair viddhaḥ sravan raktaṃ prabhinna iva kuñjaraḥc dadhre matiṃ vināśāya rājñaḥ sa piśitāśanaḥe jagrāha ca mahāśaktiṃ girīṇām api dāraṇīma saṃpradīptāṃ maholkābhām aśanīṃ maghavān ivac samudyacchan mahābāhur jighāṃsus tanayaṃ tavaa tām udyatām abhiprekṣya vaṅgānām adhipas tvaranc kuñjaraṃ girisaṃkāśaṃ rākṣasaṃ pratyacodayata sa nāgapravareṇājau balinā śīghragāmināc yato duryodhanarathas taṃ mārgaṃ pratyapadyatae rathaṃ ca vārayām āsa kuñjareṇa sutasya tea mārgam āvāritaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājñā vaṅgena dhīmatāc ghaṭotkaco mahārāja krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥe udyatāṃ tāṃ mahāśaktiṃ tasmiṃś cikṣepa vāraṇea sa tayābhihato rājaṃs tena bāhuvimuktayāc saṃjātarudhirotpīḍaḥ papāta ca mamāra caa pataty atha gaje cāpi vaṅgānām īśvaro balīc javena samabhidrutya jagāma dharaṇītalama duryodhano pi saṃprekṣya pātitaṃ varavāraṇamc prabhagnaṃ ca balaṃ dṛṣṭvā jagāma paramāṃ vyathāmd aśaktaḥ pratiyoddhuṃ vai dṛṣṭvā tasya parākramama kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya ātmanaś cābhimānitāmc prāpte pakramaṇe rājā tasthau girir ivācalaḥa saṃdhāya ca śitaṃ bāṇaṃ kālāgnisamatejasamc mumoca paramakruddhas tasmin ghore niśācarea tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya bāṇam indrāśaniprabhamc lāghavād vañcayām āsa mahākāyo ghaṭotkacaḥa bhūya eva nanādograḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥc trāsayan sarvabhūtāni yugānte jalado yathāa taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ tasya bhīṣmasya rakṣasaḥc ācāryam upasaṃgamya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bravīta yathaiṣa ninado ghoraḥ śrūyate rākṣaseritaḥc haiḍimbo yudhyate nūnaṃ rājñā duryodhanena haa naiṣa śakyo hi saṃgrāme jetuṃ bhūtena kena citc tatra gacchata bhadraṃ vo rājānaṃ parirakṣataa abhidrutaṃ mahābhāgaṃ rākṣasena durātmanāc etad dhi paramaṃ kṛtyaṃ sarveṣāṃ naḥ paraṃtapāḥa pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā tvaramāṇā mahārathāḥc uttamaṃ javam āsthāya prayayur yatra kauravaḥa droṇaś ca somadattaś ca bāhlikaś ca jayadrathaḥc kṛpo bhūriśravāḥ śalyaś citraseno viviṃśatiḥa aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca āvantyaś ca bṛhadbalaḥc rathāś cānekasāhasrā ye teṣām anuyāyinaḥe abhidrutaṃ parīpsantaḥ putraṃ duryodhanaṃ tavaa tad anīkam anādhṛṣyaṃ pālitaṃ lokasattamaiḥc ātatāyinam āyāntaṃ prekṣya rākṣasasattamaḥe nākampata mahābāhur maināka iva parvataḥa pragṛhya vipulaṃ cāpaṃ jñātibhiḥ parivāritaḥc śūlamudgarahastaiś ca nānāpraharaṇair apia tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc rākṣasānāṃ ca mukhyasya duryodhanabalasya caa dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ śabdaḥ sarvatas tumulo bhavatc aśrūyata mahārāja vaṃśānāṃ dahyatām ivaa śastrāṇāṃ pātyamānānāṃ kavaceṣu śarīriṇāmc śabdaḥ samabhavad rājann adrīṇām iva dīryatāma vīrabāhuvisṛṣṭānāṃ tomarāṇāṃ viśāṃ patec rūpam āsīd viyatsthānāṃ sarpāṇāṃ sarpatām ivaa tataḥ paramasaṃkruddho visphārya sumahad dhanuḥc rākṣasendro mahābāhur vinadan bhairavaṃ ravama ācāryasyārdhacandreṇa kruddhaś ciccheda kārmukamc somadattasya bhallena dhvajam unmathya cānadata bāhlikaṃ ca tribhir bāṇair abhyavidhyat stanāntarec kṛpam ekena vivyādha citrasenaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥa pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena samyak praṇihitena cac jatrudeśe samāsādya vikarṇaṃ samatāḍayate nyaṣīdat sa rathopasthe śoṇitena pariplutaḥa tataḥ punar ameyātmā nārācān daśa pañca cac bhūriśravasi saṃkruddhaḥ prāhiṇod bharatarṣabhae te varma bhittvā tasyāśu prāviśan medinītalama viviṃśateś ca drauṇeś ca yantārau samatāḍayatc tau petatū rathopasthe raśmīn utsṛjya vājināma sindhurājño rdhacandreṇa vārāhaṃ svarṇabhūṣitamc unmamātha mahārāja dvitīyenācchinad dhanuḥa caturbhir atha nārācair āvantyasya mahātmanaḥc jaghāna caturo vāhān krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥa pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena pītena niśitena cac nirbibheda mahārāja rājaputraṃ bṛhadbalame sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśata bhṛśaṃ krodhena cāviṣṭo rathastho rākṣasādhipaḥc cikṣepa niśitāṃs tīkṣṇāñ śarān āśīviṣopamāne bibhidus te mahārāja śalyaṃ yuddhaviśāradamf prāviśan bhūtalaṃ rājan valmīkam iva pannagāḥ saṃjaya uvācaa vimukhīkṛtya tān sarvāṃs tāvakān yudhi rākṣasaḥc jighāṃsur bharataśreṣṭha duryodhanam upādravata tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya rājānaṃ prati vegitamc abhyadhāvaj jighāṃsantas tāvakā yuddhadurmadāḥa tālamātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣanto mahābalāḥc tam ekam abhyadhāvanta nadantaḥ siṃhasaṃghavata athainaṃ śaravarṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayanc parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ śaradīva balāhakāḥa sa gāḍhaviddho vyathitas tottrārdita iva dvipaḥc utpapāta tadākāśaṃ samantād vainateyavata vyanadat sumahānādaṃ jīmūta iva śāradaḥc diśaḥ khaṃ pradiśaś caiva nādayan bhairavasvanaḥa rākṣasasya tu taṃ śabdaṃ śrutvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc uvāca bharataśreṣṭho bhīmasenam idaṃ vacaḥa yudhyate rākṣaso nūnaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrair mahārathaiḥc yathāsya śrūyate śabdo nadato bhairavaṃ svaname atibhāraṃ ca paśyāmi tatra tāta samāhitama pitāmahaś ca saṃkruddhaḥ pāñcālān hantum udyataḥc teṣāṃ ca rakṣaṇārthāya yudhyate phalgunaḥ paraiḥa etac chrutvā mahābāho kāryadvayam upasthitamc gaccha rakṣasva haiḍimbaṃ saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gatama bhrātur vacanam ājñāya tvaramāṇo vṛkodaraḥc prayayau siṃhanādena trāsayan sarvapārthivāne vegena mahatā rājan parvakāle yathodadhiḥa tam anvayāt satyadhṛtiḥ saucittir yuddhadurmadaḥc śreṇimān vasudānaś ca putraḥ kāśyasya cābhibhūḥa abhimanyumukhāś caiva draupadeyā mahārathāḥc kṣatradevaś ca vikrāntaḥ kṣatradharmā tathaiva caa anūpādhipatiś caiva nīlaḥ svabalam āsthitaḥc mahatā rathavaṃśena haiḍimbaṃ paryavārayana kuñjaraiś ca sadā mattaiḥ ṣaṭsahasraiḥ prahāribhiḥc abhyarakṣanta sahitā rākṣasendraṃ ghaṭotkacama siṃhanādena mahatā nemighoṣeṇa caiva hic khuraśabdaninādaiś ca kampayanto vasuṃdharāma teṣām āpatatāṃ śrutvā śabdaṃ taṃ tāvakaṃ balamc bhīmasenabhayodvignaṃ vivarṇavadanaṃ tathāe parivṛttaṃ mahārāja parityajya ghaṭotkacama tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tatra tatra mahātmanāmc tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca saṃgrāmeṣv anivartināma nānārūpāṇi śastrāṇi visṛjanto mahārathāḥc anyonyam abhidhāvantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakriree vyatiṣaktaṃ mahāraudraṃ yuddhaṃ bhīrubhayāvahama hayā gajaiḥ samājagmuḥ pādātā rathibhiḥ sahab rathā rathaiḥ samāgacchan nāgā nāgaiś ca saṃyugec anyonyaṃ samare rājan prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥa sahasā cābhavat tīvraṃ saṃnipātān mahad rajaḥc rathāśvagajapattīnāṃ padanemisamuddhatama dhūmrāruṇaṃ rajas tīvraṃ raṇabhūmiṃ samāvṛṇotc naiva sve na pare rājan samajānan parasparama pitā putraṃ na jānīte putro vā pitaraṃ tathāc nirmaryāde tathā bhūte vaiśase lomaharṣaṇea śastrāṇāṃ bharataśreṣṭha manuṣyāṇāṃ ca garjatāmc sumahān abhavac chabdo vaṃśānām iva dahyatāma gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ śoṇitāntrataraṅgiṇīc prāvartata nadī tatra keśaśaivalaśādvalāa narāṇāṃ caiva kāyebhyaḥ śirasāṃ patatāṃ raṇec śuśruve sumahāñ śabdaḥ patatām aśmanām ivaa viśiraskair manuṣyaiś ca chinnagātraiś ca vāraṇaiḥc aśvaiḥ saṃbhinnadehaiś ca saṃkīrṇābhūd vasuṃdharāa nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjanto mahārathāḥc anyonyam abhidhāvantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrirea hayā hayān samāsādya preṣitā hayasādibhiḥc samāhatya raṇe nyonyaṃ nipetur gatajīvitāḥa narā narān samāsādya krodharaktekṣaṇā bhṛśamc urāṃsy urobhir anyonyaṃ samāśliṣya nijaghnirea preṣitāś ca mahāmātrair vāraṇāḥ paravāraṇāḥc abhighnanti viṣāṇāgrair vāraṇān eva saṃyugea te jātarudhirāpīḍāḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtāḥc saṃsaktāḥ pratyadṛśyanta meghā iva savidyutaḥa ke cid bhinnā viṣāṇāgrair bhinnakumbhāś ca tomaraiḥc vinadanto bhyadhāvanta garjanto jaladā ivaa ke cid dhastair dvidhā chinnaiś chinnagātrās tathāparec nipetus tumule tasmiṃś chinnapakṣā ivādrayaḥa pārśvais tu dāritair anye vāraṇair varavāraṇāḥc mumucuḥ śoṇitaṃ bhūri dhātūn iva mahīdharāḥa nārācābhihatās tv anye tathā viddhāś ca tomaraiḥc hatārohā vyadṛśyanta viśṛṅgā iva parvatāḥa ke cit krodhasamāviṣṭā madāndhā niravagrahāḥc rathān hayān padātāṃś ca mamṛduḥ śataśo raṇea tathā hayā hayārohais tāḍitāḥ prāsatomaraiḥc tena tenābhyavartanta kurvanto vyākulā diśaḥa rathino rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥc parāṃ śaktiṃ samāsthāya cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavata svayaṃvara ivāmarde prajahrur itaretaramc prārthayānā yaśo rājan svargaṃ vā yuddhaśālinaḥa tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇec dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahat sainyaṃ prāyaśo vimukhīkṛtam saṃjaya uvācaa svasainyaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā duryodhanaḥ svayamc abhyadhāvata saṃkruddho bhīmasenam ariṃdamama pragṛhya sumahac cāpam indrāśanisamasvanamc mahatā śaravarṣeṇa pāṇḍavaṃ samavākirata ardhacandraṃ ca saṃdhāya sutīkṣṇaṃ lomavāhinamc bhīmasenasya ciccheda cāpaṃ krodhasamanvitaḥa tadantaraṃ ca saṃprekṣya tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥc saṃdadhe niśitaṃ bāṇaṃ girīṇām api dāraṇame tenorasi mahābāhur bhīmasenam atāḍayata sa gāḍhaviddho vyathitaḥ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihanc samālalambe tejasvī dhvajaṃ hemapariṣkṛtama tathā vimanasaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥc krodhenābhiprajajvāla didhakṣann iva pāvakaḥa abhimanyumukhāś caiva pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc samabhyadhāvan krośanto rājānaṃ jātasaṃbhramāḥa saṃprekṣya tān āpatataḥ saṃkruddhāñ jātasaṃbhramānc bhāradvājo bravīd vākyaṃ tāvakānāṃ mahārathāna kṣipraṃ gacchata bhadraṃ vo rājānaṃ parirakṣatac saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ prāptaṃ majjantaṃ vyasanārṇavea ete kruddhā maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc bhīmasenaṃ puraskṛtya duryodhanam upadrutāḥa nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjanto jaye ratāḥc nadanto bhairavān nādāṃs trāsayantaś ca bhūm imāma tad ācāryavacaḥ śrutvā somadattapurogamāḥc tāvakāḥ samavartanta pāṇḍavānām anīkinīma kṛpo bhūriśravāḥ śalyo droṇaputro viviṃśatiḥc citraseno vikarṇaś ca saindhavo tha bṛhadbalaḥe āvantyau ca maheṣvāsau kauravaṃ paryavārayana te viṃśatipadaṃ gatvā saṃprahāraṃ pracakrirec pāṇḍavā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca parasparajighāṃsavaḥa evam uktvā mahābāhur mahad visphārya kārmukamc bhāradvājas tato bhīmaṃ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayata bhūyaś cainaṃ mahābāhuḥ śaraiḥ śīghram avākiratc parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ śaradīva balāhakaḥa taṃ pratyavidhyad daśabhir bhīmasenaḥ śilīmukhaiḥc tvaramāṇo maheṣvāsaḥ savye pārśve mahābalaḥa sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito vayovṛddhaś ca bhāratac pranaṣṭasaṃjñaḥ sahasā rathopastha upāviśata guruṃ pravyathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā duryodhanaḥ svayamc drauṇāyaniś ca saṃkruddhau bhīmasenam abhidrutaua tāv āpatantau saṃprekṣya kālāntakayamopamauc bhīmaseno mahābāhur gadām ādāya satvaraḥa avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ tasthau girir ivācalaḥc samudyamya gadāṃ gurvīṃ yamadaṇḍopamāṃ raṇea tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā kailāsam iva śṛṅgiṇamc kauravo droṇaputraś ca sahitāv abhyadhāvatāma tāv āpatantau sahitau tvaritau balināṃ varauc abhyadhāvata vegena tvaramāṇo vṛkodaraḥa tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya saṃkruddhaṃ bhīmadarśanamc samabhyadhāvaṃs tvaritāḥ kauravāṇāṃ mahārathāḥa bhāradvājamukhāḥ sarve bhīmasenajighāṃsayāc nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi bhīmasyorasy apātayane sahitāḥ pāṇḍavaṃ sarve pīḍayantaḥ samantataḥa taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃśayaṃ prāptaṃ pīḍyamānaṃ mahārathamc abhimanyuprabhṛtayaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥe abhyadhāvan parīpsantaḥ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā sudustyajāna anūpādhipatiḥ śūro bhīmasya dayitaḥ sakhāc nīlo nīlāmbudaprakhyaḥ saṃkruddho drauṇim abhyayāte spardhate hi maheṣvāso nityaṃ droṇasutena yaḥa sa visphārya mahac cāpaṃ drauṇiṃ vivyādha patriṇāc yathā śakro mahārāja purā vivyādha dānavama vipracittiṃ durādharṣaṃ devatānāṃ bhayaṃkaramc yena lokatrayaṃ krodhāt trāsitaṃ svena tejasād sa rudreṇa jitaḥ pūrvaṃ nihato mātariśvanāa tathā nīlena nirbhinnaḥ sumukhena patatriṇāc saṃjātarudhirotpīḍo drauṇiḥ krodhasamanvitaḥa sa visphārya dhanuś citram indrāśanisamasvanamc dadhre nīlavināśāya matiṃ matimatāṃ varaḥa tataḥ saṃdhāya vimalān bhallān karmārapāyitānc jaghāna caturo vāhān pātayām āsa ca dhvajamd tataḥ ṣaṣṭhena bhallena rathāt sūtam apātayatd sūtaṃ caikena bhallena rathanīḍād apāharata saptamena ca bhallena nīlaṃ vivyādha vakṣasic sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśata mohitaṃ vīkṣya rājānaṃ nīlam abhracayopamamc ghaṭotkaco pi saṃkruddho bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥa abhidudrāva vegena drauṇim āhavaśobhinamc tathetare abhyadhāvan rākṣasā yuddhadurmadāḥd bhīmaseno pi samare nīlaṃ nīlāñjanaprabhamd āropya svarathaṃ vīro duryodhanam upādravata tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya rākṣasaṃ ghoradarśanamc abhyadhāvata tejasvī bhāradvājātmajas tvarana nijaghāna ca saṃkruddho rākṣasān bhīmadarśanānc yo bhavann agrataḥ kruddhā rākṣasasya puraḥsarāḥa vimukhāṃś caiva tān dṛṣṭvā drauṇicāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥc akrudhyata mahākāyo bhaimasenir ghaṭotkacaḥa prāduścakre mahāmāyāṃ ghorarūpāṃ sudāruṇāmc mohayan samare drauṇiṃ māyāvī rākṣasādhipaḥa tatas te tāvakāḥ sarve māyayā vimukhīkṛtāḥc anyonyaṃ samapaśyanta nikṛttān medinītalee viceṣṭamānān kṛpaṇāñ śoṇitena samukṣitāna droṇaṃ duryodhanaṃ śalyam aśvatthāmānam eva cac prāyaśaś ca maheṣvāsā ye pradhānāś ca kauravāḥa vidhvastā rathinaḥ sarve gajāś ca vinipātitāḥc hayāś ca sahayārohā vinikṛttāḥ sahasraśaḥa tad dṛṣṭvā tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vidrutaṃ śibiraṃ pratic mama prākrośato rājaṃs tathā devavratasya caa yudhyadhvaṃ mā palāyadhvaṃ māyaiṣā rākṣasī raṇec ghaṭotkacaprayukteti nātiṣṭhanta vimohitāḥe naiva te śraddadhur bhītā vadator āvayor vacaḥa tāṃś ca pradravato dṛṣṭvā jayaṃ prāptāś ca pāṇḍavāḥc ghaṭotkacena sahitāḥ siṃhanādān pracakriree śaṅkhadundubhighoṣāś ca samantāt sasvanur bhṛśama evaṃ tava balaṃ sarvaṃ haiḍimbena durātmanāc sūryāstamanavelāyāṃ prabhagnaṃ vidrutaṃ diśaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa tasmin mahati saṃkrande rājā duryodhanas tadāb parājayaṃ rākṣasena nāmṛṣyata paraṃtapac gāṅgeyam upasaṃgamya vinayenābhivādya caa tasya sarvaṃ yathāvṛttam ākhyātum upacakramec ghaṭotkacasya vijayam ātmanaś ca parājayama kathayām āsa durdharṣo viniḥśvasya punaḥ punaḥc abravīc ca tadā rājan bhīṣmaṃ kurupitāmahama bhavantaṃ samupāśritya vāsudevaṃ yathā paraiḥc pāṇḍavair vigraho ghoraḥ samārabdho mayā prabhoa ekādaśa samākhyātā akṣauhiṇyaś ca yā mamac nideśe tava tiṣṭhanti mayā sārdhaṃ paraṃtapaa so haṃ bharataśārdūla bhīmasenapurogamaiḥc ghaṭotkacaṃ samāśritya pāṇḍavair yudhi nirjitaḥa tan me dahati gātrāṇi śuṣkavṛkṣam ivānalaḥc tad icchāmi mahābhāga tvatprasādāt paraṃtapaa rākṣasāpasadaṃ hantuṃ svayam eva pitāmahac tvāṃ samāśritya durdharṣaṃ tan me kartuṃ tvam arhasia etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ rājño bharatasattamac duryodhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bravīta śṛṇu rājan mama vaco yat tvā vakṣyāmi kauravac yathā tvayā mahārāja vartitavyaṃ paraṃtapaa ātmā rakṣyo raṇe tāta sarvāvasthāsv ariṃdamac dharmarājena saṃgrāmas tvayā kāryaḥ sadānaghaa arjunena yamābhyāṃ vā bhīmasenena vā punaḥb na tu kāryas tvayā rājan haiḍimbena durātmanāc rājadharmaṃ puraskṛtya rājā rājānam ṛcchatia ahaṃ droṇaḥ kṛpo drauṇiḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥc śalyaś ca saumadattiś ca vikarṇaś ca mahārathaḥa tava ca bhrātaraḥ śūrā duḥśāsanapurogamāḥc tvadarthaṃ pratiyotsyāmo rākṣasaṃ taṃ mahābalama tasmin raudre rākṣasendre yadi te hṛcchayo mahānc ayaṃ vā gacchatu raṇe tasya yuddhāya durmateḥe bhagadatto mahīpālaḥ puraṃdarasamo yudhia etāvad uktvā rājānaṃ bhagadattam athābravītc samakṣaṃ pārthivendrasya vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥa gaccha śīghraṃ mahārāja haiḍimbaṃ yuddhadurmadamc vārayasva raṇe yatto miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvināme rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ yathendras tārakaṃ purāa tava divyāni cāstrāṇi vikramaś ca paraṃtapac samāgamaś ca bahubhiḥ purābhūd asuraiḥ sahaa tvaṃ tasya rājaśārdūla pratiyoddhā mahāhavec svabalena vṛto rājañ jahi rākṣasapuṃgavama etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ bhīṣmasya pṛtanāpateḥc prayayau siṃhanādena parān abhimukho drutama tam ādravantaṃ saṃprekṣya garjantam iva toyadamc abhyavartanta saṃkruddhāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥa bhimaseno bhimanyuś ca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥc draupadeyāḥ satyadhṛtiḥ kṣatradevaś ca māriṣaa cedipo vasudānaś ca daśārṇādhipatis tathāc supratīkena tāṃś cāpi bhagadatto py upādravata tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakamc pāṇḍūnāṃ bhagadattena yamarāṣṭravivardhanama pramuktā rathibhir bāṇā bhīmavegāḥ sutejanāḥc te nipetur mahārāja nāgeṣu ca ratheṣu caa prabhinnāś ca mahānāgā vinītā hastisādibhiḥc parasparaṃ samāsādya saṃnipetur abhītavata madāndhā roṣasaṃrabdhā viṣāṇāgrair mahāhavec bibhidur dantamusalaiḥ samāsādya parasparama hayāś ca cāmarāpīḍāḥ prāsapāṇibhir āsthitāḥc coditāḥ sādibhiḥ kṣipraṃ nipetur itaretarama pādātāś ca padātyoghais tāḍitāḥ śaktitomaraiḥc nyapatanta tadā bhūmau śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa rathinaś ca tathā rājan karṇinālīkasāyakaiḥc nihatya samare vīrān siṃhanādān vinedirea tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇec bhagadatto maheṣvāso bhīmasenam athādravata kuñjareṇa prabhinnena saptadhā sravatā madamc parvatena yathā toyaṃ sravamāṇena sarvataḥa kirañ śarasahasrāṇi supratīkaśirogataḥc airāvatastho maghavān vāridhārā ivānaghaa sa bhīmaṃ śaradhārābhis tāḍayām āsa pārthivaḥc parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥa bhīmasenas tu saṃkruddhaḥ pādarakṣān paraḥśatānc nijaghāna maheṣvāsaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥa tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān kruddho bhagadattaḥ pratāpavānc codayām āsa nāgendraṃ bhīmasenarathaṃ pratia sa nāgaḥ preṣitas tena bāṇo jyācodito yathāc abhyadhāvata vegena bhīmasenam ariṃdamama tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc abhyavartanta vegena bhīmasenapurogamāḥa kekayāś cābhimanyuś ca draupadeyāś ca sarvaśaḥc daśārṇādhipatiḥ śūraḥ kṣatradevaś ca māriṣae cedipaś citraketuś ca saṃkruddhāḥ sarva eva tea uttamāstrāṇi divyāni darśayanto mahābalāḥc tam ekaṃ kuñjaraṃ kruddhāḥ samantāt paryavārayana sa viddho bahubhir bāṇair vyarocata mahādvipaḥc saṃjātarudhirotpīḍo dhātucitra ivādrirāṭa daśārṇādhipatiś cāpi gajaṃ bhūmidharopamamc samāsthito bhidudrāva bhagadattasya vāraṇama tam āpatantaṃ samare gajaṃ gajapatiḥ sa cac dadhāra supratīko pi veleva makarālayamd dadhāra supratīkaṃ taṃ kṣatradharmā gajena tua vāritaṃ prekṣya nāgendraṃ daśārṇasya mahātmanaḥc sādhu sādhv iti sainyāni pāṇḍaveyāny apūjayana tataḥ prāgjyotiṣaḥ kruddhas tomarān vai caturdaśac prāhiṇot tasya nāgasya pramukhe nṛpasattamaa tasya varma mukhatrāṇaṃ śātakumbhapariṣkṛtamc vidārya prāviśan kṣipraṃ valmīkam iva pannagāḥa sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito nāgo bharatasattamac upāvṛttamadaḥ kṣipraṃ sa nyavartata vegataḥa pradudrāva ca vegena praṇadan bhairavaṃ svanamc sa mardamānaḥ svabalaṃ vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasāa tasmin parājite nāge pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccair yuddhāyaivopatasthirea tato bhīmaṃ puraskṛtya bhagadattam upādravanc kiranto vividhān bāṇāñ śastrāṇi vividhāni caa teṣām āpatatāṃ rājan saṃkruddhānām amarṣiṇāmc śrutvā sa ninadaṃ ghoram amarṣād gatasādhvasaḥe bhagadatto maheṣvāsaḥ svanāgaṃ pratyacodayata aṅkuśāṅguṣṭhanuditaḥ sa gajapravaro yudhic tasmin kṣaṇe samabhavat saṃvartaka ivānalaḥa rathasaṃghāṃs tathā nāgān hayāṃś ca saha sādibhiḥc pādātāṃś ca susaṃkruddhaḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥe amṛdnāt samare rājan saṃpradhāvaṃs tatas tataḥa tena saṃloḍyamānaṃ tu pāṇḍūnāṃ tad balaṃ mahatc saṃcukoca mahārāja carmevāgnau samāhitama bhagnaṃ tu svabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagadattena dhīmatāc ghaṭotkaco tha saṃkruddho bhagadattam upādravata vikaṭaḥ puruṣo rājan dīptāsyo dīptalocanaḥc rūpaṃ vibhīṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā roṣeṇa prajvalann ivaa jagrāha vipulaṃ śūlaṃ girīṇām api dāraṇamc nāgaṃ jighāṃsuḥ sahasā cikṣepa ca mahābalaḥe saviṣphuliṅgajvālābhiḥ samantāt pariveṣṭitama tam āpatantaṃ sahasā dṛṣṭvā jvālākulaṃ raṇec cikṣepa ruciraṃ tīkṣṇam ardhacandraṃ sa pārthivaḥe ciccheda sumahac chūlaṃ tena bāṇena vegavata nipapāta dvidhā chinnaṃ śūlaṃ hemapariṣkṛtamc mahāśanir yathā bhraṣṭā śakramuktā nabhogatāa śūlaṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā dvidhā kṛttaṃ sa pārthivaḥc rukmadaṇḍāṃ mahāśaktiṃ jagrāhāgniśikhopamāme cikṣepa tāṃ rākṣasasya tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta tām āpatantīṃ saṃprekṣya viyatsthām aśanīm ivac utpatya rākṣasas tūrṇaṃ jagrāha ca nanāda caa babhañja caināṃ tvarito jānuny āropya bhāratac paśyataḥ pārthivendrasya tad adbhutam ivābhavata tad avekṣya kṛtaṃ karma rākṣasena balīyasāc divi devāḥ sagandharvā munayaś cāpi vismitāḥa pāṇḍavāś ca maheṣvāsā bhīmasenapurogamāḥc sādhu sādhv iti nādena pṛthivīm anunādayana taṃ tu śrutvā mahānādaṃ prahṛṣṭānāṃ mahātmanāmc nāmṛṣyata maheṣvāso bhagadattaḥ pratāpavāna sa visphārya mahac cāpam indrāśanisamasvanamc abhidudrāva vegena pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāne visṛjan vimalāṃs tīkṣṇān nārācāñ jvalanaprabhāna bhīmam ekena vivyādha rākṣasaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc abhimanyuṃ tribhiś caiva kekayān pañcabhis tathāa pūrṇāyatavisṛṣṭena svarṇapuṅkhena patriṇāc bibheda dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ kṣatradevasya cāhavee papāta sahasā tasya saśaraṃ dhanur uttamama draupadeyāṃs tataḥ pañca pañcabhiḥ samatāḍayatc bhīmasenasya ca krodhān nijaghāna turaṃgamāna dhvajaṃ kesariṇaṃ cāsya ciccheda viśikhais tribhiḥc nirbibheda tribhiś cānyaiḥ sārathiṃ cāsya patribhiḥa sa gāḍhaviddho vyathito rathopastha upāviśatc viśoko bharataśreṣṭha bhagadattena saṃyugea tato bhīmo mahārāja viratho rathināṃ varaḥc gadāṃ pragṛhya vegena pracaskanda mahārathāta tam udyatagadaṃ dṛṣṭvā saśṛṅgam iva parvatamc tāvakānāṃ bhayaṃ ghoraṃ samapadyata bhārataa etasminn eva kāle tu pāṇḍavaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥc ājagāma mahārāja nighnañ śatrūn sahasraśaḥa yatra tau puruṣavyāghrau pitāputrau paraṃtapauc prāgjyotiṣeṇa saṃsaktau bhīmasenaghaṭotkacaua dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavo rājan yudhyamānān mahārathānc tvarito bharataśreṣṭha tatrāyād vikirañ śarāna tato duryodhano rājā tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥc senām acodayat kṣipraṃ rathanāgāśvasaṃkulāma tām āpatantīṃ sahasā kauravāṇāṃ mahācamūmc abhidudrāva vegena pāṇḍavaḥ śvetavāhanaḥa bhagadatto pi samare tena nāgena bhāratac vimṛdnan pāṇḍavabalaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram upādravata tadāsīt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ bhagadattasya māriṣac pāñcālaiḥ sṛñjayaiś caiva kekayaiś codyatāyudhaiḥa bhīmaseno pi samare tāv ubhau keśavārjunauc āśrāvayad yathāvṛttam irāvad vadham uttamam saṃjaya uvācaa putraṃ tu nihataṃ śrutvā irāvantaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo niḥśvasan pannago yathāa abravīt samare rājan vāsudevam idaṃ vacaḥc idaṃ nūnaṃ mahāprājño viduro dṛṣṭavān purāa kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca kṣayaṃ ghoraṃ mahāmatiḥc tato nivārayitavān dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvarama avadhyā bahavo vīrāḥ saṃgrāme madhusūdanac nihatāḥ kauravaiḥ saṃkhye tathāsmābhiś ca te hatāḥa arthahetor naraśreṣṭha kriyate karma kutsitamc dhig arthān yatkṛte hy evaṃ kriyate jñātisaṃkṣayaḥa adhanasya mṛtaṃ śreyo na ca jñātivadhād dhanamc kiṃ nu prāpsyāmahe kṛṣṇa hatvā jñātīn samāgatāna duryodhanāparādhena śakuneḥ saubalasya cac kṣatriyā nidhanaṃ yānti karṇadurmantritena caa idānīṃ ca vijānāmi sukṛtaṃ madhusūdanac kṛtaṃ rājñā mahābāho yācatā sma suyodhaname rājyārdhaṃ pañca vā grāmān nākārṣīt sa ca durmatiḥa dṛṣṭvā hi kṣatriyāñ śūrāñ śayānān dharaṇītalec nindāmi bhṛśam ātmānaṃ dhig astu kṣatrajīvikāma aśaktam iti mām ete jñāsyanti kṣatriyā raṇec yuddhaṃ mamaibhirucitaṃ jñātibhir madhusūdanaa saṃcodaya hayān kṣipraṃ dhārtarāṣṭracamūṃ pratic pratariṣye mahāpāraṃ bhujābhyāṃ samarodadhime nāyaṃ klībayituṃ kālo vidyate mādhava kva cita evam uktas tu pārthena keśavaḥ paravīrahāc codayām āsa tān aśvān pāṇḍurān vātaraṃhasaḥa atha śabdo mahān āsīt tava sainyasya bhāratac mārutoddhūtavegasya sāgarasyeva parvaṇid rathaṃ saṃprerayām āsa vegena tvaritojjvalama aparāhṇe mahārāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyatac parjanyasamanirghoṣo bhīṣmasya saha pāṇḍavaiḥa tato rājaṃs tava sutā bhīmasenam upādravanc parivārya raṇe droṇaṃ vasavo vāsavaṃ yathāa tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaś ca rathināṃ varaḥc bhagadattaḥ suśarmā ca dhanaṃjayam upādravana hārdikyo bāhlikaś caiva sātyakiṃ samabhidrutauc ambaṣṭhakas tu nṛpatir abhimanyum avārayata śeṣās tv anye mahārāja śeṣān eva mahārathānc tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvahama bhīmasenas tu saṃprekṣya putrāṃs tava janeśvarac prajajvāla raṇe kruddho haviṣā havyavāḍ ivaa putrās tu tava kaunteyaṃ chādayāṃ cakrire śaraiḥc prāvṛṣīva mahārāja jaladāḥ parvataṃ yathāa sa cchādyamāno bahudhā putrais tava viśāṃ patec sṛkkiṇī vilihan vīraḥ śārdūla iva darpitaḥa vyūḍhoraskaṃ tato bhīmaḥ pātayām āsa pārthivac kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena so bhavad gatajīvitaḥc   sumuktena mahāraṇec tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ  a apareṇa tu bhallena pītena niśitena cac apātayat kuṇḍalinaṃ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathāa tataḥ suniśitān pītān samādatta śilīmukhānb subahūn preṣayām āsa kopayāno mahābalaḥb tatas tu samare kruddho bhīmasenaḥ śilīmukhānc sa sapta tvarayā yuktaḥ putrāṃs te prāpya māriṣaa preṣitā bhīmasenena śarās te dṛḍhadhanvanāc apātayanta putrāṃs te rathebhyaḥ sumahārathāna anādhṛṣṭiṃ kuṇḍabhedaṃ vairāṭaṃ dīrghalocanamc dīrghabāhuṃ subāhuṃ ca tathaiva kanakadhvajama prapatanta sma te vīrā virejur bharatarṣabhac vasante puṣpaśabalāś cūtāḥ prapatitā ivaa tataḥ pradudruvuḥ śeṣāḥ putrās tava viśāṃ patec taṃ kālam iva manyanto bhīmasenaṃ mahābalama droṇas tu samare vīraṃ nirdahantaṃ sutāṃs tavab saṃdadhāra mahābāhur bhīmasenaṃ mahābalamc yathādriṃ vāridhārābhiḥ samantād vyakirac charaiḥa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma kuntīputrasya pauruṣamc droṇena vāryamāṇo pi nijaghne yat sutāṃs tavaa yathā hi govṛṣo varṣaṃ saṃdhārayati khāt patatc bhīmas tathā droṇamuktaṃ śaravarṣam adīdharatd nimīlya netre gṛhṇīyāt tathā jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥd droṇacāpasamudbhūtaṃ śaravarṣaṃ durāsadamd nimīlya nayane gṛhṇāt tathā bāṇān vṛkodaraḥa adbhutaṃ ca mahārāja tatra cakre vṛkodaraḥc yat putrāṃs te vadhīt saṃkhye droṇaṃ caiva nyayodhayata putreṣu tava vīreṣu cikrīḍārjunapūrvajaḥc mṛgeṣv iva mahārāja caran vyāghro mahābalaḥa yathā vā paśumadhyastho drāvayeta paśūn vṛkaḥc vṛkodaras tava sutāṃs tathā vyadrāvayad raṇea gāṅgeyo bhagadattaś ca gautamaś ca mahārathaḥc pāṇḍavaṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe vārayām āsur arjunama astrair astrāṇi saṃvārya teṣāṃ so tiratho raṇec pravīrāṃs tava sainyeṣu preṣayām āsa mṛtyavea abhimanyuś ca rājānam ambaṣṭhaṃ lokaviśrutamc virathaṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kārayām āsa sāyakaiḥa viratho vadhyamānaḥ sa saubhadreṇa yaśasvināc avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ savrīḍo manujādhipaḥa asiṃ cikṣepa samare saubhadrasya mahātmanaḥc āruroha rathaṃ caiva hārdikyasya mahātmanaḥa āpatantaṃ tu nistriṃśaṃ yuddhamārgaviśāradaḥc lāghavād vyaṃsayām āsa saubhadraḥ paravīrahāa vyaṃsitaṃ vīkṣya nistriṃśaṃ saubhadreṇa raṇe tadāc sādhu sādhv iti sainyānāṃ praṇādo bhūd viśāṃ pated nirāyudham athātmānaṃ sa saṃvīkṣya janādhipaa dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhās tv anye tava sainyam ayodhayanc tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve pāṇḍusainyam ayodhayana tatrākrando mahān āsīt tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratac nighnatāṃ bhṛśam anyonyaṃ kurvatāṃ karma duṣkaramd pravartam iva hārdikyaṃ ghoraṃ yuddham abhūt tataḥa anyonyaṃ hi raṇe śūrāḥ keśeṣv ākṣipya māriṣac nakhair dantair ayudhyanta muṣṭibhir jānubhis tathāa bāhubhiś ca talaiś caiva nistriṃśaiś ca susaṃśitaiḥc vivaraṃ prāpya cānyonyam anayan yamasādanama nyahanac ca pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ raṇec vyākulīkṛtasaṃkalpā yuyudhus tatra mānavāḥa raṇe cārūṇi cāpāni hemapṛṣṭhāni bhāratac hatānām apaviddhāni kalāpāś ca mahādhanāḥa jātarūpamayaiḥ puṅkhai rājataiś ca śitāḥ śarāḥc tailadhautā vyarājanta nirmuktabhujagopamāḥa hastidantatsarūn khaḍgāñ jātarūpapariṣkṛtānc carmāṇi cāpaviddhāni rukmapṛṣṭhāni dhanvināma suvarṇavikṛtaprāsān paṭṭiśān hemabhūṣitānc jātarūpamayāś carṣṭīḥ śaktyaś ca kanakojjvalāḥa apakṛttāś ca patitā musalāni gurūṇi cac parighān paṭṭiśāṃś caiva bhiṇḍipālāṃś ca māriṣaa patitāṃs tomarāṃś cāpi citrā hemapariṣkṛtāḥc kuthāś ca bahudhākārāś cāmaravyajanāni caa nānāvidhāni śastrāṇi visṛjya patitā narāḥc jīvanta iva dṛśyante gatasattvā mahārathāḥa gadāvimathitair gātrair musalair bhinnamastakāḥc gajavājirathakṣuṇṇāḥ śerate sma narāḥ kṣitaua tathaivāśvanṛnāgānāṃ śarīrair ābabhau tadāc saṃchannā vasudhā rājan parvatair iva sarvataḥa samare patitaiś caiva śaktyṛṣṭiśaratomaraiḥc nistriṃśaiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsair ayaskuntaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥa parighair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca śataghnībhis tathaiva cac śarīraiḥ śastrabhinnaiś ca samāstīryata medinīa niḥśabdair alpaśabdaiś ca śoṇitaughapariplutaiḥc gatāsubhir amitraghna vibabhau saṃvṛtā mahīa satalatraiḥ sakeyūrair bāhubhiś candanokṣitaiḥb sudhṛtair lakuṭaiś caiva saṃvṛtā tatra medinīc hastihastopamaiś chinnair ūrubhiś ca tarasvināmd sāṅgadaiś ca bhujaiś caiva vipraviddhair alaṃkṛtaiḥa baddhacūḍāmaṇidharaiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥc patitair vṛṣabhākṣāṇāṃ babhau bhārata medinīa kavacaiḥ śoṇitādigdhair viprakīrṇaiś ca kāñcanaiḥc rarāja subhṛśaṃ bhūmiḥ śāntārcibhir ivānalaiḥa vipraviddhaiḥ kalāpaiś ca patitaiś ca śarāsanaiḥc viprakīrṇaiḥ śaraiś cāpi rukmapuṅkhaiḥ samantataḥa rathaiś ca bahubhir bhagnaiḥ kiṅkiṇījālamālibhiḥc vājibhiś ca hataiḥ kīrṇaiḥ srastajihvaiḥ saśoṇitaiḥa anukarṣaiḥ patākābhir upāsaṅgair dhvajair apic pravīrāṇāṃ mahāśaṅkhair viprakīrṇaiś ca pāṇḍuraiḥa srastahastaiś ca mātaṅgaiḥ śayānair vibabhau mahīb śuśubhe dharaṇī rājan pradīptair iva parvataiḥb srastair ābharaṇaiś caiva vibabhau tu tadā mahīc nānārūpair alaṃkāraiḥ pramadevābhyalaṃkṛtāa dantibhiś cāparais tatra saprāsair gāḍhavedanaiḥc karaiḥ śabdaṃ vimuñcadbhiḥ śīkaraṃ ca muhur muhuḥe vibabhau tad raṇasthānaṃ dhamyamānair ivācalaiḥa nānārāgaiḥ kambalaiś ca paristomaiś ca dantināmb vivāritavicitrābhiḥ kuthābhiś ca samantataḥc vaiḍūryamaṇidaṇḍaiś ca patitair aṅkuśaiḥ śubhaiḥa ghaṇṭābhiś ca gajendrāṇāṃ patitābhiḥ samantataḥc vighāṭitavicitrābhiḥ kuthābhī rāṅkavais tathāa graiveyaiś citrarūpaiś ca rukmakakṣyābhir eva cac yantraiś ca bahudhā chinnais tomaraiś ca sakampanaiḥd rarāja subhṛśaṃ bhūmis tatra viśāṃ patea aśvānāṃ reṇukapilai rukmacchannair uraśchadaiḥc sādināṃ ca bhujaiś chinnaiḥ patitaiḥ sāṅgadais tathāa prāsaiś ca vimalais tīkṣṇair vimalābhis tatharṣṭibhiḥc uṣṇīṣaiś ca tathā chinnaiḥ praviddhaiś ca tatas tataḥa vicitrair ardhacandraiś ca jātarūpapariṣkṛtaiḥc aśvāstaraparistomai rāṅkavair mṛditais tathāa narendracūḍāmaṇibhir vicitraiś ca mahādhanaiḥc chatrais tathāpaviddhaiś ca cāmaravyajanair apia padmendudyutibhiś caiva vadanaiś cārukuṇḍalaiḥc kḷptaśmaśrubhir atyarthaṃ vīrāṇāṃ samalaṃkṛtaiḥa apaviddhair mahārāja suvarṇojjvalakuṇḍalaiḥc grahanakṣatraśabalā dyaur ivāsīd vasuṃdharāa evam ete mahāsene mṛdite tatra bhāratac parasparaṃ samāsādya tava teṣāṃ ca saṃyugea teṣu śrānteṣu bhagneṣu mṛditeṣu ca bhāratac rātriḥ samabhavad ghorā nāpaśyāma tato raṇama tato vahāraṃ sainyānāṃ pracakruḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥc ghore niśāmukhe raudre vartamāne sudāruṇea avahāraṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sahitāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥc nyaviśanta yathākālaṃ gatvā svaśibiraṃ tadā saṃjaya uvācaa tato duryodhano rājā śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥc duḥśāsanaś ca putras te sūtaputraś ca durjayaḥa samāgamya mahārāja mantraṃ cakrūr vivakṣitamc kathaṃ pāṇḍusutā yuddhe jetavyāḥ sagaṇā itia tato duryodhano rājā sarvāṃs tān āha mantriṇaḥc sūtaputraṃ samābhāṣya saubalaṃ ca mahābalama droṇo bhīṣmaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ saumadattiś ca saṃyugec na pārthān pratibādhante na jāne tatra kāraṇama avadhyamānās te cāpi kṣapayanti balaṃ mamac so smi kṣīṇabalaḥ karṇa kṣīṇaśastraś ca saṃyuged droṇasya pramukhe vīrā hatās te bhrātaro mamad
