bhīmasenena rādheya mama caiva ca paśyataḥa nikṛtaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūrair avadhyair daivatair apic so haṃ saṃśayam āpannaḥ prakariṣye kathaṃ raṇamd mahābala mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśāradad mantrajño mantravān dakṣo nītimān nītikovidaḥd sa śūraḥ sa ca vikrāntaḥ sūryaputraḥ pratāpavānd etan mahābhītikaraṃ pratariṣye raṇaṃ kathama tam abravīn mahārāja sūtaputro narādhipamc mā śuco bharataśreṣṭha prakariṣye priyaṃ tavaa bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tūrṇam apayātu mahāraṇātc nivṛtte yudhi gāṅgeye nyastaśastre ca bhārataa ahaṃ pārthān haniṣyāmi sanitān sarvasomakaiḥc paśyato yudhi bhīṣmasya śape satyena te nṛpaa pāṇḍaveṣu dayāṃ rājan sadā bhīṣmaḥ karoti vaic aśaktaś ca raṇe bhīṣmo jetum etān mahārathāna abhimānī raṇe bhīṣmo nityaṃ cāpi raṇapriyaḥc sa kathaṃ pāṇḍavān yuddhe jeṣyate tāta saṃgatāna sa tvaṃ śīghram ito gatvā bhīṣmasya śibiraṃ pratic anumānya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ śastraṃ nyāsaya bhārataa nyastaśastre tato bhīṣme nihatān paśya pāṇḍavānc mayaikena raṇe rājan sasuhṛdgaṇabāndhavāna evam uktas tu karṇena putro duryodhanas tavac abravīd bhrātaraṃ tatra duḥśāsanam idaṃ vacaḥa anuyātraṃ yathā sajjaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati sarvataḥc duḥśāsana tathā kṣipraṃ sarvam evopapādayaa evam uktvā tato rājan karṇam āha janeśvaraḥc anumānya raṇe bhīṣmam ito haṃ dvipadāṃ varama āgamiṣye tataḥ kṣipraṃ tvatsakāśam ariṃdamac tatas tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra prakariṣyasi saṃyugama niṣpapāta tatas tūrṇaṃ putras tava viśāṃ patec sahito bhrātṛbhiḥ sarvair devair iva śatakratuḥa tatas taṃ nṛpaśārdūlaṃ śārdūlasamavikramamc ārohayad dhayaṃ tūrṇaṃ bhrātā duḥśāsanas tadāa aṅgadī baddhamukuṭo hastābharaṇavān nṛpaḥc dhārtarāṣṭro mahārāja vibabhau sa mahendravata bhāṇḍīpuṣpanikāśena tapanīyanibhena cac anuliptaḥ parārdhyena candanena sugandhināa arajombarasaṃvītaḥ siṃhakhelagatir nṛpaḥc śuśubhe vimalārciṣmañ śaradīva divākaraḥa taṃ prayāntaṃ naravyāghraṃ bhīṣmasya śibiraṃ pratic anujagmur maheṣvāsāḥ sarvalokasya dhanvinaḥe bhrātaraś ca maheṣvāsās tridaśā iva vāsavama hayān anye samāruhya gajān anye ca bhāratac rathair anye naraśreṣṭhāḥ parivavruḥ samantataḥd padātayaś ca tvaritā nakharaprāsayodhinaḥd parivavrur maheṣvāsaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahārathama āttaśastrāś ca suhṛdo rakṣaṇārthaṃ mahīpateḥc prādurbabhūvuḥ sahitāḥ śakrasyevāmarā divia saṃpūjyamānaḥ kurubhiḥ kauravāṇāṃ mahārathaḥc prayayau sadanaṃ rājan gāṅgeyasya yaśasvinaḥe anvīyamānaḥ sahitaiḥ sodaraiḥ sarvato nṛpaḥa dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇaḥ kāle saṃbhṛtya svabhujaṃ tadāc hastihastopamaṃ śaikṣaṃ sarvaśatrunibarhaṇama pragṛhṇann añjalīn nṝṇām udyatān sarvatodiśamc śuśrāva madhurā vāco nānādeśanivāsināma saṃstūyamānaḥ sūtaiś ca māgadhaiś ca mahāyaśāḥc pūjayānaś ca tān sarvān sarvalokeśvareśvaraḥa pradīpaiḥ kāñcanais tatra gandhatailāvasecanaiḥc parivavrur mahātmānaṃ prajvaladbhiḥ samantataḥd devāsure yathendro sau saṃgrāme ca bhayaṃkarea sa taiḥ parivṛto rājā pradīpaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ śubhaiḥc śuśubhe candramā yukto dīptair iva mahāgrahaiḥa kañcukoṣṇīṣiṇas tatra vetrajharjharapāṇayaḥc protsārayantaḥ śanakais taṃ janaṃ sarvatodiśama saṃprāpya tu tato rājā bhīṣmasya sadanaṃ śubhamc avatīrya hayāc cāpi bhīṣmaṃ prāpya janeśvaraḥa abhivādya tato bhīṣmaṃ niṣaṇṇaḥ paramāsanec kāñcane sarvatobhadre spardhyāstaraṇasaṃvṛtee uvāca prāñjalir bhīṣmaṃ bāṣpakaṇṭho śrulocanaḥa tvāṃ vayaṃ samupāśritya saṃyuge śatrusūdanac utsahema raṇe jetuṃ sendrān api surāsurāna kim u pāṇḍusutān vīrān sasuhṛdgaṇabāndhavānc tasmād arhasi gāṅgeya kṛpāṃ kartuṃ mayi prabhoe jahi pāṇḍusutān vīrān mahendra iva dānavāna pūrvam uktaṃ mahābāho nihaniṣyāmi somakānc pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ karūṣāṃś ceti bhārataa tad vacaḥ satyam evāstu jahi pārthān samāgatānc somakāṃś ca maheṣvāsān satyavāg bhava bhārataa dayayā yadi vā rājan dveṣyabhāvān mama prabhoc mandabhāgyatayā vāpi mama rakṣasi pāṇḍavāna anujānīhi samare karṇam āhavaśobhinamc sa jeṣyati raṇe pārthān sasuhṛdgaṇabāndhavāna etāvad uktvā nṛpatiḥ putro duryodhanas tavac novāca vacanaṃ kiṃ cid bhīṣmaṃ bhīmaparākramam saṃjaya uvācaa vākśalyais tava putreṇa so tividdhaḥ pitāmahaḥc duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo novācāpriyam aṇv apia sa dhyātvā suciraṃ kālaṃ duḥkharoṣasamanvitaḥc śvasamāno yathā nāgaḥ praṇunno vai śalākayāa udvṛtya cakṣuṣī kopān nirdahann iva bhāratac sadevāsuragandharvaṃ lokaṃ lokavidāṃ varaḥe abravīt tava putraṃ tu sāmapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥa kiṃ nu duryodhanaivaṃ māṃ vākśalyair upavidhyasic ghaṭamānaṃ yathāśakti kurvāṇaṃ ca tava priyame juhvānaṃ samare prāṇāṃs tavaiva hitakāmyayāa yadā tu pāṇḍavaḥ śūraḥ khāṇḍave gnim atarpayatc parājitya raṇe śakraṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanama yadā ca tvāṃ mahābāho gandharvair hṛtam ojasāc amocayat pāṇḍusutaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanama dravamāṇeṣu śūreṣu sodareṣu tathābhibhoc sūtaputre ca rādheye paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanama yac ca naḥ sahitān sarvān virāṭanagare tadāc eka eva samudyātaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanama droṇaṃ ca yudhi saṃrabdhaṃ māṃ ca nirjitya saṃyugec karṇaṃ ca tvāṃ ca drauṇiṃ ca kṛpaṃ ca sumahārathame vāsāṃsi sa samādatta paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanamf tathā drauṇiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ śāradvatam athāpi caf gograhe jitavān pūrvaṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanamf vijitya ca yadā karṇaṃ sadā puruṣamāninamf uttarāyai dadau vastraṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanama nivātakavacān yuddhe vāsavenāpi durjayānc jitavān samare pārthaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanamd avaśyaṃ hitakāmena pārṣatena ca dhīmatāa ko hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ pāṇḍavaṃ rabhasaṃ raṇeb yasya goptā jagadgoptā śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥb vāsudevo nantaśaktiḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥb sarveśvaro devadevaḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥb ukto si bahuśo rājan nāradādyair maharṣibhiḥc tvaṃ tu mohān na jānīṣe vācyāvācyaṃ suyodhanaa mumūrṣur hi naraḥ sarvān vṛkṣān paśyati kāñcanānc tathā tvam api gāndhāre viparītāni paśyasia svayaṃ vairaṃ mahat kṛtvā pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥc yudhyasva tān adya raṇe paśyāmaḥ puruṣo bhavad aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥa ahaṃ tu somakān sarvān sapāñcālān samāgatānc nihaniṣye naravyāghra varjayitvā śikhaṇḍinama tair vāhaṃ nihataḥ saṃkhye gamiṣye yamasādanamc tān vā nihatya saṃgrāme prītiṃ dāsyāmi vai tavaa pūrvaṃ hi strī samutpannā śikhaṇḍī rājaveśmanic varadānāt pumāñ jātaḥ saiṣā vai strī śikhaṇḍinīa tām ahaṃ na haniṣyāmi prāṇatyāge pi bhāratac yāsau prāṅ nirmitā dhātrā saiṣā vai strī śikhaṇḍinīa sukhaṃ svapihi gāndhāre śvo smi kartā mahāraṇamc yaj janāḥ kathayiṣyanti yāvat sthāsyati medinīa evam uktas tava suto nirjagāma janeśvarac abhivādya guruṃ mūrdhnā prayayau svaṃ niveśanama āgamya tu tato rājā visṛjya ca mahājanamc praviveśa tatas tūrṇaṃ kṣayaṃ śatrukṣayaṃkaraḥe praviṣṭaḥ sa niśāṃ tāṃ ca gamayām āsa pārthivaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ prātar utthāya vai nṛpaḥc rājñaḥ samājñāpayata senāṃ yojayateti hae adya bhīṣmo raṇe kruddho nihaniṣyati somakāna duryodhanasya tac chrutvā rātrau vilapitaṃ bahuc manyamānaḥ sa taṃ rājan pratyādeśam ivātmanaḥa nirvedaṃ paramaṃ gatvā vinindya paravācyatāmc dīrghaṃ dadhyau śāṃtanavo yoddhukāmo rjunaṃ raṇea iṅgitena tu taj jñātvā gāṅgeyena vicintitamc duryodhano mahārāja duḥśāsanam acodayata duḥśāsana rathās tūrṇaṃ yujyantāṃ bhīṣmarakṣiṇaḥc dvātriṃśat tvam anīkāni sarvāṇy evābhicodayaa idaṃ hi samanuprāptaṃ varṣapūgābhicintitamc pāṇḍavānāṃ sasainyānāṃ vadho rājyasya cāgamaḥa tatra kāryam ahaṃ manye bhīṣmasyaivābhirakṣaṇamc sa no guptaḥ sukhāya syād dhanyāt pārthāṃś ca saṃyugea abravīc ca viśuddhātmā nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinamc strīpūrvako hy asau jātas tasmād varjyo raṇe mayāa lokas tad veda yad ahaṃ pituḥ priyacikīrṣayāc rājyaṃ sphītaṃ mahābāho striyaś ca tyaktavān purāa naiva cāhaṃ striyaṃ jātu na strīpūrvaṃ kathaṃ canac hanyāṃ yudhi naraśreṣṭha satyam etad bravīmi tea ayaṃ strīpūrvako rājañ śikhaṇḍī yadi te śrutaḥc udyoge kathitaṃ yat tat tathā jātā śikhaṇḍinīa kanyā bhūtvā pumāñ jātaḥ sa ca yotsyati bhāratac tasyāhaṃ pramukhe bāṇān na muñceyaṃ kathaṃ canaa yuddhe tu kṣatriyāṃs tāta pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaiṣiṇaḥc sarvān anyān haniṣyāmi saṃprāptān bāṇagocarāna evaṃ māṃ bharataśreṣṭho gāṅgeyaḥ prāha śāstravitc tatra sarvātmanā manye bhīṣmasyaivābhipālanama arakṣyamāṇaṃ hi vṛko hanyāt siṃhaṃ mahāvanec mā vṛkeṇeva śārdūlaṃ ghātayema śikhaṇḍinād mā siṃham iva kākena hataṃ bhīṣmaṃ śikhaṇḍinād paśyema puruṣavyāghra tathā nītir vidhīyatāma mātulaḥ śakuniḥ śalyaḥ kṛpo droṇo viviṃśatiḥc yattā rakṣantu gāṅgeyaṃ tasmin gupte dhruvo jayaḥa etac chrutvā tu rājāno duryodhanavacas tadāc sarvato rathavaṃśena gāṅgeyaṃ paryavārayana putrāś ca tava gāṅgeyaṃ parivārya yayur mudāc kampayanto bhuvaṃ dyāṃ ca kṣobhayantaś ca pāṇḍavāna tai rathaiś ca susaṃyuktair dantibhiś ca mahārathāḥc parivārya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ daṃśitāḥ samavasthitāḥa yathā devāsure yuddhe tridaśā vajradhāriṇamc sarve te sma vyatiṣṭhanta rakṣantas taṃ mahārathama tato duryodhano rājā punar bhrātaram abravītc savyaṃ cakraṃ yudhāmanyur uttamaujāś ca dakṣiṇame goptārāv arjunasyaitāv arjuno pi śikhaṇḍinaḥa sa rakṣyamāṇaḥ pārthena tathāsmābhir vivarjitaḥc yathā bhīṣmaṃ na no hanyād duḥśāsana tathā kurua bhrātus tad vacanaṃ śrutvā putro duḥśāsanas tavac bhīṣmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtvā prayayau senayā sahaa bhīṣmaṃ tu rathavaṃśena dṛṣṭvā tam abhisaṃvṛtamc arjuno rathināṃ śreṣṭho dhṛṣṭadyumnam uvāca haa śikhaṇḍinaṃ naravyāghra bhīṣmasya pramukhe naghac sthāpayasvādya pāñcālya tasya goptāham apy utaa tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo niryayau senayā sahac vyūhaṃ cāvyūhata mahat sarvatobhadram āhavea kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca śaibyaś caiva mahārathaḥc śakuniḥ saindhavaś caiva kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥa bhīṣmeṇa sahitāḥ sarve putraiś ca tava bhāratac agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ vyūhasya pramukhe sthitāḥa droṇo bhūriśravāḥ śalyo bhagadattaś ca māriṣac dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣam āśritya sthitā vyūhasya daṃśitāḥa aśvatthāmā somadatta āvantyau ca mahārathauc mahatyā senayā yuktā vāmaṃ pakṣam apālayana duryodhano mahārāja trigartaiḥ sarvato vṛtaḥc vyūhamadhye sthito rājan pāṇḍavān prati bhārataa alambuso rathaśreṣṭhaḥ śrutāyuś ca mahārathaḥc pṛṣṭhataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ sthitau vyūhasya daṃśitaua evam ete tadā vyūhaṃ kṛtvā bhārata tāvakāḥc saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta pratapanta ivāgnayaḥa tathā yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca mādrīputrāv ubhāv apie agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ sthitā vyūhasya daṃśitāḥa dhṛṣṭadyumno virāṭaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc sthitāḥ sainyena mahatā parānīkavināśanāḥd anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥd nānāvidhāyudhā vīrā nānāśastropaśobhitāḥa śikhaṇḍī vijayaś caiva rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥc cekitāno mahābāhuḥ kuntibhojaś ca vīryavāne sthitā raṇe mahārāja mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥa abhimanyur maheṣvāso drupadaś ca mahārathaḥb yuyudhāno maheṣvāso yudhāmanyuś ca vīryavānc kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca sthitā yuddhāya daṃśitāḥa evaṃ te pi mahāvyūhaṃ prativyūhya sudurjayamc pāṇḍavāḥ samare śūrāḥ sthitā yuddhāya māriṣaa tāvakās tu raṇe yattāḥ sahasenā narādhipāḥc abhyudyayū raṇe pārthān bhīṣmaṃ kṛtvāgrato nṛpaa tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan bhīmasenapurogamāḥc bhīṣmaṃ yuddhapariprepsuṃ saṃgrāme vijigīṣavaḥa kṣveḍāḥ kilikilāśabdān krakacān goviṣāṇikāḥc bherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavān nādayantaś ca puṣkarāne pāṇḍavā abhyadhāvanta nadanto bhairavān ravāna bherīmṛdaṅgaśaṅkhānāṃ dundubhīnāṃ ca nisvanaiḥc utkruṣṭasiṃhanādaiś ca valgitaiś ca pṛthagvidhaiḥa vayaṃ pratinadantas tān abhyagacchāma satvarāḥc sahasaivābhisaṃkruddhās tadāsīt tumulaṃ mahata tato nyonyaṃ pradhāvantaḥ saṃprahāraṃ pracakrirec tataḥ śabdena mahatā pracakampe vasuṃdharāa pakṣiṇaś ca mahāghoraṃ vyāharanto vibabhramuḥc saprabhaś coditaḥ sūryo niṣprabhaḥ samapadyataa vavuś ca tumulā vātāḥ śaṃsantaḥ sumahad bhayamc ghorāś ca ghoranirhrādāḥ śivās tatra vavāśiree vedayantyo mahārāja mahad vaiśasam āgatama diśaḥ prajvalitā rājan pāṃsuvarṣaṃ papāta cac rudhireṇa samunmiśram asthivarṣaṃ tathaiva caa rudatāṃ vāhanānāṃ ca netrebhyaḥ prāpataj jalamc susruvuś ca śakṛnmūtraṃ pradhyāyanto viśāṃ patea antarhitā mahānādāḥ śrūyante bharatarṣabhac rakṣasāṃ puruṣādānāṃ nadatāṃ bhairavān ravāna saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante gomāyubakavāyasāḥc śvānaś ca vividhair nādair bhaṣantas tatra tasthirea jvalitāś ca maholkā vai samāhatya divākaramc nipetuḥ sahasā bhūmau vedayānā mahad bhayama mahānty anīkāni mahāsamucchrayesamāgame pāṇḍavadhārtarāṣṭrayoḥc prakāśire śaṅkhamṛdaṅganisvanaiḥprakampitānīva vanāni vāyunāa narendranāgāśvasamākulānāmabhyāyatīnām aśive muhūrtec babhūva ghoṣas tumulaś camūnāṃvātoddhutānām iva sāgarāṇām saṃjaya uvācaa abhimanyū rathodāraḥ piśaṅgais turagottamaiḥc abhidudrāva tejasvī duryodhanabalaṃ mahate vikirañ śaravarṣāṇi vāridhārā ivāmbudaḥa na śekuḥ samare kruddhaṃ saubhadram arisūdanamc śastraughiṇaṃ gāhamānaṃ senāsāgaram akṣayame nivārayitum apy ājau tvadīyāḥ kurupuṃgavāḥa tena muktā raṇe rājañ śarāḥ śatrunibarhaṇāḥc kṣatriyān anayañ śūrān pretarājaniveśanama yamadaṇḍopamān ghorāñ jvalanāśīviṣopamānc saubhadraḥ samare kruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa sāyakāna rathinaṃ ca rathāt tūrṇaṃ hayapṛṣṭhāc ca sādinamc gajārohāṃś ca sagajān pātayām āsa phālguniḥa tasya tat kurvataḥ karma mahat saṃkhye dbhutaṃ nṛpāḥc pūjayāṃ cakrire hṛṣṭāḥ praśaśaṃsuś ca phālgunima tāny anīkāni saubhadro drāvayan bahv aśobhatac tūlarāśim ivādhūya mārutaḥ sarvatodiśama tena vidrāvyamāṇāni tava sainyāni bhāratac trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta paṅke magnā iva dvipāḥa vidrāvya sarvasainyāni tāvakāni narottamaḥc abhimanyuḥ sthito rājan vidhūmo gnir iva jvalana na cainaṃ tāvakāḥ sarve viṣehur arighātinamc pradīptaṃ pāvakaṃ yadvat pataṃgāḥ kālacoditāḥa praharan sarvaśatrubhyaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥc adṛśyata maheṣvāsaḥ savajra iva vajrabhṛta hemapṛṣṭhaṃ dhanuś cāsya dadṛśe carato diśaḥc toyadeṣu yathā rājan bhrājamānāḥ śatahvadāḥa śarāś ca niśitāḥ pītā niścaranti sma saṃyugec vanāt phulladrumād rājan bhramarāṇām iva vrajāḥa tathaiva caratas tasya saubhadrasya mahātmanaḥc rathena meghaghoṣeṇa dadṛśur nāntaraṃ janāḥa mohayitvā kṛpaṃ droṇaṃ drauṇiṃ ca sa bṛhadbalamc saindhavaṃ ca maheṣvāsaṃ vyacaral laghu suṣṭhu caa maṇḍalīkṛtam evāsya dhanuḥ paśyāma māriṣac sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśaṃ tapatas tava vāhinīma taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ pratapantaṃ śarārcibhiḥc dviphalgunam imaṃ lokaṃ menire tasya karmabhiḥa tenārditā mahārāja bhāratī sā mahācamūḥc babhrāma tatra tatraiva yoṣin madavaśād ivaa drāvayitvā ca tat sainyaṃ kampayitvā mahārathānc nandayām āsa suhṛdo mayaṃ jitveva vāsavaḥa tena vidrāvyamāṇāni tava sainyāni saṃyugec cakrur ārtasvaraṃ ghoraṃ parjanyaninadopamama taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ tava sainyasya māriṣac mārutoddhūtavegasya samudrasyeva parvaṇie duryodhanas tadā rājā ārśyaśṛṅgim abhāṣataa eṣa kārṣṇir maheṣvāso dvitīya iva phalgunaḥc camūṃ drāvayate krodhād vṛtro devacamūm ivaa tasya nānyaṃ prapaśyāmi saṃyuge bheṣajaṃ mahatc ṛte tvāṃ rākṣasaśreṣṭha sarvavidyāsu pāragama sa gatvā tvaritaṃ vīraṃ jahi saubhadram āhavec vayaṃ pārthān haniṣyāmo bhīṣmadroṇapuraḥsarāḥa sa evam ukto balavān rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavānc prayayau samare tūrṇaṃ tava putrasya śāsanāte nardamāno mahānādaṃ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥa tasya śabdena mahatā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balamc prācalat sarvato rājan pūryamāṇa ivārṇavaḥa bahavaś ca narā rājaṃs tasya nādena bhīṣitāḥc priyān prāṇān parityajya nipetur dharaṇītalea kārṣṇiś cāpi mudā yuktaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥc nṛtyann iva rathopasthe tad rakṣaḥ samupādravata tataḥ sa rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ saṃprāpyaivārjuniṃ raṇec nātidūre sthitas tasya drāvayām āsa vai camūma sā vadhyamānā samare pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūḥb nādhyagacchata vai trāṇaṃ pīḍyamānā durātmanāc pratyudyayau raṇe rakṣo devasenā yathā balima vimardaḥ sumahān āsīt tasya sainyasya māriṣac rakṣasā ghorarūpeṇa vadhyamānasya saṃyugea tataḥ śarasahasrais tāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahācamūmc vyadrāvayad raṇe rakṣo darśayad vai parākramama sā vadhyamānā ca tathā pāṇḍavānām anīkinīc rakṣasā ghorarūpeṇa pradudrāva raṇe bhayāta tāṃ pramṛdya tataḥ senāṃ padminīṃ vāraṇo yathāc tato bhidudrāva raṇe draupadeyān mahābalāna te tu kruddhā maheṣvāsā draupadeyāḥ prahāriṇaḥc rākṣasaṃ dudruvuḥ sarve grahāḥ pañca yathā ravima vīryavadbhis tatas tais tu pīḍito rākṣasottamaḥc yathā yugakṣaye ghore candramāḥ pañcabhir grahaiḥa prativindhyas tato rakṣo bibheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc sarvapāraśavais tūrṇam akuṇṭhāgrair mahābalaḥa sa tair bhinnatanutrāṇaḥ śuśubhe rākṣasottamaḥc marīcibhir ivārkasya saṃsyūto jalado mahāna viṣaktaiḥ sa śaraiś cāpi tapanīyaparicchadaiḥc ārśyaśṛṅgir babhau rājan dīptaśṛṅga ivācalaḥa tatas te bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasendraṃ mahāhavec vivyadhur niśitair bāṇais tapanīyavibhūṣitaiḥa sa nirbhinnaḥ śarair ghorair bhujagaiḥ kopitair ivac alambuso bhṛśaṃ rājan nāgendra iva cukrudhed nirbhiṇṇas tu śarair ghorair dīpyamānaḥ samantataḥd alaṃbuso bhṛśaṃ bhāti ulkābhir iva kuñjaraḥa so tividdho mahārāja muhūrtam atha māriṣac praviveśa tamo dīrghaṃ pīḍitas tair mahārathaiḥa pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ krodhena dviguṇīkṛtaḥc ciccheda sāyakais teṣāṃ dhvajāṃś caiva dhanūṃṣi caa ekaikaṃ ca tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna smayann ivac alambuso rathopasthe nṛtyann iva mahārathaḥa tvaramāṇaś ca saṃkruddho hayāṃs teṣāṃ mahātmanāmc jaghāna rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ sārathīṃś ca mahābalaḥa bibheda ca susaṃhṛṣṭaḥ punaś cainān susaṃśitaiḥc śarair bahuvidhākāraiḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa virathāṃś ca maheṣvāsān kṛtvā tatra sa rākṣasaḥc abhidudrāva vegena hantukāmo niśācaraḥa tān arditān raṇe tena rākṣasena durātmanāc dṛṣṭvārjunasutaḥ saṃkhye rākṣasaṃ samupādravata tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ vṛtravāsavayor ivac dadṛśus tāvakāḥ sarve pāṇḍavāś ca mahārathāḥa tau sametau mahāyuddhe krodhadīptau parasparamb udvṛtya cakṣuṣī rājan krodhāt prasphuritādharauc mahābalau mahārāja krodhasaṃraktalocanaue parasparam avekṣetāṃ kālānalasamau yudhif āśīviṣāv iva kruddhau netrābhyām itaretarama tayoḥ samāgamo ghoro babhūva kaṭukodayaḥc yathā devāsure yuddhe śakraśambarayor iva dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa ārjuniṃ samare śūraṃ vinighnantaṃ mahārathamc alambusaḥ kathaṃ yuddhe pratyayudhyata saṃjayaa ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ kathaṃ cāpi saubhadraḥ paravīrahāc tan mamācakṣva tattvena yathā vṛttaṃ sma saṃyugea dhanaṃjayaś ca kiṃ cakre mama sainyeṣu saṃjayac bhīmo vā balināṃ śreṣṭho rākṣaso vā ghaṭotkacaḥa nakulaḥ sahadevo vā sātyakir vā mahārathaḥc etad ācakṣva me sarvaṃ kuśalo hy asi saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa hanta te haṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃgrāmaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc yathābhūd rākṣasendrasya saubhadrasya ca māriṣaa arjunaś ca yathā saṃkhye bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca raṇe cakruḥ parākramama tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve bhīṣmadroṇapurogamāḥc adbhutāni vicitrāṇi cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavata alambusas tu samare abhimanyuṃ mahārathamc vinadya sumahānādaṃ tarjayitvā muhur muhuḥe abhidudrāva vegena tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta saubhadro pi raṇe rājan siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥc ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ pitur atyantavairiṇama tataḥ sameyatuḥ saṃkhye tvaritau nararākṣasauc rathābhyāṃ rathināṃ śreṣṭhau yathā vai devadānavaue māyāvī rākṣasaśreṣṭho divyāstrajñaś ca phālguniḥa tataḥ kārṣṇir mahārāja niśitaiḥ sāyakais tribhiḥc ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ raṇe viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥa alambuso pi saṃkruddhaḥ kārṣṇiṃ navabhir āśugaiḥc hṛdi vivyādha vegena tottrair iva mahādvipama tataḥ śarasahasreṇa kṣiprakārī niśācaraḥc arjunasya sutaṃ saṃkhye pīḍayām āsa bhārataa abhimanyus tataḥ kruddho navatiṃ nataparvaṇāmc cikṣepa niśitān bāṇān rākṣasasya mahorasia te tasya viviśus tūrṇaṃ kāyaṃ nirbhidya marmaṇic sa tair vibhinnasarvāṅgaḥ śuśubhe rākṣasottamaḥe puṣpitaiḥ kiṃśukai rājan saṃstīrṇa iva parvataḥa sa dhārayañ śarān hemapuṅkhān api mahābalaḥc vibabhau rākṣasaśreṣṭhaḥ sajvāla iva parvataḥa tataḥ kruddho mahārāja ārśyaśṛṅgir mahābalaḥc mahendrapratimaṃ kārṣṇiṃ chādayām āsa patribhiḥa tena te viśikhā muktā yamadaṇḍopamāḥ śitāḥc abhimanyuṃ vinirbhidya prāviśan dharaṇītalama tathaivārjuninirmuktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥc alambusaṃ vinirbhidya prāviśanta dharātalama saubhadras tu raṇe rakṣaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc cakre vimukham āsādya mayaṃ śakra ivāhavea vimukhaṃ ca tato rakṣo vadhyamānaṃ raṇe riṇāc prāduścakre mahāmāyāṃ tāmasīṃ paratāpanaḥa tatas te tamasā sarve hṛtā hy āsan mahītalec nābhimanyum apaśyanta naiva svān na parān raṇea abhimanyuś ca tad dṛṣṭvā ghorarūpaṃ mahat tamaḥc prāduścakre stram atyugraṃ bhāskaraṃ kurunandanaḥa tataḥ prakāśam abhavaj jagat sarvaṃ mahīpatec tāṃ cāpi jaghnivān māyāṃ rākṣasasya durātmanaḥa saṃkruddhaś ca mahāvīryo rākṣasendraṃ narottamaḥc chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa bahvīs tathānyā māyāś ca prayuktās tena rakṣasāc sarvāstravid ameyātmā vārayām āsa phālguniḥa hatamāyaṃ tato rakṣo vadhyamānaṃ ca sāyakaiḥc rathaṃ tatraiva saṃtyajya prādravan mahato bhayāta tasmin vinirjite tūrṇaṃ kūṭayodhini rākṣaseb saubhadraś ca mahābāhuḥ samare ca jitaśramaḥb parākramī mahātejāḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥc ārjuniḥ samare sainyaṃ tāvakaṃ saṃmamarda hae madāndho vanyanāgendraḥ sapadmāṃ padminīm ivaa tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ sainyaṃ dṛṣṭvābhividrutamc mahatā rathavaṃśena saubhadraṃ paryavārayata koṣṭhakīkṛtya taṃ vīraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā mahārathāḥc ekaṃ subahavo yuddhe tatakṣuḥ sāyakair dṛḍhama sa teṣāṃ rathināṃ vīraḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥc sadṛśo vāsudevasya vikrameṇa balena caa ubhayoḥ sadṛśaṃ karma sa pitur mātulasya cac raṇe bahuvidhaṃ cakre sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa tato dhanaṃjayo rājan vinighnaṃs tava sainikānc āsasāda raṇe bhīṣmaṃ putraprepsur amarṣaṇaḥa tathaiva samare rājan pitā devavratas tavac āsasāda raṇe pārthaṃ svarbhānur iva bhāskarama tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ putrās tava viśāṃ patec parivavrū raṇe bhīṣmaṃ jugupuś ca samantataḥa tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan parivārya dhanaṃjayamc raṇāya mahate yuktā daṃśitā bharatarṣabhaa śāradvatas tato rājan bhīṣmasya pramukhe sthitamc arjunaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānāṃ samācinota patyudgamyātha vivyādha sātyakis taṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥc pāṇḍavapriyakāmārthaṃ śārdūla iva kuñjarama gautamo pi tvarāyukto mādhavaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc hṛdi vivyādha saṃkruddhaḥ kaṅkapatraparicchadaiḥa śaineyo pi tataḥ kruddho bhṛśaṃ viddho mahārathaḥc gautamāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ samādatta śilīmukhama tam āpatantaṃ vegena śakrāśanisamadyutimc dvidhā ciccheda saṃkruddho drauṇiḥ paramakopanaḥa samutsṛjyātha śaineyo gautamaṃ rathināṃ varamc abhyadravad raṇe drauṇiṃ rāhuḥ khe śaśinaṃ yathāa tasya droṇasutaś cāpaṃ dvidhā ciccheda bhāratac athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ tāḍayām āsa sāyakaiḥa so nyat kārmukam ādāya śatrughnaṃ bhārasādhanamc drauṇiṃ ṣaṣṭyā mahārāja bāhvor urasi cārpayata sa viddho vyathitaś caiva muhūrtaṃ kaśmalāyutaḥc niṣasāda rathopasthe dhvajayaṣṭim upāśritaḥa pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ droṇaputraḥ pratāpavānc vārṣṇeyaṃ samare kruddho nārācena samardayata śaineyaṃ sa tu nirbhidya prāviśad dharaṇītalamc vasantakāle balavān bilaṃ sarpaśiśur yathāa tato pareṇa bhallena mādhavasya dhvajottamamc ciccheda samare drauṇiḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda caa punaś cainaṃ śarair ghoraiś chādayām āsa bhāratac nidāghānte mahārāja yathā megho divākarama sātyakiś ca mahārāja śarajālaṃ nihatya tatc drauṇim abhyapatat tūrṇaṃ śarajālair anekadhāa tāpayām āsa ca drauṇiṃ śaineyaḥ paravīrahāc vimukto meghajālena yathaiva tapanas tathāa śarāṇāṃ ca sahasreṇa punar enaṃ samudyatamc sātyakiś chādayām āsa nanāda ca mahābalaḥa dṛṣṭvā putraṃ tathā grastaṃ rāhuṇeva niśākaramc abhyadravata śaineyaṃ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavāna vivyādha ca pṛṣatkena sutīkṣṇena mahāmṛdhec parīpsan svasutaṃ rājan vārṣṇeyenābhitāpitama sātyakis tu raṇe jitvā guruputraṃ mahārathamc droṇaṃ vivyādha viṃśatyā sarvapāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥa tadantaram ameyātmā kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥc abhyadravad raṇe kruddho droṇaṃ prati mahārathaḥa tato droṇaś ca pārthaś ca sameyātāṃ mahāmṛdhec yathā budhaś ca śukraś ca mahārāja nabhastale dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ pāṇḍavaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥc samīyatū raṇe śūrau tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa priyo hi pāṇḍavo nityaṃ bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥc ācāryaś ca raṇe nityaṃ priyaḥ pārthasya saṃjayaa tāv ubhau rathinau saṃkhye dṛptau siṃhāv ivotkaṭauc kathaṃ samīyatur yuddhe bhāradvājadhanaṃjayau saṃjaya uvācaa na droṇaḥ samare pārthaṃ jānīte priyam ātmanaḥc kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya pārtho vā gurum āhaved tathaiva pāṇḍavo droṇaṃ vetty eva priyam ātmanaḥd kṣatradharmarato nityaṃ kṣatradharmeṇa yudhyatea na kṣatriyā raṇe rājan varjayanti parasparamc nirmaryādaṃ hi yudhyante pitṛbhir bhrātṛbhiḥ sahaa raṇe bhārata pārthena droṇo viddhas tribhiḥ śaraiḥc nācintayata tān bāṇān pārthacāpacyutān yudhia śaravṛṣṭyā punaḥ pārthaś chādayām āsa taṃ raṇec prajajvāla ca roṣeṇa gahane gnir ivotthitaḥa tato rjunaṃ raṇe droṇaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc vārayām āsa rājendra nacirād iva bhārataa tato duryodhano rājā suśarmāṇam acodayatc droṇasya samare rājan pārṣṇigrahaṇakāraṇāta trigartarāḍ api kruddho bhṛśam āyamya kārmukamc chādayām āsa samare pārthaṃ bāṇair ayomukhaiḥa tābhyāṃ muktāḥ śarā rājann antarikṣe virejirec haṃsā iva mahārāja śaratkāle nabhastalea te śarāḥ prāpya kaunteyaṃ samastā viviśuḥ prabhoc phalabhāranataṃ yadvat svāduvṛkṣaṃ vihaṃgamāḥa arjunas tu raṇe nādaṃ vinadya rathināṃ varaḥc trigartarājaṃ samare saputraṃ vivyadhe śaraiḥa te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kāleneva yugakṣayec pārtham evābhyavartanta maraṇe kṛtaniścayāḥe mumucuḥ śaravṛṣṭiṃ ca pāṇḍavasya rathaṃ pratia śaravṛṣṭiṃ tatas tāṃ tu śaravarṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥc pratijagrāha rājendra toyavṛṣṭim ivācalaḥa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma bībhatsor hastalāghavamc vimuktāṃ bahubhiḥ śūraiḥ śastravṛṣṭiṃ durāsadāma yad eko vārayām āsa māruto bhragaṇān ivac karmaṇā tena pārthasya tutuṣur devadānavāḥa atha kruddho raṇe pārthas trigartān prati bhāratac mumocāstraṃ mahārāja vāyavyaṃ pṛtanāmukhea prādurāsīt tato vāyuḥ kṣobhayāṇo nabhastalamc pātayan vai tarugaṇān vinighnaṃś caiva sainikāna tato droṇo bhivīkṣyaiva vāyavyāstraṃ sudāruṇamc śailam anyan mahārāja ghoram astraṃ mumoca haa droṇena yudhi nirmukte tasminn astre mahāmṛdhec praśaśāma tato vāyuḥ prasannāś cābhavan diśaḥa tataḥ pāṇḍusuto vīras trigartasya rathavrajānc nirutsāhān raṇe cakre vimukhān viparākramāna tato duryodhano rājā kṛpaś ca rathināṃ varaḥc aśvatthāmā tataḥ śalyaḥ kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥa vindānuvindāv āvantyau bāhlikaś ca sabāhlikaḥc mahatā rathavaṃśena pārthasyāvārayan diśaḥa tathaiva bhagadattaś ca śrutāyuś ca mahābalaḥc gajānīkena bhīmasya tāv avārayatāṃ diśaḥa bhūriśravāḥ śalaś caiva saubalaś ca viśāṃ patec śaraughair vividhais tūrṇaṃ mādrīputrāv avārayana bhīṣmas tu sahitaḥ sarvair dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikaiḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ samāsādya sarvataḥ paryavārayata āpatantaṃ gajānīkaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārtho vṛkodaraḥc lelihan sṛkkiṇī vīro mṛgarāḍ iva kānanea tatas tu rathināṃ śreṣṭho gadāṃ gṛhya mahāhavec avaplutya rathāt tūrṇaṃ tava sainyam abhīṣayatd   giryagrād iva kesarīd tasthau sa sagado bhīmaḥ saśṛṅga iva parvataḥd siṃho dṛṣṭvā mṛgaṃ yadvata tam udvīkṣya gadāhastaṃ tatas te gajasādinaḥc parivavrū raṇe yattā bhīmasenaṃ samantataḥa gajamadhyam anuprāptaḥ pāṇḍavaś ca vyarājatac meghajālasya mahato yathā madhyagato raviḥa vyadhamat sa gajānīkaṃ gadayā pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥc mahābhrajālam atulaṃ mātariśveva saṃtatama te vadhyamānā balinā bhīmasenena dantinaḥc ārtanādaṃ raṇe cakrur garjanto jaladā ivaa bahudhā dāritaś caiva viṣāṇais tatra dantibhiḥc phullāśokanibhaḥ pārthaḥ śuśubhe raṇamūrdhanid sādināṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ ca vyadhamad gadayā tataḥd vāyuvegasamāyukto vyacarat pāṇḍavo yudhid viṣāṇollikhitair gātrair viṣāṇābhihato bhṛśama viṣāṇe dantinaṃ gṛhya nirviṣāṇam athākarotc viṣāṇena ca tenaiva kumbhe bhyāhatya dantiname pātayām āsa samare daṇḍahasta ivāntakaḥa śoṇitāktāṃ gadāṃ bibhran medomajjākṛtacchaviḥc kṛtāṅgadaḥ śoṇitena rudravat pratyadṛśyataa evaṃ te vadhyamānās tu hataśeṣā mahāgajāḥc prādravanta diśo rājan vimṛdnantaḥ svakaṃ balama dravadbhis tair mahānāgaiḥ samantād bharatarṣabhac duryodhanabalaṃ sarvaṃ punar āsīt parāṅmukham saṃjaya uvācaa madhyāhne tu mahārāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyatac lokakṣayakaro raudro bhīṣmasya saha somakaiḥa gāṅgeyo rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc vyadhaman niśitair bāṇaiḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa saṃmamarda ca tat sainyaṃ pitā devavratas tavac dhānyānām iva lūnānāṃ prakaraṃ gogaṇā ivaa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca virāṭo drupadas tathāc bhīṣmam āsādya samare śarair jaghnur mahārathama dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato viddhvā virāṭaṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥc drupadasya ca nārācaṃ preṣayām āsa bhārataa tena viddhā maheṣvāsā bhīṣmeṇāmitrakarśināc cukrudhuḥ samare rājan pādaspṛṣṭā ivoragāḥa śikhaṇḍī taṃ ca vivyādha bharatānāṃ pitāmahamc strīmayaṃ manasā dhyātvā nāsmai prāharad acyutaḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu samare krodhād agnir iva jvalanc pitāmahaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayata drupadaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā virāṭo daśabhiḥ śaraiḥc śikhaṇḍī pañcaviṃśatyā bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥa so tividdho mahārāja bhīṣmaḥ saṃkhye mahātmabhiḥc vasante puṣpaśabalo raktāśoka ivābabhaua tān pratyavidhyad gāṅgeyas tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥc drupadasya ca bhallena dhanuś ciccheda māriṣaa so nyat kārmukam ādāya bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥc sārathiṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiḥ suśitai raṇamūrdhania tato bhīmo mahārāja draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥc kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca sātyakiś caiva sātvataḥa abhyadravanta gāṅgeyaṃ yudhiṣṭhirahitepsayāc rirakṣiṣantaḥ pāñcālyaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhan raṇea tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve bhīṣmarakṣārtham udyatāḥc pratyudyayuḥ pāṇḍusenāṃ sahasainyā narādhipaa tatrāsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkulamc narāśvarathanāgānāṃ yamarāṣṭravivardhanama rathī rathinam āsādya prāhiṇod yamasādanamc tathetarān samāsādya naranāgāśvasādinaḥa anayan paralokāya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc astraiś ca vividhair ghorais tatra tatra viśāṃ patea rathāś ca rathibhir hīnā hatasārathayas tathāc vipradrutāśvāḥ samare diśo jagmuḥ samantataḥa mardamānā narān rājan hayāṃś ca subahūn raṇec vātāyamānā dṛśyante gandharvanagaropamāḥa rathinaś ca rathair hīnā varmiṇas tejasā yutāḥc kuṇḍaloṣṇīṣiṇaḥ sarve niṣkāṅgadavibhūṣitāḥa devaputrasamā rūpe śaurye śakrasamā yudhic ṛddhyā vaiśravaṇaṃ cāti nayena ca bṛhaspatima sarvalokeśvarāḥ śūrās tatra tatra viśāṃ patec vipradrutā vyadṛśyanta prākṛtā iva mānavāḥa dantinaś ca naraśreṣṭha vihīnā varasādibhiḥc mṛdnantaḥ svāny anīkāni saṃpetuḥ sarvaśabdagāḥa varmabhiś cāmaraiś chatraiḥ patākābhiś ca māriṣac kakṣyābhir atha tottraiś ca ghaṇṭābhis tomarais tathāa viśīrṇair vipradhāvanto dṛśyante sma diśo daśac nagameghapratīkāśair jaladodayanisvanaiḥa tathaiva dantibhir hīnān gajārohān viśāṃ patec pradhāvanto nvapaśyāma tava teṣāṃ ca saṃkulea nānādeśasamutthāṃś ca turagān hemabhūṣitānc vātāyamānān adrākṣaṃ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa aśvārohān hatair aśvair gṛhītāsīn samantataḥc dravamāṇān apaśyāma drāvyamāṇāṃś ca saṃyuged tato ntare mahārāja bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānd cakāra sumahad yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ bhayānakama gajo gajaṃ samāsādya dravamāṇaṃ mahāraṇec yayau vimṛdnaṃs tarasā padātīn vājinas tathād aśvān aśvaiś ca saṃmardya rathaiś ca rathinas tathāa tathaiva ca rathān rājan saṃmamarda raṇe gajaḥc rathaś caiva samāsādya padātiṃ turagaṃ tathāa vyamṛdnāt samare rājaṃs turagāṃś ca narān raṇec evaṃ te bahudhā rājan pramṛdnantaḥ parasparamd dṛśyante sma mahābāho tatra tatra mahābalāḥa tasmin raudre tathā yuddhe vartamāne mahābhayec prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitāntrataraṅgiṇīa asthisaṃcayasaṃghāṭā keśaśaivalaśādvalāc rathahradā śarāvartā hayamīnā durāsadāa śīrṣopalasamākīrṇā hastigrāhasamākulāc kavacoṣṇīṣaphenāḍhyā dhanurdvīpāsikacchapād śaṅkhacakraughasaṃpūrṇā chatrakūrmā rathoḍupāa patākādhvajavṛkṣāḍhyā martyakūlāpahāriṇīc kravyādasaṃghasaṃkīrṇā yamarāṣṭravivardhinīa tāṃ nadīṃ kṣatriyāḥ śūrā hayanāgarathaplavaiḥc praterur bahavo rājan bhayaṃ tyaktvā mahāhavea apovāha raṇe bhīrūn kaśmalenābhisaṃvṛtānc yathā vaitaraṇī pretān pretarājapuraṃ pratia prākrośan kṣatriyās tatra dṛṣṭvā tad vaiśasaṃ mahatc duryodhanāparādhena kṣayaṃ gacchanti kauravāḥa guṇavatsu kathaṃ dveṣaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥc kṛtavān pāṇḍuputreṣu pāpātmā lobhamohitaḥa evaṃ bahuvidhā vācaḥ śrūyante smātra bhāratac pāṇḍavastavasaṃyuktāḥ putrāṇāṃ te sudāruṇāḥa tā niśamya tadā vācaḥ sarvayodhair udāhṛtāḥc āgaskṛt sarvalokasya putro duryodhanas tavaa bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ caiva śalyaṃ covāca bhāratac yudhyadhvam anahaṃkārāḥ kiṃ ciraṃ kurutheti cad iti duryodhanotsṛṣṭāḥ sarve yuyudhire nṛpāḥa tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac akṣadyūtakṛtaṃ rājan sughoraṃ vaiśasaṃ tadāa yat purā na nigṛhṇīṣe vāryamāṇo mahātmabhiḥc vaicitravīrya tasyedaṃ phalaṃ paśya tathāvidhama na hi pāṇḍusutā rājan sasainyāḥ sapadānugāḥb ayudhyanta mahāraṅge madhyaṃ prāpte divākareb sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥb nākampayata śaineyo satyavān satyakovidaḥc rakṣanti samare prāṇān kauravā vā viśāṃ patea etasmāt kāraṇād ghoro vartate sma janakṣayaḥc daivād vā puruṣavyāghra tava cāpanayān nṛpa saṃjaya uvācaa arjunas tu naravyāghra suśarmapramukhān nṛpānc anayat pretarājasya bhavanaṃ sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥa suśarmāpi tato bāṇaiḥ pārthaṃ vivyādha saṃyugec vāsudevaṃ ca saptatyā pārthaṃ ca navabhiḥ punaḥa tān nivārya śaraugheṇa śakrasūnur mahārathaḥc suśarmaṇo raṇe yodhān prāhiṇod yamasādanama te vadhyamānāḥ pārthena kāleneva yugakṣayec vyadravanta raṇe rājan bhaye jāte mahārathāḥa utsṛjya turagān ke cid rathān ke cic ca māriṣac gajān anye samutsṛjya prādravanta diśo daśaa apare tudyamānās tu vājināgarathā raṇātc tvarayā parayā yuktāḥ prādravanta viśāṃ pated kaśābhis tāḍayām āsuḥ pārṣṇibhiś ca mahur muhuḥd hayārohā dravanty eva codayanto hayottamānd tathā tottranipātaiś ca aṅkuśānāṃ ca vibhramaiḥd gajārohā gajāṃs tūrṇaṃ tvarayantaḥ pradudruvuḥd rathinaś ca pratodaiś ca vāgbhiś caiva punaḥ punaḥd bhartsayanto hayān rājan prādravanti diśo daśaa pādātāś cāpi śastrāṇi samutsṛjya mahāraṇec nirapekṣā vyadhāvanta tena tena sma bhārataa vāryamāṇāḥ sma bahuśas traigartena suśarmaṇāc tathānyaiḥ pārthivaśreṣṭhair na vyatiṣṭhanta saṃyuged putrāṃś ca patitān bhūmau mātulāṃś ca pitṝṃs tathād sodarāṃś cāvamardantaḥ pradrutās tatra tatra vaia tad balaṃ pradrutaṃ dṛṣṭvā putro duryodhanas tavac puraskṛtya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ sarvasainyapuraskṛtama sarvodyogena mahatā dhanaṃjayam upādravatc trigartādhipater arthe jīvitasya viśāṃ patea sa ekaḥ samare tasthau kiran bahuvidhāñ śarānc bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ śeṣā vipradrutā narāḥa tathaiva paṇḍavā rājan sarvodyogena daṃśitāḥc prayayuḥ phalgunārthāya yatra bhīṣmo vyavasthitaḥa jānanto pi raṇe śauryaṃ ghoraṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥc hāhākārakṛtotsāhā bhīṣmaṃ jagmuḥ samantataḥa tatas tāladhvajaḥ śūraḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīmc chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa ekībhūtās tataḥ sarve kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac ayudhyanta mahārāja madhyaṃ prāpte divākarea sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥc atiṣṭhad āhave śūraḥ kiran bāṇān sahasraśaḥa tathaiva drupado rājā droṇaṃ viddhvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥc punar vivyādha saptatyā sārathiṃ cāsya saptabhiḥa bhīmasenas tu rājānaṃ bāhlikaṃ prapitāmahamc viddhvānadan mahānādaṃ śārdūla iva kānanea ārjuniś citrasenena viddho bahubhir āśugaiḥc citrasenaṃ tribhir bāṇair vivyādha hṛdaye bhṛśama samāgatau tau tu raṇe mahāmātrau vyarocatāmc yathā divi mahāghorau rājan budhaśanaiścaraua tasyāśvāṃś caturo hatvā sūtaṃ ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥc nanāda balavan nādaṃ saubhadraḥ paravīrahāa hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥc āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ durmukhasya viśāṃ patea droṇaś ca drupadaṃ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc sārathiṃ cāsya vivyādha tvaramāṇaḥ parākramīa pīḍyamānas tato rājā drupado vāhinīmukhec apāyāj javanair aśvaiḥ pūrvavairam anusmarana bhīmasenas tu rājānaṃ muhūrtād iva bāhlikamc vyaśvasūtarathaṃ cakre sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa sasaṃbhramo mahārāja saṃśayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥc avaplutya tato vāhād bāhlikaḥ puruṣottamaḥe āruroha rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ lakṣmaṇasya mahārathaḥa sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇaṃ vārayitvā mahārathaḥc śarair bahuvidhai rājann āsasāda pitāmahama sa viddhvā bhārataṃ ṣaṣṭyā niśitair lomavāhibhiḥc nanarteva rathopasthe vidhunvāno mahad dhanuḥa tasyāyasīṃ mahāśaktiṃ cikṣepātha pitāmahaḥc hemacitrāṃ mahāvegāṃ nāgakanyopamāṃ śubhāma tām āpatantīṃ sahasā mṛtyukalpāṃ sutejanāmc dhvaṃsayām āsa vārṣṇeyo lāghavena mahāyaśāḥa anāsādya tu vārṣṇeyaṃ śaktiḥ paramadāruṇāc nyapatad dharaṇīpṛṣṭhe maholkeva gataprabhāa vārṣṇeyas tu tato rājan svāṃ śaktiṃ ghoradarśanāmc vegavad gṛhya cikṣepa pitāmaharathaṃ pratia vārṣṇeyabhujavegena praṇunnā sā mahāhavec abhidudrāva vegena kālarātrir yathā narama tām āpatantīṃ sahasā dvidhā ciccheda bhāratac kṣuraprābhyāṃ sutīkṣṇābhyāṃ sānvakīryata bhūtalea chittvā tu śaktiṃ gāṅgeyaḥ sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc ājaghānorasi kruddhaḥ prahasañ śatrukarśanaḥa tataḥ sarathanāgāśvāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajac parivavrū raṇe bhīṣmaṃ mādhavatrāṇakāraṇāta tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca samare vijayaiṣiṇām saṃjaya uvācaa dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ pāṇḍavair abhisaṃvṛtamc yathā meghair mahārāja tapānte divi bhāskarama duryodhano mahārāja duḥśāsanam abhāṣatac eṣa śūro maheṣvāso bhīṣmaḥ śatruniṣūdanaḥa chāditaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śūraiḥ samantād bharatarṣabhac tasya kāryaṃ tvayā vīra rakṣaṇaṃ sumahātmanaḥa rakṣyamāṇo hi samare bhīṣmo smākaṃ pitāmahaḥc nihanyāt samare yattān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ sahaa tatra kāryam ahaṃ manye bhīṣmasyaivābhirakṣaṇamc goptā hy eṣa maheṣvāso bhīṣmo smākaṃ pitāmahaḥa sa bhavān sarvasainyena parivārya pitāmahamc samare duṣkaraṃ karma kurvāṇaṃ parirakṣatua evam uktas tu samare putro duḥśāsanas tavac parivārya sthito bhīṣmaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥa tataḥ śatasahasreṇa hayānāṃ subalātmajaḥc vimalaprāsahastānām ṛṣṭitomaradhāriṇāma darpitānāṃ suvegānāṃ balasthānāṃ patākināmc śikṣitair yuddhakuśalair upetānāṃ narottamaiḥd nānāśastrasamākīrṇo yuddhāyaivābhidaṃśitaḥa nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca dharmarājaṃ ca pāṇḍavamc nyavārayan naraśreṣṭhaṃ parivārya samantataḥa tato duryodhano rājā śūrāṇāṃ hayasādināmc ayutaṃ preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavānāṃ nivāraṇea taiḥ praviṣṭair mahāvegair garutmadbhir ivāhavec khurāhatā dharā rājaṃś cakampe ca nanāda caa khuraśabdaś ca sumahān vājināṃ śuśruve tadāc mahāvaṃśavanasyeva dahyamānasya parvatea utpatadbhiś ca tais tatra samuddhūtaṃ mahad rajaḥc divākarapathaṃ prāpya chādayām āsa bhāskarama vegavadbhir hayais tais tu kṣobhitaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ balamc nipatadbhir mahāvegair haṃsair iva mahat saraḥe heṣatāṃ caiva śabdena na prājñāyata kiṃ canaf antardadhe mahāñ śabdas tena śabdena mohitaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc pratyaghnaṃs tarasā vegaṃ samare hayasādināma udvṛttasya mahārāja prāvṛṭkālena pūryataḥc paurṇamāsyām ambuvegaṃ yathā velā mahodadheḥa tatas te rathino rājañ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc nyakṛntann uttamāṅgāni kāyebhyo hayasādināma te nipetur mahārāja nihatā dṛḍhadhanvibhiḥc nāgair iva mahānāgā yathā syur girigahvarea te pi prāsaiḥ suniśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc nyakṛntann uttamāṅgāni vicaranto diśo daśaa atyāsannā hayārohā ṛṣṭibhir bharatarṣabhac acchinann uttamāṅgāni phalānīva mahādrumāta sasādino hayā rājaṃs tatra tatra niṣūditāḥc patitāḥ pātyamānāś ca śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa vadhyamānā hayās te tu prādravanta bhayārditāḥc yathā siṃhān samāsādya mṛgāḥ prāṇaparāyaṇāḥd evaṃ tu saubalaṃ sainyaṃ prabhagnaṃ sarvatodiśama pāṇḍavās tu mahārāja jitvā śatrūn mahāhavec dadhmuḥ śaṅkhāṃś ca bherīś ca tāḍayām āsur āhavea tato duryodhano dṛṣṭvā dīnaṃ sainyam avasthitamc abravīd bharataśreṣṭha madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥd uvāca madrādhipatiṃ rājā duryodhanas tadāa eṣa pāṇḍusuto jyeṣṭho jitvā mātula māmakānc paśyatāṃ no mahābāho senāṃ drāvayate balīa taṃ vāraya mahābāho veleva makarālayamc tvaṃ hi saṃśrūyase tyartham asahyabalavikramaḥa putrasya tava tad vākyaṃ śrutvā śalyaḥ pratāpavānc prayayau rathavaṃśena yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥa tad āpatad vai sahasā śalyasya sumahad balamc mahaughavegaṃ samare vārayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥa madrarājaṃ ca samare dharmarājo mahārathaḥc daśabhiḥ sāyakais tūrṇam ājaghāna stanāntaree nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥa madrarājo pi tān sarvān ājaghāna tribhis tribhiḥc yudhiṣṭhiraṃ punaḥ ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥe mādrīputrau ca saṃrabdhau dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām atāḍayata tato bhīmo mahābāhur dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhavec madrarājavaśaṃ prāptaṃ mṛtyor āsyagataṃ yathāe abhyadravata saṃgrāme yudhiṣṭhiram amitrajitf āpatann eva bhīmas tu madrarājam atāḍayatf sarvapāraśavais tīkṣṇair nārācair marmabhedibhiḥf tato bhīṣmaś ca droṇaś ca sainyena mahatā vṛtauf rājānam abhyapadyetām añjasā śaravarṣiṇauf dhṛṣṭadyumnas tribhir viddhvā rājānam abhyapadyataa tato yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ prāvartata sudāruṇamc aparāṃ diśam āsthāya dyotamāne divākare saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ pitā tava kruddho niśitaiḥ sāyakottamaiḥc ājaghāna raṇe pārthān sahasenān samantataḥa bhīmaṃ dvādaśabhir viddhvā sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc nakulaṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiḥ sahadevaṃ ca saptabhiḥa yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dvādaśabhir bāhvor urasi cārpayatc dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato viddhvā vinanāda mahābalaḥa taṃ dvādaśārdhair nakulo mādhavaś ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥb sahadevaś ca saptatyā pārthaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca saptatyā bhīmasenaś ca pañcabhiḥe yudhiṣṭhiro dvādaśabhiḥ pratyavidhyat pitāmahama droṇas tu sātyakiṃ viddhvā bhīmasenam avidhyataa   niśitair navabhiḥ śaraiḥa nakulaṃ ca tribhir viddhvāc ekaikaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair yamadaṇḍopamaiḥ śitaiḥa tau ca taṃ pratyavidhyetāṃ tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥc tottrair iva mahānāgaṃ droṇaṃ brāhmaṇapuṃgavama sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcyodīcyamālavāḥc abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayo tha vasātayaḥe saṃgrāme nājahur bhīṣmaṃ vadhyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa tathaivānye vadhyamānāḥ pāṇḍaveyair mahātmabhiḥc pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥe tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan parivavruḥ pitāmahama sa samantāt parivṛto rathaughair aparājitaḥc gahane gnir ivotsṛṣṭaḥ prajajvāla dahan parāna rathāgnyagāraś cāpārcir asiśaktigadendhanaḥc śarasphuliṅgo bhīṣmāgnir dadāha kṣatriyarṣabhānd yathā hi sumahān agniḥ kakṣe carati sānilaḥd tathā bhīṣmo mahārāja divyam astram udīrayana suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhir gārdhrapakṣaiḥ sutejanaiḥc karṇinālīkanārācaiś chādayām āsa tad balama apātayad dhvajāṃś caiva rathinaś ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥc muṇḍatālavanānīva cakāra sa rathavrajāna nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan gajān aśvāṃś ca saṃyugec akarot sa mahābāhuḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥc niśamya sarvabhūtāni samakampanta bhārataa amoghā hy apatan bāṇāḥ pitus te bharatarṣabhac nāsajjanta tanutreṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥa hatavīrān rathān rājan saṃyuktāñ javanair hayaiḥc apaśyāma mahārāja hriyamāṇān raṇājired matsyapāñcālakaikeyān pātayām āsa saṃyugea cedikāśikarūṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśac mahārathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥe aparāvartinaḥ sarve suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥa saṃgrāme bhīṣmam āsādya vyāditāsyam ivāntakamc nimagnāḥ paralokāya savājirathakuñjarāḥa bhagnākṣopaskarān kāṃś cid bhagnacakrāṃś ca sarvaśaḥc apaśyāma rathān rājañ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa savarūthai rathair bhagnai rathibhiś ca nipātitaiḥc śaraiḥ sukavacaiś chinnaiḥ paṭṭiśaiś ca viśāṃ patea gadābhir musalaiś caiva nistriṃśaiś ca śilīmukhaiḥc anukarṣair upāsaṅgaiś cakrair bhagnaiś ca māriṣaa bāhubhiḥ kārmukaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥc talatrair aṅgulitraiś ca dhvajaiś ca vinipātitaiḥe cāpaiś ca bahudhā chinnaiḥ samāstīryata medinīa hatārohā gajā rājan hayāś ca hatasādinaḥc paripetur drutaṃ tatra śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa yatamānāś ca te vīrā dravamāṇān mahārathānc nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ bhīṣmabāṇaprapīḍitāna mahendrasamavīryeṇa vadhyamānā mahācamūḥc abhajyata mahārāja na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥa āviddharathanāgāśvaṃ patitadhvajakūbaramc anīkaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ hāhābhūtam acetanama jaghānātra pitā putraṃ putraś ca pitaraṃ tathāc priyaṃ sakhāyaṃ cākrande sakhā daivabalātkṛtaḥa vimucya kavacān anye pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥc prakīrya keśān dhāvantaḥ pratyadṛśyanta bhārataa tad gokulam ivodbhrāntam udbhrāntarathakuñjaramc dadṛśe pāṇḍuputrasya sainyam ārtasvaraṃ codayām āsa mādhavaḥc yato bhīṣmas tato rājan duṣprekṣyo raśmivān ivaa tatas tat punar āvṛttaṃ yudhiṣṭhirabalaṃ mahatc dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ mahābāhuṃ bhīṣmāyodyantam āhavea tato bhīṣmaḥ kuruśreṣṭhaḥ siṃhavad vinadan muhuḥc dhanaṃjayarathaṃ śīghraṃ śaravarṣair avākirata kṣaṇena sa rathas tasya sahayaḥ sahasārathiḥc śaravarṣeṇa mahatā na prājñāyata kiṃ canaa vāsudevas tv asaṃbhrānto dhairyam āsthāya sātvataḥc codayām āsa tān aśvān vitunnān bhīṣmasāyakaiḥa tataḥ pārtho dhanur gṛhya divyaṃ jaladanisvanamc pātayām āsa bhīṣmasya dhanuś chittvā śitaiḥ śaraiḥa sa cchinnadhanvā kauravyaḥ punar anyan mahad dhanuḥc nimeṣāntaramātreṇa sajyaṃ cakre pitā tavaa vicakarṣa tato dorbhyāṃ dhanur jaladanisvanamc athāsya tad api kruddhaś ciccheda dhanur arjunaḥa tasya tat pūjayām āsa lāghavaṃ śaṃtanoḥ sutaḥc sādhu pārtha mahābāho sādhu kuntīsuteti caa samābhāṣyainam aparaṃ pragṛhya ruciraṃ dhanuḥc mumoca samare bhīṣmaḥ śarān pārtharathaṃ pratia adarśayad vāsudevo hayayāne paraṃ balamc moghān kurvañ śarāṃs tasya maṇḍalāni vidarśayana śuśubhāte naravyāghrau bhīṣmapārthau śarakṣatauc govṛṣāv iva saṃrabdhau viṣāṇollikhitāṅkitaud tataḥ pravavṛte raudraḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥd pāṇḍavānāṃ ca mukhyasya kurūṇāṃ pravarasya cad tālamātre vikarṣantau tāv ubhau raṇakarkaśaud dhanuṣī dṛḍhamuṣṭī tāv ubhau pautrapitāmahaud śyāmasya palitenāsau saṃgamaḥ pratyaśobhatad gaṅgāyamunayor yadvaj jalayoḥ gṛhītacāpaḥ samare vimuñcaṃś ca śitāñ śarānc śakyo jetuṃ yamaḥ kruddho vajrapāṇiś ca devarāṭa varuṇaḥ pāśabhṛd vāpi sagado vā dhaneśvaraḥc na tu bhīṣmaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ śakyo jetuṃ mahāhavea so ham evaṃ tridaśān vā samudyuktān sahitān daityadānavaiḥe nihanyād arjunaḥ saṃkhye kim u bhīṣmaṃ narādhipaa viparīto mahāvīryo gatasattvo lpajīvitaḥc bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo nūnaṃ kartavyaṃ nāvabudhyate yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa evam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi mādhavac sarve hy ete na paryāptās tava veganivāraṇea niyataṃ samavāpsyāmi sarvam eva yathepsitamc yasya me puruṣavyāghra bhavān nātho mahābalaḥa sendrān api raṇe devāñ jayeyaṃ jayatāṃ varac tvayā nāthena govinda kim u bhīṣmaṃ mahāhavea na tu tvām anṛtaṃ kartum utsahe svārthagauravātc ayudhyamānaḥ sāhāyyaṃ yathoktaṃ kuru mādhavaa samayas tu kṛtaḥ kaś cid bhīṣmeṇa mama mādhavac mantrayiṣye tavārthāya na tu yotsye kathaṃ canae duryodhanārthe yotsyāmi satyam etad iti prabhoa sa hi rājyasya me dātā mantrasyaiva ca mādhavac tasmād devavrataṃ bhūyo vadhopāyārtham ātmanaḥe bhavatā sahitāḥ sarve pṛcchāmo madhusūdanaa tad vayaṃ sahitā gatvā bhīṣmam āśu narottamamc rucite tava vārṣṇeya mantraṃ pṛcchāma kauravama sa vakṣyati hitaṃ vākyaṃ tathyaṃ caiva janārdanac yathā sa vakṣyate kṛṣṇa tathā kartāsmi saṃyugea sa no jayasya dātā ca mantrasya ca dhṛtavrataḥc bālāḥ pitrā vihīnāś ca tena saṃvardhitā vayama taṃ cet pitāmahaṃ vṛddhaṃ hantum icchāmi mādhavab yasyāṅge krīḍitaṃ nityaṃ bālye ca parivardhitāḥb astrāṇi vidhivac caiva śikṣitāni janārdanab taṃ hantum udyatāḥ kṛṣṇa rājyahetor vayaṃ yudhic pituḥ pitaram iṣṭaṃ vai dhig astu kṣatrajīvikāmd satyaṃ bṛhaspater vākyaṃ devānām agrataḥ kilad bhāṣitaṃ guruṇā pūrvaṃ tan nibodha janārdanad putraḥ pitaram āsādya pitā putraṃ ca mānadad rājyārthe ghātayed evaṃ kṣatradharmaḥ sanātanaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa tato bravīn mahārāja vārṣṇeyaḥ kurunandanamc rocate me mahābāho satataṃ tava bhāṣitama devavrataḥ kṛtī bhīṣmaḥ prekṣitenāpi nirdahetc gamyatāṃ sa vadhopāyaṃ praṣṭuṃ sāgaragāsutaḥe vaktum arhati satyaṃ sa tvayā pṛṣṭo viśeṣataḥa te vayaṃ tatra gacchāmaḥ praṣṭuṃ kurupitāmahamc praṇamya śirasā cainaṃ mantraṃ pṛcchāma mādhavae sa no dāsyati yaṃ mantraṃ tena yotsyāmahe parāna evaṃ saṃmantrya vai vīrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajac jagmus te sahitāḥ sarve vāsudevaś ca vīryavāne vimuktaśastrakavacā bhīṣmasya sadanaṃ pratia praviśya ca tadā bhīṣmaṃ śirobhiḥ pratipedirec pūjayanto mahārāja pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabhae praṇamya śirasā cainaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śaraṇam anvayuḥf caraṇopagatān gṛhya pariṣvajya ca pāṇḍavānf mūrdhni caitān upāghrāya aṅkam āropayat tadāf bāṣpaparyākulamukhaḥ smṛtvā pāṇḍuṃ punaḥ punaḥa tān uvāca mahābāhur bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥc svāgataṃ tava vārṣṇeya svāgataṃ te dhanaṃjayae svāgataṃ dharmaputrāya bhīmāya yamayos tathāa kiṃ kāryaṃ vaḥ karomy adya yuṣmatprītivivardhanamb yuddhād anyatra he vatsāḥ prīyantāṃ mā viśaṅkathac sarvātmanā ca kartāsmi yady api syāt suduṣkarama tathā bruvāṇaṃ gāṅgeyaṃ prītiyuktaṃ punaḥ punaḥc uvāca vākyaṃ dīnātmā dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd yathā pṛcchasi mām adya kathaṃ tan me ca vā vibhoa kathaṃ jayema dharmajña kathaṃ rājyaṃ labhemahic prajānāṃ saṃkṣayo na syāt kathaṃ tan me vadābhibhoa bhavān hi no vadhopāyaṃ bravītu svayam ātmanaḥc bhavantaṃ samare rājan viṣahema kathaṃ vayama na hi te sūkṣmam apy asti randhraṃ kurupitāmahac maṇḍalenaiva dhanuṣā sadā dṛśyo si saṃyugea nādadānaṃ saṃdadhānaṃ vikarṣantaṃ dhanur na cac paśyāmas tvā mahābāho rathe sūryam iva sthitama narāśvarathanāgānāṃ hantāraṃ paravīrahanc ka ivotsahate hantuṃ tvāṃ pumān bharatarṣabhaa varṣatā śaravarṣāṇi mahānti puruṣottamac kṣayaṃ nītā hi pṛtanā bhavatā mahatī mamaa yathā yudhi jayeyaṃ tvāṃ yathā rājyaṃ bhaven mamac bhavet sainyasya vā śāntis tan me brūhi pitāmahaa tato bravīc chāṃtanavaḥ pāṇḍavān pāṇḍupūrvajac na kathaṃ cana kaunteya mayi jīvati saṃyugee yuṣmāsu dṛśyate vṛddhiḥ satyam etad bravīmi vaḥa nirjite mayi yuddhe tu dhruvaṃ jeṣyatha kauravānc kṣipraṃ mayi praharata yadīcchatha raṇe jayame anujānāmi vaḥ pārthāḥ praharadhvaṃ yathāsukhama evaṃ hi sukṛtaṃ manye bhavatāṃ vidito hy ahamc hate mayi hataṃ sarvaṃ tasmād evaṃ vidhīyatām yudhiṣṭhira uvācaa brūhi tasmād upāyaṃ no yathā yuddhe jayemahic bhavantaṃ samare kruddhaṃ daṇḍapāṇim ivāntakama śakyo vajradharo jetuṃ varuṇo tha yamas tathāc na bhavān samare śakyaḥ sendrair api surāsuraiḥ bhīṣma uvācaa satyam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi pāṇḍavac nāhaṃ śakyo raṇe jetuṃ sendrair api surāsuraiḥa āttaśastro raṇe yatto gṛhītavarakārmukaḥc nyastaśastraṃ tu māṃ rājan hanyur yudhi mahārathāḥa nikṣiptaśastre patite vimuktakavacadhvajec dravamāṇe ca bhīte ca tavāsmīti ca vādinid strījite strīpradhāne ca strīpradhāyini dharmajaa striyāṃ strīnāmadheye ca vikale caikaputrakec aprasūte ca duṣprekṣye na yuddhaṃ rocate mamaa imaṃ ca śṛṇu me pārtha saṃkalpaṃ pūrvacintitamc amaṅgalyadhvajaṃ dṛṣṭvā na yudhyeyaṃ kathaṃ canaa ya eṣa draupado rājaṃs tava sainye mahārathaḥb apumāṃs tasya putras tu pūrvam āsīd viśāṃ patec śikhaṇḍī samarākāṅkṣī śūraś ca samitiṃjayaḥa yathābhavac ca strī pūrvaṃ paścāt puṃstvam upāgataḥc jānanti ca bhavanto pi sarvam etad yathātathama arjunaḥ samare śūraḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinamc mām eva viśikhais tūrṇam abhidravatu daṃśitaḥa amaṅgalyadhvaje tasmin strīpūrve ca viśeṣataḥc na prahartum abhīpsāmi gṛhīteṣuṃ kathaṃ canaa tad antaraṃ samāsādya pāṇḍavo māṃ dhanaṃjayaḥc śarair ghātayatu kṣipraṃ samantād bharatarṣabhaa na taṃ paśyāmi lokeṣu yo māṃ hanyāt samudyatamc ṛte kṛṣṇān mahābhāgāt pāṇḍavād vā dhanaṃjayāta eṣa tasmāt purodhāya kaṃ cid anyaṃ mamāgrataḥc māṃ pātayatu bībhatsur evaṃ te vijayo bhaveta etat kuruṣva kaunteya yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ mamac tato jeṣyasi saṃgrāme dhārtarāṣṭrān samāgatān saṃjaya uvācaa te nujñātās tataḥ pārthā jagmuḥ svaśibiraṃ pratic abhivādya mahātmānaṃ bhīṣmaṃ kurupitāmahama tathoktavati gāṅgeye paralokāya dīkṣitec arjuno duḥkhasaṃtaptaḥ savrīḍam idam abravīta guruṇā kulavṛddhena kṛtaprajñena dhīmatāc pitāmahena saṃgrāme kathaṃ yotsyāmi mādhavaa krīḍatā hi mayā bālye vāsudeva mahāmanāḥc pāṃsurūṣitagātreṇa mahātmā paruṣīkṛtaḥa yasyāham adhiruhyāṅkaṃ bālaḥ kila gadāgrajac tātety avocaṃ pitaraṃ pituḥ pāṇḍor mahātmanaḥa nāhaṃ tātas tava pitus tāto smi tava bhāratac iti mām abravīd bālye yaḥ sa vadhyaḥ kathaṃ mayāa kāmaṃ vadhyatu me sainyaṃ nāhaṃ yotsye mahātmanāc jayo vāstu vadho vā me kathaṃ vā kṛṣṇa manyased katham asmadvidhaḥ kṛṣṇa jānan dharmaṃ sanātanamd nyastaśastre ca vṛddhe ca prahared dhi pitāmahe śrīkṛṣṇa uvācaa pratijñāya vadhaṃ jiṣṇo purā bhīṣmasya saṃyugec kṣatradharme sthitaḥ pārtha kathaṃ nainaṃ haniṣyasia pātayainaṃ rathāt pārtha vajrāhatam iva drumamc nāhatvā yudhi gāṅgeyaṃ vijayas te bhaviṣyatia diṣṭam etat purā devair bhaviṣyaty avaśasya tec hantā bhīṣmasya pūrvendra iti tan na tad anyathāa na hi bhīṣmaṃ durādharṣaṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakamc tvad anyaḥ śaknuyād dhantum api vajradharaḥ svayama jahi bhīṣmaṃ mahābāho śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mamac yathovāca purā śakraṃ mahābuddhir bṛhaspatiḥa jyāyāṃsam api cec chakra guṇair api samanvitamc ātatāyinam āmantrya hanyād ghātakam āgatama śāśvato yaṃ sthito dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dhanaṃjayac yoddhavyaṃ rakṣitavyaṃ ca yaṣṭavyaṃ cānasūyubhiḥ arjuna uvācaa śikhaṇḍī nidhanaṃ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmasya bhavitā dhruvamc dṛṣṭvaiva hi sadā bhīṣmaḥ pāñcālyaṃ vinivartatea te vayaṃ pramukhe tasya sthāpayitvā śikhaṇḍinamc gāṅgeyaṃ pātayiṣyāma upāyeneti me matiḥa aham anyān maheṣvāsān vārayiṣyāmi sāyakaiḥc śikhaṇḍy api yudhāṃ śreṣṭho bhīṣmam evābhiyāsyatua śrutaṃ te kurumukhyasya nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinamc kanyā hy eṣā purā jātā puruṣaḥ samapadyatad saṃjaya uvācad arjunasya vacaḥ śrutvā bhīṣmasya vadhasaṃyutamd jahṛṣur hṛṣṭaromāṇaḥ sakṛṣṇāḥ pāṇḍavās tadā saṃjaya uvācaa ity evaṃ niścayaṃ kṛtvā pāṇḍavāḥ sahamādhavāḥb anumānya mahātmānaṃ prayayur hṛṣṭamānasāḥc śayanāni yathāsvāni bhejire puruṣarṣabhāḥd svān svān gṛhān abhigatās tāṃ rātrim avasan sukham dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam abhyavartata saṃyugec pāṇḍavāś ca tathā bhīṣmaṃ tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa tataḥ prabhāte vimale sūryasyodayanaṃ pratic vādyamānāsu bherīṣu mṛdaṅgeṣv ānakeṣu caa dhmāyatsu dadhivarṇeṣu jalajeṣu samantataḥc śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya niryātāḥ pāṇḍavā yudhia kṛtvā vyūhaṃ mahārāja sarvaśatrunibarhaṇamc śikhaṇḍī sarvasainyānām agra āsīd viśāṃ patea cakrarakṣau tatas tasya bhīmasenadhanaṃjayauc pṛṣṭhato draupadeyāś ca saubhadraś caiva vīryavāna sātyakiś cekitānaś ca teṣāṃ goptā mahārathaḥc dhṛṣṭadyumnas tataḥ paścāt pāñcālair abhirakṣitaḥa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā yamābhyāṃ sahitaḥ prabhuḥc prayayau siṃhanādena nādayan bharatarṣabhaa virāṭas tu tataḥ paścāt svena sainyena saṃvṛtaḥc drupadaś ca mahārāja tataḥ paścād upādravata kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavānc jaghanaṃ pālayām āsa pāṇḍusainyasya bhārataa evaṃ vyūhya mahat sainyaṃ pāṇḍavās tava vāhinīmc abhyadravanta saṃgrāme tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥa tathaiva kuravo rājan bhīṣmaṃ kṛtvā mahābalamc agrataḥ sarvasainyānāṃ prayayuḥ pāṇḍavān pratia putrais tava durādharṣai rakṣitaḥ sumahābalaiḥc tato droṇo maheṣvāsaḥ putraś cāsya mahārathaḥa bhagadattas tataḥ paścād gajānīkena saṃvṛtaḥc kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca bhagadattam anuvrataua kāmbojarājo balavāṃs tataḥ paścāt sudakṣiṇaḥc māgadhaś ca jayatsenaḥ saubalaś ca bṛhadbalaḥa tathetare maheṣvāsāḥ suśarmapramukhā nṛpāḥc jaghanaṃ pālayām āsus tava sainyasya bhārataa divase divase prāpte bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yudhic āsurān akarod vyūhān paiśācān atha rākṣasāna tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhāratac anyonyaṃ nighnatāṃ rājan yamarāṣṭravivardhanama arjunapramukhāḥ pārthāḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinamc bhīṣmaṃ yuddhe bhyavartanta kiranto vividhāñ śarāna tatra bhārata bhīmena pīḍitās tāvakāḥ śaraiḥc rudhiraughapariklinnāḥ paralokaṃ yayus tadāa nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥc tava sainyaṃ samāsādya pīḍayām āsur ojasāa te vadhyamānāḥ samare tāvakā bharatarṣabhac nāśaknuvan vārayituṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balama tatas tu tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ vadhyamānaṃ samantataḥc saṃprādravad diśo rājan kālyamānaṃ mahārathaiḥa trātāraṃ nādhyagacchanta tāvakā bharatarṣabhac vadhyamānāḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa pīḍyamānaṃ balaṃ pārthair dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaḥ parākramīc yad akārṣīd raṇe kruddhas tan mamācakṣva saṃjayaa kathaṃ vā pāṇḍavān yuddhe pratyudyātaḥ paraṃtapaḥc vinighnan somakān vīrāṃs tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa ācakṣe te mahārāja yad akārṣīt pitāmahaḥc pīḍite tava putrasya sainye pāṇḍavasṛñjayaiḥa prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajac abhyavartanta nighnantas tava putrasya vāhinīma taṃ vināśaṃ manuṣyendra naravāraṇavājināmc nāmṛṣyata tadā bhīṣmaḥ sainyaghātaṃ raṇe paraiḥa sa pāṇḍavān maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālāṃś ca sasṛñjayānc abhyadravata durdharṣas tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥa sa pāṇḍavānāṃ pravarān pañca rājan mahārathānc āttaśastrān raṇe yattān vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥd bhīṣmaḥ paramasaṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥe nārācair vatsadantaiś ca śitair añjalikais tathāf nānāśastrāstravarṣais tān vīryāmarṣapraveritaiḥa nijaghne samare kruddho hastyaśvam amitaṃ bahuc rathino pātayad rājan rathebhyaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥa sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ padātīṃś ca samāgatānc gajārohān gajebhyaś ca pareṣāṃ vidadhad bhayama tam ekaṃ samare bhīṣmaṃ tvaramāṇaṃ mahārathamc pāṇḍavāḥ samavartanta vajrapāṇim ivāsurāḥa śakrāśanisamasparśān vimuñcan niśitāñ śarānc dikṣv adṛśyata sarvāsu ghoraṃ saṃdhārayan vapuḥa maṇḍalīkṛtam evāsya nityaṃ dhanur adṛśyatac saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya śakracāpanibhaṃ mahata tad dṛṣṭvā samare karma tava putrā viśāṃ patec vismayaṃ paramaṃ prāptāḥ pitāmaham apūjayana pārthā vimanaso bhūtvā praikṣanta pitaraṃ tavac yudhyamānaṃ raṇe śūraṃ vipracittim ivāmarāḥe na cainaṃ vārayām āsur vyāttānanam ivāntakama daśame hani saṃprāpte rathānīkaṃ śikhaṇḍinaḥc adahan niśitair bāṇaiḥ kṛṣṇavartmeva kānanama taṃ śikhaṇḍī tribhir bāṇair abhyavidhyat stanāntarec āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ kālasṛṣṭam ivāntakama sa tenātibhṛśaṃ viddhaḥ prekṣya bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinamc anicchann api saṃkruddhaḥ prahasann idam abravīta kāmam abhyasa vā mā vā na tvāṃ yotsye kathaṃ canac yaiva hi tvaṃ kṛtā dhātrā saiva hi tvaṃ śikhaṇḍinīa tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā śikhaṇḍī krodhamūrchitaḥc uvāca bhīṣmaṃ samare sṛkkiṇī parilelihand sarvam eva mahāyuddhaṃ śrutavantaṃ mahāraṇea jānāmi tvāṃ mahābāho kṣatriyāṇāṃ kṣayaṃkaramc mayā śrutaṃ ca te yuddhaṃ jāmadagnyena vai sahaa divyaś ca te prabhāvo yaṃ sa mayā bahuśaḥ śrutaḥc jānann api prabhāvaṃ te yotsye dyāhaṃ tvayā sahaa pāṇḍavānāṃ priyaṃ kurvann ātmanaś ca narottamac adya tvā yodhayiṣyāmi raṇe puruṣasattamaa dhruvaṃ ca tvā haniṣyāmi śape satyena te grataḥc etac chrutvā vaco mahyaṃ yat kṣamaṃ tat samācaraa kāmam abhyasa vā mā vā na me jīvan vimokṣyasec sudṛṣṭaḥ kriyatāṃ bhīṣma loko yaṃ samitiṃjayaa evam uktvā tato bhīṣmaṃ pañcabhir nataparvabhiḥc avidhyata raṇe rājan praṇunnaṃ vākyasāyakaiḥa tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā savyasācī paraṃtapaḥc kālo yam iti saṃcintya śikhaṇḍinam acodayata ahaṃ tvām anuyāsyāmi parān vidrāvayañ śaraiḥc abhidrava susaṃrabdho bhīṣmaṃ bhīmaparākramama na hi te saṃyuge pīḍāṃ śaktaḥ kartuṃ mahābalaḥc tasmād adya mahābāho vīra bhīṣmam abhidravaa ahatvā samare bhīṣmaṃ yadi yāsyasi māriṣac avahāsyo sya lokasya bhaviṣyasi mayā sahaa nāvahāsyā yathā vīra bhavema paramāhavec tathā kuru raṇe yatnaṃ sādhayasva pitāmahama ahaṃ te rakṣaṇaṃ yuddhe kariṣyāmi paraṃtapac vārayan rathinaḥ sarvān sādhayasva pitāmahama droṇaṃ ca droṇaputraṃ ca kṛpaṃ cātha suyodhanamc citrasenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca saindhavaṃ ca jayadrathama vindānuvindāv āvantyau kāmbojaṃ ca sudakṣiṇamc bhagadattaṃ tathā śūraṃ māgadhaṃ ca mahārathama saumadattiṃ raṇe śūram ārśyaśṛṅgiṃ ca rākṣasamc trigartarājaṃ ca raṇe saha sarvair mahārathaiḥe aham āvārayiṣyāmi veleva makarālayama kurūṃś ca sahitān sarvān ye caiṣāṃ sainikāḥ sthitāḥc nivārayiṣyāmi raṇe sādhayasva pitāmaham dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ śikhaṇḍī gāṅgeyam abhyadhāvat pitāmahamc pāñcālyaḥ samare kruddho dharmātmānaṃ yatavratama ke rakṣan pāṇḍavānīke śikhaṇḍinam udāyudhamc tvaramāṇās tvarākāle jigīṣanto mahārathāḥa kathaṃ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ sa tasmin daśame hanic ayudhyata mahāvīryaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥa na mṛṣyāmi raṇe bhīṣmaṃ pratyudyātaṃ śikhaṇḍinamc kaccin na rathabhaṅgo sya dhanur vāśīryatāsyataḥ saṃjaya uvācaa nāśīryata dhanus tasya rathabhaṅgo na cāpy abhūtc yudhyamānasya saṃgrāme bhīṣmasya bharatarṣabhae nighnataḥ samare śatrūñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa anekaśatasāhasrās tāvakānāṃ mahārathāḥc rathadantigaṇā rājan hayāś caiva susajjitāḥe abhyavartanta yuddhāya puraskṛtya pitāmahama yathāpratijñaṃ kauravya sa cāpi samitiṃjayaḥc pārthānām akarod bhīṣmaḥ satataṃ samitikṣayama yudhyamānaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ vinighnantaṃ parāñ śaraiḥc pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarva evābhyavārayana daśame hani saṃprāpte tatāpa ripuvāhinīmc kīryamāṇāṃ śitair bāṇaiḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa na hi bhīṣmaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ pāṇḍupūrvajac aśaknuvan raṇe jetuṃ pāśahastam ivāntakama athopāyān mahārāja savyasācī paraṃtapaḥc trāsayan rathinaḥ sarvān bībhatsur aparājitaḥa siṃhavad vinadann uccair dhanurjyāṃ vikṣipan muhuḥc śaraughān visṛjan pārtho vyacarat kālavad raṇea tasya śabdena vitrastās tāvakā bharatarṣabhac siṃhasyeva mṛgā rājan vyadravanta mahābhayāta jayantaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvatsainyaṃ cābhipīḍitamc duryodhanas tato bhīṣmam abravīd bhṛśapīḍitaḥa eṣa pāṇḍusutas tāta śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥc dahate māmakān sarvān kṛṣṇavartmeva kānanama paśya sainyāni gāṅgeya dravamāṇāni sarvaśaḥc pāṇḍavena yudhāṃ śreṣṭha kālyamānāni saṃyugea yathā paśugaṇān pālaḥ saṃkālayati kānanec tathedaṃ māmakaṃ sainyaṃ kālyate śatrutāpanaa dhanaṃjayaśarair bhagnaṃ dravamāṇam itas tataḥc bhīmo hy eṣa durādharṣo vidrāvayati me balama sātyakiś cekitānaś ca mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc abhimanyuś ca vikrānto vāhinīṃ dahate mamaa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā śūro rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥc vyadrāvayetāṃ sahasā sainyaṃ mama mahābalaua vadhyamānasya sainyasya sarvair etair mahābalaiḥc nānyāṃ gatiṃ prapaśyāmi sthāne yuddhe ca bhārataa ṛte tvāṃ puruṣavyāghra devatulyaparākramac paryāptaś ca bhavān kṣipraṃ pīḍitānāṃ gatir bhavaa evam ukto mahārāja pitā devavratas tavac cintayitvā muhūrtaṃ tu kṛtvā niścayam ātmanaḥd pātayiṣye ripūn anyān pāṇḍavān pratipālayand pratijñāto jayo hy adya pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāme tava saṃdhārayan putram abravīc chaṃtanoḥ sutaḥa duryodhana vijānīhi sthiro bhava viśāṃ patec pūrvakālaṃ tava mayā pratijñātaṃ mahābalaa hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahātmanāmc saṃgrāmād vyapayātavyam etat karma mamāhnikame iti tat kṛtavāṃś cāhaṃ yathoktaṃ bharatarṣabhaa adya cāpi mahat karma prakariṣye mahāhavec ahaṃ vā nihataḥ śeṣye haniṣye vādya pāṇḍavānd aśakyāḥ pāṇḍavā jetuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥd kiṃ punar martyadharmeṇa kṣatriyeṇa mahābalaa adya te puruṣavyāghra pratimokṣye ṛṇaṃ mahatc bhartṛpiṇḍakṛtaṃ rājan nihataḥ pṛtanāmukhea ity uktvā bharataśreṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyān pratapañ śaraiḥc āsasāda durādharṣaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīma anīkamadhye tiṣṭhantaṃ gāṅgeyaṃ bharatarṣabhac āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ pāṇḍavāḥ paryavārayana daśame hani tasmiṃs tu darśayañ śaktim ātmanaḥc rājañ śatasahasrāṇi so vadhīt kurunandanaa pañcālānāṃ ca ye śreṣṭhā rājaputrā mahābalāḥc teṣām ādatta tejāṃsi jalaṃ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥa hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvināmc sārohāṇāṃ mahārāja hayānāṃ cāyutaṃ punaḥa pūrṇe śatasahasre dve padātīnāṃ narottamaḥc prajajvāla raṇe bhīṣmo vidhūma iva pāvakaḥa na cainaṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ ke cic chekur nirīkṣitumc uttaraṃ mārgam āsthāya tapantam iva bhāskarama te pāṇḍaveyāḥ saṃrabdhā maheṣvāsena pīḍitāḥc vadhāyābhyadravan bhīṣmaṃ sṛñjayāś ca mahārathāḥa sa yudhyamāno bahubhir bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadāc avakīrṇo mahābāhuḥ śailo meghair ivāsitaiḥa putrās tu tava gāṅgeyaṃ samantāt paryavārayanc mahatyā senayā sārdhaṃ tato yuddham avartata saṃjaya uvācaa arjunas tu raṇe rājan dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramamc śikhaṇḍinam athovāca samabhyehi pitāmahama na cāpi bhīs tvayā kāryā bhīṣmād adya kathaṃ canac aham enaṃ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ pātayiṣye rathottamāta evam uktas tu pārthena śikhaṇḍī bharatarṣabhac abhyadravata gāṅgeyaṃ śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitama dhṛṣṭadyumnas tathā rājan saubhadraś ca mahārathaḥc hṛṣṭāv ādravatāṃ bhīṣmaṃ śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitama virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau kuntibhojaś ca daṃśitaḥc abhyadravata gāṅgeyaṃ putrasya tava paśyataḥa nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dharmarājaś ca vīryavānc tathetarāṇi sainyāni sarvāṇy eva viśāṃ patee samādravanta gāṅgeyaṃ śrutvā pārthasya bhāṣitama pratyudyayus tāvakāś ca sametās tān mahārathānc yathāśakti yathotsāhaṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇua citraseno mahārāja cekitānaṃ samabhyayātc bhīṣmaprepsuṃ raṇe yāntaṃ vṛṣaṃ vyāghraśiśur yathāa dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahārāja bhīṣmāntikam upāgatamc tvaramāṇo raṇe yattaṃ kṛtavarmā nyavārayatd tvaramāṇaṃ raṇe yattaṃ saumadattir avārayata bhīmasenaṃ susaṃkruddhaṃ gāṅgeyasya vadhaiṣiṇamc tvaramāṇo mahārāja saumadattir nyavārayata tathaiva nakulaṃ vīraṃ kirantaṃ sāyakān bahūnc vikarṇo vārayām āsa icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitama sahadevaṃ tathā yāntaṃ yattaṃ bhīṣmarathaṃ pratic vārayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvato yudhia rākṣasaṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ bhaimaseniṃ mahābalamc bhīṣmasya nidhanaṃ prepsuṃ durmukho bhyadravad balīa sātyakiṃ samare kruddham ārśyaśṛṅgir avārayatb bhīṣmasya vadham icchantaṃ pāṇḍavaprītikāmyayāc abhimanyuṃ mahārāja yāntaṃ bhīṣmarathaṃ pratie sudakṣiṇo mahārāja kāmbojaḥ pratyavārayata virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau sametāv arimardanauc aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddho vārayām āsa bhārataa tathā pāṇḍusutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣiṇamc bhāradvājo raṇe yatto dharmaputram avārayata arjunaṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinamc bhīṣmaprepsuṃ mahārāja tāpayantaṃ diśo daśae duḥśāsano maheṣvāso vārayām āsa saṃyugea anye ca tāvakā yodhāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathānc bhīṣmāyābhimukhaṃ yātān vārayām āsur āhavea dhṛṣṭadyumnas tu sainyāni prākrośata punaḥ punaḥc abhidravata saṃrabdhā bhīṣmam ekaṃ mahābalama eṣo rjuno raṇe bhīṣmaṃ prayāti kurunandanaḥc abhidravata mā bhaiṣṭa bhīṣmo na prāpsyate hi vaḥa arjunaṃ samare yoddhuṃ notsahetāpi vāsavaḥc kim u bhīṣmo raṇe vīrā gatasattvo lpajīvitaḥa iti senāpateḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc abhyadravanta saṃhṛṣṭā gāṅgeyasya rathaṃ pratia āgacchatas tān samare vāryoghān prabalān ivac nyavārayanta saṃhṛṣṭās tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥa duḥśāsano mahārāja bhayaṃ tyaktvā mahārathaḥc bhīṣmasya jīvitākāṅkṣī dhanaṃjayam upādravata tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrā gāṅgeyasya rathaṃ pratic abhyadravanta saṃgrāme tava putrān mahārathānd ayodhayac ca samare tava putro mahārathaḥa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma citrarūpaṃ viśāṃ patec duḥśāsanarathaṃ prāpto yat pārtho nātyavartataa yathā vārayate velā kṣubhitaṃ vai mahārṇavamc tathaiva pāṇḍavaṃ kruddhaṃ tava putro nyavārayata ubhau hi rathināṃ śreṣṭhāv ubhau bhārata durjayauc ubhau candrārkasadṛśau kāntyā dīptyā ca bhārataa tau tathā jātasaṃrambhāv anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇauc samīyatur mahāsaṃkhye mayaśakrau yathā purāa duḥśāsano mahārāja pāṇḍavaṃ viśikhais tribhiḥc vāsudevaṃ ca viṃśatyā tāḍayām āsa saṃyugea tato rjuno jātamanyur vārṣṇeyaṃ vīkṣya pīḍitamc duḥśāsanaṃ śatenājau nārācānāṃ samārpayate te tasya kavacaṃ bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhavef yathaiva pannagā rājaṃs taṭākaṃ tṛṣitā yathāa duḥśāsanas tataḥ kruddhaḥ pārthaṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥc lalāṭe bharataśreṣṭha śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa lalāṭasthais tu tair bāṇaiḥ śuśubhe pāṇḍavottamaḥc yathā merur mahārāja śṛṅgair atyartham ucchritaiḥa so tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ putreṇa tava dhanvināc vyarājata raṇe pārthaḥ kiṃśukaḥ puṣpavān ivaa duḥśāsanaṃ tataḥ kruddhaḥ pīḍayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥc parvaṇīva susaṃkruddho rāhur ugro niśākarama pīḍyamāno balavatā putras tava viśāṃ patec vivyādha samare pārthaṃ kaṅkapatraiḥ śilāśitaiḥa tasya pārtho dhanuś chittvā tvaramāṇaḥ parākramīc ājaghāna tataḥ paścāt putraṃ te navabhiḥ śaraiḥa so nyat kārmukam ādāya bhīṣmasya pramukhe sthitaḥc arjunaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā bāhvor urasi cārpayata tasya kruddho mahārāja pāṇḍavaḥ śatrukarśanaḥc apraiṣīd viśikhān ghorān yamadaṇḍopamān bahūna aprāptān eva tān bāṇāṃś ciccheda tanayas tavac yatamānasya pārthasya tad adbhutam ivābhavate pārthaṃ ca niśitair bāṇair avidhyat tanayas tavaa tataḥ kruddho raṇe pārthaḥ śarān saṃdhāya kārmukec preṣayām āsa samare svarṇapuṅkhāñ śilāśitāna nyamajjaṃs te mahārāja tasya kāye mahātmanaḥc yathā haṃsā mahārāja taḍāgaṃ prāpya bhārataa pīḍitaś caiva putras te pāṇḍavena mahātmanāc hitvā pārthaṃ raṇe tūrṇaṃ bhīṣmasya ratham āśrayate agādhe majjatas tasya dvīpo bhīṣmo bhavat tadāa pratilabhya tataḥ saṃjñāṃ putras tava viśāṃ patec avārayat tataḥ śūro bhūya eva parākramīa śaraiḥ suniśitaiḥ pārthaṃ yathā vṛtraḥ puraṃdaramc nirbibheda mahāvīryo vivyathe naiva cārjunāt saṃjaya uvācaa sātyakiṃ daṃśitaṃ yuddhe bhīṣmāyābhyudyataṃ tadāc ārśyaśṛṅgir maheṣvāso vārayām āsa saṃyugea mādhavas tu susaṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc ājaghāna raṇe rājan prahasann iva bhārataa tathaiva rākṣaso rājan mādhavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc ardayām āsa rājendra saṃkruddhaḥ śinipuṃgavama śaineyaḥ śarasaṃghaṃ tu preṣayām āsa saṃyugec rākṣasāya susaṃkruddho mādhavaḥ paravīrahāa tato rakṣo mahābāhuṃ sātyakiṃ satyavikramamc vivyādha viśikhais tīkṣṇaiḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda caa mādhavas tu bhṛśaṃ viddho rākṣasena raṇe tadāc dhairyam ālambya tejasvī jahāsa ca nanāda caa bhagadattas tataḥ kruddho mādhavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc tāḍayām āsa samare tottrair iva mahāgajama vihāya rākṣasaṃ yuddhe śaineyo rathināṃ varaḥc prāgjyotiṣāya cikṣepa śarān saṃnataparvaṇaḥa tasya prāgjyotiṣo rājā mādhavasya mahad dhanuḥc ciccheda śitadhāreṇa bhallena kṛtahastavata athānyad dhanur ādāya vegavat paravīrahāc bhagadattaṃ raṇe kruddho vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa so tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ sṛkkiṇī saṃlihan muhuḥc śaktiṃ kanakavaiḍūryabhūṣitām āyasīṃ dṛḍhāme yamadaṇḍopamāṃ ghorāṃ prāhiṇot sātyakāya vaia tām āpatantīṃ sahasā tasya bāhor baleritāmc sātyakiḥ samare rājaṃs tridhā ciccheda sāyakaiḥd sā hemavikṛtā śaktir mādhavasya bhujacyutaiḥe sā papāta tadā bhūmau maholkeva hataprabhāa śaktiṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā putras tava viśāṃ patec mahatā rathavaṃśena vārayām āsa mādhavama tathā parivṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā vārṣṇeyānāṃ mahārathamc duryodhano bhṛśaṃ hṛṣṭo bhrātṝn sarvān uvāca haa tathā kuruta kauravyā yathā vaḥ sātyako yudhic na jīvan pratiniryāti mahato smād rathavrajāte asmin hate hataṃ manye pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balama tat tatheti vacas tasya parigṛhya mahārathāḥc śaineyaṃ yodhayām āsur bhīṣmasya pramukhe tadāa abhimanyuṃ tadāyāntaṃ bhīṣmāyābhyudyataṃ mṛdhec kāmbojarājo balavān vārayām āsa saṃyugea ārjunir nṛpatiṃ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc punar eva catuḥṣaṣṭyā rājan vivyādha taṃ nṛpama sudakṣiṇas tu samare kārṣṇiṃ vivyādha pañcabhiḥc sārathiṃ cāsya navabhir icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitama tad yuddham āsīt sumahat tayos tatra parākramec yad abhyadhāvad gāṅgeyaṃ śikhaṇḍī śatrutāpanaḥa virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau vārayantau mahācamūmc bhīṣmaṃ ca yudhi saṃrabdhāv ādravantau mahārathaua aśvatthāmā tataḥ kruddhaḥ samāyād rathasattamaḥc tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tava teṣāṃ ca bhārataa virāṭo daśabhir bhallair ājaghāna paraṃtapab tato droṇasutaṃ yodhān dravamāṇaṃ mahāraṇec yatamānaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ drauṇim āhavaśobhinamc visṛjantaṃ śarān dṛṣṭvāa drupadaś ca tribhir bāṇair vivyādha niśitais tathāc guruputraṃ samāsādya bhīṣmasya purataḥ sthitama aśvatthāmā tatas tau tu vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥc virāṭadrupadau vṛddhau bhīṣmaṃ prati samudyataua tatrādbhutam apaśyāma vṛddhayoś caritaṃ mahatc yad drauṇeḥ sāyakān ghorān pratyavārayatāṃ yudhia sahadevaṃ tathā yāntaṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvato bhyayātc yathā nāgo vane nāgaṃ matto mattam upādravata kṛpaś ca samare rājan mādrīputraṃ mahārathamc ājaghāna śarais tūrṇaṃ saptatyā rukmabhūṣaṇaiḥa tasya mādrīsutaś cāpaṃ dvidhā ciccheda sāyakaiḥc athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥa so nyat kārmukam ādāya samare bhārasādhanamc mādrīputraṃ susaṃhṛṣṭo daśabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥe ājaghānorasi kruddha icchan bhīṣmasya jīvitama tathaiva pāṇḍavo rājañ śāradvatam amarṣaṇamc ājaghānorasi kruddho bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣayāe tayor yuddhaṃ samabhavad ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvahama nakulaṃ tu raṇe kruddhaṃ vikarṇaḥ śatrutāpanaḥc vivyādha sāyakaiḥ ṣaṣṭyā rakṣan bhīṣmasya jīvitama nakulo pi bhṛśaṃ viddhas tava putreṇa dhanvināb tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇamc vikarṇaṃ saptasaptatyā nirbibheda śilīmukhaiḥa tatra tau naraśārdūlau bhīṣmahetoḥ paraṃtapauc anyonyaṃ jaghnatur vīrau goṣṭhe govṛṣabhāv ivaa ghaṭotkacaṃ raṇe yattaṃ nighnantaṃ tava vāhinīmc durmukhaḥ samare prāyād bhīṣmahetoḥ parākramīa haiḍimbas tu tato rājan durmukhaṃ śatrutāpanamc ājaghānorasi kruddho navatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa bhīmasenasutaṃ cāpi durmukhaḥ sumukhaiḥ śaraiḥc ṣaṣṭyā vīro nadan hṛṣṭo vivyādha raṇamūrdhania dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ raṇe yāntaṃ bhīṣmasya vadhakāṅkṣiṇamc hārdikyo vārayām āsa rakṣan bhīṣmasya jīvitama vārṣṇeyaḥ pārṣataṃ śūraṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥc punaḥ pañcāśatā tūrṇam ājaghāna stanāntared   tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravītd ājaghāna mahābāhuḥ pārṣataṃ taṃ mahārathama tathaiva pārṣato rājan hārdikyaṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc vivyādha niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ kaṅkapatraparicchadaiḥa tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ bhīṣmahetor mahāraṇec anyonyātiśayair yuktaṃ yathā vṛtramahendrayoḥa bhīmasenam athāyāntaṃ bhīṣmaṃ prati mahābalamc bhūriśravābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta saumadattir atho bhīmam ājaghāna stanāntarec nārācena sutīkṣṇena rukmapuṅkhena saṃyugea uraḥsthena babhau tena bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānc skandaśaktyā yathā krauñcaḥ purā nṛpatisattamaa tau śarān sūryasaṃkāśān karmāraparimārjitānc anyonyasya raṇe kruddhau cikṣipāte muhur muhuḥa bhīmo bhīṣmavadhākānṣkī saumadattiṃ mahārathamc tathā bhīṣmajaye gṛdhnuḥ saumadattiś ca pāṇḍavamd ayodhayetāṃ samare tulyavegau narottamaue kṛtapratikṛte yattau yodhayām āsatū raṇea yudhiṣṭhiraṃ mahārāja mahatyā senayā vṛtamc bhīṣmāyābhimukhaṃ yāntaṃ bhāradvājo nyavārayatd tatra yuddham abhūd ghoraṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥa droṇasya rathanirghoṣaṃ parjanyaninadopamamc śrutvā prabhadrakā rājan samakampanta māriṣaa sā senā mahatī rājan pāṇḍuputrasya saṃyugec droṇena vāritā yattā na cacāla padāt padama cekitānaṃ raṇe kruddhaṃ bhīṣmaṃ prati janeśvarac citrasenas tava sutaḥ kruddharūpam avārayata bhīṣmahetoḥ parākrāntaś citraseno mahārathaḥc cekitānaṃ paraṃ śaktyā yodhayām āsa bhārataa tathaiva cekitāno pi citrasenam ayodhayatc tad yuddham āsīt sumahat tayos tatra parākramea arjuno vāryamāṇas tu bahuśas tanayena tec vimukhīkṛtya putraṃ te tava senāṃ mamarda haa duḥśāsano pi parayā śaktyā pārtham avārayatc kathaṃ bhīṣmaṃ paro hanyād iti niścitya bhārataa sā vadhyamānā samare putrasya tava vāhinīc loḍyate rathibhiḥ śreṣṭhais tatra tatraiva bhārata saṃjaya uvācaa atha vīro maheṣvāso mattavāraṇavikramaḥc samādāya mahac cāpaṃ mattavāraṇavāraṇama vidhunvāno dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ drāvayāṇo mahārathānc pṛtanāṃ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ pātayāno mahārathaḥd yuktaḥ prītyā pāṇḍavānāṃ gāhamāno mahācamūma nimittāni nimittajñaḥ sarvato vīkṣya vīryavānc pratapantam anīkāni droṇaḥ putram abhāṣataa ayaṃ sa divasas tāta yatra pārtho mahārathaḥc jighāṃsuḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ paraṃ yatnaṃ kariṣyatia utpatanti hi me bāṇā dhanuḥ prasphuratīva mec yogam astrāṇi gacchanti krūre me vartate matiḥa dikṣu śāntāsu ghorāṇi vyāharanti mṛgadvijāḥc nīcair gṛdhrā nilīyante bhāratānāṃ camūṃ pratia naṣṭaprabha ivādityaḥ sarvato lohitā diśaḥc rasate vyathate bhūmir anuṣṭanati vāhanama kaṅkā gṛdhrā balākāś ca vyāharanti muhur muhuḥc śivāś cāśivanirghoṣā vedayantyo mahad bhayama papāta mahatī colkā madhyenādityamaṇḍalātc sakabandhaś ca parigho bhānum āvṛtya tiṣṭhatia pariveṣas tathā ghoraś candrabhāskarayor abhūtc vedayāno bhayaṃ ghoraṃ rājñāṃ dehāvakartanama devatāyatanasthāś ca kauravendrasya devatāḥc kampante ca hasante ca nṛtyanti ca rudanti caa apasavyaṃ grahāś cakrur alakṣmāṇaṃ niśākaramc avākśirāś ca bhagavān udatiṣṭhata candramāḥa vapūṃṣi ca narendrāṇāṃ vigatānīva lakṣayec dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu na ca bhrājanti daṃśitāḥa senayor ubhayoś caiva samantāc chrūyate mahānc pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣo gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanaḥd tathā kilakilāśabdaḥ śrūyate vānarasya cad yasya lāṅgūlaśabdena sphuṭatīva nabhastalaṃa dhruvam āsthāya bībhatsur uttamāstrāṇi saṃyugec apāsyānyān raṇe yodhān abhyasyati pitāmahama hṛṣyanti romakūpāni sīdatīva ca me manaḥc cintayitvā mahābāho bhīṣmārjunasamāgamama taṃ caiva nikṛtiprajñaṃ pāñcālyaṃ pāpacetasamc puraskṛtya raṇe pārtho bhīṣmasyāyodhanaṃ gataḥa abravīc ca purā bhīṣmo nāhaṃ hanyāṃ śikhaṇḍinamc strī hy eṣā vihitā dhātrā daivāc ca sa punaḥ pumāna amaṅgalyadhvajaś caiva yājñasenir mahārathaḥc na cāmaṅgalaketoḥ sa prahared āpagāsutaḥa etad vicintayānasya prajñā sīdati me bhṛśamb abhyudyataṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā bhairavāstraṃ ca pāṇḍavamc adyaiva tu raṇe pārthaḥ kuruvṛddham upādravata yudhiṣṭhirasya ca krodho bhīṣmārjunasamāgamaḥc mama cāstrābhisaṃrambhaḥ prajānām aśubhaṃ dhruvama manasvī balavāñ śūraḥ kṛtāstro dṛḍhavikramaḥc dūrapātī dṛḍheṣuś ca nimittajñaś ca pāṇḍavaḥa ajeyaḥ samare caiva devair api savāsavaiḥc balavān buddhimāṃś caiva jitakleśo yudhāṃ varaḥa vijayī ca raṇe nityaṃ bhairavāstraś ca pāṇḍavaḥc tasya mārgaṃ pariharan drutaṃ gaccha yatavratama paśya caitan mahābāho vaiśasaṃ samupasthitamc hemacitrāṇi śūrāṇāṃ mahānti ca śubhāni caa kavacāny avadīryante śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc chidyante ca dhvajāgrāṇi tomarāṇi dhanūṃṣi caa prāsāś ca vimalās tīkṣṇāḥ śaktyaś ca kanakojjvalāḥc vaijayantyaś ca nāgānāṃ saṃkruddhena kirīṭināa nāyaṃ saṃrakṣituṃ kālaḥ prāṇān putropajīvibhiḥc yāhi svargaṃ puraskṛtya yaśase vijayāya caa hayanāgarathāvartāṃ mahāghorāṃ sudustarāmc rathena saṃgrāmanadīṃ taraty eṣa kapidhvajaḥd pūrvaṃ caiva mayāśrāvi tapasā ghorarūpiṇād brahmacaryeṇa mahatā phālgunaś carate tapaḥd tat tapaḥ saphalaṃ ceha kairāte savyasācināa brahmaṇyatā damo dānaṃ tapaś ca caritaṃ mahatc ihaiva dṛśyate rājño bhrātā yasya dhanaṃjayaḥa bhīmasenaś ca balavān mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavauc vāsudevaś ca vārṣṇeyo yasya nātho vyavasthitaḥa tasyaiṣa manyuprabhavo dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥc tapodagdhaśarīrasya kopo dahati bhāratāna eṣa saṃdṛśyate pārtho vāsudevavyapāśrayaḥc dārayan sarvasainyāni dhārtarāṣṭrāṇi sarvaśaḥa etad ālokyate sainyaṃ kṣobhyamāṇaṃ kirīṭināc mahorminaddhaṃ sumahat timineva nadīmukhama hāhākilakilāśabdāḥ śrūyante ca camūmukhec yāhi pāñcāladāyādam ahaṃ yāsye yudhiṣṭhirama durlabhaṃ hy antaraṃ rājño vyūhasyāmitatejasaḥc samudrakukṣipratimaṃ sarvato tirathaiḥ sthitaiḥa sātyakiś cābhimanyuś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnavṛkodarauc parirakṣanti rājānaṃ yamau ca manujeśvarama upendrasadṛśaḥ śyāmo mahāśāla ivodgataḥc eṣa gacchaty anīkāni dvitīya iva phalgunaḥa uttamāstrāṇi cādatsva gṛhītvānyan mahad dhanuḥc pārśvato yāhi rājānaṃ yudhyasva ca vṛkodarama ko hi necchet priyaṃ putraṃ jīvantaṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥc kṣatradharmaṃ puraskṛtya tatas tvā viniyujmahea eṣa cāpi raṇe bhīṣmo dahate vai mahācamūmc yuddhe susadṛśas tāta yamasya varuṇasya cad saṃjayaḥd putraṃ samanuśāsyaiva bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānd mahāraṇe mahārājaṃ dharmarājam ayodhayat etac chrutvā vacas tasya droṇasya ca mahātmanaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa bhagadattaḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥc vindānuvindāv āvantyau saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥa citraseno vikarṇaś ca tathā durmarṣaṇo yuvāc daśaite tāvakā yodhā bhīmasenam ayodhayana mahatyā senayā yuktā nānādeśasamutthayāc bhīṣmasya samare rājan prārthayānā mahad yaśaḥa śalyas tu navabhir bāṇair bhīmasenam atāḍayatc kṛtavarmā tribhir bāṇaiḥ kṛpaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥa citraseno vikarṇaś ca bhagadattaś ca māriṣac daśabhir daśabhir bhallair bhīmasenam atāḍayana saindhavaś ca tribhir bāṇair jatrudeśe bhyatāḍayatc vindānuvindāv āvantyau pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥe durmarṣaṇaś ca viṃśatyā pāṇḍavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa sa tān sarvān mahārāja bhrājamānān pṛthak pṛthakc pravīrān sarvalokasya dhārtarāṣṭrān mahārathāne vivyādha bahubhir bāṇair bhīmaseno mahābalaḥa śalyaṃ pañcāśatā viddhvā kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥc kṛpasya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ madhye ciccheda bhāratae athainaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥa vindānuvindau ca tathā tribhis tribhir atāḍayatc durmarṣaṇaṃ ca viṃśatyā citrasenaṃ ca pañcabhiḥa vikarṇaṃ daśabhir bāṇaiḥ pañcabhiś ca jayadrathamc viddhvā bhīmo nadad dhṛṣṭaḥ saindhavaṃ ca punas tribhiḥd droṇasya ca dhanur bhīmas tribhir bāṇair acicchidea athānyad dhanur ādāya gautamo rathināṃ varaḥc bhīmaṃ vivyādha saṃrabdho daśabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa sa viddho bahubhir bāṇais tottrair iva mahādvipaḥc tataḥ kruddho mahābāhur bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavāne gautamaṃ tāḍayām āsa śarair bahubhir āhavea saindhavasya tathāśvāṃś ca sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥc prāhiṇon mṛtyulokāya kālāntakasamadyutiḥa hatāśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahārathaḥc śarāṃś cikṣepa niśitān bhīmasenasya saṃyugea tasya bhīmo dhanurmadhye dvābhyāṃ ciccheda bhāratac bhallābhyāṃ bharataśreṣṭha saindhavasya mahātmanaḥa sa cchinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥc citrasenarathaṃ rājann āruroha tvarānvitaḥa atyadbhutaṃ raṇe karma kṛtavāṃs tatra pāṇḍavaḥc mahārathāñ śarair viddhvā vārayitvā mahārathaḥe virathaṃ saindhavaṃ cakre sarvalokasya paśyataḥa nātīva mamṛṣe śalyo bhīmasenasya vikramamc sa saṃdhāya śarāṃs tīkṣṇān karmāraparimārjitāne bhīmaṃ vivyādha saptatyā tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca bhagadattaś ca māriṣac vindānuvindāv āvantyau citrasenaś ca saṃyugea durmarṣaṇo vikarṇaś ca sindhurājaś ca vīryavānc bhīmaṃ te vivyadhus tūrṇaṃ śalyahetor ariṃdamāḥa sa tu tān prativivyādha pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥc śalyaṃ vivyādha saptatyā punaś ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa taṃ śalyo navabhir viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥc sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena gāḍhaṃ vivyādha marmaṇia viśokaṃ vīkṣya nirbhinnaṃ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavānc madrarājaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayata tathetarān maheṣvāsāṃs tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥc tāḍayām āsa samare siṃhavac ca nanāda caa te hi yattā maheṣvāsāḥ pāṇḍavaṃ yuddhadurmadamc tribhis tribhir akuṇṭhāgrair bhṛśaṃ marmasv atāḍayana so tividdho maheṣvāso bhīmaseno na vivyathec parvato vāridhārābhir varṣamāṇair ivāmbudaiḥd sa tu krodhasamāviṣṭo bhīmaseno mahābalaḥd madreśvaraṃ tribhir bāṇair bhṛśaṃ viddhvā mahāyaśāḥa śalyaṃ ca navabhir bāṇair bhṛśaṃ viddhvā mahāyaśāḥc prāgjyotiṣaṃ śatenājau rājan vivyādha vai dṛḍhama tatas tu saśaraṃ cāpaṃ sātvatasya mahātmanaḥc kṣurapreṇa sutīkṣṇena ciccheda kṛtahastavata athānyad dhanur ādāya kṛtavarmā vṛkodaramc ājaghāna bhruvor madhye nārācena paraṃtapad virarāja mahābāhur lalāṭasthena patriṇād ekaśṛṅgo mahārāja yathā parvatasattamaḥd atha bhīmo mahābāhuḥ kruddhaḥ sarvān mahārathānd vimukhīkṛtya bāṇaughais tasthau girir ivācalaḥa bhīmas tu samare viddhvā śalyaṃ navabhir āyasaiḥc bhagadattaṃ tribhiś caiva kṛtavarmāṇam aṣṭabhiḥa dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ ca vivyādha gautamaprabhṛtīn rathānc te tu taṃ samare rājan vivyadhur niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa sa tathā pīḍyamāno pi sarvatas tair mahārathaiḥc matvā tṛṇena tāṃs tulyān vicacāra gatavyathaḥa te cāpi rathināṃ śreṣṭhā bhīmāya niśitāñ śarānc preṣayām āsur avyagrāḥ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥa tasya śaktiṃ mahāvegāṃ bhagadatto mahārathaḥc cikṣepa samare vīraḥ svarṇadaṇḍāṃ mahādhanāma tomaraṃ saindhavo rājā paṭṭiśaṃ ca mahābhujaḥc śataghnīṃ ca kṛpo rājañ śaraṃ śalyaś ca saṃyugea athetare maheṣvāsāḥ pañca pañca śilīmukhānc bhīmasenaṃ
