samuddiśya preṣayām āsur ojasād tataḥ kruddho mahābāhur bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥd vivyādha samare vīras tribhis tribhir ajihmagaiḥd gautamapreritaṃ cāpi tomaraṃ tv anilātmajaḥd kṣurapreṇa dvidhā cakre prahasann iva bhāratad hārdikyaprahitaṃ cāpi paṭṭasaṃ tilakāṇḍavatd ciccheda samare vīro hy asaṃbhrāntarathaḥ śaraiḥd sa ciccheda śataghnīṃ ca saindhaveneritāṃ bhṛśamd bhīmaseno raṇaślāghī navabhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥa tomaraṃ sa dvidhā cakre kṣurapreṇānilātmajaḥc paṭṭiśaṃ ca tribhir bāṇaiś ciccheda tilakāṇḍavata sa bibheda śataghnīṃ ca navabhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥc madrarājaprayuktaṃ ca śaraṃ chittvā mahābalaḥa śaktiṃ ciccheda sahasā bhagadatteritāṃ raṇec tathetarāñ śarān ghorāñ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa bhīmaseno raṇaślāghī tridhaikaikaṃ samācchinatc tāṃś ca sarvān maheṣvāsāṃs tribhis tribhir atāḍayata tato dhanaṃjayas tatra vartamāne mahāraṇec jagāma sa rathenājau bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahārathame nighnantaṃ samare śatrūn yodhayānaṃ ca sāyakaiḥa tau tu tatra mahātmānau sametau vīkṣya pāṇḍavauc nāśaśaṃsur jayaṃ tatra tāvakāḥ puruṣarṣabhaa athārjuno raṇe bhīṣmaṃ yodhayan vai mahārathamc bhīṣmasya nidhanākāṅkṣī puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinama āsasāda raṇe yodhāṃs tāvakān daśa bhāratac ye sma bhīmaṃ raṇe rājan yodhayanto vyavasthitāḥe bībhatsus tān athāvidhyad bhīmasya priyakāmyayāa tato duryodhano rājā suśarmāṇam acodayatc arjunasya vadhārthāya bhīmasenasya cobhayoḥa suśarman gaccha śīghraṃ tvaṃ balaughaiḥ parivāritaḥc jahi pāṇḍusutāv etau dhanaṃjayavṛkodaraua tac chrutvā śāsanaṃ tasya trigartaḥ prasthalādhipaḥc abhidrutya raṇe bhīmam arjunaṃ caiva dhanvinaua rathair anekasāhasraiḥ parivavre samantataḥc tataḥ pravavṛte yuddham arjunasya paraiḥ saha saṃjaya uvācaa arjunas tu raṇe śalyaṃ yatamānaṃ mahārathamc chādayām āsa samare śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa suśarmāṇaṃ kṛpaṃ caiva tribhis tribhir avidhyatac prāgjyotiṣaṃ ca samare saindhavaṃ ca jayadrathama citrasenaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca kṛtavarmāṇam eva cac durmarṣaṇaṃ ca rājendra āvantyau ca mahārathaua ekaikaṃ tribhir ānarchat kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥc śarair atiratho yuddhe pīḍayan vāhinīṃ tavaa jayadratho raṇe pārthaṃ bhittvā bhārata sāyakaiḥc bhīmaṃ vivyādha tarasā citrasenarathe sthitaḥa śalyaś ca samare jiṣṇuṃ kṛpaś ca rathināṃ varaḥc vivyadhāte mahābāhuṃ bahudhā marmabhedibhiḥa citrasenādayaś caiva putrās tava viśāṃ patec pañcabhiḥ pañcabhis tūrṇaṃ saṃyuge niśitaiḥ śaraiḥe ājaghnur arjunaṃ saṃkhye bhīmasenaṃ ca māriṣaa tau tatra rathināṃ śreṣṭhau kaunteyau bharatarṣabhauc apīḍayetāṃ samare trigartānāṃ mahad balama suśarmāpi raṇe pārthaṃ viddhvā bahubhir āyasaiḥc nanāda balavan nādaṃ nādayan vai nabhastalama anye ca rathinaḥ śūrā bhīmasenadhanaṃjayauc vivyadhur niśitair bāṇai rukmapuṅkhair ajihmagaiḥa teṣāṃ tu rathināṃ madhye kaunteyau rathināṃ varauc krīḍamānau rathodārau citrarūpau vyarocatāme āmiṣepsū gavāṃ madhye siṃhāv iva balotkaṭaua chittvā dhanūṃṣi vīrāṇāṃ śarāṃś ca bahudhā raṇec pātayām āsatur vīrau śirāṃsi śataśo nṛṇāma rathāś ca bahavo bhagnā hayāś ca śataśo hatāḥc gajāś ca sagajārohāḥ petur urvyāṃ mahāmṛdhea rathinaḥ sādinaś caiva tatra tatra nisūditāḥc dṛśyante bahudhā rājan veṣṭamānāḥ samantataḥa hatair gajapadātyoghair vājibhiś ca nisūditaiḥc rathaiś ca bahudhā bhagnaiḥ samāstīryata medinīa chatraiś ca bahudhā chinnair dhvajaiś ca vinipātitaiḥb cāmarair hemadaṇḍaiś ca samāstīryata medinīc aṅkuśair apaviddhaiś ca paristomaiś ca bhāratad ghaṇṭābhiś ca kaśābhiś ca samāstīryata medinīa keyūrair aṅgadair hārai rāṅkavair mṛditais tathāb kuṇḍalair maṇicitraiś ca samāstīryata medinīc uṣṇīṣair apaviddhaiś ca cāmaravyajanair apia tatra tatrāpaviddhaiś ca bāhubhiś candanokṣitaiḥc ūrubhiś ca narendrāṇāṃ samāstīryata medinīa tatrādbhutam apaśyāma raṇe pārthasya vikramamc śaraiḥ saṃvārya tān vīrān nijaghāna balaṃ tavaa putras tu tava taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmārjunasamāgamamc gāṅgeyasya rathābhyāśam upajagme mahābhayea kṛpaś ca kṛtavarmā ca saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥc vindānuvindāv āvantyāv ājagmuḥ saṃyugaṃ tadāa tato bhīmo maheṣvāsaḥ phalgunaś ca mahārathaḥc kauravāṇāṃ camūṃ ghorāṃ bhṛśaṃ dudruvatū raṇea tato barhiṇavājānām ayutāny arbudāni cac dhanaṃjayarathe tūrṇaṃ pātayanti sma saṃyugea tatas tāñ śarajālena saṃnivārya mahārathānc pārthaḥ samantāt samare preṣayām āsa mṛtyavea śalyas tu samare jiṣṇuṃ krīḍann iva mahārathaḥc ājaghānorasi kruddho bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa tasya pārtho dhanuś chittvā hastāvāpaṃ ca pañcabhiḥc athainaṃ sāyakais tīkṣṇair bhṛśaṃ vivyādha marmaṇia athānyad dhanur ādāya samare bhārasādhanamc madreśvaro raṇe jiṣṇuṃ tāḍayām āsa roṣitaḥa tribhiḥ śarair mahārāja vāsudevaṃ ca pañcabhiḥc bhīmasenaṃ ca navabhir bāhvor urasi cārpayata tato droṇo mahārāja māgadhaś ca mahārathaḥc duryodhanasamādiṣṭau taṃ deśam upajagmatuḥa yatra pārtho mahārāja bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥc kauravyasya mahāsenāṃ jaghnatus tau mahārathaua jayatsenas tu samare bhīmaṃ bhīmāyudhaṃ yuvāc vivyādha niśitair bāṇair aṣṭabhir bharatarṣabhaa taṃ bhīmo daśabhir viddhvā punar vivyādha saptabhiḥc sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharata udbhrāntais turagaiḥ so tha dravamāṇaiḥ samantataḥc māgadho pahṛto rājā sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa droṇas tu vivaraṃ labdhvā bhīmasenaṃ śilīmukhaiḥc vivyādha bāṇaiḥ suśitaiḥ pañcaṣaṣṭyā tam āyasaiḥa taṃ bhīmaḥ samaraślāghī guruṃ pitṛsamaṃ raṇec vivyādha navabhir bhallais tathā ṣaṣṭyā ca bhārataa arjunas tu suśarmāṇaṃ viddhvā bahubhir āyasaiḥc vyadhamat tasya tat sainyaṃ mahābhrāṇi yathānilaḥa tato bhīṣmaś ca rājā ca saubalaś ca bṛhadbalaḥc abhyadravanta saṃkruddhā bhīmasenadhanaṃjayaua tathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ śūrā dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc abhyadravan raṇe bhīṣmaṃ vyāditāsyam ivāntakama śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bhāratānāṃ pitāmahamc abhyadravata saṃhṛṣṭo bhayaṃ tyaktvā yatavratama yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ pārthāḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinamc ayodhayan raṇe bhīṣmaṃ saṃhatāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥa tathaiva tāvakāḥ sarve puraskṛtya yatavratamc śikhaṇḍipramukhān pārthān yodhayanti sma saṃyugea tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kauravāṇāṃ bhayāvahamc tatra pāṇḍusutaiḥ sārdhaṃ bhīṣmasya vijayaṃ pratia tāvakānāṃ raṇe bhīṣmo glaha āsīd viśāṃ patec tatra hi dyūtam āyātaṃ vijayāyetarāya vāa dhṛṣṭadyumno mahārāja sarvasainyāny acodayatc abhidravata gāṅgeyaṃ mā bhaiṣṭa narasattamāḥa senāpativacaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍavānāṃ varūthinīc bhīṣmam evābhyayāt tūrṇaṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā mahāhavea bhīṣmo pi rathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pratijagrāha tāṃ camūmc āpatantīṃ mahārāja velām iva mahodadhiḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa kathaṃ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo daśame hani saṃjayac ayudhyata mahāvīryaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahasṛñjayaiḥa kuravaś ca kathaṃ yuddhe pāṇḍavān pratyavārayanc ācakṣva me mahāyuddhaṃ bhīṣmasyāhavaśobhinaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ yathāyudhyanta bhāratac yathā ca tad abhūd yuddhaṃ tat te vakṣyāmi śṛṇvataḥa preṣitāḥ paralokāya paramāstraiḥ kirīṭināc ahany ahani saṃprāptās tāvakānāṃ rathavrajāḥa yathāpratijñaṃ kauravyaḥ sa cāpi samitiṃjayaḥc pārthānām akarod bhīṣmaḥ satataṃ samitikṣayama kurubhiḥ sahitaṃ bhīṣmaṃ yudhyamānaṃ mahārathamc arjunaṃ ca sapāñcālyaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃśayitā janāḥa daśame hani tasmiṃs tu bhīṣmārjunasamāgamec avartata mahāraudraḥ satataṃ samitikṣayaḥa tasminn ayutaśo rājan bhūyaś ca sa paraṃtapaḥc bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo yodhāñ jaghāna paramāstravita yeṣām ajñātakalpāni nāmagotrāṇi pārthivac te hatās tatra bhīṣmeṇa śūrāḥ sarve nivartinaḥa daśāhāni tatas taptvā bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍavavāhinīmc niravidyata dharmātmā jīvitena paraṃtapaḥa sa kṣipraṃ vadham anvicchann ātmano bhimukhaṃ raṇec na hanyāṃ mānavaśreṣṭhān saṃgrāme bhimukhān itia cintayitvā mahābāhuḥ pitā devavratas tavac abhyāśasthaṃ mahārāja pāṇḍavaṃ vākyam abravīta yudhiṣṭhira mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśāradac śṛṇu me vacanaṃ tāta dharmyaṃ svargyaṃ ca jalpataḥa nirviṇṇo smi bhṛśaṃ tāta dehenānena bhāratac ghnataś ca me gataḥ kālaḥ subahūn prāṇino raṇea tasmāt pārthaṃ purodhāya pāñcālān sṛñjayāṃs tathāc madvadhe kriyatāṃ yatno mama ced icchasi priyama tasya tan matam ājñāya pāṇḍavaḥ satyadarśanaḥc bhīṣmaṃ pratiyayau yattaḥ saṃgrāme saha sṛñjayaiḥa dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato rājan pāṇḍavaś ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥc śrutvā bhīṣmasya tāṃ vācaṃ codayām āsatur balama abhidravata yudhyadhvaṃ bhīṣmaṃ jayata saṃyugec rakṣitāḥ satyasaṃdhena jiṣṇunā ripujiṣṇunāa ayaṃ cāpi maheṣvāsaḥ pārṣato vāhinīpatiḥc bhīmasenaś ca samare pālayiṣyati vo dhruvama na vai bhīṣmād bhayaṃ kiṃ cit kartavyaṃ yudhi sṛñjayāḥc dhruvaṃ bhīṣmaṃ vijeṣyāmaḥ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinamd te tatheti pratijñāya puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinama tathā tu samayaṃ kṛtvā daśame hani pāṇḍavāḥc brahmalokaparā bhūtvā saṃjagmuḥ krodhamūrchitāḥa śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayamc bhīṣmasya pātane yatnaṃ paramaṃ te samāsthitāḥa tatas tava sutādiṣṭā nānājanapadeśvarāḥc droṇena sahaputreṇa sahasenā mahābalāḥa duḥśāsanaś ca balavān saha sarvaiḥ sahodaraiḥc bhīṣmaṃ samaramadhyasthaṃ pālayāṃ cakrire tadāa tatas tu tāvakāḥ śūrāḥ puraskṛtya yatavratamc śikhaṇḍipramukhān pārthān yodhayanti sma saṃyugea cedibhiś ca sapāñcālaiḥ sahito vānaradhvajaḥc yayau śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinama droṇaputraṃ śiner naptā dhṛṣṭaketus tu pauravamc yudhāmanyuḥ sahāmātyaṃ duryodhanam ayodhayata virāṭas tu sahānīkaḥ sahasenaṃ jayadrathamc vṛddhakṣatrasya dāyādam āsasāda paraṃtapaḥd citrasenas tava sutaṃ vicitraśarakārmukama madrarājaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ sahasainyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥc bhīmasenābhiguptaś ca nāgānīkam upādravata apradhṛṣyam anāvāryaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varamc droṇaṃ prati yayau yattaḥ pāñcālyaḥ saha somakaiḥa karṇikāradhvajaṃ cāpi siṃhaketur ariṃdamaḥc pratyujjagāma saubhadraṃ rājaputro bṛhadbalaḥa śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca putrās te pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayamc rājabhiḥ samare sārdham abhipetur jighāṃsavaḥa tasminn atimahābhīme senayor vai parākramec saṃpradhāvatsv anīkeṣu medinī samakampataa tāny anīkāny anīkeṣu samasajjanta bhāratac tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā śāṃtanavaṃ raṇea tatas teṣāṃ prayatatām anyonyam abhidhāvatāmc prādurāsīn mahāñ śabdo dikṣu sarvāsu bhārataa śaṅkhadundubhighoṣaiś ca vāraṇānāṃ ca bṛṃhitaiḥc siṃhanādaiś ca sainyānāṃ dāruṇaḥ samapadyataa sā ca sarvanarendrāṇāṃ candrārkasadṛśī prabhāc vīrāṅgadakirīṭeṣu niṣprabhā samapadyataa rajomeghāś ca saṃjajñuḥ śastravidyudbhir āvṛtāḥc dhanuṣāṃ caiva nirghoṣo dāruṇaḥ samapadyataa bāṇaśaṅkhapraṇādāś ca bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanāḥc rathagoṣaś ca saṃjagmuḥ senayor ubhayor apia prāsaśaktyṛṣṭisaṃghaiś ca bāṇaughaiś ca samākulamc niṣprakāśam ivākāśaṃ senayoḥ samapadyataa anyonyaṃ rathinaḥ petur vājinaś ca mahāhavec kuñjarāḥ kuñjarāñ jaghnuḥ padātīṃś ca padātayaḥa tad āsīt sumahad yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ sahac bhīṣmahetor naravyāghra śyenayor āmiṣe yathāa tayoḥ samāgamo ghoro babhūva yudhi bhāratac anyonyasya vadhārthāya jigīṣūṇāṃ raṇājire saṃjaya uvācaa abhimanyur mahārāja tava putram ayodhayatc mahatyā senayā yukto bhīṣmahetoḥ parākramīa duryodhano raṇe kārṣṇiṃ navabhir nataparvabhiḥc ājaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ punaś cainaṃ tribhiḥ śaraiḥa tasya śaktiṃ raṇe kārṣṇir mṛtyor ghorām iva svasāmc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho duryodhanarathaṃ pratia tām āpatantīṃ sahasā ghorarūpāṃ viśāṃ patec dvidhā ciccheda te putraḥ kṣurapreṇa mahārathaḥa tāṃ śaktiṃ patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā kārṣṇiḥ paramakopanaḥc duryodhanaṃ tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārpayata punaś cainaṃ śarair ghorair ājaghāna stanāntarec daśabhir bharataśreṣṭha duryodhanam amarṣaṇama tad yuddham abhavad ghoraṃ citrarūpaṃ ca bhāratac īkṣitṛprītijananaṃ sarvapārthivapūjitama bhīṣmasya nidhanārthāya pārthasya vijayāya cac yuyudhāte raṇe vīrau saubhadrakurupuṃgavaua sātyakiṃ rabhasaṃ yuddhe drauṇir brāhmaṇapuṃgavaḥc ājaghānorasi kruddho nārācena paraṃtapaḥa śaineyo pi guroḥ putraṃ sarvamarmasu bhāratac atāḍayad ameyātmā navabhiḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥa aśvatthāmā tu samare sātyakiṃ navabhiḥ śaraiḥc triṃśatā ca punas tūrṇaṃ bāhvor urasi cārpayata so tividdho maheṣvāso droṇaputreṇa sātvataḥc droṇaputraṃ tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna mahāyaśāḥa pauravo dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca śarair āsādya saṃyugec bahudhā dārayāṃ cakre maheṣvāsaṃ mahārathama tathaiva pauravaṃ yuddhe dhṛṣṭaketur mahārathaḥc triṃśatā niśitair bāṇair vivyādha sumahābalaḥa pauravas tu dhanuś chittvā dhṛṣṭaketor mahārathaḥc nanāda balavan nādaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa so nyat kārmukam ādāya pauravaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc ājaghāna mahārāja trisaptatyā śilīmukhaiḥa tau tu tatra maheṣvāsau mahāmātrau mahārathauc mahatā śaravarṣeṇa parasparam avarṣatāma anyonyasya dhanuś chittvā hayān hatvā ca bhāratac virathāv asiyuddhāya saṃgatau tau mahārathaua ārṣabhe carmaṇī citre śatacandrapariṣkṛtec tārakāśatacitrau ca nistriṃśau sumahāprabhaua pragṛhya vimalau rājaṃs tāv anyonyam abhidrutauc vāśitāsaṃgame yattau siṃhāv iva mahāvanea maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi gatapratyāgatāni cac ceratur darśayantau ca prārthayantau parasparama pauravo dhṛṣṭaketuṃ tu śaṅkhadeśe mahāsināc tāḍayām āsa saṃkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta cedirājo pi samare pauravaṃ puruṣarṣabhamc ājaghāna śitāgreṇa jatrudeśe mahāsināa tāv anyonyaṃ mahārāja samāsādya mahāhavec anyonyavegābhihatau nipetatur ariṃdamaua tataḥ svaratham āropya pauravaṃ tanayas tavac jayatseno rathe rājann apovāha raṇājirāta dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca samare mādrīputraḥ paraṃtapaḥc apovāha raṇe rājan sahadevaḥ pratāpavāna citrasenaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ viddhvā navabhir āśugaiḥc punar vivyādha taṃ ṣaṣṭyā punaś ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥa suśarmā tu raṇe kruddhas tava putraṃ viśāṃ patec daśabhir daśabhiś caiva vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa citrasenaś ca taṃ rājaṃs triṃśatā nataparvaṇāmc ājaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ sa ca taṃ pratyavidhyatae bhīṣmasya samare rājan yaśo mānaṃ ca vardhayana saubhadro rājaputraṃ tu bṛhadbalam ayodhayatb pārthahetoḥ parākrānto bhīṣmasyāyodhanaṃ pratic ārjuniṃ kosalendras tu viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥe punar vivyādha viṃśatyā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa bṛhadbalaṃ ca saubhadro viddhvā navabhir āyasaiḥc nākampayata saṃgrāme vivyādha ca punaḥ punaḥa kausalyasya punaś cāpi dhanuś ciccheda phālguṇiḥc ājaghāna śaraiś caiva triṃśatā kaṅkapatribhiḥa so nyat kārmukam ādāya rājaputro bṛhadbalaḥc phālguniṃ samare kruddho vivyādha bahubhiḥ śaraiḥa tayor yuddhaṃ samabhavad bhīṣmahetoḥ paraṃtapac saṃrabdhayor mahārāja samare citrayodhinoḥe yathā devāsure yuddhe mayavāsavayor abhūta bhīmaseno gajānīkaṃ yodhayan bahv aśobhatac yathā śakro vajrapāṇir dārayan parvatottamāna te vadhyamānā bhīmena mātaṅgā girisaṃnibhāḥc nipetur urvyāṃ sahitā nādayanto vasuṃdharāma girimātrā hi te nāgā bhinnāñjanacayopamāḥc virejur vasudhāṃ prāpya vikīrṇā iva parvatāḥa yudhiṣṭhiro maheṣvāso madrarājānam āhavec mahatyā senayā guptaṃ pīḍayām āsa saṃgataḥa madreśvaraś ca samare dharmaputraṃ mahārathamc pīḍayām āsa saṃrabdho bhīṣmahetoḥ parākramīa virāṭaṃ saindhavo rājā viddhvā saṃnataparvabhiḥc navabhiḥ sāyakais tīkṣṇais triṃśatā punar ardayata virāṭaś ca mahārāja saindhavaṃ vāhinīmukhec triṃśatā niśitair bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntarea citrakārmukanistriṃśau citravarmāyudhadhvajauc rejatuś citrarūpau tau saṃgrāme matsyasaindhavaua droṇaḥ pāñcālaputreṇa samāgamya mahāraṇec mahāsamudayaṃ cakre śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥa tato droṇo mahārāja pārṣatasya mahad dhanuḥc chittvā pañcāśateṣūṇāṃ pārṣataṃ samavidhyataa so nyat kārmukam ādāya pārṣataḥ paravīrahāc droṇasya miṣato yuddhe preṣayām āsa sāyakāna tāñ śarāñ śarasaṃghais tu saṃnivārya mahārathaḥc droṇo drupadaputrāya prāhiṇot pañca sāyakāna tasya kruddho mahārāja pārṣataḥ paravīrahāc droṇāya cikṣepa gadāṃ yamadaṇḍopamāṃ raṇea tām āpatantīṃ sahasā hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitāmc śaraiḥ pañcāśatā droṇo vārayām āsa saṃyugea sā chinnā bahudhā rājan droṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥc cūrṇīkṛtā viśīryantī papāta vasudhātalea gadāṃ vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā pārṣataḥ śatrusūdanaḥc droṇāya śaktiṃ cikṣepa sarvapāraśavīṃ śubhāma tāṃ droṇo navabhir bāṇaiś ciccheda yudhi bhāratac pārṣataṃ ca maheṣvāsaṃ pīḍayām āsa saṃyugea evam etan mahad yuddhaṃ droṇapārṣatayor abhūtc bhīṣmaṃ prati mahārāja ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakama arjunaḥ prāpya gāṅgeyaṃ pīḍayan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc abhyadravata saṃyattaṃ vane mattam iva dvipama pratyudyayau ca taṃ pārthaṃ bhagadattaḥ pratāpavānc tridhā bhinnena nāgena madāndhena mahābalaḥa tam āpatantaṃ sahasā mahendragajasaṃnibhamc paraṃ yatnaṃ samāsthāya bībhatsuḥ pratyapadyataa tato gajagato rājā bhagadattaḥ pratāpavānc arjunaṃ śaravarṣeṇa vārayām āsa saṃyugea arjunas tu raṇe nāgam āyāntaṃ rajatopamamc vimalair āyasais tīkṣṇair avidhyata mahāraṇea śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca kaunteyo yāhi yāhīty acodayatc bhīṣmaṃ prati mahārāja jahy enam iti cābravīta prāgjyotiṣas tato hitvā pāṇḍavaṃ pāṇḍupūrvajac prayayau tvarito rājan drupadasya rathaṃ pratia tato rjuno mahārāja bhīṣmam abhyadravad drutamc śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya tato yuddham avartataa tatas te tāvakāḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavaṃ rabhasaṃ raṇec sarve bhyadhāvan krośantas tad adbhutam ivābhavata nānāvidhāny anīkāni putrāṇāṃ te janādhipac arjuno vyadhamat kāle divīvābhrāṇi mārutaḥa śikhaṇḍī tu samāsādya bharatānāṃ pitāmahamc iṣubhis tūrṇam avyagro bahubhiḥ sa samācinota somakāṃś ca raṇe bhīṣmo jaghne pārthapadānugānc nyavārayata sainyaṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥa rathāgnyagāraś cāpārcir asiśaktigadendhanaḥc śarasaṃghamahājvālaḥ kṣatriyān samare dahata yathā hi sumahān agniḥ kakṣe carati sānilaḥc tathā jajvāla bhīṣmo pi divyāny astrāṇy udīrayana suvarṇapuṅkhair iṣubhiḥ śitaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc nādayan sa diśo bhīṣmaḥ pradiśaś ca mahāyaśāḥa pātayan rathino rājan gajāṃś ca saha sādibhiḥc muṇḍatālavanānīva cakāra sa rathavrajāna nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan gajān aśvāṃś ca saṃyugec cakāra sa tadā bhīṣmaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥc niśamya sarvato rājan samakampanta sainikāḥa amoghā hy apatan bāṇāḥ pitus te manujeśvarac nāsajjanta śarīreṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutāḥ śarāḥa nirmanuṣyān rathān rājan suyuktāñ javanair hayaiḥc vātāyamānān paśyāma hriyamāṇān viśāṃ patea cedikāśikarūṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśac mahārathāḥ samākhyātāḥ kulaputrās tanutyajaḥa aparāvartinaḥ śūrāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥc saṃgrāme bhīṣmam āsādya savājirathakuñjarāḥe jagmus te paralokāya vyāditāsyam ivāntakama na tatrāsīn mahārāja somakānāṃ mahārathaḥc yaḥ saṃprāpya raṇe bhīṣmaṃ jīvite sma mano dadhea tāṃś ca sarvān raṇe yodhān pretarājapuraṃ pratic nītān amanyanta janā dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasya vikramama na kaś cid enaṃ samare pratyudyāti mahārathaḥc ṛte pāṇḍusutaṃ vīraṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathime śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca samare pāñcālyam amitaujasama śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe bhīṣmam āsādya bharatarṣabhac daśabhir daśabhir bāṇair ājaghāna mahāhavea śikhaṇḍinaṃ tu gāṅgeyaḥ krodhadīptena cakṣuṣāc avaikṣata kaṭākṣeṇa nirdahann iva bhārataa strītvaṃ tat saṃsmaran rājan sarvalokasya paśyataḥc na jaghāna raṇe bhīṣmaḥ sa ca taṃ nāvabuddhavāna arjunas tu mahārāja śikhaṇḍinam abhāṣatac abhitvarasva tvarito jahi cainaṃ pitāmahama kiṃ te vivakṣayā vīra jahi bhīṣmaṃ mahārathamc na hy anyam anupaśyāmi kaṃ cid yaudhiṣṭhire balea yaḥ śaktaḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ yodhayeta pitāmahamc ṛte tvāṃ puruṣavyāghra satyam etad bravīmi tea evam uktas tu pārthena śikhaṇḍī bharatarṣabhac śarair nānāvidhais tūrṇaṃ pitāmaham upādravata acintayitvā tān bāṇān pitā devavratas tavac arjunaṃ samare kruddhaṃ vārayām āsa sāyakaiḥa tathaiva ca camūṃ sarvāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥc apraiṣīt samare tīkṣṇaiḥ paralokāya māriṣaa tathaiva pāṇḍavā rājan sainyena mahatā vṛtāḥc bhīṣmaṃ pracchādayām āsur meghā iva divākarama sa samantāt parivṛto bhārato bharatarṣabhac nirdadāha raṇe śūrān vanaṃ vahnir iva jvalana tatrādbhutam apaśyāma tava putrasya pauruṣamc ayodhayata yat pārthaṃ jugopa ca yatavratama karmaṇā tena samare tava putrasya dhanvinaḥc duḥśāsanasya tutuṣuḥ sarve lokā mahātmanaḥa yad ekaḥ samare pārthān sānugān samayodhayatc na cainaṃ pāṇḍavā yuddhe vāyarām āsur ulbaṇama duḥśāsanena samare rathino virathīkṛtāḥc sādinaś ca mahārāja dantinaś ca mahābalāḥa vinirbhinnāḥ śarais tīkṣṇair nipetur dharaṇītalec śarāturās tathaivānye dantino vidrutā diśaḥa yathāgnir indhanaṃ prāpya jvaled dīptārcir ulbaṇaḥc tathā jajvāla putras te pāṇḍavān vai vinirdahana taṃ bhāratamahāmātraṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥc jetuṃ notsahate kaś cin nāpy udyātuṃ kathaṃ canae ṛte mahendratanayaṃ śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathima sa hi taṃ samare rājan vijitya vijayo rjunaḥc bhīṣmam evābhidudrāva sarvasainyasya paśyataḥa vijitas tava putro pi bhīṣmabāhuvyapāśrayaḥc punaḥ punaḥ samāśvasya prāyudhyata raṇotkaṭaḥe arjunaṃ ca raṇe rājan yodhayan sa vyarājataa śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe rājan vivyādhaiva pitāmahamc śarair aśanisaṃsparśais tathā sarpaviṣopamaiḥa na ca te sya rujaṃ cakruḥ pitus tava janeśvarab jaghāna bāṇān gāṅgeyas tathā muktāñ śikhaṇḍinaḥc smayamānaś ca gāṅgeyas tān bāṇāñ jagṛhe tadāa uṣṇārto hi naro yadvaj jaladhārāḥ pratīcchatic tathā jagrāha gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhārāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa taṃ kṣatriyā mahārāja dadṛśur ghoram āhavec bhīṣmaṃ dahantaṃ sainyāni pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāma tato bravīt tava sutaḥ sarvasainyāni māriṣac abhidravata saṃgrāme phalgunaṃ sarvato rathaiḥa bhīṣmo vaḥ samare sarvān palayiṣyati dharmavitc te bhayaṃ sumahat tvaktvā pāṇḍavān pratiyudhyataa eṣa tālena dīptena bhīṣmas tiṣṭhati pālayanc sarveṣāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ raṇe śarma ca varma caa tridaśāpi samudyuktā nālaṃ bhīṣmaṃ samāsitumc kim u pārthā mahātmānaṃ martyabhūtās tathābalāḥe tasmād dravata he yodhāḥ phalgunaṃ prāpya saṃyugea aham adya raṇe yatto yodhayiṣyāmi phalgunamc sahitaḥ sarvato yattair bhavadbhir vasudhādhipāḥa tac chrutvā tu vaco rājaṃs tava putrasya dhanvinaḥc arjunaṃ prati saṃyattā balavanto mahārathāḥa te videhāḥ kaliṅgāś ca dāśerakagaṇaiḥ sahac abhipetur niṣādāś ca sauvīrāś ca mahāraṇea bāhlikā daradāś caiva prācyodīcyāś ca mālavāḥc abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayo tha vasātayaḥa śālvāśrayās trigartāś ca ambaṣṭhāḥ kekayaiḥ sahac abhipetū raṇe pārthaṃ pataṃgā iva pāvakamd śalabhā iva rājendra pārtham apratimaṃ raṇea sa tān sarvān sahānīkān mahārāja mahārathānc divyāny astrāṇi saṃcintya prasaṃdhāya dhanaṃjayaḥa sa tair astrair mahāvegair dadāhāśu mahābalaḥc śarapratāpair bībhatsuḥ pataṃgān iva pāvakaḥa tasya bāṇasahasrāṇi sṛjato dṛḍhadhanvinaḥc dīpyamānam ivākāśe gāṇḍīvaṃ samadṛśyataa te śarārtā mahārāja viprakīrṇarathadhvajāḥc nābyavartanta rājānaḥ sahitā vānaradhvajama sadhvajā rathinaḥ petur hayārohā hayaiḥ sahac gajāḥ saha gajārohaiḥ kirīṭiśaratāḍitāḥa tato rjunabhujotsṛṣṭair āvṛtāsīd vasuṃdharāc vidravadbhiś ca bahudhā balai rājñāṃ samantataḥa atha pārtho mahābāhur drāvayitvā varūthinīmc duḥśāsanāya samare preṣayām āsa sāyakāna te tu bhittvā tava sutaṃ duḥśāsanam ayomukhāḥc dharaṇīṃ viviśuḥ sarve valmīkam iva pannagāḥe hayāṃś cāsya tato jaghne sārathiṃ ca nyapātayata viviṃśatiṃ ca viṃśatyā virathaṃ kṛtavān prabhoc ājaghāna bhṛśaṃ caiva pañcabhir nataparvabhiḥa kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca viddhvā bahubhir āyasaiḥc cakāra virathāṃś caiva kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥa evaṃ te virathāḥ pañca kṛpaḥ śalyaś ca māriṣac duḥśāsano vikarṇaś ca tathaiva ca viviṃśatiḥe saṃprādravanta samare nirjitāḥ savyasācināa pūrvāhṇe tu tathā rājan parājitya mahārathānc prajajvāla raṇe pārtho vidhūma iva pāvakaḥa tathaiva śaravarṣeṇa bhāskaro raśmivān ivac anyān api mahārāja pātayām āsa pārthivāna parāṅmukhīkṛtya tadā śaravarṣair mahārathānc prāvartayata saṃgrāme śoṇitodāṃ mahānadīme madhyena kurusainyānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca bhārataa gajāś ca rathasaṃghāś ca bahudhā rathibhir hatāḥc rathāś ca nihatā nāgair nāgā hayapadātibhiḥa antarā chidhyamānāni śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi cac nipetur dikṣu sarvāsu gajāśvarathayodhināma channam āyodhanaṃ reje kuṇḍalāṅgadadhāribhiḥc patitaiḥ pātyamānaiś ca rājaputrair mahārathaiḥa rathaneminikṛttāś ca gajaiś caivāvapothitāḥc pādātāś cāpy adṛśyanta sāśvāḥ sahayasādinaḥa gajāśvarathasaṃghāś ca paripetuḥ samantataḥc viśīrṇāś ca rathā bhūmau bhagnacakrayugadhvajāḥa tad gajāśvarathaughānāṃ rudhireṇa samukṣitamc channam āyodhanaṃ reje raktābhram iva śāradama śvānaḥ kākāś ca gṛdhrāś ca vṛkā gomāyubhiḥ sahac praṇedur bhakṣyam āsādya vikṛtāś ca mṛgadvijāḥa vavur bahuvidhāś caiva dikṣu sarvāsu mārutāḥc dṛśyamāneṣu rakṣaḥsu bhūteṣu vinadatsu caa kāñcanāni ca dāmāni patākāś ca mahādhanāḥc dhūmāyamānā dṛśyante sahasā māruteritāḥa śvetacchatrasahasrāṇi sadhvajāś ca mahārathāḥc vinikīrṇāḥ sma dṛśyante śataśo tha sahasraśaḥe sapatākāś ca mātaṅgā diśo jagmuḥ śarāturāḥa kṣatriyāś ca manuṣyendra gadāśaktidhanurdharāḥc samantato vyadṛśyanta patitā dharaṇītaled samadṛśyanta samare dhāvamānāḥ samantataḥa tato bhīṣmo mahārāja divyam astram udīrayanc abhyadhāvata kaunteyaṃ miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvināma taṃ śikhaṇḍī raṇe yattam abhyadhāvata daṃśitaḥc saṃjahāra tato bhīṣmas tad astraṃ pāvakopamama etasminn eva kāle tu kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥc nijaghne tāvakaṃ sainyaṃ mohayitvā pitāmaham saṃjaya uvācaa evaṃ vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu bhūyiṣṭham anuvartiṣuc brahmalokaparāḥ sarve samapadyanta bhārataa na hy anīkam anīkena samasajjata saṃkulec na rathā rathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ na padātāḥ padātibhiḥa aśvā nāśvair ayudhyanta na gajā gajayodhibhiḥb unmattavan mahārāja yudhyante tatra bhāratac mahān vyatikaro raudraḥ senayoḥ samapadyataa naranāgaratheṣv evaṃ vyavakīrṇeṣu sarvaśaḥc kṣaye tasmin mahāraudre nirviśeṣam ajāyataa tataḥ śalyaḥ kṛpaś caiva citrasenaś ca bhāratac duḥśāsano vikarṇaś ca rathān āsthāya satvarāḥe pāṇḍavānāṃ raṇe śūrā dhvajinīṃ samakampayana sā vadhyamānā samare pāṇḍusenā mahātmabhiḥc trātāraṃ nādhyagacchad vai majjamāneva naur jalea yathā hi śaiśiraḥ kālo gavāṃ marmāṇi kṛntatic tathā pāṇḍusutānāṃ vai bhīṣmo marmāṇy akṛntatad somakāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarve te yuddhadurmadāḥa atīva tava sainyasya pārthena ca mahātmanāc nagameghapratīkāśāḥ pātitā bahudhā gajāḥa mṛdyamānāś ca dṛśyante pārthena narayūthapāḥc iṣubhis tāḍyamānāś ca nārācaiś ca sahasraśaḥa petur ārtasvaraṃ kṛtvā tatra tatra mahāgajāḥc ābaddhābharaṇaiḥ kāyair nihatānāṃ mahātmanāma channam āyodhanaṃ reje śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥc tasminn atimahābhīme rājan vīravarakṣayee bhīṣme ca yudhi vikrānte pāṇḍave ca dhanaṃjayea te parākrāntam ālokya rājan yudhi pitāmahamc na nyavartanta kauravyā brahmalokapuraskṛtāḥa icchanto nidhanaṃ yuddhe svargaṃ kṛtvā parāyaṇamc pāṇḍavān abhyavartanta tasmin vīravarakṣayed pāṇḍavānāṃ yayuḥ senām ātmano jayagṛddhinaḥa pāṇḍavāpi mahārāja smaranto vividhān bahūnc kleśān kṛtān saputreṇa tvayā pūrvaṃ narādhipaa bhayaṃ tyaktvā raṇe śūrā brahmalokapuraskṛtāḥc tāvakāṃs tava putrāṃś ca yodhayanti sma hṛṣṭavata senāpatis tu samare prāha senāṃ mahārathaḥc abhidravata gāṅgeyaṃ somakāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ sahaa senāpativacaḥ śrutvā somakāḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥc abhyadravanta gāṅgeyaṃ śastravṛṣṭyā samantataḥa vadhyamānas tato rājan pitā śāṃtanavas tavac amarṣavaśam āpanno yodhayām āsa sṛñjayāna tasya kīrtimatas tāta purā rāmeṇa dhīmatāc saṃpradattāstraśikṣā vai parānīkavināśinīa sa tāṃ śikṣām adhiṣṭhāya kṛtvā parabalakṣayamc ahany ahani pārthānāṃ vṛddhaḥ kurupitāmahaḥe bhīṣmo daśa sahasrāṇi jaghāna paravīrahāa tasmiṃs tu divase prāpte daśame bharatarṣabhac bhīṣmeṇaikena matsyeṣu pāñcāleṣu ca saṃyugee gajāśvam amitaṃ hatvā hatāḥ sapta mahārathāḥa hatvā pañca sahasrāṇi rathināṃ prapitāmahaḥc narāṇāṃ ca mahāyuddhe sahasrāṇi caturdaśaa tathā dantisahasraṃ ca hayānām ayutaṃ punaḥc śikṣābalena nihataṃ pitrā tava viśāṃ patea tataḥ sarvamahīpānāṃ kṣobhayitvā varūthinīmc virāṭasya priyo bhrātā śatānīko nipātitaḥa śatānīkaṃ ca samare hatvā bhīṣmaḥ pratāpavānc sahasrāṇi mahārāja rājñāṃ bhallair nyapātayatd udvignāḥ samare yodhā vikrośanti dhanaṃjayaa ye ca ke cana pārthānām abhiyātā dhanaṃjayamc rājāno bhīṣmam āsādya gatās te yamasādanama evaṃ daśa diśo bhīṣmaḥ śarajālaiḥ samantataḥc atītya senāṃ pārthānām avatasthe camūmukhea sa kṛtvā sumahat karma tasmin vai daśame hanib yāvāyavābhyāṃ śuciśukrayogeb ātānataptā iva bāṇasaṃghāḥb bhīṣmasya cāpacyutabāṇasaṃghaiḥb pārthasya senā kṛśatām avāpac senayor antare tiṣṭhan pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥa na cainaṃ pārthivā rājañ śekuḥ ke cin nirīkṣitumc madhyaṃ prāptaṃ yathā grīṣme tapantaṃ bhāskaraṃ divia yathā daityacamūṃ śakras tāpayām āsa saṃyugec tathā bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍaveyāṃs tāpayām āsa bhārataa tathā ca taṃ parākrāntam ālokya madhusūdanaḥc uvāca devakīputraḥ prīyamāṇo dhanaṃjayama eṣa śāṃtanavo bhīṣmaḥ senayor antare sthitaḥc nānihatya balād enaṃ vijayas te bhaviṣyatia yattaḥ saṃstambhayasvainaṃ yatraiṣā bhidyate camūḥc na hi bhīṣmaśarān anyaḥ soḍhum utsahate vibhoa tatas tasmin kṣaṇe rājaṃś codito vānaradhvajaḥc sadhvajaṃ sarathaṃ sāśvaṃ bhīṣmam antardadhe śaraiḥa sa cāpi kurumukhyānām ṛṣabhaḥ pāṇḍaveritānc śaravrātaiḥ śaravrātān bahudhā vidudhāva tāna tena pāñcālarājaś ca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavānc pāṇḍavo bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥa yamau ca cekitānaś ca kekayāḥ pañca caiva hac sātyakiś ca mahārāja saubhadro tha ghaṭotkacaḥa draupadeyāḥ śikhaṇḍī ca kuntibhojaś ca vīryavānc suśarmā ca virāṭaś ca pāṇḍaveyā mahābalāḥa ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pīḍitā bhīṣmasāyakaiḥc samuddhṛtāḥ phalgunena nimagnāḥ śokasāgarea tataḥ śikhaṇḍī vegena pragṛhya paramāyudhamc bhīṣmam evābhidudrāva rakṣyamāṇaḥ kirīṭināa tato syānucarān hatvā sarvān raṇavibhāgavitc bhīṣmam evābhidudrāva bībhatsur aparājitaḥa sātyakiś cekitānaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc virāṭo drupadaś caiva mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavaue dudruvur bhīṣmam evājau rakṣitā dṛḍhadhanvanāa abhimanyuś ca samare draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥc dudruvuḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ samudyatamahāyudhāḥa te sarve dṛḍhadhanvānaḥ saṃyugeṣv apalāyinaḥc bahudhā bhīṣmam ānarchan mārgaṇaiḥ kṛtamārgaṇāḥa vidhūya tān bāṇagaṇān ye muktāḥ pārthivottamaiḥc pāṇḍavānām adīnātmā vyagāhata varūthinīme kṛtvā śaravighātaṃ ca krīḍann iva pitāmahaḥa nābhisaṃdhatta pāñcālyaṃ smayamāno muhur muhuḥc strītvaṃ tasyānusaṃsmṛtya bhīṣmo bāṇāñ śikhaṇḍinaḥe jaghāna drupadānīke rathān sapta mahārathaḥa tataḥ kilakilāśabdaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyatac matsyapāñcālacedīnāṃ tam ekam abhidhāvatāma te varāśvarathavrātair vāraṇaiḥ sapadātibhiḥc tam ekaṃ chādayām āsur meghā iva divākarame bhīṣmaṃ bhāgīrathīputraṃ pratapantaṃ raṇe ripūna tatas tasya ca teṣāṃ ca yuddhe devāsuropamec kirīṭī bhīṣmam ānarchat puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinam saṃjaya uvācaa evaṃ te paṇḍavāḥ sarve puraskṛtya śikhaṇḍinamc vivyadhuḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ parivārya samantataḥa śataghnībhiḥ sughorābhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ saparaśvadhaiḥc mudgarair musalaiḥ prāsaiḥ kṣepaṇībhiś ca sarvaśaḥa śaraiḥ kanakapuṅkhaiś ca śaktitomarakampanaiḥc nārācair vatsadantaiś ca bhuśuṇḍībhiś ca bhāratae atāḍayan raṇe bhīṣmaṃ sahitāḥ sarvasṛñjayāḥa sa viśīrṇatanutrāṇaḥ pīḍito bahubhis tadāc vivyathe naiva gāṅgeyo bhidyamāneṣu marmasua sa dīptaśaracāpārcir astraprasṛtamārutaḥc neminirhrādasaṃnādo mahāstrodayapāvakaḥa citracāpamahājvālo vīrakṣayamahendhanaḥc yugāntāgnisamo bhīṣmaḥ pareṣāṃ samapadyataa nipatya rathasaṃghānām antareṇa viniḥsṛtaḥc dṛśyate sma narendrāṇāṃ punar madhyagataś carana tataḥ pāñcālarājaṃ ca dhṛṣṭaketum atītya cac pāṇḍavānīkinīmadhyam āsasāda sa vegitaḥa tataḥ sātyakibhīmau ca pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayamc drupadaṃ ca virāṭaṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatama bhīmaghoṣair mahāvegair vairivāraṇabhedibhiḥc ṣaḍ etān ṣaḍbhir ānarchad bhāskarapratimaiḥ śaraiḥa tasya te niśitān bāṇān saṃnivārya mahārathāḥc daśabhir daśabhir bhīṣmam ardayām āsur ojasāa śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe bāṇān yān mumoca mahāvratec te bhīṣmaṃ viviśus tūrṇaṃ svarṇapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥa tataḥ kirīṭī saṃrabdho bhīṣmam evābhyavartatac śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya dhanuś cāsya samācchinata bhīṣmasya dhanuṣaś chedaṃ nāmṛṣyanta mahārathāḥc droṇaś ca kṛtavarmā ca saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥa bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ śalyo bhagadattas tathaiva cac saptaite paramakruddhāḥ kirīṭinam abhidrutāḥa uttamāstrāṇi divyāni darśayanto mahārathāḥc abhipetur bhṛśaṃ kruddhāś chādayanta sma pāṇḍavāna teṣām āpatatāṃ śabdaḥ śuśruve phalgunaṃ pratic udvṛttānāṃ yathā śabdaḥ samudrāṇāṃ yugakṣayea hatānayata gṛhṇīta yudhyatāpi ca kṛntatac ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ phalgunasya rathaṃ pratia taṃ śabdaṃ tumulaṃ śrutvā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥc abhyadhāvan parīpsantaḥ phalgunaṃ bharatarṣabhaa sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥc virāṭadrupadau cobhau rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥa abhimanyuś ca saṃkruddhaḥ saptaite krodhamūrchitāḥc samabhyadhāvaṃs tvaritāś citrakārmukadhāriṇaḥa teṣāṃ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc saṃgrāme bharataśreṣṭha devānāṃ dānavair ivaa śikhaṇḍī tu rathaśreṣṭho rakṣyamāṇaḥ kirīṭināc avidhyad daśabhir bhīṣmaṃ chinnadhanvānam āhavee sārathiṃ daśabhiś cāsya dhvajaṃ caikena cicchidef dhanuś caikena bāṇena cicchide samare tadāa so nyat kārmukam ādāya gāṅgeyo vegavattaramc tad apy asya śitair bhallais tribhiś ciccheda phalgunaḥa evaṃ sa pāṇḍavaḥ kruddha āttam āttaṃ punaḥ punaḥc dhanur bhīṣmasya ciccheda savyasācī paraṃtapaḥa sa cchinnadhanvā saṃkruddhaḥ sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihanc śaktiṃ jagrāha saṃkruddho girīṇām api dāraṇīme tāṃ ca cikṣepa saṃkruddhaḥ phalgunasya rathaṃ pratifA preṣayām āsa śaktiṃ ca yamadaṃṣṭropamāṃ dṛḍhāma tām āpatantīṃ saṃprekṣya jvalantīm aśanīm ivac samādatta śitān bhallān pañca pāṇḍavanandanaḥa tasya ciccheda tāṃ śaktiṃ pañcadhā pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥc saṃkruddho bharataśreṣṭha bhīṣmabāhubaleritāma sā papāta paricchinnā saṃkruddhena kirīṭināc meghavṛndaparibhraṣṭā vicchinneva śatahradāa chinnāṃ tāṃ śaktim ālokya bhīṣmaḥ krodhasamanvitaḥc acintayad raṇe vīro buddhyā parapuraṃjayaḥa śakto haṃ dhanuṣaikena nihantuṃ sarvapāṇḍavānc yady eṣāṃ na bhaved goptā viṣvakseno mahābalaḥd ajayyaś caiva sarveṣāṃ lokānām iti me matiḥa kāraṇadvayam āsthāya nāhaṃ yotsyāmi pāṇḍavaiḥc avadhyatvāc ca pāṇḍūnāṃ strībhāvāc ca śikhaṇḍinaḥa pitrā tuṣṭena me pūrvaṃ yadā kālīm udāvahatc svacchandamaraṇaṃ dattam avadhyatvaṃ raṇe tathāe tasmān mṛtyum ahaṃ manye prāptakālam ivātmanaḥa evaṃ jñātvā vyavasitaṃ bhīṣmasyāmitatejasaḥc ṛṣayo vasavaś caiva viyatsthā bhīṣmam abruvana yat te vyavasitaṃ vīra asmākaṃ sumahat priyamc tat kuruṣva maheṣvāsa yuddhād buddhiṃ nivartayaa tasya vākyasya nidhane prādurāsīc chivo nilaḥc anulomaḥ sugandhī ca pṛṣataiś ca samanvitaḥa devadundubhayaś caiva saṃpraṇedur mahāsvanāḥc papāta puṣpavṛṣṭiś ca bhīṣmasyopari pārthivaa na ca tac chuśruve kaś cit teṣāṃ saṃvadatāṃ nṛpac ṛte bhīṣmaṃ mahābāhuṃ māṃ cāpi munitejasāa saṃbhramaś ca mahān āsīt tridaśānāṃ viśāṃ patec patiṣyati rathād bhīṣme sarvalokapriye tadāa iti devagaṇānāṃ ca śrutvā vākyaṃ mahāmanāḥc tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo bībhatsuṃ nābhyavartatae bhidyamānaḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ sarvāvaraṇabhedibhiḥa śikhaṇḍī tu mahārāja bharatānāṃ pitāmahamc ājaghānorasi kruddho navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa sa tenābhihataḥ saṃkhye bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥc nākampata mahārāja kṣitikampe yathācalaḥa tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur vyākṣipan gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥc gāṅgeyaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samarpayata punaḥ śaraśatenainaṃ tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥc sarvagātreṣu saṃkruddhaḥ sarvamarmasv atāḍayata evam anyair api bhṛśaṃ vadhyamāno mahāraṇeb tān apy āśu śarair bhīṣmaḥ pravivyādha mahārathaḥb taiś ca muktāñ śarān bhīṣmo yudhi satyaparākramaḥb nivārayām āsa śaraiḥ samaṃ saṃnataparvabhiḥb śikhaṇḍī tu raṇe bāṇān yān mumoca mahārathaḥc na cakrus te rujaṃ tasya rukmapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥa tataḥ kirīṭī saṃrabdho bhīṣmam evābhyavartatac śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya dhanuś cāsya samācchinata athainaṃ daśabhir viddhvā dhvajam ekena cicchidec sārathiṃ viśikhaiś cāsya daśabhiḥ samakampayata so nyat kārmukam ādatta gāṅgeyo balavattaramc tad apy asya śitair bhallais tridhā tribhir upānudate nimeṣāntaramātreṇa āttam āttaṃ mahāraṇea evam asya dhanūṃṣy ājau ciccheda subahūny apic tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo bībhatsuṃ nābhyavartataa athainaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇāṃ samardayatb paśyatāṃ kuruvīrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tatra bhāratac so tividdho maheṣvāso duḥśāsanam abhāṣataa eṣa pārtho raṇe kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaḥc śarair anekasāhasrair mām evābhyasate raṇea na caiṣa śakyaḥ samare jetuṃ vajrabhṛtā apic na cāpi sahitā vīrā devadānavarākṣasāḥe māṃ caiva śaktā nirjetuṃ kim u martyāḥ sudurbalāḥf na cāham api śaktas tu sarvair api mahārathaiḥf ṛte rjunaṃ susaṃkruddhair etat satyaṃ bravīmi tea evaṃ tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ phalguno niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc śikhaṇḍinaṃ puraskṛtya bhīṣmaṃ vivyādha saṃyugea tato duḥśāsanaṃ bhūyaḥ smayamāno bhyabhāṣatac atividdhaḥ śitair bāṇair bhṛśaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanāa vajrāśanisamasparśāḥ śitāgrāḥ saṃpraveśitāḥc vimuktā avyavacchinnā neme bāṇāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa nikṛntamānā marmāṇi dṛḍhāvaraṇabhedinaḥc musalānīva me ghnanti neme bāṇāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa brahmadaṇḍasamasparśā vajravegā durāsadāḥc mama prāṇān ārujanti neme bāṇāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa bhujagā iva saṃkruddhā lelihānā viṣolbaṇāḥc mamāviśanti marmāṇi neme bāṇāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa nāśayantīva me prāṇān yamadūtā ivāhitāḥc gadāparighasaṃsparśā neme bāṇāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa kṛntanti mama gātrāṇi māghamāse gavām ivac arjunasya ime bāṇā neme bāṇāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥa sarve hy api na me duḥkhaṃ kuryur anye narādhipāḥc vīraṃ gaṇḍīvadhanvānam ṛte jiṣṇuṃ kapidhvajama iti bruvañ śāṃtanavo didhakṣur iva pāṇḍavamc saviṣphuliṅgāṃ dīptāgrāṃ śaktiṃ cikṣepa bhārataa tām asya viśikhaiś chittvā tridhā tribhir apātayatc paśyatāṃ kuruvīrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tatra bhārataa carmāthādatta gāṅgeyo jātarūpapariṣkṛtamc khaḍgaṃ cānyataraṃ prepsur mṛtyor agre jayāya vāa tasya tac chatadhā carma vyadhamad daṃśitātmanaḥc rathād anavarūḍhasya tad adbhutam ivābhavata vinadyoccaiḥ siṃha iva svāny anīkāny acodayatc abhidravata gāṅgeyaṃ māṃ vo stu bhayam aṇv apia atha te tomaraiḥ prāsair bāṇaughaiś ca samantataḥc paṭṭiśaiś ca sanistriṃśair nānāpraharaṇais tathāa vatsadantaiś ca bhallaiś ca tam ekam abhidudruvuḥc siṃhanādas tato ghoraḥ pāṇḍavānām ajāyataa tathaiva tava putrāś ca rājan bhīṣmajayaiṣiṇaḥc tam ekam abhyavartanta siṃhanādāṃś ca nedirea tatrāsīt tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ tāvakānāṃ paraiḥ sahac daśame hani rājendra bhīṣmārjunasamāgamea āsīd gāṅga ivāvarto muhūrtam udadher ivac sainyānāṃ yudhyamānānāṃ nighnatām itaretarama agamyarūpā pṛthivī śoṇitāktā tadābhavatc samaṃ ca viṣamaṃ caiva na prājñāyata kiṃ canaa yodhānām ayutaṃ hatvā tasmin sa daśame hanic atiṣṭhad āhave bhīṣmo bhidyamāneṣu marmasua tataḥ senāmukhe tasmin sthitaḥ pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥc madhyena kurusainyānāṃ drāvayām āsa vāhinīmd tatrādbhutam apaśyāma pāṇḍavānāṃ parākramamd drāvayām āsur iṣubhiḥ sarvān bhīṣmapadānugāna vayaṃ śvetahayād bhītāḥ kuntīputrād dhanaṃjayātc pīḍyamānāḥ śitaiḥ śastraiḥ pradravāma mahāraṇāta sauvīrāḥ kitavāḥ prācyāḥ pratīcyodīcyamālavāḥb pāṇḍavaiḥ pañcabhiḥ sārdhaṃ sātyakena ca dhanvināb dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhaiḥ sarvaiḥ pāñcālaiś ca samantataḥb bhidyamānāḥ śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ sarve kārṣṇipurogamaiḥb droṇadrauṇikṛpaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarve śalyakṛpādayaḥb tāvakāḥ samare rājañ jahur bhīṣmaṃ mahāmṛdhec abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayo tha vasātayaḥa śālvāśrayās trigartāś ca ambaṣṭhāḥ kekayaiḥ sahac dvādaśaite janapadāḥ śarārtā vraṇapīḍitāḥe saṃgrāme na jahur bhīṣmaṃ yudhyamānaṃ kirīṭināa tatas tam ekaṃ bahavaḥ parivārya samantataḥc parikālya kurūn sarvāñ śaravarṣair avākirana nipātayata gṛhṇīta vidhyatātha ca karṣatac ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdo rājan bhīṣmarathaṃ pratia abhihatya śaraughais taṃ śataśo tha sahasraśaḥc na tasyāsīd anirbhinnaṃ gātreṣv aṅgulamātrakama evaṃ vibho tava pitā śarair viśakalīkṛtaḥc śitāgraiḥ phalgunenājau prākśirāḥ prāpatad rathāte kiṃciccheṣe dinakare putrāṇāṃ tava paśyatāma hā heti divi devānāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥc patamāne rathād bhīṣme babhūva sumahān svanaḥa taṃ patantam abhiprekṣya mahātmānaṃ pitāmahamc saha bhīṣmeṇa sarveṣāṃ prāpatan hṛdayāni naḥa sa papāta mahābāhur vasudhām anunādayanc indradhvaja ivotsṛṣṭaḥ ketuḥ sarvadhanuṣmatāme dharaṇīṃ nāspṛśac cāpi śarasaṃghaiḥ samācitaḥa śaratalpe maheṣvāsaṃ śayānaṃ puruṣarṣabhamc rathāt prapatitaṃ cainaṃ divyo bhāvaḥ samāviśata abhyavarṣata parjanyaḥ prākampata ca medinīc patan sa dadṛśe cāpi kharvitaṃ ca divākarama saṃjñāṃ caivālabhad vīraḥ kālaṃ saṃcintya bhāratac antarikṣe ca śuśrāva divyāṃ vācaṃ samantataḥa kathaṃ mahātmā gāṅgeyaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥc kālaṃ kartā naravyāghraḥ saṃprāpte dakṣiṇāyanea sthito smīti ca gāṅgeyas tac chrutvā vākyam abravītc dhārayām āsa ca prāṇān patito pi hi bhūtalee uttarāyaṇam anvicchan bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥa tasya tan matam ājñāya gaṅgā himavataḥ sutāc maharṣīn haṃsarūpeṇa preṣayām āsa tatra vaia tataḥ saṃpātino haṃsās tvaritā mānasaukasaḥc ājagmuḥ sahitā draṣṭuṃ bhīṣmaṃ kurupitāmahame yatra śete naraśreṣṭhaḥ śaratalpe pitāmahaḥa te tu bhīṣmaṃ samāsādya munayo haṃsarūpiṇaḥc apaśyañ śaratalpasthaṃ bhīṣmaṃ kurupitāmahama te taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇamc gāṅgeyaṃ bharataśreṣṭhaṃ dakṣiṇena ca bhāskarama itaretaram āmantrya prāhus tatra manīṣiṇaḥc bhīṣma eva mahātmā san saṃsthātā dakṣiṇāyanea ity uktvā prasthitān haṃsān dakṣiṇām abhito diśamc saṃprekṣya vai mahābuddhiś cintayitvā ca bhārataa tān abravīc chāṃtanavo nāhaṃ gantā kathaṃ canac dakṣiṇāvṛtta āditye etan me manasi sthitama gamiṣyāmi svakaṃ sthānam āsīd yan me purātanamc udagāvṛtta āditye haṃsāḥ satyaṃ bravīmi vaḥa dhārayiṣyāmy ahaṃ prāṇān uttarāyaṇakāṅkṣayāc aiśvaryabhūtaḥ prāṇānām utsarge niyato hy ahame tasmāt prāṇān dhārayiṣye mumūrṣur udagāyanea yaś ca datto varo mahyaṃ pitrā tena mahātmanāc chandato mṛtyur ity evaṃ tasya cāstu varas tathāa dhārayiṣye tataḥ prāṇān utsarge niyate satic ity uktvā tāṃs tadā haṃsān aśeta śaratalpagaḥa evaṃ kurūṇāṃ patite śṛṅge bhīṣme mahaujasic pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāś caiva siṃhanādaṃ pracakrirea tasmin hate mahāsattve bharatānām amadhyamec na kiṃ cit pratyapadyanta putrās te bharatarṣabhae saṃmohaś caiva tumulaḥ kurūṇām abhavat tadāa nṛpā duryodhanamukhā niḥśvasya rurudus tataḥc viṣādāc ca ciraṃ kālam atiṣṭhan vigatendriyāḥa dadhyuś caiva mahārāja na yuddhe dadhire manaḥc ūrugrāhagṛhītāś ca nābhyadhāvanta pāṇḍavāna avadhye śaṃtanoḥ putre hate bhīṣme mahaujasib duḥkhārtās te tadā rājan kurūṇāṃ patayo bhavanc abhāvaḥ sumahān rājan kurūn āgād atandritaḥa hatapravīrāś ca vayaṃ nikṛttāś ca śitaiḥ śaraiḥc kartavyaṃ nābhijānīmo nirjitāḥ savyasācināa pāṇḍavās tu jayaṃ labdhvā paratra ca parāṃ gatimc sarve dadhmur mahāśaṅkhāñ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥe somakāś ca sapañcālāḥ prāhṛṣyanta janeśvaraa tatas tūryasahasreṣu nadatsu sumahābalaḥc āsphoṭayām āsa bhṛśaṃ bhīmaseno nanarta caa senayor ubhayoś cāpi gāṅgeye vinipātitec saṃnyasya vīrāḥ śastrāṇi prādhyāyanta samantataḥa prākrośan prāpataṃś cānye jagmur mohaṃ tathāparec kṣatraṃ cānye bhyanindanta bhīṣmaṃ caike bhyapūjayana ṛṣayaḥ pitaraś caiva praśaśaṃsur mahāvratamc bharatānāṃ ca ye pūrve te cainaṃ praśaśaṃsirea mahopaniṣadaṃ caiva yogam āsthāya vīryavānc japañ śāṃtanavo dhīmān kālākāṅkṣī sthito bhavat dhṛtarāṣṭra uvācaa katham āsaṃs tadā yodhā hīnā bhīṣmeṇa saṃjayac balinā devakalpena gurvarthe brahmacāriṇāa tadaiva nihatān manye kurūn anyāṃś ca pārthivānc na prāharad yadā bhīṣmo ghṛṇitvād drupadātmajea tato duḥkhataraṃ manye kim anyat prabhaviṣyatic yad adya pitaraṃ śrutvā nihataṃ mama durmateḥa aśmasāramayaṃ nūnaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama saṃjayac śrutvā vinihataṃ bhīṣmaṃ śatadhā yan na dīryatea punaḥ punar na mṛṣyāmi hataṃ devavrataṃ raṇec na hato jāmadagnyena divyair astraiḥ sma yaḥ purād sa hato draupadeyena pāñcālyena śikhaṇḍināa yad adya nihatenājau bhīṣmeṇa jayam icchatāc ceṣṭitaṃ narasiṃhena tan me kathaya saṃjaya saṃjaya uvācaa sāyāhne nyapatad bhūmau dhārtarāṣṭrān viṣādayanc pāñcālānāṃ dadad dharṣaṃ kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥa sa śete śaratalpastho medinīm aspṛśaṃs tadāc bhīṣmo rathāt prapatitaḥ pracyuto dharaṇītalea hā heti tumulaḥ śabdo bhūtānāṃ samapadyatac sīmāvṛkṣe nipatite kurūṇāṃ samitikṣayea ubhayoḥ senayo rājan kṣatriyān bhayam āviśatc bhīṣmaṃ śaṃtanavaṃ dṛṣṭvā viśīrṇakavacadhvajame kuravaḥ paryavartanta pāṇḍavāś ca viśāṃ patea khaṃ tamovṛtam āsīc ca nāsīd bhānumataḥ prabhāb kurupāṇḍavayoś chatre ādhāre ca dhanuṣmatāmc rarāsa pṛthivī caiva bhīṣme śāṃtanave hatea ayaṃ brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho ayaṃ brahmavidāṃ gatiḥc ity abhāṣanta bhūtāni śayānaṃ bharatarṣabhama ayaṃ pitaram ājñāya kāmārtaṃ śaṃtanuṃ purāc ūrdhvaretasam ātmānaṃ cakāra puruṣarṣabhaḥa iti sma śaratalpasthaṃ bharatānām amadhyamamc ṛṣayaḥ paryadhāvanta sahitāḥ siddhacāraṇaiḥa hate śāṃtanave bhīṣme bharatānāṃ pitāmahec na kiṃ cit pratyapadyanta putrās tava ca bhārataa vivarṇavadanāś cāsan gataśrīkāś ca bhāratac atiṣṭhan vrīḍitāś caiva hriyā yuktā hy adhomukhāḥa pāṇḍavāś ca jayaṃ labdhvā saṃgrāmaśirasi sthitāḥc sarve dadhmur mahāśaṅkhān hemajālapariṣkṛtāna bhṛśaṃ tūryaninādeṣu vādyamāneṣu cānaghac apaśyāma raṇe rājan bhīmasenaṃ mahābalame ākrīḍamānaṃ kaunteyaṃ harṣeṇa mahatā yutama nihatya samare śatrūn mahābalasamanvitānc saṃmohaś cāpi tumulaḥ kurūṇām abhavat tadāa karṇaduryodhanau cāpi niḥśvasetāṃ muhur muhuḥc tathā nipatite bhīṣme kauravāṇāṃ dhuraṃdharee hāhākāram abhūt sarvaṃ nirmaryādam avartataa dṛṣṭvā ca patitaṃ bhīṣmaṃ putro duḥśāsanas tavac uttamaṃ javam āsthāya droṇānīkaṃ samādravatd āgatas tvaramāṇas tu balena mahatā vṛtaḥd sametya puruṣavyāghra tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥd duḥśāsanaṃ drutataraṃ droṇavijñāpanāya tata bhrātrā prasthāpito vīraḥ svenānīkena daṃśitaḥc prayayau puruṣavyāghraḥ svasainyam abhicodayana tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya kuravaḥ paryavārayanc duḥśāsanaṃ mahārāja kim ayaṃ vakṣyatīti vaia tato droṇāya nihataṃ bhīṣmam ācaṣṭa kauravaḥc droṇas tad apriyaṃ śrutvā sahasā nyapatad rathāta sa saṃjñām upalabhyātha bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavānc nivārayām āsa tadā svāny anīkāni māriṣaa vinivṛttān kurūn dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavāpi svasainikānc dūtaiḥ śīghrāśvasaṃyuktair avahāram akārayana vinivṛtteṣu sainyeṣu pāraṃparyeṇa sarvaśaḥc vimuktakavacāḥ sarve bhīṣmam īyur narādhipāḥa vyupāramya tato yuddhād yodhāḥ śatasahasraśaḥc upatasthur mahātmānaṃ prajāpatim ivāmarāḥa te tu bhīṣmaṃ samāsādya śayānaṃ bharatarṣabhamc abhivādya vyatiṣṭhanta pāṇḍavāḥ kurubhiḥ sahaa atha pāṇḍūn kurūṃś caiva praṇipatyāgrataḥ sthitānc abhyabhāṣata dharmātmā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas tadāa svāgataṃ vo mahābhāgāḥ svāgataṃ vo mahārathāḥc tuṣyāmi darśanāc cāhaṃ yuṣmākam amaropamāḥa abhinandya sa tān evaṃ śirasā lambatābravītb paripārśve tava sutān sthitān udvīkṣya bhāratac śiro me lambate tyartham upadhānaṃ pradīyatāmd etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ bhīṣmād bhāgīrathīsutāta tato nṛpāḥ samājahrus tanūni ca mṛdūni cac upadhānāni mukhyāni naicchat tāni pitāmahaḥa abravīc ca naravyāghraḥ prahasann iva tān nṛpānc naitāni vīraśayyāsu yuktarūpāṇi pārthivāḥa tato vīkṣya naraśreṣṭham abhyabhāṣata pāṇḍavamc dhanaṃjayaṃ dīrghabāhuṃ sarvalokamahārathama dhanaṃjaya mahābāho śiraso me sya lambataḥc dīyatām upadhānaṃ vai yad yuktam iha manyasea sa saṃnyasya mahac cāpam abhivādya pitāmahamc netrābhyām aśrupūrṇābhyām idaṃ vacanam abravīta ājñāpaya kuruśreṣṭha sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varac preṣyo haṃ tava durdharṣa kriyatāṃ kiṃ pitāmahaa tam abravīc chāṃtanavaḥ śiro me tāta lambatec upadhānaṃ kuruśreṣṭha phalgunopanayasva mee śayanasyānurūpaṃ hi śīghraṃ vīra prayaccha mea tvaṃ hi pārtha mahābāho śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadhanuṣmatāmc kṣatradharmasya vettā ca buddhisattvaguṇānvitaḥa phalgunas tu tathety uktvā vyavasāyapurojavaḥc pragṛhyāmantrya gāṇḍīvaṃ śarāṃś ca nataparvaṇaḥa anumānya mahātmānaṃ bharatānām amadhyamamc tribhis tīkṣṇair mahāvegair udagṛhṇāc chiraḥ śaraiḥa abhiprāye tu vidite dharmātmā savyasācināc atuṣyad bharataśreṣṭho bhīṣmo dharmārthatattvavitd upadhāne tathā datte bhīṣmasya savyasācinād bhīṣmo pi bharatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvadharmārthatattvavita upadhānena dattena pratyanandad dhanaṃjayamb prāha sarvān samudvīkṣya bharatān bhārataṃ pratic kuntīputraṃ yudhāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ suhṛdāṃ prītivardhanama anurūpaṃ śayānasya pāṇḍavopahitaṃ tvayāc yady anyathā pravartethāḥ śapeyaṃ tvām ahaṃ ruṣāa evam etan mahābāho dharmeṣu pariniṣṭhitamc svaptavyaṃ kṣatriyeṇājau śaratalpagatena vaia evam uktvā tu bībhatsuṃ sarvāṃs tān abravīd vacaḥc rājñaś ca rājaputrāṃś ca pāṇḍavenābhi saṃsthitānd paśyadhvam upadhānaṃ me pāṇḍavenābhisaṃdhitama śayeyam asyāṃ śayyāyāṃ yāvad āvartanaṃ raveḥc ye tadā pārayiṣyanti te māṃ drakṣyanti vai nṛpāḥa diśaṃ vaiśravaṇākrāntāṃ yadā gantā divākaraḥc arciṣmān pratapaṃl lokān rathenottamatejasāe vimokṣye haṃ tadā prāṇān suhṛdaḥ supriyān apia parikhā khanyatām atra mamāvasadane nṛpāḥc upāsiṣye vivasvantam evaṃ śaraśatācitaḥe upāramadhvaṃ saṃgrāmād vairāṇy utsṛjya pārthivāḥa upātiṣṭhann atho vaidyāḥ śalyoddharaṇakovidāḥc sarvopakaraṇair yuktāḥ kuśalās te suśikṣitāḥa tān dṛṣṭvā jāhnavīputraḥ provāca vacanaṃ tadāc dattadeyā visṛjyantāṃ pūjayitvā cikitsakāḥa evaṃgate na hīdānīṃ vaidyaiḥ kāryam ihāsti meb bhavantaḥ kuśalā nityaṃ bhiṣajo vedanāharāḥb uvāca putro gaṃgāyā na vaidyaiḥ kāryam asti mec kṣatradharmapraśastāṃ hi prāpto smi paramāṃ gatima naiṣa dharmo mahīpālāḥ śaratalpagatasya meb etān pūjaya rājendra vastrālaṃkaraṇādibhiḥc etair eva śaraiś cāhaṃ dagdhavyo nte narādhipāḥd vidyās tiṣṭhanti kuśalāḥ sadā vyādhicikitsanea tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya putro duryodhanas tavac vaidyān visarjayām āsa pūjayitvā yathārhataḥa tatas te vismayaṃ jagmur nānājanapadeśvarāḥc sthitiṃ dharme parāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmasyāmitatejasaḥa upadhānaṃ tato dattvā pitus tava janeśvarac sahitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve kuravaś ca mahārathāḥa upagamya mahātmānaṃ śayānaṃ śayane śubhec te bhivādya tato bhīṣmaṃ kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇama vidhāya rakṣāṃ bhīṣmasya sarva eva samantataḥc vīrāḥ svaśibirāṇy eva dhyāyantaḥ paramāturāḥe niveśāyābhyupāgacchan sāyāhne rudhirokṣitāḥa niviṣṭān pāṇḍavāṃś cāpi prīyamāṇān mahārathānc bhīṣmasya patanād dhṛṣṭān upagamya mahārathāne uvāca yādavaḥ kāle dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhirama diṣṭyā jayasi kauravya diṣṭyā bhīṣmo nipātitaḥc avadhyo mānuṣair eṣa satyasaṃdho mahārathaḥa atha vā daivataiḥ pārtha sarvaśastrāstrapāragaḥc tvāṃ tu cakṣurhaṇaṃ prāpya dagdho ghoreṇa cakṣuṣāa evam ukto dharmarājaḥ pratyuvāca janārdanamc tava prasādād vijayaḥ krodhāt tava parājayaḥe tvaṃ hi naḥ śaraṇaṃ kṛṣṇa bhaktānām abhayaṃkaraḥa anāścaryo jayas teṣāṃ yeṣāṃ tvam asi keśavac raṣkitā samare nityaṃ nityaṃ cāpi hite rataḥe sarvathā tvāṃ samāsādya nāścaryam iti me matiḥa evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca smayamāno janārdanaḥc tvayy evaitad yuktarūpaṃ vacanaṃ pārthivottama saṃjaya uvācaa vyuṣṭāyāṃ tu mahārāja rajanyāṃ sarvapārthivāḥc pāṇḍavā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca abhijagmuḥ pitāmahama taṃ vīraśayane vīraṃ śayānaṃ kurusattamamc abhivādyopatasthur vai kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyarṣabhama kanyāś candanacūrṇaiś ca lājair mālyaiś ca sarvaśaḥb avākirañ śāṃtanavaṃ tatra gatvā sahasraśaḥc striyo bālās tathā vṛddhāḥ prekṣakāś ca pṛthagjanāḥe samabhyayuḥ śāṃtanavaṃ bhūtānīva tamonudama tūryāṇi gaṇikā vārās tathaiva naṭanartakāḥc upānṛtyañ jaguś caiva vṛddhaṃ kurupitāmahama upāramya ca yuddhebhyaḥ saṃnāhān vipramucya cac āyudhāni ca nikṣipya sahitāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥa anvāsata durādharṣaṃ devavratam ariṃdamamc anyonyaṃ prītimantas te yathāpūrvaṃ yathāvayaḥa sā pārthivaśatākīrṇā samitir bhīṣmaśobhitāc śuśubhe bhāratī dīptā divīvādityamaṇḍalamd upāsāṃ cakrire sarve kurupāṇḍavasainikāḥa vibabhau ca nṛpāṇāṃ sā pitāmaham upāsatāmc devānām iva deveśaṃ pitāmaham upāsatāma bhīṣmas tu vedanāṃ dhairyān nigṛhya bharatarṣabhab nānāpraharaṇair viddhaḥ śaratalpagatas tathāc abhitaptaḥ śaraiś caiva nātihṛṣṭamanābravīta śarābhitaptakāyo haṃ śarasaṃtāpamūrchitaḥc pānīyam abhikāṅkṣe haṃ rājñas tān pratyabhāṣataa tatas te kṣatriyā rājan samājahruḥ samantataḥc bhakṣyān uccāvacāṃs tatra vārikumbhāṃś ca śītalāna upanītaṃ ca tad dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo bravītc nādya tāta mayā śakyaṃ bhogān kāṃś cana mānuṣānd nedaṃ mama jalaṃ yogyaṃ pātuṃ naiva kṣamo hy ahama upabhoktuṃ manuṣyebhyaḥ śaraśayyāgato hy ahamc pratīkṣamāṇas tiṣṭhāmi nivṛttiṃ śaśisūryayoḥd evam uktvā tatovāca bhīṣmaḥ śaraśataiś citaḥd payaḥ pāsyāmi gopālā gomayaṃ na tu gomayamd gomayenāgnivarṇena gomayaṃ na tu gomayama evam uktvā śāṃtanavo dīnavāk sarvapārthivānc dhanaṃjayaṃ mahābāhum abhyabhāṣata bhārataa athopetya mahābāhur abhivādya pitāmahamc atiṣṭhat prāñjaliḥ prahvaḥ kiṃ karomīti cābravīta taṃ dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavaṃ rājann abhivādyāgrataḥ sthitamc abhyabhāṣata dharmātmā bhīṣmaḥ prīto dhanaṃjayama dahyate daḥ śarīraṃ me saṃsyūto smi maheṣubhiḥc marmāṇi paridūyante vadanaṃ mama śuṣyatia hlādanārthaṃ śarīrasya prayacchāpo mamārjunab gomukhaiḥ pīḍyamānasya gaur naṣṭo mama gopateb gorasaṃ pātum icchāmi gobhir yac ca na dūṣitamc tvaṃ hi śakto maheṣvāsa dātum ambho yathāvidhia arjunas tu tathety uktvā ratham āruhya vīryavānc adhijyaṃ balavat kṛtvā gāṇḍīvaṃ vyākṣipad dhanuḥa tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥc vitresuḥ sarvabhūtāni śrutvā sarve ca pārthivāḥa tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā rathena rathināṃ varaḥc śayānaṃ bharataśreṣṭhaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varama saṃdhāya ca śaraṃ dīptam abhimantrya mahāyaśāḥc parjanyāstreṇa saṃyojya sarvalokasya paśyataḥe avidhyat pṛthivīṃ pārthaḥ pārśve bhīṣmasya dakṣiṇea utpapāta tato dhārā vimalā vāriṇaḥ śivāc śītasyāmṛtakalpasya divyagandharasasya caa atarpayat tataḥ pārthaḥ śītayā vāridhārayāc bhīṣmaṃ kurūṇām ṛṣabhaṃ divyakarmaparākramaḥa karmaṇā tena pārthasya śakraṣyeva vikurvataḥc vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmus tatas te vasudhādhipāḥa tat karma prekṣya bībhatsor atimānuṣam adbhutamc saṃprāvepanta kuravo gāvaḥ śītārditā ivaa vismayāc cottarīyāṇi vyāvidhyan sarvato nṛpāḥc śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣais tumulaṃ sarvato bhavata tṛptaḥ śāṃtanavaś cāpi rājan bībhatsum abravītc sarvapārthivavīrāṇāṃ saṃnidhau pūjayann ivaa naitac citraṃ mahābāho tvayi kauravanandanac kathito nāradenāsi pūrvarṣir amitadyutiḥa vāsudevasahāyas tvaṃ mahat karma kariṣyasic yan notsahati devendraḥ saha devair api dhruvama vidus tvāṃ nidhanaṃ pārtha sarvakṣatrasya tadvidaḥc dhanurdharāṇām ekas tvaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pravaro nṛṣua manuṣyā jagati śreṣṭhāḥ pakṣiṇāṃ garuḍo varaḥc sarasāṃ sāgaraḥ śreṣṭho gaur variṣṭhā catuṣpadāma ādityas tejasāṃ śreṣṭho girīṇāṃ himavān varaḥc jātīnāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhas tvam asi dhanvināma na vai śrutaṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṇa vākyaṃsaṃbodhyamānaṃ vidureṇa caivac droṇena rāmeṇa janārdanenamuhur muhuḥ saṃjayenāpi coktama parītabuddhir hi visaṃjñakalpoduryodhano nābhyanandad vaco mec sa śeṣyate vai nihataś cirāyaśāstrātigo bhīmabalābhibhūtaḥa tataḥ śrutvā tad vacaḥ kauravendroduryodhano dīnamanā babhūvac tam abravīc chāṃtanavo bhivīkṣyanibodha rājan bhava vītamanyuḥa dṛṣṭaṃ duryodhanedaṃ te yathā pārthena dhīmatāc jalasya dhārā janitā śītasyāmṛtagandhinaḥe etasya kartā loke smin nānyaḥ kaś cana vidyatea āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ saumyaṃ vāyavyam atha vaiṣṇavamc aindraṃ pāśupataṃ brāhmaṃ pārameṣṭhyaṃ prajāpateḥe dhātus tvaṣṭuś ca savitur divyāny astrāṇi sarvaśaḥa sarvasmin mānuṣe loke vetty eko hi dhanaṃjayaḥc kṛṣṇo vā devakīputro nānyo vai veda kaś canae na śakyāḥ pāṇḍavās tāta yuddhe jetuṃ kathaṃ canaa amānuṣāṇi karmāṇi yasyaitāni mahātmanaḥc tena sattvavatā saṃkhye śūreṇāhavaśobhināe kṛtinā samare rājan saṃdhis te tāta yujyatāma yāvat kṛṣṇo mahābāhuḥ svādhīnaḥ kurusaṃsadic tāvat pārthena śūreṇa saṃdhis te tāta yujyatāma yāvac camūṃ na te śeṣāṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc nāśayaty arjunas tāvat saṃdhis te tāta yujyatāma yāvat tiṣṭhanti samare hataśeṣāḥ sahodarāḥc nṛpāś ca bahavo rājaṃs tāvat saṃdhiḥ prayujyatāma na nirdahati te yāvat krodhadīptekṣaṇaś camūmc yudhiṣṭhiro hi tāvad vai saṃdhis te tāta yujyatāma nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥb yāvat kṣatraṃ na nighnanti tāvat saṃdhir vidhīyatāmc yāvac camūṃ mahārāja nāśayanti na sarvaśaḥe tāvat te pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ saubhrātraṃ tāta rocatāma yuddhaṃ madantam evāstu tāta saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥc etat te rocatāṃ vākyaṃ yad ukto si mayānaghae etat kṣemam ahaṃ manye tava caiva kulasya caa tyaktvā manyum upaśāmyasva pārthaiḥparyāptam etad yat kṛtaṃ phalgunenac bhīṣmasyāntād astu vaḥ sauhṛdaṃ vāsaṃpraśleṣaḥ sādhu rājan prasīdaa rājyasyārdhaṃ dīyatāṃ pāṇḍavānāmindraprasthaṃ dharmarājo nuśāstuc mā mitradhruk pārthivānāṃ jaghanyaḥpāpāṃ kīrtiṃ prāpsyase kauravendraa mamāvasānāc chāntir astu prajānāṃsaṃgacchantāṃ pārthivāḥ prītimantaḥc pitā putraṃ mātulaṃ bhāgineyobhrātā caiva bhrātaraṃ praitu rājana na ced evaṃ prāptakālaṃ vaco memohāviṣṭaḥ pratipatsyasy abuddhyāb tapsyasyante lobhabhāvāt tvam evaṃb ye cāpy anye bhūmipālāḥ sametāḥc bhīṣmasyāntād etadantāḥ stha sarvesatyām etāṃ bhāratīm īrayāmic diṣṭaṃ gantā tyaktadharmārthakāmaḥc putrabhrātṛjñātisaṃbandhihīnaḥc evaṃ vo stu viditaṃ kauraveyāḥa etad vākyaṃ sauhṛdād āpageyomadhye rājñāṃ bhārataṃ śrāvayitvāc tūṣṇīm āsīc chalyasaṃtaptamarmāyatvātmānaṃ vedanāṃ saṃnigṛhyad dharmārthasahitaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā hitam anāmayamd nārocayata putras te mumūrṣur iva bheṣajam saṃjaya uvācaa tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve jagmuḥ svān ālayān punaḥc tūṣṇīṃbhūte mahārāja bhīṣme śaṃtanunandanea śrutvā tu nihataṃ bhīṣmaṃ rādheyaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥc īṣad āgatasaṃtrāsaḥ tvarayopajagāma haa sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ śaratalpagataṃ tadāc janmaśayyāgataṃ devaṃ kārttikeyam iva prabhuma nimīlitākṣaṃ taṃ vīraṃ sāśrukaṇṭhas tadā vṛṣaḥb bhīṣma bhīṣma mahābāho ity uvāca mahādyutiḥc abhyetya pādayos tasya nipapāta mahādyutiḥa rādheyo haṃ kuruśreṣṭha nityaṃ cāṣkigatas tavac dveṣyo tyantam anāgāḥ sann iti cainam uvāca haa tac chrutvā kuruvṛddhaḥ sa balāt saṃvṛttalocanaḥc śanair udvīkṣya sasneham idaṃ vacanam abravīta rahitaṃ dhiṣṇyam ālokya samutsārya ca rakṣiṇaḥc piteva putraṃ gāṅgeyaḥ pariṣvajyaikabāhunāa ehy ehi me vipratīpa spardhase tvaṃ mayā sahac yadi māṃ nābhigacchethā na te śreyo bhaved dhruvama kaunteyas tvaṃ na rādheyo vidito nāradān mamaa   na tavādhirathaḥ pitāa sūryajas tvaṃ mahābāhoc kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāc caiva keśavāc ca na saṃśayaḥa na ca dveṣo sti me tāta tvayi satyaṃ bravīmi tec tejovadhanimittaṃ tu paruṣāṇy aham uktavāna akasmāt pāṇḍavān hi tvaṃ dviṣasīti matir mamac yenāsi bahuśo rūkṣaṃ coditaḥ sūryanandanad jāto si dharmalopena tatas te buddhir īdṛśīd nīcāśrayān matsareṇa dveṣiṇī guṇinām apid tenāsi bahuśo rūkṣaṃ śrāvitaḥ kurusaṃsadia jānāmi samare vīryaṃ śatrubhir duḥsahaṃ tavac brahmaṇyatāṃ ca śauryaṃ ca dāne ca paramāṃ gatima na tvayā sadṛśaḥ kaś cit puruṣeṣv amaropamac kulabhedaṃ ca matvāhaṃ sadā paruṣam uktavāna iṣvastre bhārasaṃdhāne lāghave strabale tathāc sadṛśaḥ phalgunenāsi kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanāa karṇa rājapuraṃ gatvā tvayaikena dhanuṣmatāc tasyārthe kururājasya rājāno mṛditā yudhia tathā ca balavān rājā jarāsaṃdho durāsadaḥc samare samaraślāghī tvayā na sadṛśo bhavata brahmaṇyaḥ satyavādī ca tejasārka ivāparaḥc devagarbho jitaḥ saṃkhye manuṣyair adhiko bhuvia vyapanīto dya manyur me yas tvāṃ prati purā kṛtaḥc daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa na śakyam ativartituma sodaryāḥ pāṇḍavā vīrā bhrātaras te risūdanac saṃgaccha tair mahābāho mama ced icchasi priyama mayā bhavatu nirvṛttaṃ vairam ādityanandanac pṛthivyāṃ sarvarājāno bhavantv adya nirāmayāḥ karṇa uvācaa jānāmy ahaṃ mahāprājña sarvam etan na saṃśayaḥc yathā vadasi durdharṣa kaunteyo haṃ na sūtajaḥa avakīrṇas tv ahaṃ kuntyā sūtena ca vivardhitaḥc bhuktvā duryodhanaiśvaryaṃ na mithyā kartum utsahed vasudevasuto yadvat pāṇḍavāya dṛḍhavrataḥa vasu caiva śarīraṃ ca yad udāraṃ tathā yaśaḥc sarvaṃ duryodhanasyārthe tyaktaṃ me bhūridakṣiṇae kopitāḥ pāṇḍavā nityaṃ mayāśritya suyodhanamf tathā duryodhanasyārthe vīramārganiṣeviṇāf mā caitad vyādhimaraṇaṃ kṣatraṃ syād iti kauravaa avaśyabhāvī vai yo rtho na sa śakyo nivartitumc daivaṃ puruṣakāreṇa ko nivartitum utsaheta pṛthivīkṣayaśaṃsīni nimittāni pitāmahac bhavadbhir upalabdhāni kathitāni ca saṃsadia pāṇḍavā vāsudevaś ca viditā mama sarvaśaḥc ajeyāḥ puruṣair anyair iti tāṃś cotsahāmahed vijayiṣye raṇe pāṇḍūn iti me niścitaṃ matamd na cec chakyam avasraṣṭuṃ vairam etat sudāruṇamd dhanaṃjayena yotsye haṃ svadharmaprītamānasaḥd adharmaṃ vyādhimaraṇaṃ kṣatriyasya pitāmahaa anujānīṣva māṃ tāta yuddhe prītamanāḥ sadāc anujñātas tvayā vīra yudhyeyam iti me matiḥa duruktaṃ vipratīpaṃ vā saṃrambhāc cāpalāt tathāc yan mayāpakṛtaṃ kiṃ cit tad anukṣantum arhasi bhīṣma uvācaa na cec chakyam athotsraṣṭuṃ vairam etat sudāruṇamc anujānāmi karṇa tvāṃ yudhyasva svargakāmyayāa vimanyur gatasaṃrambhaḥ kuru karma nṛpasya hic yathāśakti yathotsāhaṃ satāṃ vṛtteṣu vṛttavāna ahaṃ tvām anujānāmi yad icchasi tad āpnuhic kṣatradharmajitāṃl lokān saṃprāpsyasi na saṃśayaḥa yudhyasva nirahaṃkāro balavīryavyapāśrayaḥc dharmo hi yuddhāc chreyo nyat kṣatriyasya na vidyatea praśame hi kṛto yatnaḥ sucirāt suciraṃ mayāc na caiva śakitaḥ kartuṃ yato dharmas tato jayaḥ saṃjaya uvācaa evaṃ bruvantaṃ gāṅgeyam abhivādya prasādya cac rādheyo ratham āruhya prāyāt tava sutaṃ pratid ya idaṃ śṛṇuyād bhaktyā bhīṣmaparva mahādbhutamd ājanmasaṃcitāt pāpān mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥd bhīṣmaparva idaṃ śrutvā śatabhojyaṃ tu dāpayetd sarvatīrthaphalaṃ caiva sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhetd etad vai parvadānaṃ ca dattvā svarṇādidakṣiṇāmd samāhitaphalāvāptir jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥd aśvamedhasahasrasya rājasūyaśatasya cad gavāṃ koṭipradānasya phalaṃ syād bhīṣmaparvaṇid bhīṣmaparva idaṃ śrutvā pūjayed yas tu vācakamd tena brahmā ca rudraś ca viṣṇuś ca vasavas tathād pūjitā ṛṣayaḥ sarve pitaraś ca sahāgnibhiḥd prasanne vācake vipre prasannāḥ sarvadevatāḥd dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ sa phalaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥd pañca ślokasahasrāṇi tathā hy aṣṭau śatāni cad ślokāś ca caturāśītiḥ proktā vyāsena dhīmatād śraddhayā parayā yukto bhīṣmaparva śṛṇoti yaḥd mucyate brahmahatyāyā jayaṃ vai labhate dhruvamd brāhmaṇān bhojayet samyag vastrālaṃkāragodhanaiḥd pūjayec caiva vaktāraṃ bhīṣmaparvaṇi vai gṛhī
